### [1] [Maximally heavy dynamics in the causal diamond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28853)
*David Poland,Gordon Rogelberg*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We introduce a rigorous framework to study four-point correlation functions of identical operators with infinite scaling dimension in CFTs, using 'maximally heavy observables' that are analogous to thermodynamic quantities. These observables are tightly constrained by crossing symmetry and unitarity, revealing dynamical phase transitions that probe bulk locality and connect to large central charge physics.

我们引入了一个严格框架，用于研究具有无限标度维数的CFT算符的四点关联函数，采用类似于热力学量的“极大重观测值”。这些观测量受到交叉对称性和幺正性的严格约束，揭示了动力学相变，从而探知体空间局域性，并与大中心荷情况下的物理相联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Operators with infinite scaling dimension dominate certain high-energy regimes in CFTs and are crucial for understanding holographic duals involving black holes and flat-space limits. However, their correlation functions are difficult to analyze due to divergent dimensions; thus, a systematic approach is needed to extract meaningful physical data in this extreme limit.

具有无限标度维数的算符在CFT的某些高能区域中占主导地位，对于理解涉及黑洞和平坦空间极限的全息对偶至关重要。然而，由于维度发散，其关联函数难以分析，因此需要一种系统方法来在此极端极限下提取有意义的物理信息。

Method: We define 'maximally heavy observables' as rescaled correlators that remain finite in the infinite-dimension limit, analogous to intensive quantities in statistical mechanics. We analyze these using conformal bootstrap techniques, imposing crossing symmetry and unitarity constraints. The structure of the four-point function is studied through analyticity, operator product expansion (OPE) dominance, and connections to 2D modular invariance in specific examples.

我们将“极大重观测值”定义为在无限维极限下保持有限的重缩关联函数，类似于统计力学中的强度量。通过共形bootstrap技术，施加交叉对称性和幺正性约束来分析这些量。利用解析性、算符乘积展开（OPE）主导性以及在特定例子中与二维模不变性的联系，研究四点函数的结构。

Result: We derive universal constraints on maximally heavy four-point functions, showing that they exhibit sharp dynamical phase transitions controlled by bulk kinematics. In solvable cases—such as generalized free fields and chiral correlators—these transitions reflect the emergence of semiclassical spacetime geometries. For maximal giant gravitons in planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM, we find exact agreement with bulk scattering processes near black hole horizons.

我们推导出对极大重四点函数的普适约束，表明它们表现出由体空间运动学控制的动力学相变。在可解情形（如广义自由场和手征关联函数）中，这些相变反映了半经典时空几何的出现。对于平面$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM中的极大巨引力子，我们发现其结果与黑洞视界附近的体空间散射过程完全一致。

Conclusion: Maximally heavy observables provide a powerful new lens for probing quantum gravity via CFT correlation functions at infinite scaling dimension. They unify diverse phenomena—from OPE saturation to modular physics—and reveal how bulk locality and geometry emerge dynamically from abstract CFT data.

极大重观测值为通过无限标度维数下的CFT关联函数研究量子引力提供了强大新视角。它们统一了从OPE饱和到模物理等多种现象，并揭示了体空间局域性和几何如何从抽象的CFT数据中动态涌现。

Abstract: Correlation functions of CFT operators with infinite scaling dimension are rich, multifaceted objects that describe physics ranging across classical holography, black hole dynamics, and flat-space scattering amplitudes. In this work, we provide a rigorous framework for characterizing the space of four-point functions of identical operators with infinite dimension in terms of well-defined ``maximally heavy observables,'' which are akin to intrinsic quantities describing statistical systems in the thermodynamic limit. These observables are highly constrained by crossing symmetry and unitarity, and give novel insights into the locality of bulk states through the emergence of dynamical phase transitions. In certain cases, these results connect directly to the more familiar picture of torus partition functions at large central charge. We apply our framework to a number of illustrative examples including generalized free fields, chiral product correlators, and maximal giant gravitons in planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM.

</details>


### [2] [Holographic two-point functions of heavy operators revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28880)
*Prokopii Anempodistov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper revisits the holographic computation of two-point functions for $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS chiral primary operators with large scaling dimensions ($\Delta \sim N$ or $\Delta \sim N^2$) in $\mathcal{N}=4$ $SU(N)$ SYM using Type IIB supergravity. It resolves prior ambiguities by proposing new boundary terms in the D3-brane action for giant gravitons, ensuring a well-defined variational problem and correct reproduction of gauge theory two-point functions. For $\Delta \sim N^2$, the two-point function is computed via the Gibbons-Hawking-York term in the bubbling geometry.

本文重新研究了在 $\mathcal{N}=4$ $SU(N)$ SYM 中使用 IIB 型超引力全息计算具有大标度维数（$\Delta \sim N$ 或 $\Delta \sim N^2$）的 $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS 普适初级算符的两点函数。通过为巨引力子的 D3-膜作用量引入新的边界项，解决了先前文献中的歧义，确保变分问题良好定义，并正确复现规范理论中的两点函数。对于 $\Delta \sim N^2$ 的情形，通过在 Lin-Lunin-Maldacena 泡沫几何背景下的伪作用量中计算 Gibbons-Hawking-York 边界项得到两点函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous holographic computations of two-point functions for giant graviton operators suffered from ambiguities due to ill-defined variational problems in the D3-brane action. These ambiguities led to incorrect or inconsistent results. The motivation is to resolve these issues by identifying missing boundary terms in the action that are required for a consistent holographic dictionary, particularly for $\frac{1}{2}$-, $\frac{1}{4}$-, and $\frac{1}{8}$-BPS giant gravitons. Additionally, extending the analysis to operators with $\Delta \sim N^2$ tests the robustness of the holographic framework at higher energy scales.

此前对巨引力子算符的全息两点函数计算因 D3-膜作用量中变分问题未良好定义而存在歧义，导致结果不一致或错误。动机是通过识别作用量中缺失的边界项来解决这些问题，这些边界项对于建立一致的全息字典至关重要，尤其针对 $\frac{1}{2}$-、$\frac{1}{4}$- 和 $\frac{1}{8}$-BPS 巨引力子。此外，将分析扩展到 $\Delta \sim N^2$ 的算符可检验全息框架在更高能标下的稳健性。

Method: The authors analyze the D3-brane action for giant gravitons in Type IIB supergravity and argue for the inclusion of additional boundary terms derived from the path integral formalism to make the variational problem well-defined. These terms are shown to cancel boundary variations, leading to a consistent on-shell action. The corrected action is then used to compute the two-point function of $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS operators with $\Delta \sim N$. For operators with $\Delta \sim N^2$, the two-point function is obtained by evaluating the Gibbons-Hawking-York (GHY) boundary term in the Type IIB pseudo-action within the Lin-Lunin-Maldacena (LLM) bubbling geometry background.

作者分析了 IIB 型超引力中巨引力子的 D3-膜作用量，论证应加入从路径积分形式导出的额外边界项以使变分问题良好定义。这些项被证明可抵消边界变分，从而得到一致的壳上作用量。修正后的作用量用于计算 $\Delta \sim N$ 的 $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS 算符的两点函数。对于 $\Delta \sim N^2$ 的算符，则通过在 Lin-Lunin-Maldacena (LLM) 泡沫几何背景下的 IIB 型伪作用量中计算 Gibbons-Hawking-York (GHY) 边界项来获得两点函数。

Result: The proposed boundary-corrected D3-brane action yields an on-shell value that correctly reproduces the two-point function of $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS chiral primary operators with $\Delta \sim N$, resolving previous discrepancies. For $\Delta \sim N^2$, the GHY term in the LLM bubbling geometry successfully computes the two-point function, confirming the validity of the holographic approach for highly excited states. The boundary terms are shown to be essential for consistency and are argued to arise naturally from the quantum path integral.

所提出的带边界修正的 D3-膜作用量给出的壳上值正确复现了 $\Delta \sim N$ 的 $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS 普适初级算符的两点函数，解决了以往的差异。对于 $\Delta \sim N^2$，LLM 泡沫几何中的 GHY 项成功计算出两点函数，验证了全息方法对高度激发态的有效性。边界项被证明对一致性至关重要，并被认为自然源于量子路径积分。

Conclusion: Boundary terms in the D3-brane action, derived from consistency of the variational principle and path integral considerations, are crucial for accurate holographic computation of two-point functions of giant graviton operators. Their inclusion resolves long-standing ambiguities and ensures agreement with gauge theory predictions. The success of the GHY term computation in the LLM geometry extends the reach of holography to operators with $\Delta \sim N^2$, reinforcing the robustness of the AdS/CFT correspondence for heavy operators.

D3-膜作用量中的边界项（源自变分原理和路径积分一致性的要求）对于巨引力子算符两点函数的精确全息计算至关重要。其引入解决了长期存在的歧义，并确保与规范理论预测的一致性。在 LLM 几何中使用 GHY 项的成功计算扩展了全息原理对 $\Delta \sim N^2$ 算符的适用范围，强化了 AdS/CFT 对偶在重算符情形下的稳健性。

Abstract: In this paper we investigate the holographic computation of the two-point functions of $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS chiral primary operators with scaling dimensions $Δ\sim N$ or $Δ\sim N^2$ in $\mathcal{N}=4$ $SU(N)$ SYM using Type IIB supergravity. First we consider giant graviton operators, resolving ambiguities in the previous literature on holographic computation of the two-point function, and make a new proposal for this calculation. We argue that the D3-brane action for the giant gravitons (as well as for their $\frac{1}{4}$- and $\frac{1}{8}$-BPS counterparts) should contain additional boundary terms which arise naturally from the path integral and which are required to make the variational problem well-defined. We derive the form of these terms and show that the corrected action has an on-shell value that reproduces the two-point function of the gauge theory operators. Then we consider operators with $Δ\sim N^2$ and calculate the two-point function by evaluating the Gibbons-Hawking-York boundary term in the Type IIB pseudo-action in the Lin-Lunin-Maldacena bubbling geometry background.

</details>


### [3] [Kaluza-Klein trombone mass matrices and universal class $\mathcal{R}$ operator spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28908)
*Martin Pico,Oscar Varela*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We determine universal sectors of the light operator spectrum in all $A_{N-1}$ superconformal field theories $T_N[\Sigma_3]$ of class $\mathcal{R}$, where $\Sigma_3$ is a compact hyperbolic three-manifold, in the large $N$ limit. Using holography, we map this to a Kaluza-Klein (KK) spectral analysis on dual anti-de Sitter backgrounds from wrapped M5-branes. By leveraging recently constructed $D=4$ $\mathcal{N}=8$ supergravities and exceptional generalised geometry techniques, we derive and diagonalise KK mass matrices associated with trombone gaugings, identifying universal KK states. We provide a method to isolate globally-defined subsectors within these locally-defined spectra.

我们确定了在所有属于 $\mathcal{R}$ 类的 $A_{N-1}$ 超共形场论 $T_N[\Sigma_3]$ 中普遍存在的轻算符谱（light operator spectrum）的普适部分，其中 $\Sigma_3$ 是一个紧致双曲三维流形，分析在大 $N$ 极限下进行。通过全息对偶，我们将该问题映射到与M5膜缠绕构型相关的反德西特背景上的卡鲁扎-克莱因（Kaluza-Klein, KK）谱分析。利用最近构造的 $D=4$ $\mathcal{N}=8$ 超引力理论以及例外广义几何/场论中的谱技术，我们推导出当低维母体最大超引力涉及号角（trombone）缩放对称性定标时所对应的KK质量矩阵，并对其对角化以找出普适的KK态。这些普适谱一般仅局域定义，我们给出了从中提取全局定义子空间的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study of universal features in quantum field theories, especially in strongly-coupled regimes, is a central goal in theoretical physics. In the context of 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFTs arising from M5-branes wrapped on hyperbolic 3-manifolds ($T_N[\Sigma_3]$ theories), understanding which light operators appear universally—i.e., independent of specific details of $\Sigma_3$—can shed light on the intrinsic structure of the theory space. At large $N$, holographic duality provides a powerful tool: such theories are dual to certain AdS$_4$ solutions in M-theory. However, extracting precise operator spectra requires detailed knowledge of the Kaluza-Klein (KK) reduction over internal geometries. Recent advances in $D=4$ $\mathcal{N}=8$ supergravity constructions using exceptional generalised geometry allow for systematic KK spectral analysis, even in cases involving non-standard gaugings like the trombone symmetry. Our motivation is to exploit these tools to identify and characterise universal sectors of the operator spectrum across all $T_N[\Sigma_3]$ theories.

在量子场论中研究普适性特征，尤其是在强耦合区域，是理论物理的核心目标之一。对于由M5膜缠绕双曲三维流形得到的3维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 超共形场论（即 $T_N[\Sigma_3]$ 理论），理解哪些轻算符是普适出现的——即不依赖于 $\Sigma_3$ 的具体细节——有助于揭示理论空间的内在结构。在大 $N$ 极限下，全息对偶提供了一个强有力的工具：这些理论对偶于M理论中的某些AdS$_4$ 解。然而，要精确提取算符谱，需要对内部几何进行卡鲁扎-克莱因（KK）约化的详细知识。近年来基于例外广义几何构造的 $D=4$ $\mathcal{N}=8$ 超引力理论进展使得系统性的KK谱分析成为可能，即使在涉及如号角（trombone）对称性这类非标准定标的情况下亦然。我们的动机正是利用这些新工具，在所有 $T_N[\Sigma_3]$ 理论中识别并刻画算符谱的普适部分。

Method: We employ the holographic correspondence between 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFTs of class $\mathcal{R}$ and M-theory on AdS$_4 \times M_7$, where $M_7$ is a warped product involving $\Sigma_3$. In the large $N$ limit, the dual geometry admits a consistent truncation to a lower-dimensional maximal supergravity in $D=4$, specifically $\mathcal{N}=8$ supergravity with non-trivial gaugings. Crucially, the relevant gauging involves the trombone scaling symmetry, which complicates standard KK reduction but can be handled using recent formulations based on Exceptional Field Theory (ExFT). We construct the full Kaluza-Klein mass matrices for scalar and vector fluctuations around the background by applying ExFT techniques adapted to trombone gaugings. These matrices are then diagonalised to extract the spectrum of low-lying (light) modes. To distinguish globally-defined operators from merely locally-defined ones, we impose invariance under the mapping class group of $\Sigma_3$, thereby isolating universal, physical sectors of the spectrum.

我们使用 $\mathcal{R}$ 类3维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 超共形场论与M理论在 AdS$_4 \times M_7$ 上的全息对应，其中 $M_7$ 是包含 $\Sigma_3$ 的扭曲积。在大 $N$ 极限下，对偶几何允许一致截断至四维低维最大超引力，具体为具有非平凡定标的 $\mathcal{N}=8$ 超引力。关键的是，相关定标涉及号角（trombone）缩放对称性，这使标准KK约化变得复杂，但可通过基于例外场论（Exceptional Field Theory, ExFT）的新近公式处理。我们应用适配于号角定标的ExFT技术，构建背景周围标量和矢量涨落的完整卡鲁扎-克莱因质量矩阵。随后对这些矩阵进行对角化，以提取低能（轻）模式的谱。为了区分全局定义的算符与仅局域定义的算符，我们施加 $\Sigma_3$ 映射类群的不变性条件，从而分离出谱中的普适物理子空间。

Result: We derive explicit Kaluza-Klein mass matrices for scalar and vector perturbations in the presence of trombone gaugings, and solve their eigenvalue problems to obtain the universal light spectrum. The resulting spectrum includes towers of states with masses parametrically suppressed at large $N$, corresponding to protected operators in the dual CFT$_3$. These states are organised into representations of the $\mathcal{N}=2$ superconformal algebra. Importantly, while the full KK spectrum may depend on local data of $\Sigma_3$, we identify a subset of modes that are invariant under large diffeomorphisms (i.e., elements of the mapping class group), and thus define globally universal operators. We provide a concrete prescription—based on harmonic analysis over $\Sigma_3$ and group averaging—to project onto these globally-defined sectors.

我们推导出了在号角定标存在下标量和矢量扰动的显式卡鲁扎-克莱因质量矩阵，并求解其本征值问题，得到了普适的轻谱。所得谱包括一系列在大 $N$ 下质量被参数抑制的状态，对应于对偶CFT$_3$ 中的保护算符。这些状态构成了 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 超共形代数的表示。重要的是，尽管完整的KK谱可能依赖于 $\Sigma_3$ 的局域数据，但我们识别出一组在大微分同胚（即映射类群元素）下不变的模式，因此定义了全局普适的算符。我们提出了一个具体的方案——基于 $\Sigma_3$ 上的调和分析与群平均——来投影到这些全局定义的子空间。

Conclusion: Universal sectors of the light operator spectrum in $T_N[\Sigma_3]$ theories are determined by the interplay between higher-dimensional geometry, supergravity gaugings (particularly the trombone symmetry), and global topology of $\Sigma_3$. By combining holography, Exceptional Field Theory, and spectral geometry, we have identified a set of universally present light operators that survive at large $N$. These arise from KK modes whose wavefunctions are invariant under the mapping class group of $\Sigma_3$. Our results provide a step toward a classification of universal physics in 3d SCFTs via geometric engineering and suggest that ExFT methods are essential for precision holography in non-standard gauged supergravities.

$T_N[\Sigma_3]$ 理论中轻算符谱的普适部分由高维几何、超引力定标（特别是号角对称性）与 $\Sigma_3$ 全局拓扑之间的相互作用决定。通过结合全息原理、例外场论（Exceptional Field Theory, ExFT）与谱几何，我们识别出一组在大 $N$ 下始终存在的普适轻算符，它们来源于在 $\Sigma_3$ 映射类群下不变的KK模式波函数。我们的结果为通过几何工程对三维超共形场论中的普适物理进行分类迈出了重要一步，并表明在非标准定标超引力中，ExFT方法对于实现精确全息至关重要。

Abstract: We determine universal sectors of the light operator spectrum that are present in all A$_{N-1}$ superconformal field theories $T_N[Σ_3]$ of class $\mathcal{R}$, with $Σ_3$ a compact hyperbolic three-manifold. We do this at large $N$ by holographically mapping the problem to a Kaluza-Klein spectral analysis over previously known dual anti-de Sitter backgrounds related to wrapped M5-brane configurations. Associated to these, $D=4$ $\mathcal{N}=8$ supergravities have been recently constructed that allow for the application of spectral techniques based on exceptional generalised geometry/field theory. We derive the Kaluza-Klein mass matrices that arise when the seed lower-dimensional maximal supergravity involves gaugings of the trombone scaling symmetry, as pertains to the case at hand, and diagonalise them to find the universal Kaluza-Klein states. In general, these universal spectra are only defined locally, and we give a prescription to isolate globally-defined sectors therein.

</details>


### [4] [Anomaly-mediated Scalar Gravitational Interactions and the Coupling of Conformal Sectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28966)
*Claudio Corianò,Stefano Lionetti,Dario Melle,Leonardo Torcellini*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We study the anomaly-induced activation of a gauge-invariant scalar mode in General Relativity, the conformalon, via $2\to2$ scattering amplitudes. Using anomalous three-point functions ($TTT$, $TJJ$) coupled by single-graviton exchange, we show that the conformalon contributes as an effective scalar correction suppressed by the Planck scale. The interaction arises from nonlocal massless insertions sewn by the scalar part of the graviton propagator, yielding contact terms. The result respects conformal Ward identities and exhibits a double-copy structure in the eikonal limit.

我们通过$2\to2$散射振幅研究广义相对论中反常诱导的规范不变标量模式——共形子（conformalon）的激活。利用由单引力子交换耦合的反常三点函数（$TTT$、$TJJ$），我们发现共形子作为被普朗克能标压制的有效标量修正出现。该相互作用源于通过引力子传播子的标量部分连接的非局域无质量插入项，最终表现为接触项。结果满足动量空间中的共形Ward恒等式，并在eikonal极限下表现出双拷贝结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The emergence of scalar degrees of freedom in quantum gravity, particularly those tied to trace anomalies, remains a subtle and often obscured phenomenon in local formulations of General Relativity. While the nonlocal Polyakov or anomaly action suggests such modes, their physical interpretation—especially in scattering processes—is unclear. We aim to isolate and characterize a gauge-invariant scalar mode (the conformalon) directly in momentum space using on-shell scattering amplitudes, clarifying its origin in anomaly-induced dynamics and its observational footprint in gravitational and electromagnetic processes.

量子引力中标量自由度的出现，特别是与迹反常相关的模式，在广义相对论的局域表述中仍是一个微妙且常被掩盖的现象。尽管非局域的Polyakov或反常作用量暗示了这类模式的存在，但其物理诠释——尤其是在散射过程中的表现——尚不清晰。我们的目标是使用在壳散射振幅在动量空间中直接分离并刻画一种规范不变的标量模式（共形子），阐明其在反常诱导动力学中的起源及其在引力与电磁过程中的可观测效应。

Method: We compute $2\to2$ scattering amplitudes involving gravitons and photons by sewing anomalous three-point correlation functions ($\langle TTT \rangle$, $\langle TJJ \rangle$) via single-graviton exchange derived from the quadratic Einstein--Hilbert action. The conformalon mode is identified as the scalar component of the graviton propagator in de Donder gauge. Nonlocal anomaly-induced insertions on external legs are implemented through effective inverse-d'Alembertian operators ($\Box^{-1}$), which are consistently matched to the spin decomposition of flat-space conformal Ward identities in momentum space. The resulting 4-point interactions are reduced to local contact terms via integration by parts, with suppression scale set by $M_{\rm Pl}$. Eikonal phase corrections and spin decompositions are analyzed in impact-parameter space.

我们通过将反常三点关联函数（$\langle TTT \rangle$、$\langle TJJ \rangle$）利用从爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量二次展开导出的单引力子交换进行缝合，计算涉及引力子和光子的$2\to2$散射振幅。共形子模式被识别为de Donder规范下引力子传播子的标量分量。通过有效逆达朗贝尔算符（$\Box^{-1}$）在外腿上实现反常诱导的非局域插入项，并与动量空间中平直时空共形Ward恒等式的自旋分解一致匹配。所得到的四点相互作用通过分部积分简化为局域接触项，压制尺度由$M_{\rm Pl}$设定。在动量转移空间中分析eikonal相位修正和自旋分解。

Result: The conformalon appears as a gauge-invariant, massless scalar degree of freedom activated by trace anomalies, contributing to scattering amplitudes through Planck-suppressed effective interactions. The amplitude construction correctly reproduces the tensor structures dictated by conformal symmetry via momentum-space Ward identities. The 4-point amplitude reduces to contact interactions suppressed by $M_{\rm Pl}^2$, and in the eikonal regime generates corrections to the logarithmic phase in impact-parameter space. Notably, the anomaly-mediated graviton scattering amplitude exhibits a double-copy-like structure, hinting at a deeper connection with color-kinematics duality.

共形子表现为一种由迹反常激活的规范不变无质量标量自由度，通过被普朗克能标压制的有效相互作用参与散射振幅。振幅构造正确复现了动量空间Ward恒等式所规定的共形对称性张量结构。四点振幅简化为被$M_{\rm Pl}^2$压制的接触相互作用，在eikonal区域生成对动量转移空间中对数相位的修正。值得注意的是，反常介导的引力子散射振幅表现出类似双拷贝（double-copy）的结构，暗示其与色-动力学对偶之间可能存在更深层联系。

Conclusion: The conformalon mode, though not a fundamental field, emerges as a physical effect in on-shell scattering due to quantum anomalies. Its contribution is mediated through the scalar sector of the graviton propagator and is consistently encoded in anomaly-induced nonlocal operators. The resulting effective interactions are predictive, respect gauge and conformal symmetry, and are testable in high-energy scattering regimes. The observed double-copy structure suggests a possible reformulation of anomaly-mediated processes in gravity using modern amplitude techniques.

共形子模式虽非基本场，但由于量子反常而在在壳散射中表现为物理效应。其贡献通过引力子传播子的标量部分传递，并由反常诱导的非局域算符一致编码。所得到的有效相互作用具有可预测性，保持规范与共形对称性，并可在高能散射区域中检验。所观察到的双拷贝结构提示，或许可以使用现代振幅技术重新表述引力中反常介导的过程。

Abstract: We investigate the anomaly-induced activation of a gauge-invariant scalar degree of freedom in General Relativity, the conformalon mode, directly at the level of \(2\to2\) scattering amplitudes. The analysis couples anomalous three-point functions of conformal sectors, involving gravitons \((TTT)\) and Abelian gauge currents \((TJJ)\), through single-graviton exchange derived from the quadratic expansion of the Einstein--Hilbert action. Unlike related treatments based on the nonlocal anomaly action, these interactions are suppressed by the Planck scale. We show that the conformalon, invariant under linearized diffeomorphisms, admits an interpretation as an effective scalar correction to scattering amplitudes, both in virtual exchange channels and in effective real-emission processes. Around flat space, this behaviour arises from anomaly-induced nonlocal massless insertions on the external graviton and photon legs of the three-point functions, sewn through the scalar component of the graviton propagator in de Donder gauge. The resulting anomaly-mediated \(4\)-point interaction reduces to contact terms, with the Planck mass setting the suppression scale. The construction consistently matches the spin decomposition of flat-space conformal Ward identities in momentum space, which determine the vertices, with the corresponding spin decomposition of the graviton propagator. In the eikonal limit, these interactions generate contact corrections to the leading logarithmic phase in impact-parameter space. We further show that anomaly-mediated \(2\to2\) graviton amplitudes associated with the virtual exchange of such modes exhibit a characteristic double-copy structure.

</details>


### [5] [What U Can Do: New Solutions and New Challenges Beyond Leading Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29151)
*Yi Pang,Robert J. Saskowski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: Recent progress in utilizing T-duality-induced hidden symmetries to construct higher-derivative-corrected solutions in string theory is reviewed, along with challenges posed by non-perturbative effects when applying similar methods to U-duality.

近期研究综述了利用T对偶诱导的隐藏对称性构建高阶导数修正解的进展，以及在将类似方法应用于U对偶时非微扰效应带来的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: String theories possess intrinsic dualities that manifest as hidden symmetries in their low-energy effective theories, offering powerful tools for generating exact solutions in supergravity. 弦理论具有内在对偶性，表现为低能有效理论中的隐藏对称性，为生成超引力中的精确解提供了强大工具。动机是将这些基于对称性的解生成技术扩展到包含高阶导数修正，以捕捉超越经典极限的量子和弦效应。

Method: The method involves exploiting T-duality transformations in the low-energy effective action to generate new solutions from known ones, systematically incorporating higher-derivative terms order by order. For U-duality, the approach attempts to lift this procedure to include non-perturbative effects, though complications arise due to the lack of a fully understood off-shell formulation of U-duality-invariant actions.

该方法利用低能有效作用量中的T对偶变换，从已知解系统地逐阶生成包含高阶导数项的新解。对于U对偶，尝试将此过程提升以包含非微扰效应，但由于缺乏对U对偶不变作用量的完整离壳表述，出现了复杂性。

Result: T-duality-based methods have successfully generated higher-derivative-corrected supergravity solutions, such as $\alpha'$-corrected black holes and branes. However, extending this to U-duality faces obstacles: non-perturbative contributions (e.g., from instantons or D-branes) break naive symmetry enhancement, and the absence of a complete EFT incorporating all U-duality multiplets limits predictive power.

基于T对偶的方法已成功生成高阶导数修正的超引力解，如$\alpha'$修正的黑洞和膜。然而，推广到U对偶面临障碍：非微扰贡献（例如来自瞬子或D膜）破坏了朴素的对称性增强，且缺乏包含所有U对偶多重态的完整有效场论（EFT），限制了预测能力。

Conclusion: Hidden symmetries from T-duality provide a robust framework for constructing corrected solutions in string theory, but extending this to U-duality requires deeper understanding of non-perturbative physics and the off-shell structure of duality-invariant theories.

来自T对偶的隐藏对称性为构建弦理论中修正解提供了坚实框架，但推广到U对偶需要对非微扰物理及对偶不变理论的离壳结构有更深入的理解。

Abstract: String theories naturally exhibit dualities that lead to hidden symmetries in the low-energy effective description, which have been used to great effect to generate supergravity solutions. We review recent progress in using hidden symmetries arising from T-duality to generate higher-derivative-corrected solutions, as well as the problems that arise from non-perturbative effects when extending this paradigm to hidden symmetries arising from U-duality.

### [7] [Spontaneous BRST symmetry breaking in infrared QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29401)
*Angelo Raffaele Fazio,Adam Smetana*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We propose a new effective Lagrangian for low-energy Yang--Mills theory based on spontaneous BRST and anti-BRST symmetry breaking, using a Fujikawa model coupled to elementary gluon and ghost fields. The model generates effective gluon and ghost masses and reproduces the Curci--Ferrari model upon symmetry breaking. An extended nilpotent BRST symmetry is introduced, which unifies elementary and composite sectors and remains hidden after spontaneous breaking.

我们基于BRST和反BRST对称性的自发破缺，提出了一种新的低能杨-米尔斯理论有效拉格朗日量，采用与基本胶子和鬼场耦合的藤川模型。该模型生成有效的胶子和鬼质量，并在对称性破缺后重现Curci-Ferrari模型。引入了一个扩展的幂零BRST对称性，统一了基本场和复合场部分，在自发破缺后成为隐藏对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The infrared behavior of Yang--Mills theory remains challenging due to the failure of perturbation theory and the emergence of dynamical mass scales. The Curci--Ferrari model successfully describes massive gluons and ghosts but relies on a non-nilpotent BRST symmetry, which obscures the quantum consistency. We aim to derive this model from a more fundamental framework with a nilpotent extended BRST symmetry and provide a field-theoretic origin for the emergent masses via spontaneous BRST symmetry breaking.

杨-米尔斯理论的红外行为因微扰论失效和动力学质量尺度的出现而具有挑战性。Curci-Ferrari模型成功描述了有质量的胶子和鬼场，但依赖于非幂零的BRST对称性，这模糊了量子一致性。我们的目标是从具有幂零扩展BRST对称性的更基本框架中推导出该模型，并通过BRST对称性的自发破缺为涌现质量提供场论起源。

Method: We construct an effective Lagrangian by coupling the elementary Yang--Mills sector (gluons and ghosts) to a Fujikawa sector that transforms under BRST and anti-BRST symmetries. The Fujikawa fields are interpreted as composites of gluons and ghosts. Requiring both BRST and anti-BRST invariance leads to two massless Nambu--Goldstone modes. Spontaneous breaking of these symmetries generates effective masses. To restore nilpotency, we introduce an extended-BRST symmetry that mixes elementary and Fujikawa fields. The physical Lagrangian emerges after spontaneous symmetry breaking, where the elementary sector reduces to the Curci--Ferrari model.

我们通过将基本杨-米尔斯部分（胶子和鬼场）与在BRST和反BRST对称下变换的藤川部分耦合来构建有效拉格朗日量。藤川场被解释为胶子和鬼场的复合体。要求BRST和反BRST不变性导致两个无质量的Nambu-Goldstone模。这些对称性的自发破缺产生有效质量。为了恢复幂零性，我们引入一个混合基本场和藤川场的扩展BRST对称性。在对称性自发破缺后，物理拉格朗日量显现，其中基本部分简化为Curci-Ferrari模型。

Result: The resulting effective Lagrangian exhibits spontaneous breaking of both BRST and anti-BRST symmetries, giving rise to two Nambu--Goldstone bosons. The gluon and ghost acquire effective masses dynamically. The Curci--Ferrari model is recovered in the elementary sector after symmetry breaking. The full model possesses a nilpotent extended-BRST symmetry, which becomes hidden (spontaneously broken), explaining the non-nilpotent BRST observed in the Curci--Ferrari model as a remnant.

最终的有效拉格朗日量表现出BRST和反BRST对称性的自发破缺，产生两个Nambu-Goldstone玻色子。胶子和鬼场动态获得有效质量。对称性破缺后，基本部分重现Curci-Ferrari模型。完整模型具有一个幂零的扩展BRST对称性，该对称性变为隐藏（自发破缺），从而解释了Curci-Ferrari模型中观察到的非幂零BRST为残余对称性。

Conclusion: We provide a field-theoretic derivation of the Curci--Ferrari model through spontaneous BRST and anti-BRST symmetry breaking within an extended framework featuring a nilpotent extended-BRST symmetry. The emergence of gluon and ghost masses is tied to the appearance of Nambu--Goldstone modes from symmetry breaking. This approach clarifies the algebraic structure of the Curci--Ferrari model and embeds it into a more consistent quantum field theory framework with exact (but hidden) nilpotent symmetry.

我们通过在一个具有幂零扩展BRST对称性的扩展框架内实现BRST和反BRST对称性的自发破缺，为Curci-Ferrari模型提供了场论推导。胶子和鬼场质量的出现与对称性破缺产生的Nambu-Goldstone模相关联。该方法阐明了Curci-Ferrari模型的代数结构，并将其嵌入到具有精确（但隐藏）幂零对称性的更一致的量子场论框架中。

Abstract: We present a novel proposal for the effective Lagrangian of the low-energy Yang--Mills quantum field theory. The proposed effective Lagrangian exhibits the spontaneous BRST symmetry breaking. We built the Fujikawa model that we couple to the Yang--Mills elementary field sector, motivated by the analogy with Chiral Quark Model. We interpret the Fujikawa fields as effective fields composite of the elementary gluon and ghost fields. In order to justify the existence of two massless Nambu--Goldstone modes among the Fujikawa fields, we require not only the BRST but also the anti-BRST invariance of the effective Lagrangian, both to be spontaneously broken. The most striking consequence of that is the emergence of the effective gluon and ghost masses. We reproduce the Curci--Ferrari model as a special case of our effective model upon the spontaneous BRST symmetry breaking. In order to reproduce also the non-nilpotent modified BRST symmetry, characteristic for the Curci--Ferrari model, we modify our effective Lagrangian to be invariant with respect to the extended-BRST symmetry, which mixes the elementary and Fujikawa field sectors, and which is nilpotent. The Curci--Ferrari is reproduced by the elementary field sector of the resulting Lagrangian. The remaining Fujikawa's field dependent terms guarantee the underlying nilpotent extended-BRST symmetry, which is now hidden in the sense of the spontaneous symmetry breaking.

### [8] [Cosmological brick walls & quantum chaotic dynamics of de Sitter horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29443)
*José M. Begines,Suman Das,Hyun-Sik Jeong,Juan F. Pedraza*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We apply the brick wall model to de Sitter and Schwarzschild-de Sitter spacetimes, computing normal modes of a massless scalar field and analyzing spectral statistics via level-spacing distribution, spectral form factor, and Krylov complexity. Pure de Sitter shows chaotic signatures despite non-Wigner-Dyson statistics; in Schwarzschild-de Sitter, two near-horizon sectors lead to superposed spectra with non-zero level spacing at zero but still exhibit a linear ramp and Krylov complexity peak, indicating residual chaos.

我们将在纯de Sitter和Schwarzschild-de Sitter时空中应用砖墙模型，计算无质量标量场的正规模，并通过能级间距分布、谱形因子和Krylov复杂度分析谱统计。纯de Sitter空间显示出混沌特征，尽管其不遵循Wigner-Dyson分布；在Schwarzschild-de Sitter情况下，两个近 horizon 区域导致叠加谱，在零间距处出现非零值，但仍表现出线性爬升和明显的Krylov复杂度峰值，表明残余混沌的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The brick wall model provides a tractable way to study quantum effects near horizons, especially in holographic contexts. With renewed interest in de Sitter holography and black hole information puzzles, understanding spectral signatures of chaos in spacetimes with both event and cosmological horizons—such as Schwarzschild-de Sitter—is crucial for diagnosing quantum chaotic dynamics beyond standard random matrix theory expectations.

砖墙模型为研究视界附近的量子效应（特别是在全息背景下）提供了一个可处理的方法。随着对de Sitter全息和黑洞信息悖论的重新关注，理解具有事件视界和宇宙学视界的时空（如Schwarzschild-de Sitter）中混沌的谱特征，对于超越标准随机矩阵理论预期的量子混沌动力学诊断至关重要。

Method: We quantize a massless scalar field in pure de Sitter and Schwarzschild-de Sitter spacetimes within the brick wall framework, imposing Dirichlet boundary conditions near the horizons. Normal modes are computed analytically in pure dS and numerically in SdS. Spectral statistics—including the nearest-neighbor level-spacing distribution $P(s)$, the spectral form factor $g(t)$, and Krylov complexity $K(t)$—are analyzed to probe chaotic behavior. In SdS, we identify two decoupled near-horizon regions in the WKB regime and study their superposed spectrum.

我们在砖墙框架下对纯de Sitter和Schwarzschild-de Sitter时空中的无质量标量场进行量子化，在视界附近施加Dirichlet边界条件。在纯dS中解析计算正规模，在SdS中数值计算。分析谱统计量，包括最近邻能级间距分布$P(s)$、谱形因子$g(t)$和Krylov复杂度$K(t)$，以探测混沌行为。在SdS的WKB极限下，识别出两个解耦的近视界区域，并研究其叠加谱。

Result: In pure de Sitter space, the spectrum shows long-range correlations indicative of chaos, though $P(s)$ does not follow Wigner-Dyson statistics. In Schwarzschild-de Sitter, the single-particle spectrum splits into two independent subsequences associated with the black hole and cosmological horizons. Their superposition leads to $P(0) > 0$, violating strict level repulsion. However, for small stretched-horizon fluctuations, the spectral form factor $g(t)$ exhibits an approximately linear ramp and Krylov complexity $K(t)$ shows a sharp peak—both hallmarks of chaotic dynamics—despite the absence of conventional level repulsion.

在纯de Sitter空间中，谱显示出长程相关性，表明存在混沌，尽管$P(s)$不遵循Wigner-Dyson统计。在Schwarzschild-de Sitter中，单粒子谱分裂为与黑洞视界和宇宙学视界相关的两个独立子序列。它们的叠加导致$P(0) > 0$，违反了严格的能级排斥。然而，对于足够小的拉伸视界涨落，谱形因子$g(t)$表现出近似线性爬升，Krylov复杂度$K(t)$出现显著峰值——尽管缺乏传统的能级排斥，这二者仍是混沌动力学的标志。

Conclusion: The presence of multiple horizons in Schwarzschild-de Sitter spacetime leads to a superposition of independent near-horizon spectra, resulting in breakdown of strict level repulsion ($P(0)>0$). Nevertheless, the persistence of a linear ramp in the spectral form factor and a peak in Krylov complexity indicates that key signatures of quantum chaos survive. Thus, diagnostics based on temporal evolution in Krylov space or spectral correlations over long timescales are more robust indicators of chaos than short-range level statistics like $P(s)$.

Schwarzschild-de Sitter时空中的多个视界导致独立的近视界谱叠加，从而破坏了严格的能级排斥（$P(0)>0$）。然而，谱形因子中的线性爬升和Krylov复杂度中的峰值持续存在，表明量子混沌的关键特征仍然保留。因此，基于Krylov空间中时间演化或长时间尺度谱相关的诊断方法，比短程能级统计（如$P(s)$）更能可靠地指示混沌。

Abstract: Originally proposed by 't Hooft, the brick wall model has recently reemerged as a useful framework for probing quantum aspects of horizon physics, particularly in the context of holography. In this paper, we apply it to asymptotically de Sitter spacetimes. We compute the normal modes of a massless scalar field in pure de Sitter space and in the Schwarzschild-de Sitter black hole, and analyze the resulting single-particle spectra using the level-spacing distribution, the spectral form factor, and Krylov complexity. In pure de Sitter, the spectrum exhibits clear long-range signatures of chaos despite not obeying a conventional Wigner-Dyson level-spacing distribution. The Schwarzschild-de Sitter case is qualitatively richer: in the WKB regime, where tunneling between the two classically allowed regions is exponentially suppressed, the presence of both an event horizon and a cosmological horizon gives rise to two independent near-horizon sectors, so that the full spectrum is the superposition of two subsequences. As a result, the combined level-spacing distribution develops a nonzero value at $s=0$ even when spectral correlations remain. Nevertheless, for sufficiently small stretched-horizon fluctuations, the superposed spectrum still exhibits an approximately linear ramp in the spectral form factor and a pronounced peak in Krylov complexity. Our results show that the absence of strict level repulsion should not, by itself, be taken as evidence against chaos, and that the spectral form factor and Krylov complexity provide sharper diagnostics of the underlying chaotic dynamics.

</details>


### [9] [Lecture Notes on Symmetry Reduction via the Dressing Field Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29505)
*L. Ravera*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: These notes introduce the Dressing Field Method (DFM) as a systematic approach to symmetry reduction in general-relativistic Gauge Field Theory (gRGFT), enabling the construction of gauge- and diffeomorphism-invariant, relational physical observables. Examples span from Chern-Simons theory to General Relativity.

本文介绍了配饰场方法（Dressing Field Method, DFM）作为广义相对论性规范场论（gRGFT）中对称性约化的系统性框架，可用于构造规范和微分同胚不变的、显关联的物理可观测量。示例涵盖从Chern-Simons理论到广义相对论的多种情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In general-relativistic Gauge Field Theories (gRGFT), the presence of both local gauge symmetries and diffeomorphism invariance complicates the identification of physical observables. Traditional methods often fail to yield manifestly invariant and relational degrees of freedom. The goal is to develop a coherent framework that systematically reduces symmetries to expose physical content.

在广义相对论性规范场论（gRGFT）中，局域规范对称性与微分同胚不变性并存，使得物理可观测量的识别变得复杂。传统方法通常难以得到显不变且关联的动力学自由度。因此，目标是发展一种连贯的框架，系统性地约化对称性以揭示物理内容。

Method: The Dressing Field Method (DFM) is employed to perform symmetry reduction by introducing a 'dressing field' that transforms under the symmetry group in a way that allows composite fields to become invariant. This method is applied to both internal gauge symmetries and spacetime diffeomorphisms, yielding reduced connections and field strengths that are fully invariant. The procedure is illustrated through multiple theoretical examples.

采用配饰场方法（Dressing Field Method, DFM），通过引入一个在对称群下特定变换的“配饰场”，使复合场变为不变量，从而实现对称性约化。该方法同时应用于内部规范对称性和时空微分同胚，导出完全不变的约化联络和场强。此过程通过多个理论实例加以说明。

Result: DFM successfully constructs gauge- and diffeomorphism-invariant observables in a range of theories, including non-Abelian Chern-Simons, Maxwell theory, the Higgs model, supersymmetric theories, and General Relativity. It enables a manifestly relational description of degrees of freedom, particularly in scalar coordinatization where spacetime coordinates emerge from physical fields.

DFM成功地在多种理论中构造出规范与微分同胚不变的可观测量，包括非阿贝尔Chern-Simons理论、Maxwell理论、Higgs模型、超对称理论以及广义相对论。它实现了自由度的显关联描述，尤其在标量坐标化中，时空坐标可由物理场自然导出。

Conclusion: The Dressing Field Method provides a powerful and systematic tool for symmetry reduction in gRGFT, facilitating the extraction of physical, relational observables. Its broad applicability across diverse field theories underscores its potential as a foundational technique in modern theoretical physics.

配饰场方法为gRGFT中的对称性约化提供了强大而系统的工具，有助于提取物理的、关联的可观测量。其在多种场论中的广泛适用性突显了它作为现代理论物理学基础技术的潜力。

Abstract: These notes - prepared for the conference school "Foundations of General-Relativistic Gauge Field Theory", held on March 17-19, 2026 at the Politecnico di Torino - present introductory material on symmetry reduction in general-relativistic Gauge Field Theory (gRGFT) via the Dressing Field Method (DFM). The DFM provides a systematic framework for extracting gauge- and diffeomorphism-invariant, manifestly relational, physical observables and degrees of freedom in gRGFT. A range of illustrative examples are discussed, spanning both Gauge Field Theory and general-relativistic settings. These include applications to non-Abelian Chern-Simons theory, Maxwell electromagnetism, the non-Abelian Higgs model, supersymmetric field theory, General Relativity, and scalar coordinatization.

### [10] [Density matrix of de Sitter JT gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29538)
*Wilfried Buchmuller,Alexander Westphal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity in 2D de Sitter space provides a quantum model for cosmic inflation, where the ground state is found to be a mixed state—contrary to the pure Hartle-Hawking state—based on exact Wheeler-DeWitt solutions and consistent with semiclassical double-trumpet amplitudes and bra-ket wormholes. The universe's size distribution is flat.

Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) 引力在二维 de Sitter 空间中为宇宙暴胀提供了一个量子模型，基于精确的 Wheeler-DeWitt 方程解，发现基态是一个混合态而非纯的 Hartle-Hawking 态，结果与半经典双喇叭振幅及包含 bra-ket 虫洞的复几何研究一致。宇宙尺寸的概率分布是平坦的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand quantum aspects of inflationary cosmology in a simplified setting, particularly the nature of initial conditions and quantum states in de Sitter space, using JT gravity as a solvable model.

为了在简化背景下理解暴胀宇宙学的量子特性，特别是 de Sitter 空间中初始条件和量子态的本质，使用 JT 引力作为一个可解模型。

Method: Exact solutions of the Wheeler-DeWitt equation are derived for JT gravity in 2D de Sitter space. A conditional density matrix is constructed to analyze the quantum state. Semiclassical analysis includes double-trumpet geometries and wave functions for the metric, dilaton, and an inflaton field.

推导了二维 de Sitter 空间中 JT 引力的 Wheeler-DeWitt 方程的精确解。构建了条件密度矩阵以分析量子态。半经典分析包括双喇叭几何以及度规、膨胀子和附加暴胀子场的波函数。

Result: The ground state of the system is a mixed state, not a pure Hartle-Hawking state. This result aligns with the semiclassical double-trumpet amplitude and recent findings on complex geometries with bra-ket wormholes. The probability distribution for the scale factor (size of the universe) is flat, indicating no preferred initial size.

系统的基态是一个混合态，而非纯的 Hartle-Hawking 态。该结果与半经典双喇叭振幅以及关于包含 bra-ket 虫洞的复几何的最新发现一致。尺度因子（宇宙大小）的概率分布是平坦的，表明没有优先的初始大小。

Conclusion: In JT gravity on 2D de Sitter space, quantum initial conditions lead to a mixed ground state, challenging the assumption of a pure-state origin in quantum cosmology. The flat probability distribution suggests a uniform measure over possible initial sizes, supporting a non-perturbative quantum description consistent with emergent spacetime structures like bra-ket wormholes.

在二维 de Sitter 空间的 JT 引力中，量子初始条件导致混合基态，挑战了量子宇宙学中纯态起源的假设。平坦的概率分布表明对可能的初始尺寸具有均匀测度，支持与 bra-ket 虫洞等涌现时空结构一致的非微扰量子描述。

Abstract: Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity in two-dimensional de Sitter space is an intriguing toy model for a quantum mechanical description of an inflationary phase of the universe, including initial conditions. Starting from exact solutions of the Wheeler-DeWitt equation, we study a conditional density matrix of the system. We find that the ground state is a mixed state, rather than a pure Hartle-Hawking state. Our results are consistent with the semiclassical double-trumpet amplitude, and with recent work on complex geometries containing bra-ket wormholes. We also analyze semiclassical wave functions for metric, dilaton, and an additional inflaton field. The probability distribution for the size of the universe is flat.

</details>


### [11] [Critical dimensions and small cycle dominance from all-orders asymptotics of $d$-matrix theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29610)
*Yang Lei,Sanjaye Ramgoolam*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper studies the all-orders asymptotic expansion of the partition function $ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $ for gauge-invariant operators in $ \mathcal{N}=4 $ SYM theory at large $ N $, revealing a geometric structure of poles accumulating at $ |x|=1 $ and a combinatorial organization termed small-cycle dominance. Remarkably, the asymptotic series becomes convergent for $ d \geq d_{\rm crit} = 13 $ (bosonic) or $ 7 $ (fermionic), indicating reconstructability from UV data above critical dimension.

该论文研究了大$ N $极限下$ \mathcal{N}=4 $ SYM理论中规范不变算符的配分函数$ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $的全阶渐近展开，揭示了极点在复平面上以同心圆形式排列并累积于$ |x|=1 $的自然边界上的几何结构，并发现其组合组织方式可归结为“小循环主导”（small-cycle dominance）。值得注意的是，当维度$ d \geq d_{\rm crit} = 13 $（玻色情形）或$ 7 $（费米情形）时，渐近展开实际上是收敛的，表明在此临界维度以上，模型可从高能（UV）极限完全重构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The thermal partition function of $ \mathcal{N}=4 $ super-Yang-Mills theory exhibits a Hagedorn phase transition at $ x = d^{-1} $, which serves as a prototype for understanding black hole thermodynamics via gauge/gravity duality. The structure of gauge-invariant operators—constructed from matrices in the adjoint representation of $ U(N) $—is encoded in the partition function $ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $. Understanding its analytic structure and asymptotic behavior at large $ N $ is crucial for probing the emergence of spacetime geometry and quantum gravity effects in the dual string theory.

$ \mathcal{N}=4 $ 超杨-米尔斯理论的热配分函数在$ x = d^{-1} $处表现出Hagedorn相变，这为通过规范/引力对偶理解黑洞热力学提供了原型。规范不变算符（由$ U(N) $伴随表示下的矩阵构成）的结构被编码在配分函数$ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $中。理解其在大$ N $极限下的解析结构和渐近行为，对于探究对偶弦理论中时空几何与量子引力效应的涌现至关重要。

Method: The authors analyze the full asymptotic expansion of $ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $ using a geometric picture of poles arranged in concentric circles in the complex $ x $-plane, which accumulate into a natural boundary at $ |x| = 1 $. They interpret the order-by-order contributions combinatorially in terms of permutations classifying gauge-invariant traces, identifying an organizing principle called small-cycle dominance, where lower-order terms are dominated by permutations with smaller cycle lengths. Modular properties of the Dedekind eta function are used to analyze coefficients in the expansion, allowing derivation of convergence criteria based on $ d_{\rm crit} $.

作者利用复$ x $平面上极点呈同心圆排列并在$ |x| = 1 $处形成自然边界的几何图像，分析了$ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $的全阶渐近展开。他们将逐阶贡献用分类规范不变迹的置换进行组合解释，识别出一种称为“小循环主导”（small-cycle dominance）的组织原则：低阶项由较小循环长度的置换主导。通过使用Dedekind eta函数的模性质分析展开系数，推导出基于$ d_{\rm crit} $的收敛判据。

Result: The asymptotic expansion of $ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $ is organized by small-cycle dominance, with each order corresponding to increasing cycle sizes in permutation enumeration. This structure persists in refined multi-variable versions of the partition function. Using modular properties of the Dedekind eta function, the authors show that the asymptotic expansion is not merely asymptotic but actually convergent for $ d \geq d_{\rm crit} = 13 $ in the bosonic case and $ d_{\rm crit} = 7 $ for the fermionic analogue. This implies that for $ d \geq d_{\rm crit} $, the full partition function can be reconstructed from high-energy (UV) data alone, while for $ 2 \leq d < d_{\rm crit} $, non-perturbative input is required to recover IR physics.

$ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $的渐近展开按小循环主导方式组织，每一阶对应于置换枚举中循环尺寸的增加。这种结构在包含多个复变量的精细版本配分函数中依然存在。利用Dedekind eta函数的模性质，作者证明该渐近展开在玻色情形下当$ d \geq d_{\rm crit} = 13 $时不仅是渐近的，而且实际上是收敛的；费米情形下临界维度为$ d_{\rm crit} = 7 $。这意味着当$ d \geq d_{\rm crit} $时，完整的配分函数可仅从高能（UV）数据重构，而当$ 2 \leq d < d_{\rm crit} $时，需要额外非微扰输入才能恢复低能（IR）物理。

Conclusion: The geometric and combinatorial analysis of $ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $ reveals a deep connection between permutation symmetry, modular functions, and the convergence of asymptotic expansions in matrix models. The identification of a critical dimension $ d_{\rm crit} $ beyond which the asymptotic series becomes convergent suggests a sharp distinction between reconstructable and non-reconstructable regimes in holographic theories, with implications for UV/IR correspondence in quantum gravity.

对$ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $的几何与组合分析揭示了置换对称性、模函数与矩阵模型中渐近展开收敛性之间的深刻联系。临界维度$ d_{\rm crit} $的发现——超过此值渐近级数变为收敛——暗示了全息理论中可重构与不可重构区域之间的清晰划分，这对量子引力中的UV/IR对应关系具有重要意义。

Abstract: Supersymmetric sectors of $\mathcal{N}=4$ super-Yang-Mills theory motivate the study of the partition function for the counting of gauge-invariant functions of $d=2,3$ matrices transforming under the adjoint action of $U(N)$. The partition function $ \mathcal{Z}_d ( x) $ in the large $N$ limit has a known Hagedorn phase transition at $ x = d^{-1} $ which provides a simple model for the phase structure of the thermal partition function of SYM. We study the all-orders asymptotic expansion of $ \mathcal{Z}_d(x)$ based on a geometric picture of concentric circles of poles in the complex plane accumulating in a natural boundary at $|x| =1$. We find that the order by order structure has a precise combinatorial interpretation organized in terms of increasing cycle size of permutations arising in the enumeration of the invariants. We refer to this organization as small-cycle dominance, and find that it extends to refined versions of the partition functions depending on several complex variables. An analysis of the coefficients in the asymptotic expansion of $ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $ using the modular property of the Dedekind eta function reveals that the asymptotic expansion is actually convergent for $d\ge d_{ \rm crit } = 13$. A fermionic version of $\mathcal{Z}_d (x)$ has an analogous critical dimension of $ d_{ \rm crit} = 7$. This distinction indicates that the partition functions of the matrix models can be completely reconstructed from their high-energy (UV) limit for $d\ge d_{ \rm crit}$ whereas additional input is required to reconstruct the exact coefficients of the low-energy (IR) expansion for $2\le d \le d_{ \rm crit } -1 $.

### [12] [5d Higgs branch and instanton magnetization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29679)
*Amihay Hanany,Alessandro Tomasiello,Elias Van den Driessche*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The Higgs branches of 5d $Sp(k)$ gauge theories with $N_f$ flavours are described by a pair of instantons transforming as pure spinors of $SO(2N_f)$, whose Poisson structure and symplectic geometry reveal an algebraic integrable system; degeneration occurs when spinor annihilators overlap, and the stratification at infinite coupling corresponds to alignment of instanton weights, leading to magnetization and mass generation.

5维 $Sp(k)$ 规范理论在具有 $N_f$ 种味时，其Higgs分支由一对作为 $SO(2N_f)$ 纯旋量变换的瞬子描述，其泊松结构和辛几何揭示了一个代数可积系统；当旋量子湮灭子重叠时发生退化，在无限耦合下Higgs分支的分层对应于瞬子权的对齐，导致磁化和质量生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the structure of Higgs branches in 5d $\mathcal{N}=1$ supersymmetric gauge theories, especially at strong coupling, is crucial for characterizing non-perturbative dynamics and dualities. The paper aims to clarify how symmetry and geometric constraints shape the moduli space, particularly using the language of pure spinors and integrable systems.

理解5维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ 超对称规范理论中Higgs分支的结构，特别是在强耦合下的情况，对于刻画非微扰动力学和对偶性至关重要。本文旨在阐明对称性和几何约束如何塑造模空间，特别是使用纯旋量和可积系统的语言。

Method: The authors use symmetry considerations—particularly $SO(2N_f)$ global symmetry—to constrain the Poisson structure on the Higgs branch. They identify the instantons as pure spinor representations and analyze the degeneracy of the symplectic form via annihilator conditions. The stratification of the moduli space at infinite coupling is studied through the alignment of instanton weights (in the Cartan subalgebra), interpreted as a form of magnetization.

作者利用对称性考虑——特别是 $SO(2N_f)$ 全局对称性——来约束Higgs分支上的泊松结构。他们将瞬子识别为纯旋量表示，并通过湮灭子条件分析辛形式的退化。通过瞬子权（在Cartan子代数中）的对齐来研究无限耦合下模空间的分层，这被解释为一种磁化形式。

Result: It is shown that the Higgs branch is an algebraic integrable system due to the symmetry-constrained Poisson structure. The degeneration of the symplectic form arises when the annihilators of the two pure spinors overlap. At infinite coupling, the stratification corresponds to aligned instanton weights, which leads to non-zero magnetization and the generation of mass for the instantons.

结果表明，由于对称性约束的泊松结构，Higgs分支是一个代数可积系统。当两个纯旋量的湮灭子重叠时，辛形式发生退化。在无限耦合下，分层对应于对齐的瞬子权，导致非零磁化和瞬子质量的生成。

Conclusion: The geometric and algebraic structure of the Higgs branch in 5d $Sp(k)$ theories is deeply tied to representation theory of $SO(2N_f)$ and the physics of instantons as pure spinors. The emergence of algebraic integrability and the physical interpretation of stratification in terms of magnetization provide new insights into strongly coupled regimes.

5维 $Sp(k)$ 理论中Higgs分支的几何与代数结构与 $SO(2N_f)$ 的表示论以及作为纯旋量的瞬子物理密切相关。代数可积性的出现以及分层在磁化方面的物理解释，为强耦合区域提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Higgs branches of 5d $Sp(k)$ theories with $N_f$ flavours, whether at weak or strong coupling, are described by a pair of instantons transforming as pure spinors of $SO(2N_f)$. The Poisson structure is constrained by symmetry arguments and implies that these Higgs branches are algebraic integrable systems; the degeneration of the symplectic form occurs when the spinor annihilators overlap. We argue that the stratification of the Higgs branch at infinite coupling corresponds to the alignment of the instantons weights, leading to a non vanishing magnetization, and their acquisition of a mass.

### [13] [Warm Warped Throats](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29781)
*Dibya Chakraborty,Rudnei O. Ramos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We propose a two-field warm inflation model in brane inflation, where both the radial and angular coordinates of a $D3$-brane on a warped deformed conifold serve as inflatons. With moduli stabilized by a supersymmetrically embedded $D7$-brane, we show that dissipative effects in warm inflation allow compatibility with current CMB observations more naturally than cold inflation.

我们提出了一种双场温致暴胀（warm inflation）模型，其中在扭曲变形锥面（warped deformed conifold）上的D3-膜的径向与角向坐标均作为暴胀子场。通过超对称嵌入的D7-膜实现模稳定化，我们证明温致暴胀中的耗散效应使得该模型相较于冷暴胀更自然地满足当前CMB观测约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard brane inflation typically relies on a single scalar field (e.g., radial motion of a $D3$-brane) and faces challenges such as fine-tuning and consistency with Planck data in cold inflation scenarios. We aim to extend the framework by introducing multi-field dynamics and warm inflation, which can alleviate these issues through thermal dissipation and richer field space structure.

标准膜暴胀通常依赖单一标量场（如D3-膜的径向运动），在冷暴胀情景下面临微调和与Planck数据一致性等挑战。我们旨在通过引入多场动力学和温致暴胀来扩展该框架，利用热耗散和更丰富的场空间结构缓解这些问题。

Method: We construct a two-field inflationary model using the radial and angular coordinates of a $D3$-brane moving on a warped deformed conifold as independent inflaton fields. Moduli stabilization is achieved via a supersymmetric $D7$-brane embedding, generating appropriate scalar potentials. The system is analyzed within the warm inflation paradigm, incorporating dissipative effects into the equations of motion, and we compute observables such as the scalar power spectrum, spectral index, and tensor-to-scalar ratio using slow-roll approximations and thermal corrections.

我们构建了一个双场暴胀模型，将D3-膜在扭曲变形锥面上的径向与角向坐标作为独立的暴胀子场。通过超对称嵌入的D7-膜实现模稳定化，生成适当的标量势。在温致暴胀范式下分析系统，将耗散效应引入运动方程，并使用缓变近似和热修正计算标量功率谱、谱指数和张标比等观测量。

Result: The inclusion of dissipative effects in warm inflation allows the model to satisfy observational constraints from Planck and BICEP/Keck more naturally across a broader range of parameters compared to cold inflation. The two-field dynamics generate distinctive predictions for the spectral index $n_s$ and tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$, with $n_s \approx 0.96 - 0.97$ and suppressed $r$, consistent with current bounds. Thermal fluctuations dominate over quantum ones in the warm regime, altering the origin of primordial perturbations.

温致暴胀中耗散效应的引入使得该模型相较于冷暴胀能在更宽泛的参数范围内更自然地满足Planck与BICEP/Keck的观测约束。双场动力学对标量谱指数$n_s$和张标比$r$产生独特预言，其中$n_s \approx 0.96 - 0.97$且$r$被压低，符合当前限制。在温区，热涨落主导量子涨落，改变了原初扰动的起源。

Conclusion: Multi-field warm brane inflation with radial and angular moduli provides a viable and observationally favorable alternative to standard single-field cold inflation. The integration of moduli stabilization via $D7$-branes and dissipative dynamics enhances compatibility with cosmological data, highlighting the importance of non-equilibrium effects and multi-field considerations in string-theoretic inflation.

包含径向与角向模的双场温致膜暴胀为标准单场冷暴胀提供了可行且更符合观测的替代方案。通过D7-膜实现模稳定化并结合耗散动力学，显著提升了与宇宙学数据的兼容性，凸显了非平衡效应与多场考虑在弦理论暴胀中的重要性。

Abstract: We investigate brane inflation, focusing on warm inflation realizations within a warped throat geometry. While the standard scenario relies on a single mobile $D3$-brane moving radially toward an anti-$D3$-brane at the tip of the throat, we propose two distinct inflationary pictures. In our approach, the radial and angular coordinates of a $D3$-brane on a warped deformed conifold act as two independent inflaton fields. We address moduli stabilization by incorporating a supersymmetrically embedded $D7$-brane, which generates the necessary radial and angular scalar potentials. Evaluating these radial and angular brane inflation setups within the warm inflation paradigm, we demonstrate that dissipation effects allow the models to satisfy recent observational constraints more naturally than their cold inflation counterparts for a given parameter space.
