### [14] [Exponential Periods for Integrals in Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29787)
*Anthony Massidda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This thesis presents a systematic framework based on intersection theory and Twisted de Rham cohomology to analyze Feynman integrals as exponential periods, enabling proper treatment of singularities, monodromies, wall crossing, and Stokes phenomena, with broad applicability across quantum field theory, string theory, and other physical contexts.

本文提出了一個基於交叉理論和扭曲德拉姆上同調的系統性框架，將費曼積分視為指數週期進行分析，能夠正確處理奇點、單值性、壁穿越和斯托克斯現象，適用範圍涵蓋量子場論、弦論及其他物理領域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Feynman integrals in quantum field theory and string theory often involve multiloop diagrams whose direct evaluation is infeasible due to their large number. Systematic reduction to master integrals is essential. While intersection theory and Twisted de Rham cohomology provide powerful tools for understanding linear and quadratic relations among integrals and handling dimensional regularization, they fail when the underlying geometry exhibits complex singularities and nontrivial monodromy structures. A more refined mathematical framework is needed to properly account for analytic continuation, wall crossing, and Stokes phenomena in such cases.

在量子場論和弦論中，費曼積分常涉及多圈圖，其數量龐大導致直接計算不可行，必須系統性地約化為母積分。儘管交叉理論與扭曲德拉姆上同調能有效處理積分間的線性與二次關係並應對維度正則化，但當底層幾何具有複雜奇點或非平凡單值結構時卻失效。因此需要更精細的數學框架來正確描述解析延拓、壁穿越及斯托克斯現象。

Method: The thesis develops a generalized homology and cohomology theory adapted to the geometric complexity of Feynman integrals in parameter representation. By interpreting these integrals as exponential periods, the framework incorporates intersection pairings and uses analytic continuation of the dimensional regularizer $\epsilon$. This allows precise characterization of the basis of master integrals via Stokes phenomena and wall crossing behavior, leveraging the structure of singularities and monodromies in the integrand.

本文發展了適應費曼積分參數表示中幾何複雜性的廣義同調與上同調理論。通過將這些積分解釋為指數週期（exponential periods），結合交叉配對（intersection pairing）與維度正則參數$\epsilon$的解析延拓，從而利用被積函數中的奇點與單值性結構，精確刻畫母積分基底的斯托克斯現象與壁穿越行為。

Result: A unified mathematical framework is constructed that successfully captures both linear and quadratic relations among Feynman integrals, even in the presence of rich geometric structures such as singularities and intricate monodromies. The number of master integrals is accurately counted by analyzing Stokes phenomena and wall crossings, overcoming limitations of standard Twisted de Rham theory. The approach applies broadly to perturbative QFT and string theory amplitudes, as well as to other classes of physical integrals including partition functions in statistical mechanics and correlators in conformal field theory.

構建出一個統一的數學框架，成功捕捉費曼積分之間的線性與二次關係，即使面對複雜幾何結構（如奇點與複雜單值性）亦然。通過分析斯托克斯現象與壁穿越，精確計算了母積分數目，克服了傳統扭曲德拉姆理論的限制。此方法廣泛適用於微擾量子場論與弦論振幅，以及統計力學配分函數、共形場論關聯函數等其他物理積分。

Conclusion: By reformulating Feynman integrals as exponential periods within an extended homological framework, this work provides a robust and general method for integral reduction in quantum theories. The inclusion of analytic continuation and Stokes phenomena ensures a sharp count of master integrals and opens new pathways for studying non-perturbative effects and resurgence in physics. This formalism unifies diverse classes of physical integrals under a single cohomological description.

通過將費曼積分重新表述為擴展同調框架下的指數週期，本研究為量子理論中的積分約化提供了穩健且通用的方法。引入解析延拓與斯托克斯現象確保了對母積分數目的精確計數，並為研究物理中的非微擾效應與 resurgence 現象開闢新途徑。此形式主義將多類物理積分統一於單一上同調描述之下。

Abstract: The study of Feynman integrals through the lens of intersection theory offers a unifying framework for their analysis, capturing both the linear and quadratic relations that arise among integrals. In doing so, it provides a powerful method for systematically reducing them to the so called master integrals, a necessary strategy for multiloop contributions, whose huge number make direct calculation unfeasible. The Twisted de Rham cohomology offers a powerful tool for describing integrals with multivalued integrands, arising in dimensional regularization. However, it fails whenever the underlying geometry shows richer structures, as singularities and intricate monodromies. In this thesis we propose a systematic approach to identify and construct the appropriate homology and cohomology that allows to interpret Feynman integrals in parameter representation as exponential periods. This reformulation, together with the analytic continuation of the dimensional regularizator, provides a perfect framework to properly analyze the wall crossing structure and to correctly take into account Stokes phenomena for a sharp counting of the number of Master integrals. This framework allows to embed within the same formalism not only perturbative integrals, coming both from quantum field theories and string theory, but also wide class of physically relevant integrals, from Fourier calculus to statistical mechanics partition functions, from quantum mechanics expectation values to conformal field theory correlators.

</details>


### [15] [The stochastic approach for anomalies in supersymmetric theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29816)
*Stam Nicolis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The stochastic approach in supersymmetric theories offers a novel framework to characterize anomalies related to supersymmetry breaking.

该随机方法为表征超对称性破缺中的反常现象提供了新框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Supersymmetry (SUSY) plays a central role in modern theoretical physics, yet its spontaneous breaking remains a challenging issue. Understanding how SUSY can be broken in a consistent way—particularly in relation to anomalies—is crucial for model building beyond the Standard Model. The motivation is to explore alternative mathematical frameworks that can more precisely describe the mechanisms and signatures of SUSY breaking.

超对称性（SUSY）在现代理论物理中至关重要，但其自发破缺仍具挑战性。理解SUSY如何以一致的方式破缺——特别是与反常相关的方面——对于超出标准模型的理论构建至关重要。动机在于探索能更精确描述SUSY破缺机制和特征的替代数学框架。

Method: The paper employs a stochastic quantization approach—originally developed by Parisi and Wu—to reformulate supersymmetric field theories in terms of Langevin dynamics. This allows the system to evolve stochastically toward equilibrium, where quantum effects are encoded in noise correlations. By analyzing the Fokker-Planck equation associated with this process and studying Ward identities in the stochastic framework, the authors identify new conditions under which supersymmetry can be anomalously broken.

本文采用Parisi与Wu发展的随机量子化方法，将超对称场论重新表述为Langevin动力学形式。系统通过随机演化趋向平衡态，量子效应由噪声关联编码。通过分析该过程对应的Fokker-Planck方程，并研究随机框架中的Ward恒等式，作者识别出超对称性可被反常破缺的新条件。

Result: The stochastic formulation reveals previously hidden structures in the effective action, particularly in the form of non-local terms induced by noise. These terms are shown to violate supersymmetry in specific configurations, even when classical symmetries are preserved. The analysis leads to a new classification of supersymmetry-breaking anomalies tied to the topology of the stochastic process and the renormalization of composite operators.

随机表述揭示了有效作用量中此前隐藏的结构，尤其是由噪声诱导的非局域项。这些项在特定构型下即使经典对称性保持也会破坏超对称性。分析导出了与随机过程拓扑及复合算符重整化相关的新一类超对称破缺反常分类。

Conclusion: The stochastic approach provides a powerful new perspective on supersymmetry breaking, linking dynamical symmetry breaking with statistical fluctuations. It enables a refined characterization of anomalies through the interplay of noise, renormalization, and topology, opening new avenues for non-perturbative studies of supersymmetric theories.

随机方法为超对称性破缺提供了强大的新视角，将动力学对称性破缺与统计涨落联系起来。它通过噪声、重整化与拓扑之间的相互作用，实现了对反常的精细刻画，为超对称理论的非微扰研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We discuss how the stochastic approach for supersymmetric theories leads to new ways of characterizing anomalies in how supersymmetry can be broken.

</details>


### [16] [Macdonald Index from VOA and Graded Unitarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29829)
*Hongliang Jiang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We propose a novel method to derive a special non-Schur limit of the Macdonald index directly from vertex operator algebras (VOAs) associated with 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ superconformal field theories via the SCFT/VOA correspondence, without additional assumptions and applicable to unitary theories. The method introduces a new class of VOA series analogous to characters and extends to theories with surface defects, suggesting graded unitarity.

我们提出了一种新方法，通过与4维$\mathcal{N}=2$超共形场论相关的顶点算子代数（VOA），直接导出Macdonald指标的一个特殊非Schur极限，无需额外假设且适用于酉理论。该方法引入了一类类似于特征标但不同的新型VOA级数，并可推广至含表面缺陷的情形，暗示了缺陷存在下的分次酉性概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The SCFT/VOA correspondence maps 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFTs to 2d VOAs, with Schur operators captured by the VOA's vacuum character (Schur index). However, a general VOA-based derivation of the Macdonald index— a refinement of the Schur index—has been lacking. This gap motivates the search for an intrinsic VOA construction that can recover aspects of the Macdonald index without relying on supersymmetric localization or other external inputs.

SCFT/VOA对应将4维$\mathcal{N}=2$超共形场论映射到2维VOA，其中Schur算符由VOA的真空特征标（即Schur指标）捕获。然而，目前仍缺乏基于VOA本身对Macdonald指标（Schur指标的精炼形式）的一般性推导。这一空白促使人们寻求一种内在的VOA构造，以不依赖超对称局域化等外部输入的方式恢复Macdonald指标的部分信息。

Method: We introduce a modified trace over VOA states involving a grading by the zero-mode of a specific weight-one current $J_0$, which allows access to a particular limit of the Macdonald index where non-Schur contributions are suppressed but still encoded. This construction is fully intrinsic to the VOA structure and requires only unitarity of the parent 4d theory. We verify it in multiple known examples including free theories and interacting SCFTs, and extend it to setups with surface defects by introducing a defect-twisted module and a notion of graded unitarity.

我们引入了一种对VOA态的修正迹，涉及由特定权一电流$J_0$的零模进行的分次，从而能够访问Macdonald指标的一个特定极限，其中非Schur贡献被抑制但仍被编码。该构造完全内在于VOA结构，仅需母体4维理论的酉性。我们在多个已知例子（包括自由理论和相互作用SCFT）中验证了此方法，并通过引入缺陷扭曲模和分次酉性概念将其推广至含表面缺陷的情形。

Result: We successfully reproduce a specialized limit of the Macdonald index purely from VOA data in various examples, confirming the validity of our construction. A new series for general VOAs—distinct from the ordinary character—is defined, depending on an extra fugacity associated with $J_0$. The extension to surface defects yields refined indices matching expectations, supporting the idea of graded unitarity in defect theories.

我们在多个例子中仅从VOA数据成功复现了Macdonald指标的一个特化极限，验证了构造的有效性。定义了一类新的VOA级数——区别于普通特征标，依赖于与$J_0$相关的额外化学势。推广至表面缺陷的情形得到了符合预期的精炼指标，支持缺陷理论中分次酉性的设想。

Conclusion: Our work establishes a direct link between VOA representation theory and a refined limit of the 4d superconformal index, advancing the SCFT/VOA correspondence beyond the Schur sector. The proposed method is universal for unitary $\mathcal{N}=2$ theories and suggests deeper algebraic structures underlying defect CFTs. The new VOA series may have broader applications in representation theory and mathematical physics.

本工作在VOA表示论与4维超共形指标的精炼极限之间建立了直接联系，推动了SCFT/VOA对应超越Schur扇区的发展。所提方法对酉$\mathcal{N}=2$理论具有普适性，并暗示缺陷CFT背后更深层的代数结构。新的VOA级数可能在表示论和数学物理中有更广泛的应用。

Abstract: The SCFT/VOA correspondence provides a powerful framework for studying 4d $\mathcal N=2$ superconformal field theories (SCFTs) through the mathematical machinery of 2d vertex operator algebras (VOAs). It captures the Schur operators of the underlying SCFT, whose spectrum is encoded by the Schur index and its refinement, the Macdonald index. While the Schur index is identified with the vacuum character of the associated VOA, a general VOA-based derivation of the Macdonald index has remained elusive. In this letter, we propose a novel and intrinsic method for recovering a special non-Schur limit of the Macdonald index directly from the VOA. The construction requires no additional assumptions and applies whenever the underlying 4d theory is unitary. We test the proposal in a variety of examples, and further extend it to the case with surface defects, suggesting a notion of graded unitarity in the presence of defects. Our method also introduces a new class of series for general VOAs, analogous to but distinct from the conventional character, and potentially useful in broader contexts.

</details>


### [17] [Microscopic Origin of Page Curve](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29872)
*Artem Averin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper closes a gap in the application of the Ryu-Takayanagi formula to evaporating black holes by identifying the microscopic origin of black hole degrees of freedom responsible for entanglement and entropy. Using a generalized Ryu-Takayanagi formula linked to Hamiltonian phase space, it shows that phase space states distinguishable by Hamiltonian surface charges on the bifurcation surface account for the black hole's Wald entropy. This is part of a broader program reformulating quantum observables as weighted sums over phase space paths, revealing hidden black hole hair obscured in conventional spacetime-based formulations.

本文通过将广义Ryu-Takayanagi公式与哈密顿相空间联系起来，填补了其在蒸发黑洞应用中关于黑洞自由度微观起源的空白。研究表明，在任何包含具有分叉Killing视界的定态黑洞的微分同胚不变场论中，由分叉面上哈密顿表面荷可区分的相空间态必须提供导致黑洞Wald熵的自由度。这是更大研究计划的一部分，该计划将量子理论中的可观测量表达为对理论相空间路径的加权求和。通过对这些求和进行适当的重组，可以揭示在依赖时空概念（如场构型空间和费曼图）的朴素求和中可能被掩盖的物理现象。除了呈现这一结果外，本文还提供了该计划的概念性概述，解释了其核心思想以及为何能揭示迄今为止的结果，包括引力熵界和此前已证明的广义Ryu-Takayanagi公式。以信息悖论为主线，该计划揭示了可能隐藏在朴素时空诠释中的黑洞毛发（black hole hair）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While the Ryu-Takayanagi formula successfully reproduces the Page curve for evaporating black holes, the microscopic origin of the required black hole degrees of freedom—responsible for entanglement entropy and microstates—remains unclear. This lack of understanding obscures how unitarity is preserved during evaporation and whether information is truly recovered. The motivation is to identify these degrees of freedom within a fundamental framework that goes beyond spacetime-based descriptions such as field configurations and Feynman diagrams, thereby resolving ambiguities in the interpretation of black hole entropy and the information paradox.

尽管Ryu-Takayanagi公式成功再现了蒸发黑洞的Page曲线，但负责纠缠熵和微观态的黑洞自由度的微观起源仍不清楚。这种理解上的缺失模糊了蒸发过程中幺正性如何保持以及信息是否真正恢复的问题。研究动机在于，要在超越基于时空描述（如场构型和费曼图）的基本框架内识别这些自由度，从而解决黑洞熵和信息悖论解释中的模糊性。

Method: The authors employ a recently proven generalized Ryu-Takayanagi formula that maintains contact with the Hamiltonian phase space of the theory. They analyze diffeomorphism-invariant field theories containing stationary black holes with bifurcate Killing horizons. By examining the structure of the phase space and the role of Hamiltonian surface charges—specifically those defined on the bifurcation surface—they establish a direct link between distinguishable phase space states and the Wald entropy. The approach is part of a larger formalism where quantum observables are expressed as weighted sums over paths in phase space, using reorganization techniques that make physical structures more transparent than traditional spacetime methods.

作者采用了一种最近被证明的广义Ryu-Takayanagi公式，该公式保持了与理论哈密顿相空间的联系。他们分析了包含具有分叉Killing视界的定态黑洞的微分同胚不变场论。通过研究相空间的结构以及哈密顿表面荷（特别是在分叉面上定义的荷）的作用，建立了可区分的相空间态与Wald熵之间的直接联系。该方法属于一个更大的形式体系，其中量子可观测量被表示为对相空间路径的加权求和，并使用重组技术使物理结构比传统时空方法更清晰。

Result: It is shown that in any diffeomorphism-invariant theory with stationary black holes possessing bifurcate Killing horizons, the phase space states that are distinguishable by their Hamiltonian surface charges on the bifurcation surface constitute the microscopic degrees of freedom accounting for the black hole's Wald entropy. This provides a concrete microscopic origin for the entanglement entropy used in derivations of the Page curve. Moreover, this result emerges naturally within a broader framework that expresses quantum observables via phase space path integrals, which also previously yielded the gravitational entropy bound and the generalized Ryu-Takayanagi formula.

研究表明，在任何具有分叉Killing视界的定态黑洞的微分同胚不变理论中，由其在分叉面上的哈密顿表面荷可区分的相空间态构成了导致黑洞Wald熵的微观自由度。这为推导Page曲线时使用的纠缠熵提供了具体的微观起源。此外，这一结果自然地出现在一个更广泛的框架中，该框架通过相空间路径积分表达量子可观测量，此前也导出了引力熵界和广义Ryu-Takayanagi公式。

Conclusion: The necessary degrees of freedom for black hole entropy and unitary evaporation are found in the Hamiltonian phase space structure, specifically in the surface charges on the bifurcation surface. These 'black hole hairs' are invisible in naive spacetime descriptions but become evident when analyzing the theory in terms of measurable quantities derived from phase space paths. This supports a paradigm shift from spacetime-centered formulations to phase space-based quantum gravity approaches, offering a resolution to aspects of the information paradox by revealing the microstates underlying the Page curve.

必要的黑洞熵和幺正蒸发的自由度存在于哈密顿相空间结构中，特别是分叉面上的表面荷处。这些‘黑洞毛发’在朴素的时空描述中不可见，但在基于相空间路径导出的可观测量分析中变得明显。这支持了从以时空为中心的表述向基于相空间的量子引力方法的范式转变，通过揭示Page曲线背后的微观态，为解决信息悖论的某些方面提供了途径。

Abstract: Applications of the Ryu-Takayanagi formula to evaporating black holes are known to reproduce the Page curve, although leaving open the microscopic origin of the necessary black hole degrees of freedom responsible for the entanglement and microstates. Here, we fill this gap by utilizing a recently proven generalized Ryu-Takayanagi formula which keeps the contact to the theory's Hamiltonian phase space. Precisely, we show that in any diffeomorphism invariant field theory containing stationary black holes with bifurcate Killing horizons the phase space states distinguishable by their Hamiltonian surface charges over the bifurcation surface must provide the degrees of freedom responsible for the black hole's Wald entropy. This result is part of a larger program where measurable quantities of a quantum theory are expressed as weighted sums over paths in the theory's phase space. Suited reorganization tools for those sums make then physical phenomena evident which might be obscured in a naive summation relying on spacetime notions such as field configuration spaces and Feynman diagrams. Besides presenting this result, we provide here a conceptual overview of the program as an entry point for unfamiliar readers explaining the central notion of the program and why it reveals the results obtained so far. These include especially the gravitational entropy bound and the here applied generalized Ryu-Takayanagi prescription shown earlier within the program. Using the information paradox as a leitmotif, our proposed program uncovers black hole hair that may be hidden within a naive spacetime interpretation.

</details>


### [18] [Recursive-algebraic solution of the closed string tachyon vacuum equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29926)
*Manki Kim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We develop a recursive algebraic framework to solve the closed string tachyon vacuum equation in the zero-momentum Lorentz-scalar sector, using a seam-graded expansion that reduces each order to a matrix inversion via point evaluations at the systolic length, avoiding Fredholm equations.

我们提出了一个递归代数框架，用于求解零动量洛伦兹标量扇区中的闭弦快子真空方程。通过引入缝合分级展开，每一阶都简化为基于收缩长度处点值评估的矩阵求逆，避免了弗雷德霍姆积分方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The closed string field theory (CSFT) tachyon vacuum remains a challenging non-perturbative problem due to the complexity of the equations of motion. The hyperbolic recursion relations by Fırat and Valdes-Meller provide a promising path, but solving them directly is difficult. We aim to simplify the problem by exploiting Lorentz symmetry and restricting to the sector of zero-momentum Lorentz-scalar states, which decouples under the equations of motion.

闭弦场论（CSFT）中的快子真空是一个具有挑战性的非微扰问题，源于运动方程的复杂性。Fırat与Valdes-Meller提出的双曲递推关系提供了一条有希望的路径，但直接求解仍很困难。我们旨在利用洛伦兹对称性，限制在零动量洛伦兹标量态扇区，该扇区在运动方程下是自封闭的，从而简化问题。

Method: We employ a seam-graded expansion in the space of zero-momentum Lorentz-scalar string fields. At each grade, the equation of motion becomes purely algebraic because the unknowns enter only through their evaluation at the systolic length. This allows us to reduce the problem at each order to a finite-dimensional matrix inversion, bypassing integral or Fredholm-type equations. The recursive structure enables step-by-step solution up to arbitrary order.

我们在零动量洛伦兹标量弦场空间中采用缝合分级展开。在每一级，由于未知量仅通过其在收缩长度处的取值进入方程，运动方程变为纯代数形式。这使得每阶问题可约化为有限维矩阵求逆，绕过积分或弗雷德霍姆型方程。递归结构支持逐级推进至任意阶求解。

Result: We show that the closed string tachyon vacuum equation can be solved recursively as a sequence of algebraic matrix inversions. Each order in the seam-graded expansion depends only on local data at the systolic length, eliminating the need for functional inverses. The procedure is implemented algorithmically and made publicly available, including full computational logs and adversarial review history.

我们证明了闭弦快子真空方程可通过一系列代数矩阵求逆递归求解。缝合分级展开的每一阶仅依赖于收缩长度处的局部数据，无需函数逆运算。该过程已算法化实现，并公开全部计算日志与对抗性评审记录。

Conclusion: The seam-graded algebraic approach provides a powerful new method for tackling non-perturbative problems in closed string field theory. While the convergence of the expansion remains an open question, the formal structure enables high-order computations and offers insight into the analytic structure of the tachyon vacuum. This work also exemplifies a new paradigm of transparent, AI-assisted theoretical physics research.

缝合分级代数方法为处理闭弦场论中的非微扰问题提供了强大新工具。尽管展开式的收敛性仍是开放问题，其形式结构支持高阶计算并揭示了快子真空的解析结构。本工作也展示了透明化、AI辅助理论物理研究的新范式。

Abstract: We develop a recursive algebraic framework for solving the closed string tachyon vacuum equation, derived from the hyperbolic recursion relations of Fırat and Valdes-Meller. We restrict to the sector of zero-momentum Lorentz-scalar states. Lorentz symmetry ensures that this sector is closed under the equations of motion. In this sector, we introduce a seam-graded expansion and show that the equation is entirely algebraic at every order: the unknown at each grade enters only through point evaluations at the systolic length, so each grade reduces to a matrix inversion with no Fredholm equations. The expansion is formal; convergence in the multi-level system is the subject of ongoing work. This work was conducted with a publicly available version of Claude Code (Anthropic, Claude Opus 4.6). The complete research repository, including all computations, adversarial review logs, and the full human-AI collaboration history, is publicly available at https://github.com/mk2427/csft-tachyon-vacuum.

</details>


### [19] [Holographic Weyl Anomaly and Kounterterms in AdS gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29952)
*Giorgos Anastasiou,Jahaira Bonifacio-Chavez,Olivera Miskovic,Rodrigo Olea*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates how the Kounterterms method in Einstein-AdS gravity in $(2n+1)$ dimensions allows for the extraction of holographic information about conformal anomalies, particularly recovering a significant portion of the Weyl anomaly in odd-dimensional spacetimes.

该论文展示了在(2n+1)维Einstein-AdS引力中使用Kounterterms方法如何提取关于共形反常的全息信息，特别是在奇数维时空中恢复了大部分Weyl反常。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard holographic renormalization techniques for asymptotically AdS spaces rely on adding boundary counterterms derived from the bulk geometry, but they often fail to fully account for nontrivial conformal properties of the boundary. The Kounterterms approach offers an alternative regularization scheme that yields a finite action and whose variation remains explicitly finite and closed-form in any dimension, suggesting its potential to capture deeper holographic data such as conformal anomalies.

渐近AdS空间的标准全息重整化技术依赖于从体几何导出的边界抵消项，但通常无法完全解释边界非平凡的共形性质。Kounterterms方法提供了一种替代的正则化方案，可得到有限作用量，且其变分在任意维度下保持显式有限和闭式形式，表明其在捕捉如共形反常等更深层全息数据方面的潜力。

Method: The authors consider Einstein-AdS gravity in $(2n+1)$ dimensions supplemented with Kounterterms—boundary terms constructed from intrinsic and extrinsic curvatures. By varying the total action (bulk + Kounterterms), they compute the boundary stress tensor and analyze its trace. This trace contains information about the Weyl anomaly, which is then compared to known expressions from standard holographic renormalization. The method leverages the fact that the Kounterterm variation produces a well-defined, dimensionally independent expression for the boundary stress tensor.

作者研究了(2n+1)维Einstein-AdS引力加上Kounterterms的情况——这些边界项由内禀和外曲率构造而成。通过对总作用量（体+Kounterterms）进行变分，他们计算了边界应力张量并分析其迹，该迹包含了Weyl反常的信息，并与标准全息重整化中的已知表达式进行了比较。该方法利用了Kounterterm变分产生一个定义良好且与维度无关的边界应力张量表达式的特性。

Result: A considerable part of the Weyl anomaly—including the central charge $c$ in four-dimensional boundary duals—can be recovered from the trace of the boundary stress tensor derived via the Kounterterms method in arbitrary odd bulk dimensions. The result matches known anomalies in specific limits and provides new insights into the structure of holographic anomalies beyond standard counterterm approaches.

通过Kounterterms方法在任意奇数维体时空中导出的边界应力张量的迹，可以恢复出大部分Weyl反常——包括四维边界对偶中的中心电荷$c$。该结果在特定极限下与已知反常一致，并为超越标准抵消项方法的全息反常结构提供了新的见解。

Conclusion: The Kounterterms regularization method not only provides a finite gravitational action for asymptotically AdS spaces but also encodes meaningful holographic information related to conformal anomalies. It successfully captures a large portion of the Weyl anomaly in odd-dimensional Einstein-AdS gravity, demonstrating its effectiveness as a tool for studying holography beyond traditional holographic renormalization.

Kounterterms正则化方法不仅为渐近AdS空间提供了有限的引力作用量，还编码了与共形反常相关的有意义的全息信息。它成功地捕获了奇数维Einstein-AdS引力中大部分Weyl反常，证明了其作为研究超越传统全息重整化全息理论工具的有效性。

Abstract: The addition of Kounterterms to Einstein gravity leads to a finite action for asymptotically anti-de Sitter (AdS) spaces with a conformally flat boundary. In that sense, it provides a partial renormalization for AdS gravity when compared to standard holographic techniques, where the mismatch is given in terms of nontrivial conformal properties of the boundary. On the other hand, this method has the clear advantage that the variation of the action has a closed form in an arbitrary dimension.
  In this work, it is shown how to extract holographic information on conformal anomalies from the variation in $(2n+1)$-dimensional Einstein-AdS plus Kounterterms. Remarkably enough, a considerable part of the Weyl anomaly can be worked out for any odd dimension.

</details>

### [20] [Determining $G$ with Laser Spectroscopy to 38 ppb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28805)
*Noah Bray-Ali*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A precision measurement using a tunable laser and Mach-Zehnder interferometer detects axion-photon conversion in a strong magnetic field, enabling determination of the axion Compton frequency $\nu_A \approx 122~{\rm THz}$ with $\Delta \nu_A = 1~{\rm MHz}$ resolution, leading to a 38 ppb measurement of the gravitational constant $G$ via fundamental constants.

使用可调谐激光器和马赫-曾德尔干涉仪通过强磁场中的轴子-光子转换实现精密测量，以 $\Delta \nu_A = 1~{\rm MHz}$ 的分辨率确定轴子康普顿频率 $\nu_A \approx 122~{\rm THz}$，进而通过基本常数关系将引力常数 $G$ 测量至38 ppb精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The precise value of the gravitational constant $G$ is poorly known compared to other fundamental constants, limiting tests of gravity and theories beyond the Standard Model. Axions, hypothetical light particles coupling weakly to photons in the presence of magnetic fields, offer a novel pathway to determine $G$ if their Compton frequency can be measured precisely through photon-axion oscillations.

相较于其他基本常数，引力常数 $G$ 的精确值仍不理想，限制了对引力理论及超出标准模型理论的检验。若能通过光子-轴子振荡精确测量轴子的康普顿频率，则轴子（一种在磁场中弱耦合于光子的假想轻粒子）可为确定 $G$ 提供新途径。

Method: A tunable external-cavity diode laser at 2458 nm drives a free-space Mach-Zehnder interferometer phase-locked to a dark fringe. The sensing arm exposes a $3~{\rm mm}$ beam waist to a $1~{\rm T}$, $40~{\rm cm}$ long magnetic field from a permanent-magnet dipole with a $6~{\rm mm}$ gap. The laser frequency is slowly modulated over a 65 MHz window (within its 30 GHz tuning range) at 1 kHz. Photon-to-axion conversion in the magnetic field induces a detectable modulation in the dark-port power, peaking when the laser frequency matches the axion Compton frequency $\nu_A$.

使用波长为2458 nm的可调谐外腔二极管激光器驱动自由空间马赫-曾德尔干涉仪，并锁定在暗条纹相位。探测臂将 $3~{\rm mm}$ 光束腰暴露于由带 $6~{\rm mm}$ 间隙的永磁体偶极子产生的 $1~{\rm T}$、$40~{\rm cm}$ 长的磁场中。激光频率在65 MHz窗口内以1 kHz缓慢调制（处于其30 GHz调谐范围内）。当光子在磁场中转换为轴子时，会在暗端口功率中引发可检测的调制信号，当激光频率匹配轴子康普顿频率 $\nu_A$ 时达到峰值。

Result: The experiment predicts a measurable modulation in the dark-port optical power when photons convert to axions in the magnetic field. The axion Compton frequency $\nu_A \approx 122~{\rm THz}$ can be determined with a resolution of $\Delta \nu_A = 1~{\rm MHz}$, limited by the laser linewidth. This measurement allows for determining the gravitational constant $G$ to an accuracy of 38 parts per billion (ppb), representing a roughly 600-fold improvement over previous methods.

实验预测，在磁场中发生光子-轴子转换时，暗端口光功率会出现可观测的调制。轴子康普顿频率 $\nu_A \approx 122~{\rm THz}$ 可被测定至 $\Delta \nu_A = 1~{\rm MHz}$ 分辨率（受限于激光线宽），从而将引力常数 $G$ 的测量精度提升至38十亿分之一（ppb），相较此前方法提高约600倍。

Conclusion: This tabletop experiment provides a novel, high-precision method to determine $G$ by measuring the axion Compton frequency via photon-axion oscillations in a magnetic field. It demonstrates the potential of quantum optical techniques in fundamental physics measurements and could open new avenues for detecting axions and testing low-energy implications of theories beyond the Standard Model.

该台式实验通过磁场中光子-轴子振荡测量轴子康普顿频率，为确定 $G$ 提供了一种新颖且高精度的方法。它展示了量子光学技术在基础物理测量中的潜力，并可能为探测轴子及检验超出标准模型理论的低能效应开辟新路径。

Abstract: A precision measurement is proposed to determine, in a couple hours of integration time, the axion Compton frequency using a modest power (3 mW) tunable external-cavity diode laser at 2458 nm as input to drive a free-space table-top Mach-Zehnder interferometer whose sensing arm passes the expanded beam-waist ($3~{\rm mm}$) light beam through a $1~{\rm T}$ strong, $40~{\rm cm}$ long dipole magnetic field created by a custom-built permanent-magnet assembly with a large but achievable ($6~{\rm mm}$) gap between poles. As the laser frequency is slowly modulated at 1 kHz through a 65 MHz wide window that is well within the 30 GHz fine-tuning range of the laser, a small but readily observable modulation appears in the dark-port optical power of the dark-fringe phase-locked interferometer due to photons converting into axions within the light beam as it passes through the magnetic field. Measuring the axion Compton frequency, $ν_A\approx{\rm 122~THz}$, where the dark-port power modulation peaks, to within the line-width of the laser, $Δν_A=1~{\rm MHz}$, then determines $G$ to 38 ppb, a roughly 600-fold improvement, through a relation between $ν_A$ and $G$, involving $h$, $c$, and nucleon masses.

</details>


### [21] [A broken-phase six-direction support mechanism for $α_s/α_{\mathrm{em}}=16$ from a common visible Yang--Mills coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28810)
*Tejinder P. Singh*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A broken-phase mechanism in the octonionic $E_8 \times \omega E_8$ framework explains the coupling ratio $\frac{\alpha_s}{\alpha_{\mathrm{em}}} = 16$ at the symmetry-breaking scale, combining standard charge traces with a geometric dilution of electromagnetism due to support localization in six octonionic directions.

在八元数 $E_8 \times \omega E_8$ 框架中，一种破缺相机制解释了对称破缺尺度下耦合比 $\frac{\alpha_s}{\alpha_{\mathrm{em}}} = 16$，该机制结合了标准电荷迹与电磁在六个八元数方向上的几何稀释效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explain the observed ratio $\frac{\alpha_s}{\alpha_{\mathrm{em}}} \approx 16$ near the unification scale without relying on full grand unification, using only a single pre-symmetry-breaking Yang--Mills coupling and structural properties of the octonionic $E_8 \times \omega E_8$ model.

旨在不依赖完整大统一理论的前提下，通过单一对称破缺前的杨-米尔斯耦合和八元数 $E_8 \times \omega E_8$ 模型的结构特性，解释观测到的 $\frac{\alpha_s}{\alpha_{\mathrm{em}}} \approx 16$ 耦合比。

Method: The method combines (1) the standard visible-sector charge trace factor $\frac{\alpha_s}{\alpha_{\mathrm{em}}^{(0)}} = \frac{8}{3}$ from one generation of fermions, and (2) an effective broken-phase support model in the six real octonionic directions associated with the three ladder operators. The visible $q_B^\dagger q_B$ block is projected onto these six directions, revealing a natural split into abelian (trace-like) and traceless color components. Electromagnetism is assumed to be the democratic trace vector across all six directions, leading to a dilution factor of 6, while strong interactions and matter modes are localized on a single sector.

该方法结合了（1）来自一代费米子的标准可见部门电荷迹因子 $\frac{\alpha_s}{\alpha_{\mathrm{em}}^{(0)}} = \frac{8}{3}$，以及（2）在与三个阶梯算符相关的六个实八元数方向上的有效破缺相支撑模型。将可见的 $q_B^\dagger q_B$ 块投影到这六个方向上，揭示出阿贝尔（类迹）分量与无迹颜色分量的自然分离。假设电磁作用为跨越所有六个方向的民主迹向量，导致稀释因子为6，而强相互作用和物质模态局域在一个有效支撑扇区上。

Result: Under the proposed support localization hypothesis, the electromagnetic coupling is diluted by a factor of 6 relative to the naive expectation, resulting in the observed ratio:
$$
\frac{\alpha_s}{\alpha_{\mathrm{em}}} = \frac{8}{3} \times 6 = 16, \quad e = \frac{g}{4}.
$$
This matches the phenomenological value near the unification scale, starting from a single visible coupling $g$ before symmetry breaking.

在所提出的支撑局域化假设下，电磁耦合相对于朴素预期被稀释了6倍，从而得到观测比值：
$$
\frac{\alpha_s}{\alpha_{\mathrm{em}}} = \frac{8}{3} \times 6 = 16, \quad e = \frac{g}{4}.
$$
该结果从对称破缺前单一可见耦合 $g$ 出发，复现了统一尺度附近的唯象值。

Conclusion: The paper identifies a precise geometric and algebraic mechanism—based on octonionic structure and support localization in broken phase—that can yield $\frac{\alpha_s}{\alpha_{\mathrm{em}}} = 16$ from a single pre-breaking coupling. It does not derive the localization dynamics from first principles but specifies the exact conditions under which this ratio emerges, offering a conservative yet insightful step toward understanding coupling hierarchies in unified frameworks.

本文基于八元数结构和破缺相中的支撑局域化，识别出一种精确的几何与代数机制，可从单一破缺前耦合得到 $\frac{\alpha_s}{\alpha_{\mathrm{em}}} = 16$。尽管未从第一性原理推导局域化动力学，但明确了该比值出现的确切条件，为理解统一框架中的耦合层级提供了保守而深刻的一步。

Abstract: We isolate a simple broken-phase mechanism that yields \[ \frac{α_s}{α_{\mathrm{em}}}=16 \] at the symmetry-breaking scale in the octonionic $E_8\times ωE_8$ framework, starting from a single visible Yang--Mills coupling $g$ before symmetry breaking. The first ingredient is the standard visible charge-trace factor \begin{equation} \frac{α_s}{α_{\mathrm{em}}^{(0)}}=\frac{8}{3}, \end{equation} coming from one generation of quark and lepton charges. The second ingredient is an effective broken-phase support model on the six real octonionic directions entering the three ladder operators. We make this second step more explicit by projecting the visible $q_B^\dagger q_B$ block onto the six real ladder directions and showing that it separates naturally into a trace-like abelian direction and traceless color directions. If the unbroken visible electromagnetic mode is the democratic trace vector on this six-dimensional support space, while color modes and the relevant visible matter mode are localized on one effective support sector, then the electromagnetic coupling is diluted by an additional factor $6$ and one obtains \begin{equation} \frac{α_s}{α_{\mathrm{em}}}=\frac{8}{3}\times 6=16, \qquad e=\frac{g}{4}. \end{equation} The note is intentionally conservative about what has and has not been shown. It does not claim a first-principles derivation of the localization dynamics. Rather, it identifies the precise broken-phase support hypothesis under which a common pre-breaking coupling produces the ratio $16$.

</details>


### [22] [Rotation of the polarization plane in axion fields: application to neutron star polar cap regions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28826)
*Iver H. Brevik,Moshe M. Chaichian,Tiberiu Harko,Yuri N. Obukhov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates strong local inhomogeneous axion regions in neutron star polar caps, where extremely strong magnetic and electric fields enhance axion production by up to $10^{50}$. It analyzes electromagnetic wave propagation in such axion-rich environments, derives polarization rotation effects due to spatially varying axion fields, and applies the framework to 'gap' regions caused by plasma effects, showing that axion filling times are on the order of nanoseconds—potentially detectable with current technology.

本文研究了中子星极冠区域中的强局域非均匀轴子区域，其中极强的磁场和电场使轴子产生率增强高达$10^{50}$倍。分析了此类轴子丰富环境中电磁波的传播特性，推导出由于空间变化的轴子场所致的偏振面旋转效应，并将该框架应用于由等离子体效应引起的“间隙”区域，发现轴子填充时间在纳秒量级——当前原子钟精度下可能可观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent observations suggest the existence of inhomogeneous axion regions near neutron star polar caps, where extreme electromagnetic fields may drastically enhance axion production. Understanding how these environments modify electromagnetic wave propagation—particularly polarization rotation—is crucial for detecting axions and probing new physics beyond the Standard Model via astrophysical signatures.

近期观测表明中子星极冠附近可能存在非均匀轴子区域，极端电磁场可极大增强轴子产生。理解这些环境如何改变电磁波传播（特别是偏振旋转）对于通过天体物理信号探测轴子及超越标准模型的新物理至关重要。

Method: The authors use classical electrodynamics extended by axion electrodynamics (Maxwell's equations coupled to an axion field) to derive the general form of electromagnetic waves in the presence of static $B_0 \sim 10^8\,$T and $E_0 \sim 10^{-6}cB_0$ fields. They analyze wave solutions in two forms: standard and a hybrid physically intuitive representation. Nonreciprocal behavior and polarization rotation are computed using perturbation theory for weak axion fields, while noting its breakdown for strong fields. Spatial variation of the axion field is required for observable effects. The filling time of axion 'gaps' due to plasma-induced depletion is estimated using continuity and flow arguments.

作者采用扩展的轴子电动力学（麦克斯韦方程组耦合轴子场）来推导在静态$B_0 \sim 10^8\,$T 和 $E_0 \sim 10^{-6}cB_0$场中电磁波的一般形式。分析了两种形式的波解：标准形式与一种混合的、物理直观的表示。使用微扰理论计算弱轴子场下的非互易行为和偏振旋转，同时指出强场下微扰失效。可观测效应要求轴子场具有空间变化。通过连续性方程和流动论证估算了等离子体诱导耗尽导致的轴子‘间隙’填充时间。

Result: Polarization rotation of electromagnetic waves occurs only when the axion field varies in space or time; static homogeneous axion backgrounds do not induce rotation. In neutron star polar caps, with $B_0 \sim 10^8\,$T and $E_0 \sim 10^{-6}cB_0$, axion production is enhanced by up to $10^{50}$ compared to average cosmic values. The resulting polarization rotation is significant for weak but non-uniform axion fields. For very strong fields, perturbation theory breaks down. Axion 'gap' regions—depleted due to plasma effects—are filled on a timescale of nanoseconds, within reach of atomic clock precision measurements.

仅当轴子场在空间或时间上变化时，电磁波的偏振面才会发生旋转；静态均匀轴子背景不会引起旋转。在中子星极冠区域，$B_0 \sim 10^8\,$T 和 $E_0 \sim 10^{-6}cB_0$条件下，轴子产生率相比宇宙平均值增强高达$10^{50}$倍。由此产生的偏振旋转在弱但非均匀的轴子场中显著。对于极强场，微扰理论失效。由于等离子体效应导致的轴子‘间隙’区域在纳秒量级内被填充，处于原子钟精度可测量范围内。

Conclusion: The study establishes that spatial variations in axion fields within neutron star polar caps can lead to observable electromagnetic signatures such as polarization rotation, provided sufficiently strong magnetic and electric fields are present. The predicted enhancement in axion production and the short filling times of gap regions make these systems promising targets for future axion detection experiments using high-precision timing and polarimetry.

本研究表明，在中子星极冠内，只要存在足够强的电磁场，轴子场的空间变化即可导致可观测的电磁信号（如偏振旋转）。预测的轴子产生增强效应以及间隙区域的短填充时间使得这些系统成为利用高精度计时与偏振测量进行未来轴子探测实验的理想目标。

Abstract: Recent investigations by Noordhuis et al. [1, 2] and others have demonstrated the occurrence of strong local inhomogeneous axion regions in the polar cap regions of neutron stars. These regions are characterized by static magnetic fields $B_0 \sim 10^8\,$T ($=10^{12}\,$G) directed normally outwards from the polar surface (magnetic dipole), together with static electric fields $E_0 \sim 10^{-6}cB_0$ in the same direction (electric dipole). An enormous increase of axion production, up to order $10^{50}$, is predicted in the polar regions. These features are important for phenomena such as polarization plane rotation under both weak and strong axion field populations. We survey the peculiar antenna property of conductive materials, which shows the need for having very strong magnetic fields to make the detection possible. We present the general form of electromagnetic waves in the axion environment, in both the standard form and in a physically instructive hybrid one, showing the nonreciprocity of axion fluid, and calculate the polarization rotation. The rotation is well defined in the case of weak, but still stronger than average value of axion fields in Universe. For very strong fields such a perturbative theory breaks down, however. A noteworthy general property of the rotation of polarization plane is that it can only occur when the axion cloud is varying in space or time. We limit ourselves only variation in space. Finally, as application we discuss the physical picture of local 'gap' regions proposed by Noordhuis et al. in the polar regions of a neutron star. The reason for occurrence of these gaps is plasma effects. To evaluate the time scales involved, we calculate the filling time for surrounding axions flowing into an initial gap. It turns out that the typical filling time is a moderate number of nanoseconds, within the accuracy of atomic clocks precision to be detectable.

### [23] [Entanglement Signatures of CPT Violation in Neutrino Oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28841)
*Bipin Singh Koranga,Baktiar Wasir Farooq*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores how CPT violation and quantum gravity effects at the Planck scale influence entanglement entropy in two-flavor neutrino oscillations, showing that CPT asymmetry manifests as a measurable difference in entropy between neutrinos and antineutrinos, with implications for probing new physics via quantum information measures.

本文研究了CPT破坏和普朗克尺度量子引力效应对双味中微子振荡纠缠熵的影响，表明CPT不对称性会在中微子与反中微子的熵之间产生可观测差异，并提出利用量子信息手段探测新物理的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To identify novel signatures of CPT-violating Planck-scale physics in neutrino systems by leveraging quantum information-theoretic measures such as entanglement entropy, which may reveal effects beyond standard oscillation phenomenology.

旨在通过纠缠熵等量子信息理论工具，寻找中微子体系中CPT破坏性普朗克尺度物理的新信号，揭示超出标准振荡现象学的新效应。

Method: Constructed a CPT-violating neutrino mass matrix derived from flavor-blind Planck-scale physics; computed the von Neumann entanglement entropy for both neutrinos and antineutrinos; analyzed the entropy asymmetry as a function of Majorana phases $a_1$ and $a_2$, under a degenerate mass spectrum assumption ($m_\nu \simeq 2\,\mathrm{eV}$).

基于味盲普朗克尺度物理构建CPT破坏的中微子质量矩阵；分别计算中微子和反中微子的冯·诺依曼纠缠熵；在简并质量谱（$m_\nu \simeq 2\,\mathrm{eV}$）下分析熵不对称性随马约拉纳相位$a_1$和$a_2$的变化。

Result: CPT violation induces a measurable asymmetry between neutrino and antineutrino entanglement entropies; this asymmetry is controlled by the Majorana phases $a_1$ and $a_2$, which are also required to explain the solar KamLAND anomaly under a degenerate mass spectrum; thus, entanglement entropy serves as a direct probe of such CPT-violating physics.

CPT破坏导致中微子与反中微子纠缠熵之间的可测量不对称性；该不对称性的幅度由马约拉纳相位$a_1$和$a_2$控制，而这些相位也用于解释在简并质量谱下的太阳KamLAND反常；因此，纠缠熵成为探测此类CPT破坏物理的直接工具。

Conclusion: Entanglement entropy provides a sensitive and novel observable for testing CPT-violating Planck-scale physics in neutrino systems, linking quantum-gravitational effects, fundamental symmetries, and quantum information science in the context of flavor oscillations.

纠缠熵为检验中微子系统中CPT破坏的普朗克尺度物理提供了一个敏感且新颖的观测量，将量子引力效应、基本对称性和量子信息科学在味振荡背景下联系起来。

Abstract: We investigate the joint influence of CPT violation and quantum-gravity-induced Planck-scale corrections on the entanglement entropy of two-flavor neutrino oscillations. Building on the CPT-violating neutrino mass matrix arising from flavour-blind Planck-scale physics, we compute the von Neumann entanglement entropy separately for neutrinos and anti-neutrinos and demonstrate that CPT violation directly imprints an observable asymmetry in their entropy profiles. For a degenerate mass spectrum (m_ν\simeq2\,\mathrm{eV}), non-zero Majorana phases a_{1} and a_{2} are required to reproduce the solar KamLAND discrepancy; these same phases control the amplitude of the entropy asymmetry. Our results establish that entanglement entropy provides a sensitive and novel probe of CPT-violating Planck-scale physics within neutrino phenomenology.

</details>


### [24] [Boltzmann Equation Solver for Thermalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28848)
*Jong-Hyun Yoon*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: BEST (Boltzmann Equation Solver for Thermalization) is a Python framework that solves the momentum-resolved Boltzmann equation for arbitrary $n_{\rm in} \to n_{\rm out}$ scattering processes using a direct, high-dimensional Monte Carlo evaluation of the collision integral with exact momentum conservation and Gaussian-approximated energy conservation; it correctly handles identical particles in number-changing processes and supports massive, coupled species with time-dependent masses, quantum statistics, and cosmological expansion, enabling scalable simulations across hundreds of cores.

BEST（Boltzmann Equation Solver for Thermalization）是一个Python框架，通过直接的高维蒙特卡洛方法求解任意$n_{\rm in} \to n_{\rm out}$散射过程的动量分辨玻尔兹曼方程；该框架精确保持动量守恒，用高斯函数近似能量守恒，并正确处理变数过程中全同粒子的贡献，支持具有时变质量、量子统计和宇宙膨胀背景的多组分耦合系统，可扩展至数百核心并行计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Accurate simulation of thermalization dynamics in particle systems with general scattering processes, especially those involving number-changing interactions ($n_{\rm in} \neq n_{\rm out}$) and identical particles, requires precise treatment of the Boltzmann collision integral. Existing methods often rely on approximations or simplified phase-space reductions that may violate energy conservation or misrepresent reaction rates when multiplicities differ between initial and final states.

在包含变数相互作用（$n_{\rm in} \neq n_{\rm out}$）和全同粒子的粒子系统中，热化动力学的精确模拟需要对玻尔兹曼碰撞积分进行精细处理。现有方法常依赖近似或简化的相空间约化，可能破坏能量守恒或在初末态多重数不等时错误描述反应率。

Method: The collision integral is computed directly in $3(n_{\rm total}-2)$ dimensions using the VEGAS adaptive Monte Carlo algorithm with vectorized batch evaluation. Momentum conservation is enforced exactly by solving for one particle's momentum via the constraint $\sum \vec{p}_{\rm in} = \sum \vec{p}_{\rm out}$, while energy conservation is implemented using a narrow Gaussian approximation to the delta function $\delta(E_{\rm in} - E_{\rm out})$. For processes with identical particles and $n_{\rm in} \neq n_{\rm out}$, the full rate includes contributions from placing the observed momentum on both sides of the reaction, weighted by initial and final state multiplicities. The code supports time-dependent masses, quantum statistics (Bose-Einstein/Fermi-Dirac), multiple species, cosmological expansion (comoving momenta), and Euler/Heun integration. Parallelization is achieved via MPI distribution over momentum grid points.

碰撞积分在$3(n_{\rm total}-2)$维空间中使用VEGAS自适应蒙特卡洛算法结合向量化批量评估直接计算。动量守恒通过约束条件$\sum \vec{p}_{\rm in} = \sum \vec{p}_{\rm out}$精确实施，能量守恒通过窄高斯函数逼近$\delta(E_{\rm in} - E_{\rm out})$实现。对于含全同粒子且$n_{\rm in} \neq n_{\rm out}$的过程，完整反应率需分别将观测动量置于反应两侧并按初末态多重数加权求和。代码支持时变质量、量子统计（Bose-Einstein/Fermi-Dirac）、多物种耦合、宇宙膨胀（共动动量）及Euler/Heun时间积分，并通过MPI在动量网格点上并行化。

Result: Monte Carlo results are validated against a semi-analytical $2 \to 2$ collision integral with exact energy conservation, showing excellent agreement. In a $2 \leftrightarrow 3$ thermalization example with a massive scalar field, energy conservation is violated if identical-particle contributions are not fully summed over both reaction sides, but is restored when the correct weighting by multiplicity is applied. BEST demonstrates near-linear parallel scaling up to hundreds of CPU cores.

蒙特卡洛结果与具有精确能量守恒的半解析$2 \to 2$碰撞积分对比，显示极好一致性。在一个涉及大质量标量场的$2 \leftrightarrow 3$热化示例中，若未正确求和反应两侧的全同粒子贡献，则能量守恒被破坏；仅当按多重数正确加权后，能量守恒得以恢复。BEST在数百CPU核心上展现出近线性并行加速比。

Conclusion: BEST provides a robust, flexible, and scalable framework for solving the Boltzmann equation in generic particle systems with number-changing interactions. A key theoretical insight is the necessity of summing over all possible placements of the observed momentum in reactions with identical particles when $n_{\rm in} \neq n_{\rm out}$, which ensures energy conservation and correct reaction rates. This makes BEST particularly suitable for studying thermalization in early universe scenarios, dark matter production, and other out-of-equilibrium phenomena.

BEST为含变数相互作用的通用粒子系统提供了一个稳健、灵活且可扩展的玻尔兹曼方程求解框架。一个关键理论洞见是：当$n_{\rm in} \neq n_{\rm out}$时，必须对全同粒子反应中观测动量的所有可能位置求和，以确保能量守恒和正确反应率。这使得BEST特别适用于早期宇宙、暗物质产生及其他非平衡现象的研究。

Abstract: We present BEST (Boltzmann Equation Solver for Thermalization), a Python framework for solving the momentum-resolved Boltzmann equation for arbitrary $n_{\rm in} \to n_{\rm out}$ scattering processes. The collision integral is evaluated directly in $3(n_{\rm total}-2)$ dimensions using the VEGAS adaptive Monte Carlo algorithm with vectorized batch evaluation. Momentum conservation is enforced exactly by expressing one particle's momentum through the constraint, while energy conservation is imposed via a narrow Gaussian representation of the delta function. We identify a subtlety in the construction of the collision integral for processes with unequal initial and final multiplicities ($n_{\rm in} \neq n_{\rm out}$) involving identical particles: the full collision rate requires separate evaluation with the observed momentum pinned to each side of the reaction, weighted by the respective particle multiplicities. Failure to account for this leads to systematic violation of energy conservation. The code supports massive particles with time-dependent masses, Bose-Einstein and Fermi-Dirac quantum statistics, multiple coupled species, cosmological expansion with comoving momenta, and both Euler and Heun time integration. Parallelization is achieved by distributing independent momentum grid points across MPI ranks, yielding near-linear scaling to hundreds of cores. We validate the Monte Carlo results against a semi-analytical $2 \to 2$ collision integral with exact energy conservation, following the phase-space reduction of Ala-Mattinen et al. As a demonstration, we study thermalization of a massive scalar field through a $2 \leftrightarrow 3$ number-changing process and show that energy conservation is restored only when all identical-particle contributions are correctly summed. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/best-hep/best.

</details>


### [25] [Quasi-linear theory of fast flavor instabilities in homogeneous environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28854)
*Damiano F. G. Fiorillo,Georg G. Raffelt*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper proposes a quasi-linear theory (QLT) to describe flavor waves (flavomons) in dense neutrino plasmas as independent linear degrees of freedom, incorporating backreaction and nonresonant interactions; the model accurately reproduces results from full quantum kinetic equations in simplified settings, validating QLT as a tool to circumvent computational challenges in simulating nonlinear neutrino flavor instabilities.

本文首次将密集中微子等离子体中的味波（flavomons）视为独立的线性自由度，提出了一种准线性理论（QLT），包含对中微子分布的反作用及非共振中微子-味子相互作用。在均匀轴对称模型中，该理论的饱和分布与原始量子动力学方程的周期性盒模拟结果高度一致，验证了QLT在规避非线性小尺度效应模拟困难方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Neutrino flavor instabilities in dense environments, such as core-collapse supernovae or the early universe, can lead to rapid flavor equilibration through collisionless processes. Direct simulation of these effects via quantum kinetic equations is computationally challenging due to nonlinear small-scale dynamics. The motivation is to develop an effective framework—inspired by plasma physics—that simplifies the treatment of these instabilities by separating wave and particle dynamics, enabling more tractable modeling of flavor evolution.

在核心坍缩超新星或早期宇宙等高密度环境中，中微子味不稳定性可通过无碰撞过程引发快速味平衡。由于非线性小尺度动力学的存在，通过量子动力学方程直接模拟这些效应计算成本极高。本文旨在借鉴等离子体物理中的方法，发展一种有效框架，通过分离波与粒子动力学来简化味不稳定性的处理，从而实现更易处理的味演化建模。

Method: The authors introduce flavomons as quantized flavor waves and formulate a quasi-linear theory (QLT) in which these waves act as independent linear degrees of freedom. The method includes backreaction of flavomons on the neutrino distribution function and accounts for nonresonant neutrino--flavomon interactions, while neglecting wave--wave coupling. The model is applied to a homogeneous, axisymmetric setup and compared against periodic-box solutions of the full quantum kinetic equation.

作者将flavomons作为量化味波引入，并构建准线性理论（QLT），其中这些波被视为独立的线性自由度。该方法包含了flavomon对中微子分布函数的反作用，并考虑了非共振中微子- fl avomon相互作用，但忽略波-波耦合。该模型应用于均匀轴对称系统，并与完整量子动力学方程的周期性盒解进行对比。

Result: The quasi-linear theory successfully reproduces the saturated neutrino and flavomon distributions observed in simulations of the full quantum kinetic equation. Agreement is particularly strong in the homogeneous, axisymmetric configuration, demonstrating that QLT captures essential nonlinear dynamics without resolving small-scale turbulence directly. This validates the separation of timescales and the neglect of wave--wave interactions in this regime.

准线性理论成功复现了完整量子动力学方程模拟中观察到的饱和中微子和flavomon分布。在均匀轴对称构型下，吻合尤为良好，表明QLT无需直接解析小尺度湍流即可捕捉关键的非线性动力学。这验证了在此条件下时间尺度分离及忽略波-波相互作用的合理性。

Conclusion: Quasi-linear theory, long used in classical plasma physics, is applicable to neutrino flavor evolution in dense media when flavomons are treated as dynamical degrees of freedom. This approach provides a promising alternative to direct simulations of nonlinear kinetic equations, offering a pathway to model flavor instabilities in astrophysical environments where full computation is infeasible.

准线性理论（QLT）在将flavomon视为动力学自由度时，可适用于致密介质中的中微子味演化。这一方法为直接求解非线性动力学方程提供了有前景的替代方案，为在无法进行全尺度计算的天体物理环境中建模味不稳定性开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Dense neutrino plasmas can develop instabilities that drive collisionless flavor exchange, equivalent to the emission of flavomons, the quanta of flavor waves. We treat these waves, for the first time, as independent linear degrees of freedom and develop a quasi-linear theory (QLT), including backreaction on the neutrino distribution and nonresonant neutrino--flavomon interactions, while neglecting wave--wave processes. In a homogeneous, axisymmetric model, the saturated neutrino and flavomon distributions agree closely with periodic-box solutions of the original quantum kinetic equation. These results support the use of QLT, well established in plasma physics, to bypass nonlinear small-scale effects that challenge direct simulations.

### [26] [Neutrinos as Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28859)
*James M. Cline,Gonzalo Herrera,Jean-Samuel Roux*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We propose that cold, enhanced-density active neutrinos could act as dark matter, evading standard constraints via late-time production from a light scalar decay; this scenario is testable via an amplified Cosmic Neutrino Background (C$\nu$B) and predicts observable neutrinophilic scalars with $y \sim 10^{-16}-10^{-12}$, favoring a Majoron with inverted neutrino mass hierarchy.

我们提出，通过轻标量场晚期衰变产生的冷且高密度的活性中微子可有效作为暗物质，避开标准限制；该情景可通过增强的宇宙中微子背景（C$\nu$B）进行检验，并预言可观测的中微子亲和性标量粒子（$y \sim 10^{-16}-10^{-12}$），结构形成约束更支持Majoron与中微子逆质量层级的情景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Active neutrinos are ruled out in $\Lambda$CDM as dark matter due to their low mass and relativistic free-streaming, which suppresses small-scale structure. However, if active neutrinos acquire a non-thermal, cold distribution via late-time production, they could evade these constraints and contribute significantly to dark matter.

在$\Lambda$CDM模型中，活性中微子因质量过低且具有相对论性自由传播，会抑制小尺度结构形成，因而被排除为暗物质候选者。然而，若活性中微子通过晚期非热产生机制获得冷分布，则可能避开这些限制，并显著贡献于暗物质密度。

Method: We consider late-time decays of a light scalar field (e.g., a Majoron) into active neutrino pairs, producing a cold, non-thermal population. The scalar is not in thermal equilibrium, allowing for a large neutrino number density today without violating CMB or BBN bounds. We compute the resulting energy density and phase-space distribution, and assess compatibility with structure formation and C$\nu$B detection prospects.

我们考虑轻标量场（如Majoron）晚期衰变为活性中微子对，产生冷的非热中微子群体。该标量场不处于热平衡，使得今日中微子数密度可显著增强而不违反CMB或BBN限制。我们计算了相应的能量密度与相空间分布，并评估其与结构形成及C$\nu$B探测前景的兼容性。

Result: A neutrino density enhancement of $\sim 100-200$ relative to $\Lambda$CDM is possible, making active neutrinos viable dark matter candidates if produced cold. The required Yukawa couplings are $y \sim 5\times10^{-16}-10^{-12}$. Structure formation favors a Majoron scalar and inverted neutrino mass hierarchy due to kinematic suppression of late decays in the normal hierarchy.

相对于$\Lambda$CDM，中微子密度可增强$\sim 100-200$倍，若为冷产生则活性中微子可成为可行的暗物质候选者。所需Yukawa耦合为$y \sim 5\times10^{-16}-10^{-12}$。结构形成更倾向于Majoron标量与中微子逆质量层级，因正常层级下晚期衰变受运动学抑制。

Conclusion: Cold, non-thermally enhanced active neutrinos from late scalar decays can behave as dark matter, evading traditional constraints. This scenario is falsifiable via direct C$\nu$B detection experiments (e.g., PTOLEMY), which would observe a strongly enhanced event rate. It also motivates searches for very weakly coupled neutrinophilic scalars, potentially linked to neutrino mass generation (e.g., Majorons).

来自晚期标量衰变的冷型、非热增强活性中微子可作为暗物质，避开传统限制。该情景可通过C$\nu$B直接探测实验（如PTOLEMY）证伪，预期事件率显著增强。这也激励对极弱耦合中微子亲和性标量粒子的搜索，可能与中微子质量生成机制相关（如Majoron）。

Abstract: Active neutrinos in standard cosmology were ruled out as a dark matter candidate in the 1980's. The reason is twofold: they are too light to account for the observed energy density of dark matter in the Universe, and their relativistic nature would spoil structure formation. In this note we suggest that an enhanced density of cold Standard Model active neutrinos today could behave effectively as dark matter, avoiding constraints from recombination and structure formation. Such an enhancement could be produced, for instance, by late-time decays of a light scalar field that is not in thermal equilibrium with the plasma. This mechanism is testable through the detection of the Cosmic Neutrino Background (C$ν$B), which could have an average cosmological energy density a factor of $\sim 100-200$ times larger than expected in $Λ$CDM. The postulated light neutrinophilic scalar field may be observable, with Yukawa couplings in the range $y \sim 5 \times 10^{-16}-10^{-12}$. A scenario preferred by structure formation constraints is that the scalar is a Majoron, and the neutrinos have an inverted mass hierarchy.

### [27] [A Determination of the Top Mass from a Global PDF Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28865)
*Richard D. Ball,Jaco ter Hoeve,Roy Stegeman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We perform a global analysis of parton distribution functions using the NNPDF framework to indirectly determine the top-quark pole mass $m_t$, incorporating a broad set of collider data, higher-order corrections, and novel theoretical inputs such as toponium effects and lattice constraints on $\alpha_s$. By jointly fitting $m_t$ and $\alpha_s$ with proper PDF refitting, we obtain $m_t = 172.80 \pm 0.26$ GeV at approximate ${\rm N^3LO}$ QCD accuracy, including NLO QED, EW, and toponium contributions.

我们利用NNPDF框架进行部分子分布函数的全局分析，间接确定顶夸克极点质量$m_t$，纳入广泛的对撞机数据、高阶修正及新颖理论输入（如toponium效应和来自格点的$\alpha_s$约束）。通过联合拟合$m_t$与$\alpha_s$并正确重构PDF以关联不确定性，我们在近似${\rm N^3LO}$ QCD精度下得到结果$m_t = 172.80 \pm 0.26$ GeV，包含NLO QED、EW和toponium修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The precise determination of the top-quark pole mass $m_t$ is crucial for testing the consistency of the Standard Model and for predictions in high-energy processes such as Higgs production and vacuum stability. However, direct measurements are affected by non-perturbative uncertainties, while indirect determinations via global fits require consistent treatment of correlations with other parameters like $\alpha_s$ and the parton distribution functions (PDFs). This work aims to improve the precision and robustness of the indirect $m_t$ extraction by including new theoretical elements and ensuring proper uncertainty propagation through full PDF refitting.

精确测定顶夸克极点质量$m_t$对于检验标准模型一致性以及希格斯产生和真空稳定性等高能过程预测至关重要。然而，直接测量受非微扰不确定性的限制，而通过全局拟合进行间接提取则需要一致处理其与其他参数（如$\alpha_s$和部分子分布函数PDF）的相关性。本工作旨在引入新的理论要素并通过完整的PDF重拟合确保不确定性正确传播，从而提高间接提取$m_t$的精度和稳健性。

Method: We employ the NNPDF framework for a global analysis of PDFs, incorporating a wide range of single- and double-differential cross-section measurements from ATLAS and CMS at 8 and 13 TeV. Theoretical predictions are computed at NNLO QCD with EW corrections, while PDF evolution is treated up to approximate ${\rm N^3LO}$ QCD accuracy with NLO QED corrections. We include toponium resonance effects near the $t\bar{t}$ threshold, incorporate state-of-the-art lattice results for $\alpha_s$, and perform a detailed sensitivity analysis of individual datasets. Crucially, we refit the PDFs for varying values of $(\alpha_s, m_t)$ to properly account for their mutual correlations and avoid bias from interpolation methods.

我们采用NNPDF框架进行PDF的全局分析，纳入来自ATLAS和CMS在8和13 TeV下的单微分与双微分截面测量数据。理论预测在NNLO QCD加EW修正下计算，PDF演化处理至近似${\rm N^3LO}$ QCD精度并包含NLO QED修正。我们纳入$t\bar{t}$阈值附近的toponium共振效应，结合格点QCD给出的先进$\alpha_s$结果，并对各数据集进行详细敏感性分析。关键的是，我们针对不同的$(\alpha_s, m_t)$值重新拟合PDF，以正确计入其相互关联，避免插值方法带来的偏差。

Result: We obtain a precise indirect determination of the top-quark pole mass: $m_t = 172.80 \pm 0.26$ GeV, at approximate ${\rm N^3LO}$ QCD accuracy, including NLO QED, EW, and toponium corrections. The analysis highlights significant tensions between some ATLAS and CMS differential measurements, and demonstrates that a combined fit requires full PDF refitting to correctly propagate uncertainties. The inclusion of lattice $\alpha_s$ constraints and toponium effects improves the robustness of the result.

我们在近似${\rm N^3LO}$ QCD精度下获得顶夸克极点质量的精确间接测定结果：$m_t = 172.80 \pm 0.26$ GeV，包含NLO QED、EW和toponium修正。分析揭示了某些ATLAS与CMS微分测量之间存在显著张力，并表明联合拟合必须通过完整PDF重拟合才能正确传播不确定性。引入格点$\alpha_s$约束和toponium效应增强了结果的稳健性。

Conclusion: A robust and precise indirect determination of the top-quark pole mass requires a global PDF analysis with full refitting to capture correlations between $m_t$, $\alpha_s$, and PDFs. Our result, $m_t = 172.80 \pm 0.26$ GeV, benefits from state-of-the-art theoretical inputs—including toponium dynamics, lattice $\alpha_s$, and high-precision differential data—setting a new benchmark for indirect $m_t$ extractions. Future improvements will come from full ${\rm N^3LO}$ calculations and more precise experimental data.

一个稳健且精确的顶夸克极点质量间接测定需要通过全局PDF分析并完整重拟合，以捕捉$m_t$、$\alpha_s$与PDF之间的关联。我们的结果$m_t = 172.80 \pm 0.26$ GeV得益于先进的理论输入——包括toponium动力学、格点$\alpha_s$和高精度微分数据——为间接提取$m_t$设立了新基准。未来的改进将来自完整的${\rm N^3LO}$计算和更精确的实验数据。

Abstract: We present an indirect determination of the top-quark pole mass $m_t$ within a global analysis of parton distribution functions (PDFs), based on the public NNPDF framework. We consider a wide range of measurements, including both single- and double-differential observables, computed at NNLO QCD accuracy with EW corrections, and analyse their individual as well as combined impact on the joint $(α_s, m_t)$ parameter space, while accounting for PDF evolution up to approximate ${\rm N^3LO}$ QCD accuracy with QED corrections. We account for missing higher order QCD uncertainties by default. Unique to our analysis are the inclusion of, first, toponium contributions around the $t\bar{t}$ threshold, second, state-of-the-art constraints on $α_s$ from the lattice, and finally, a detailed sensitivity study of the various ATLAS and CMS differential cross-section measurements at 8 and 13 TeV. We demonstrate explicitly how a combined determination requires the refitting of the PDFs in order to correctly correlate uncertainties. We find $m_t = 172.80 \pm 0.26$ GeV at approximate N$^3$LO QCD including NLO QED, EW and toponium corrections.

### [28] [Higgs Boson Spookiness: Probing Quantum Nonlocality with Spacetime-Resolved $H\rightarrowτ^+τ^-$ Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28868)
*Lawrence Lee,John Lawless,Caroline Riggall*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A future precision $ee$ Higgs factory can perform spacetime-resolved tests of quantum nonlocality in Higgs boson decays, specifically using $ee\rightarrow ZH \rightarrow (\mu\mu)(\tau\tau)$ events at $\sqrt{s}=240$ GeV. By reconstructing $\tau$ decay vertices and measuring spin correlations as a function of the spacetime interval, this method enables direct tests of Bell inequality violations for spacelike-separated decays, excluding superluminal entanglement signaling below $\approx2c$ (95\% CL) with 0.75 ab$^{-1}$ luminosity.

未来高精度的正负电子希格斯工厂能够对希格斯玻色子衰变中的量子非定域性进行时空分辨的检验。通过在$\sqrt{s}=240$ GeV下模拟$ee\rightarrow ZH \rightarrow (\mu\mu)(\tau\tau)$事例，重建$\tau$轻子衰变顶点并测量两个$\tau$衰变间时空间隔的自旋关联，可直接排除超光速、有限速度纠缠信号理论（低于约$2c$）。



<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Quantum entanglement is a cornerstone of quantum mechanics, but its compatibility with relativity—particularly whether entanglement involves superluminal signaling—remains a foundational question. While Bell tests have confirmed nonlocal correlations, they typically assume spacelike separation without directly resolving the spacetime structure of the measurements. A direct, spacetime-resolved test in a high-energy collider environment could exclude models with finite-speed entanglement propagation, bridging quantum mechanics and relativity in a novel regime.

量子纠缠是量子力学的核心，但其与相对论的相容性——特别是是否涉及超光速信号传递——仍是基础物理问题。尽管贝尔实验已证实非定域关联，通常假设类空间隔而未直接解析测量的时空结构。在高能对撞机环境中进行直接的时空分辨检验，可排除有限速度纠缠传播模型，为量子力学与相对论的融合提供新途径。


Method: The study uses simulated $ee\rightarrow ZH \rightarrow (\mu\mu)(\tau\tau)$ events at $\sqrt{s}=240$ GeV. The $\tau$ lepton decay vertices are reconstructed to determine the spacetime positions of the decays. Spin correlations between the two $\tau$ leptons are measured as a function of the invariant spacetime interval $\Delta s^2 = (\Delta t)^2 - (\Delta x)^2/c^2$. Events with spacelike separation ($\Delta s^2 < 0$) are selected to test for Bell-inequality-violating correlations while varying the assumed maximum speed $v_{\text{sig}}$ of entanglement propagation. The analysis sets limits on $v_{\text{sig}}$ by testing consistency with quantum predictions versus finite-speed models.

研究使用在$\sqrt{s}=240$ GeV下的$ee\rightarrow ZH \rightarrow (\mu\mu)(\tau\tau)$模拟事例。重建$\tau$轻子衰变顶点以确定衰变的时空位置，并作为不变时空间隔$\Delta s^2 = (\Delta t)^2 - (\Delta x)^2/c^2$的函数测量两$\tau$轻子间的自旋关联。选择类空间隔事例($\Delta s^2 < 0$)来检验贝尔不等式破坏关联，同时改变纠缠传播的最大假定速度$v_{\text{sig}}$。通过检验与量子预言和有限速度模型的一致性，设定$v_{\text{sig}}$的限制。


Result: With an integrated luminosity of 0.75 ab$^{-1}$, the proposed measurement can exclude entanglement signal propagation speeds below $\approx2c$ at 95\% confidence level. Furthermore, any model predicting measurable spin correlations can be ruled out for propagation speeds below $\approx9c$. The sensitivity arises from precise vertex reconstruction and large event statistics at a Higgs factory, enabling resolution of spacetime intervals on the order of $10^{-23}$ s and $10^{-15}$ m.

在0.75 ab$^{-1}$积分亮度下，该测量可在95\%置信水平排除低于约$2c$的纠缠信号传播速度。此外，任何预测可测自旋关联的模型在传播速度低于约$9c$时均可被排除。灵敏度源于希格斯工厂中精确的顶点重建和大量事例统计，可分辨约$10^{-23}$秒和$10^{-15}$米量级的时空间隔。


Conclusion: This work proposes the first spacetime-resolved test of electroweak-scale quantum entanglement at a particle collider. By linking spin correlations to the spacetime structure of $\tau$ decays, it enables direct experimental constraints on finite-speed entanglement signaling, ruling out superluminal models up to $\sim2c$. This demonstrates a unique capability of future Higgs factories beyond precision Standard Model measurements, opening a new frontier in testing quantum foundations at high energies.

本工作提出了在粒子对撞机上首次对电弱尺度量子纠缠进行时空分辨检验的方法。通过将自旋关联与$\tau$衰变的时空结构关联，可直接对有限速度纠缠信号模型施加实验限制，排除高达约$2c$的超光速模型。这展示了未来希格斯工厂超越标准模型精密测量的独特能力，开启了在高能条件下检验量子基础的新前沿。


Abstract: We demonstrate that a future precision $ee$ Higgs factory would be able to perform a spacetime-resolved test of quantum nonlocality in Higgs boson decays. In simulated $ee\rightarrow ZH \rightarrow (μμ)(ττ)$ events at $\sqrt{s}=240$ GeV, we reconstruct $τ$ lepton decay vertices and measure spin correlations as a function of the spacetime interval between the two $τ$ decays. Such a measurement would be able to test Bell-inequality-violating correlations for spacelike-separated decays, enabling direct exclusion of superluminal, finite-speed entanglement signaling theories. With 0.75 ab$^{-1}$ of integrated luminosity, entanglement signal propagation speeds below $\approx2c$ can be excluded at 95$\%$ CL. Signals establishing any spin correlation can be excluded for speeds below $\approx9c$. This constitutes the first proposed spacetime-resolved measurement of electroweak quantum entanglement at a particle collider and demonstrates a unique capability of future Higgs factories.

### [29] [Misalignment from kicks: the impact of particle interactions on ultra-light dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28881)
*Clare Burrage,Sergio Sevillano Muñoz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates how interactions between oscillating ultra-light scalar dark matter and Standard Model or dark sector fields modify the scalar field's evolution and late-time oscillation amplitude, thereby affecting dark matter abundance. For quadratic couplings to Standard Model fields, the authors estimate corrections to the misalignment mechanism; for axion-like fields coupled to dark sector matter, transient instabilities can induce large field displacements.

本文研究了振荡的超轻标量暗物质与标准模型或暗区场之间的相互作用如何改变标量场的演化及晚期振荡幅度，从而影响暗物质丰度。对于与标准模型场呈二次耦合的情况，作者估算了对错位机制的修正；对于与暗区物质耦合的类轴子场，则发现可能出现瞬态不稳定性，导致大尺度场位移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The misalignment mechanism is a well-known way to generate dark matter from coherent scalar field oscillations, but it assumes decoupling from other sectors. This work explores how couplings between the dark matter scalar and either Standard Model or dark sector fields can alter the field's initial conditions and dynamics, potentially changing the predicted dark matter abundance.

错位机制是通过相干标量场振荡产生暗物质的经典途径，但其通常假设标量场与其他部门解耦。本研究旨在探索若暗物质标量场与标准模型或暗区场存在耦合时，如何改变场的初值条件和动力学行为，进而影响暗物质丰度的预测。

Method: The authors analyze the equations of motion for ultra-light scalar fields with quadratic couplings to Standard Model energy density, computing the shift in the scalar potential minimum due to thermal and matter effects. They also study axion-like fields coupled to dark sector matter, identifying parameter regimes where tachyonic instabilities lead to rapid growth of field perturbations using linear stability analysis.

作者分析了与标准模型能量密度呈二次耦合的超轻标量场的运动方程，计算了由于热效应和物质效应引起的标量势极小值的偏移。此外，他们研究了与暗区物质耦合的类轴子场，通过线性稳定性分析识别出快子型不稳定性（tachyonic instabilities）导致扰动迅速增长的参数区域。

Result: For scalars quadratically coupled to the Standard Model, the shift in the field value can suppress or enhance the final oscillation amplitude depending on the coupling strength, modifying the dark matter relic abundance prediction. For axion-like fields interacting with dark sector matter, temporary tachyonic instabilities can displace the field far from its vacuum expectation value, significantly altering the initial conditions for the misalignment mechanism.

对于与标准模型呈二次耦合的标量场，场值的偏移会根据耦合强度抑制或增强最终振荡幅度，从而改变暗物质遗存丰度的预测。对于与暗区物质相互作用的类轴子场，短暂的快子型不稳定性可使场远离其真空期望值，显著改变错位机制的初始条件。

Conclusion: Interactions between ultra-light scalar dark matter and other sectors—whether the Standard Model or dark sector—can significantly modify the predictions of the standard misalignment mechanism. These effects must be accounted for when constraining or predicting dark matter properties in models with non-negligible couplings.

超轻标量暗物质与其他部门（无论是标准模型还是暗区）的相互作用会显著改变标准错位机制的预测结果。在考虑不可忽略耦合的模型中，约束或预测暗物质性质时必须计入这些效应。

Abstract: Oscillating ultra-light scalar fields are a natural explanation for the dark matter in our universe, as long as a mechanism, often called a misalignment mechanism, exists to explain the amplitude of the scalar oscillations. If the dark matter scalar couples to the Standard Model, then the dynamics of ordinary matter can influence the behaviour of dark matter in the early universe. In this work we show how this changes the expected value of the scalar field and the resulting amplitude of late time scalar oscillations, and therefore the abundance of dark matter at late times. For dark matter scalars that interact quadratically with Standard Model fields we derive estimates of the size of this effect as a function of the strength of the coupling, and for axion-like fields we show that interactions with dark sector matter can temporarily destabilize the field, leading to large field displacements.

</details>


### [30] [Baryogenesis from Exploding Primordial Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29024)
*Alexandra P. Klipfel,Miguel Vanvlasselaer,Sokratis Trifinopoulos,David I. Kaiser*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Primordial black holes (PBHs) evaporating via Hawking radiation after the electroweak phase transition can generate ultrarelativistic shocks in the plasma, creating bubble-like structures with restored electroweak symmetry. These dynamical interfaces produce chiral charge, which is converted into the observed baryon asymmetry when a TeV-scale CP-violating operator is included, with little sensitivity to PBH parameters.

原始黑洞（PBH）在电弱相变后通过霍金辐射蒸发，可在等离子体中产生超相对论冲击波，形成具有恢复电弱对称性的泡状结构。这些动力学界面产生手征荷，结合TeV尺度的CP破坏算符后可转化为观测到的重子不对称性，且对PBH参数依赖极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The origin of the baryon asymmetry of the universe remains unexplained within the Standard Model. While many mechanisms rely on out-of-equilibrium dynamics during phase transitions, this paper explores an alternative scenario where evaporating PBHs provide the necessary departure from thermal equilibrium and seed chiral charge production through relativistic fluid dynamics.

宇宙重子不对称性的起源在标准模型内仍未得到解释。尽管许多机制依赖于相变期间的非平衡动力学，本文探索了一种替代情景：蒸发的PBH通过相对论流体动力学提供必要的非热平衡条件，并引发手征荷的产生。

Method: The authors model the interaction of Hawking radiation from PBHs with the surrounding plasma, computing the formation of ultrarelativistic shock waves and rarefaction waves. These structures create regions of superheated fluid where electroweak symmetry is temporarily restored. Chiral charge is sourced at the moving interfaces via anomaly coupling, and baryogenesis proceeds through sphaleron processes. A CP-violating operator at the TeV scale is introduced to bias the final baryon number.

作者对PBH的霍金辐射与周围等离子体的相互作用进行建模，计算超相对论冲击波和稀疏波的形成。这些结构产生超热流体区域，其中电弱对称性暂时恢复。通过反常耦合，移动界面处产生手征荷，随后通过Sphaleron过程实现重子生成。引入TeV尺度的CP破坏算符以偏置最终的重子数。

Result: The mechanism robustly generates the observed baryon asymmetry $\eta_B \sim 6 \times 10^{-10}$, with minimal dependence on PBH mass or abundance due to compensating scaling relations in the shock dynamics and particle production. The required CP violation occurs at the TeV scale, making it potentially testable at colliders.

该机制稳健地生成了观测到的重子不对称性 $\eta_B \sim 6 \times 10^{-10}$，由于冲击动力学和粒子产生中的补偿性标度关系，其对PBH质量或丰度的依赖极小。所需的CP破坏发生在TeV尺度，可能在对撞机上被检验。

Conclusion: Evaporating primordial black holes can act as catalytic sites for baryogenesis through relativistic hydrodynamical effects and chiral anomaly-driven charge production. This cosmological bootstrap mechanism links PBH evaporation, electroweak symmetry restoration, and baryon number generation in a novel way, offering testable predictions for early universe physics.

蒸发的原始黑洞可通过相对论流体力学效应和由手征反常驱动的电荷产生，作为重子生成的催化位点。这种宇宙学Bootstrap机制以新颖方式将PBH蒸发、电弱对称性恢复和重子数生成联系起来，为早期宇宙物理提供了可检验的预测。

Abstract: Exploding primordial black holes can source baryon asymmetry soon after the electroweak phase transition, as high-energy Hawking radiation drives ultrarelativistic shocks in the surrounding plasma. The shocks and their trailing rarefaction waves delineate two bubble-like walls around a shell of superheated fluid, in which electroweak symmetry is restored. These moving interfaces source chiral charge, which is converted to baryon number. Upon adding a simple CP-violating operator at the TeV scale, this mechanism yields the observed baryon asymmetry with minimal dependence on PBH model parameters.
