### [31] [Dark photon and U(1)$_{B-L}$ gauge boson from dark Higgs boson decays at FASER and SHiP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28882)
*Takeshi Araki,Kento Asai,Yohei Nakashima,Osamu Seto,Takashi Shimomura,Yoshiki Uchida*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We investigate the production of dark photons and U(1)$_{B-L}$ gauge bosons via dark Higgs decays at FASER, FASER2, and SHiP experiments, including both pair and single vector boson production mechanisms. Updated constraints from FASER data are presented, and future sensitivities are projected, along with implications for freeze-in sterile neutrino dark matter in the U(1)$_{B-L}$ model.

我们研究了FASER和SHiP实验中通过暗希格斯玻色子衰变产生暗光子和U(1)$_{B-L}$规范玻色子的灵敏度，包括来自实壳和虚壳暗希格斯衰变的规范玻色子对产生以及伴随标准模型粒子的单个规范玻色子新产生机制。结合FASER实验的最新结果，给出了对暗光子参数空间的限制，并预测了未来FASER2和SHiP实验对暗光子和U(1)$_{B-L}$规范玻色子的预期灵敏度区域，同时讨论了该模型在冻结-注入型惰性中微子暗物质下的物理含义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Light weakly interacting particles such as dark photons and U(1)$_{B-L}$ gauge bosons are well-motivated candidates in beyond the Standard Model physics, particularly in scenarios involving dark sectors and neutrino mass generation. The detection of these particles through exotic Higgs or dark Higgs decays offers a promising avenue at high-intensity frontier experiments. However, previous analyses often neglect single vector boson production associated with SM particles, which can enhance sensitivity, especially in low-mass and weak-coupling regimes.

诸如暗光子和U(1)$_{B-L}$规范玻色子等轻弱相互作用粒子是超出标准模型物理中极具吸引力的候选者，特别是在涉及暗区和中微子质量生成的场景中。通过奇异希格斯或暗希格斯衰变探测这些粒子，在高强度前沿实验中提供了有前景的探索途径。然而，以往的分析通常忽略了伴随标准模型粒子的单个规范玻色子产生过程，而这一过程在低质量和弱耦合区域可能显著增强探测灵敏度。

Method: We compute the production rates of dark photons and U(1)$_{B-L}$ gauge bosons from both on-shell and off-shell dark Higgs decays, including the novel channel of single vector boson production in association with SM particles (e.g., via $h_d \to V + X_{\text{SM}}$). Decay branching ratios and detector-level event yields are simulated for the FASER, FASER2, and SHiP experiments. Existing limits from FASER are incorporated using public data, and projected sensitivities are derived by estimating signal significance above expected backgrounds.

我们计算了来自实壳和虚壳暗希格斯衰变产生暗光子和U(1)$_{B-L}$规范玻色子的产率，包括新的单个规范玻色子与标准模型粒子（例如通过 $h_d \to V + X_{\text{SM}}$）关联产生的通道。针对FASER、FASER2和SHiP实验模拟了衰变分支比和探测器层面的事例产额。利用公开数据纳入FASER现有的限制，并通过估计信号显著性高于预期背景来推导预期灵敏度。

Result: Updated exclusion bounds on the dark photon parameter space ($m_V$, $\epsilon$) are obtained using FASER data, improving upon previous limits in certain mass-coupling regions. Projections show that FASER2 and SHiP will significantly extend sensitivity to both dark photons and U(1)$_{B-L}$ gauge bosons, particularly in the MeV--GeV mass range. The inclusion of single vector boson production enhances reach in low-$\epsilon$ regions. For the U(1)$_{B-L}$ model with freeze-in sterile neutrino dark matter, the experiments probe viable parameter space where DM is produced via non-thermal mechanisms.

利用FASER数据获得了对暗光子参数空间（$m_V$, $\epsilon$）的更新排除界限，在某些质量和耦合区域优于先前限制。预测表明，FASER2和SHiP将在MeV至GeV质量范围内显著扩展对暗光子和U(1)$_{B-L}$规范玻色子的探测灵敏度。包含单个规范玻色子产生过程增强了在低$\epsilon$区域的探测能力。对于具有冻结-注入型惰性中微子暗物质的U(1)$_{B-L}$模型，这些实验能够探测通过非热机制产生暗物质的可行参数空间。

Conclusion: The search for dark sector vector bosons via dark Higgs decays at forward experiments like FASER and SHiP is highly promising. Including single production channels improves sensitivity, especially for weakly coupled and light bosons. Future data from FASER2 and SHiP will critically test the existence of dark photons and U(1)$_{B-L}$ gauge bosons, and their role in explaining sterile neutrino dark matter via the freeze-in mechanism.

通过FASER和SHiP等前向实验中暗希格斯衰变搜寻暗区规范玻色子极具前景。包含单产生通道可提升对弱耦合和轻质量玻色子的探测灵敏度。FASER2和SHiP未来的数据将对暗光子和U(1)$_{B-L}$规范玻色子的存在性及其在冻结-注入机制下解释惰性中微子暗物质的作用进行关键性检验。

Abstract: We study the sensitivity to dark photons and U(1)$_{B-L}$ gauge bosons produced via dark Higgs boson decays at the FASER and SHiP experiments. In addition to pair production of these vector bosons from both on-shell and off-shell dark Higgs boson decays, a new production process of single vector boson associated with the standard model particles is taken into account. Constraints on the parameter space of dark photon are derived with including the latest results from the FASER experiment. The expected sensitivity regions to the dark photon and U(1)$_{B-L}$ gauge boson of the future FASER2 and SHiP experiments are presented. The sensitivity to the U(1)$_{B-L}$ model with freeze-in sterile neutrino dark matter is also discussed.

### [32] [Revisiting QCD-induced little inflation with chiral density wave state and its implications on pulsar timing array gravitational-wave signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29772)
*Tae Hyun Jung,Seyong Kim,Jong-Wan Lee,Chang Sub Shin,Hee Beom Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates a QCD-induced little inflation scenario driven by a strong first-order QCD phase transition at large baryon chemical potential, aiming to explain pulsar timing array (PTA)-observable nano-Hz gravitational waves. It highlights difficulties in achieving sufficient supercooling in the standard homogeneous transition picture given observational constraints on the baryon density. The authors explore the role of the chiral density wave (CDW) phase—a spatially inhomogeneous QCD phase—using a nucleon-meson model with isoscalar vector mesons, mapping its critical and spinodal lines in the ($\mu_B$, $T$) plane. While the CDW phase shows metastability at low baryon densities in some parameter regions, the latent heat from subsequent liquid-gas transitions proves too small to support viable inflation or generate detectable gravitational waves. The study tightens theoretical requirements for QCD-phase-transition-driven cosmological phenomena and underscores the importance of inhomogeneous phases in early-universe dynamics.

本文研究了一种由强一阶QCD相变驱动的QCD诱导小规模暴胀（QCD-induced little inflation）情景，该相变发生在高重子化学势下，旨在解释脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing array, PTA）可观测到的纳赫兹频段随机引力波背景。文章指出，在标准均匀相变图景中，为满足观测重子密度要求而实现足够深度过冷存在不可避免的困难。为此，作者探讨了在高重子化学势下是否存在定性不同的相结构，可能改变重子密度与化学势之间的关系，从而影响过冷历史。通过使用包含同位旋标量矢量介子的核子-介子模型，他们确定了手征密度波（chiral density wave, CDW）相在($\mu_B$, $T$)平面上的临界点和自旋odal边界。研究发现，CDW相具有非平凡结构，并在某些参数区域内可在低重子密度下保持亚稳态。然而，考虑后续液气相变及相分离后，释放的潜热太小，不足以支持可行的小规模暴胀场景及其相关的PTA尺度引力波信号。本分析收紧了QCD相变作为宇宙学纳米赫兹引力波源所需满足的条件，同时阐明了非均匀QCD相在宇宙早期动力学中的潜在重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from recent PTA observations suggesting a stochastic gravitational-wave background in the nano-Hertz range, which may originate from strong first-order phase transitions in the early universe. QCD-induced little inflation has been proposed as one such mechanism, relying on a large initial baryon chemical potential $\mu_B$ and significant supercooling during the QCD phase transition to trigger a brief period of accelerated expansion. However, the conventional assumption of a homogeneous transition from quark-gluon plasma to hadronic gas struggles to achieve the required level of supercooling without violating constraints on the observed baryon asymmetry. This tension motivates the exploration of alternative phase structures—particularly inhomogeneous ones like the chiral density wave (CDW) phase—that may modify the thermodynamic relation between $n_B$ and $\mu_B$, thereby altering the supercooling dynamics and potentially reviving the scenario.

研究动机源于近期脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）观测显示可能存在纳赫兹频段的随机引力波背景，这或许起源于早期宇宙中的强一阶相变。QCD诱导的小规模暴胀曾被提出作为此类机制之一，依赖于初始较大的重子化学势$\mu_B$以及QCD相变过程中显著的过冷效应，以触发短暂的加速膨胀阶段。然而，传统假设下的均匀相变（从夸克胶子等离子体到强子气体）难以在不违反观测重子不对称性约束的前提下实现所需的过冷程度。这一矛盾促使人们探索其他可能的相结构——特别是像手征密度波（chiral density wave, CDW）这样的非均匀相——它们可能改变$n_B$与$\mu_B$之间的热力学关系，从而改变过冷动力学，甚至使该暴胀情景得以恢复。

Method: The authors employ an effective field theory approach based on a nucleon-meson model that includes isoscalar vector mesons ($\omega$ meson) to describe dense baryonic matter. They analyze the chiral phase structure at finite temperature $T$ and baryon chemical potential $\mu_B$, focusing on the formation and stability of the chiral density wave (CDW) phase. By solving the gap equations derived from the thermodynamic potential, they map out the critical and spinodal lines in the ($\mu_B$, $T$) plane, identifying regions of metastability. They further incorporate the effects of the nuclear liquid-gas transition and phase separation after chiral symmetry restoration, computing the latent heat available for driving inflation. The analysis combines mean-field approximation with thermodynamic consistency checks to assess the viability of generating sufficient supercooling and post-transition energy release.

作者采用基于核子-介子模型的有效场论方法，其中包含同位旋标量矢量介子（$\omega$介子），用于描述高温高密下的重子物质。他们在有限温度$T$和重子化学势$\mu_B$下分析手征相结构，重点关注手征密度波（CDW）相的形成与稳定性。通过求解由热力学势导出的能隙方程，他们在($\mu_B$, $T$)平面上绘制出临界线和自旋odal线，识别出亚稳区域。此外，他们还纳入了手征对称性恢复后的核液气相变及相分离效应，计算可用于驱动暴胀的潜热。该分析结合平均场近似与热力学一致性检验，评估是否能产生足够的过冷程度以及相变后的能量释放。

Result: The analysis reveals that the chiral density wave (CDW) phase exhibits a complex phase structure and can remain metastable down to relatively low baryon densities in certain regions of the model parameter space, particularly when vector meson interactions are sufficiently strong. This suggests that non-uniform chiral phases could play a role in modifying the equation of state during the QCD epoch. However, when the full phase evolution—including chiral symmetry breaking, CDW formation, and subsequent liquid-gas transition—is considered, the total latent heat released is found to be insufficient to power a sustained period of inflation or produce a detectable stochastic gravitational-wave signal in the PTA frequency band. Thus, while the CDW phase enriches the phase diagram, it does not rescue the QCD-induced little inflation scenario under realistic conditions.

分析结果显示，手征密度波（CDW）相展现出复杂的相结构，在模型参数空间的某些区域（尤其是当矢量介子相互作用足够强时），其亚稳态可延续至相对较低的重子密度。这表明非均匀手征相可能在QCD时期修改物态方程。然而，当考虑完整的相演化过程——包括手征对称性破缺、CDW形成以及随后的液气相变——时，所释放的总潜热被发现不足以维持一段持续的暴胀或在PTA频段产生可探测的随机引力波信号。因此，尽管CDW相丰富了QCD相图，但在现实条件下仍无法挽救QCD诱导的小规模暴胀情景。

Conclusion: While inhomogeneous QCD phases such as the chiral density wave (CDW) phase introduce new features in the QCD phase diagram at large $\mu_B$, they do not provide sufficient energy release through latent heat to realize a viable QCD-induced little inflation scenario compatible with both baryogenesis constraints and PTA observations. The study concludes that alternative mechanisms beyond standard or modified QCD phase transitions—such as exotic dark sectors or primordial black holes—are likely needed to explain the putative nano-Hz gravitational-wave signals. Nevertheless, the work highlights the cosmological significance of studying inhomogeneous phases in dense QCD matter, urging further theoretical and lattice efforts to map the high-$\mu_B$ regime reliably.

尽管诸如手征密度波（CDW）之类的非均匀QCD相在高$\mu_B$区域为QCD相图引入了新的特征，但它们通过潜热释放的能量仍不足以实现一个与重子生成约束和PTA观测相容的可行QCD诱导小暴胀情景。研究得出结论：要解释假定的纳赫兹引力波信号，可能需要超出标准或修正QCD相变的新机制——例如奇异暗区（exotic dark sectors）或原初黑洞。尽管如此，这项工作突显了研究致密QCD物质中非均匀相的宇宙学意义，呼吁进一步开展理论和格点QCD研究，以更可靠地描绘高$\mu_B$区域的相结构。

Abstract: We revisit QCD-induced little inflation in which the Universe starts with a large baryon chemical potential and undergoes a strong first-order QCD phase transition, generating an observable stochastic gravitational-wave background in the nano-Hz range relevant for pulsar timing array (PTA) observations. We point out that the conventional homogeneous transition from the quark-gluon plasma phase to the hadronic gas phase faces an unavoidable difficulty in achieving the required strength of supercooling for the observed baryon density. This motivates us to explore whether a qualitatively different phase structure at a large baryon chemical potential can alter the relation between the baryon density and the chemical potential, and thereby modify the supercooling history of the transition. Using the nucleon-meson model with isoscalar vector mesons, we determine the critical and spinodal structure of the chiral density wave (CDW) phase in the $(μ_B, T)$ plane. We find that the CDW phase exhibits a nontrivial structure and can remain metastable down to a low baryon density in a certain region of the parameter space. Taking into account the subsequent liquid-gas transition and phase separation, however, the released latent heat is too small to realize a viable QCD-induced little inflation scenario and its associated PTA-scale gravitational-wave signal. Our analysis sharpens the conditions under which QCD phase transitions may act as cosmological sources of nano-Hz gravitational waves, while clarifying the possible cosmological relevance of inhomogeneous QCD phases.

</details>


### [33] [Autonomous Discovery of Particle Physics Theories from Experimental Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28935)
*Stephon Alexander,Benjamin Bradley,Loukas Gouskos,Cooper Niu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: ALBERT, a neuro-symbolic AI framework, uses formal language and reinforcement learning to explore particle physics theories without hallucinations, successfully rediscovering the Standard Model and predicting the top quark mass as $178.9\pm 5.0~\text{GeV}$ using only LEP data.

ALBERT是一个神经符号AI框架，利用形式语言和强化学习探索粒子物理理论，无幻觉地成功重建标准模型，并仅用LEP数据预测顶夸克质量为$178.9\pm 5.0~\text{GeV}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The vast number of possible extensions to the Standard Model creates a combinatorial challenge for traditional theoretical methods, necessitating a systematic, scalable, and reliable approach to theory exploration that avoids the hallucinations typical of large language models.

标准模型可能的扩展数量巨大，给传统理论方法带来组合爆炸挑战，因此需要一种系统性、可扩展且可靠的理论探索方法，避免大语言模型常见的幻觉问题。

Method: ALBERT encodes particle physics into a formal language with a rule-based grammar, generating tokenized sequences for symmetries, particles, and interactions. A reinforcement learning environment enforces first-principles constraints, computes observables including radiative corrections, and evaluates theories via $\chi^2$ analysis against experimental data. A 25-million-parameter transformer model is trained on legacy LEP collider data.

ALBERT将粒子物理编码为基于规则语法的形式语言，生成对称性、粒子和相互作用的标记序列。强化学习环境强加第一性原理约束，计算包含辐射修正的可观测量，并通过$\chi^2$分析与实验数据对比评估理论。使用2500万参数的transformer模型在LEP对撞机的历史数据上进行训练。

Result: ALBERT successfully rediscovered the Standard Model and autonomously predicted the existence and properties of the top quark—despite no direct evidence in the training data—yielding a mass prediction of $178.9 \pm 5.0~\text{GeV}$, consistent with the established value from LHC measurements.

ALBERT成功重建了标准模型，并自主预测了顶夸克的存在及其性质——尽管训练数据中无直接证据——得到质量预测为$178.9 \pm 5.0~\text{GeV}$，与LHC测量结果一致。

Conclusion: Neuro-symbolic AI frameworks like ALBERT enable rigorous, scalable, and hallucination-free exploration of high-energy physics theory space, demonstrating autonomous discovery potential for new physics beyond the Standard Model.

类似ALBERT的神经符号AI框架能够实现严格、可扩展且无幻觉的高能物理理论空间探索，展示了超越标准模型的新物理自主发现潜力。

Abstract: The search for physics beyond the Standard Model is hindered by a combinatorial explosion of possible theories. We introduce \textsc{Albert}, a neuro-symbolic artificial intelligence framework to systematically navigate this vast theory space. By encoding particle physics as a formal language, \textsc{Albert} generates tokenized sequences representing symmetries, particles, and interactions under a rule-based grammar, eliminating the hallucinations common in large language models. The reinforcement learning environment enforces first-principle theoretical constraints, computes observables with radiative corrections, and evaluates statistical likelihood via $χ^2$ analysis against experimental data. As a proof of concept, we train a 25-million-parameter transformer model using only legacy data from the Large Electron-Positron Collider, which contains no direct evidence of the top quark. Remarkably, \textsc{Albert} successfully rediscovered the Standard Model and autonomously inferred necessity and properties of the top quark, predicting its mass at $178.9\pm 5.0~\text{GeV}$, consistent with its modern measurement at the Large Hadron Collider. These results demonstrate the potential of AI-driven theory exploration as a rigorous, hallucination-free, and scalable paradigm for autonomous discovery of new physics.

### [34] [Conventional and Unitarity-Conserving Pecci-Quinn Inflation Models and ACT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29780)
*J. McDonald*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The unitarity-conserving Peccei-Quinn inflation model agrees better with ACT data on the scalar spectral index and allows a significantly larger axion decay constant $f_a$ due to relaxed isocurvature constraints, especially for large PQ self-coupling $\lambda$, unlike conventional PQ inflation.

单位性守恒的Peccei-Quinn暴胀模型在标量谱指数上更符合ACT数据，并由于等曲率约束的放松，尤其在较大的PQ自耦合$\lambda$下，允许显著更大的轴子衰变常数$f_a$，而传统的PQ暴胀模型则不能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To resolve tensions between conventional non-minimally coupled Peccei-Quinn (PQ) inflation and observational data, particularly the scalar spectral index from ACT, and to alleviate strong axion isocurvature bounds that limit the axion decay constant $f_a$ in standard scenarios.

为了解决传统的非最小耦合Peccei-Quinn（PQ）暴胀模型与观测数据（特别是ACT给出的标量谱指数）之间的紧张关系，并缓解限制轴子衰变常数$f_a$的标准情景下的强轴子等曲率约束。

Method: We analyze two versions of PQ inflation: conventional non-minimally coupled PQ inflation and a unitarity-conserving variant with additional Jordan frame interactions. We compute predictions for the scalar spectral index $n_s$ and tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$ under instantaneous reheating. We derive axion isocurvature constraints assuming no restoration of PQ symmetry after inflation and compare bounds on $f_a$ as a function of the PQ self-coupling $\lambda$. A new isocurvature bound for conventional PQ inflation is derived, and the impact of reheating temperature on symmetry non-restoration is studied.

我们分析了两种PQ暴胀模型：传统的非最小耦合PQ暴胀和具有额外Jordan框架相互作用的单位性守恒变体。在瞬时再加热假设下计算了标量谱指数$n_s$和张量标量比$r$的预测。假设暴胀后PQ对称性未恢复，推导了轴子等曲率约束，并比较了作为PQ自耦合$\lambda$函数的$f_a$边界。推导了传统PQ暴胀的新等曲率边界，并研究了再加热温度对对称性不恢复的影响。

Result: The unitarity-conserving PQ inflation model predicts a scalar spectral index within 1$\sigma$ of the ACT central value, while conventional PQ inflation lies over 2$\sigma$ below. For $\lambda = 0.1$, the axion isocurvature upper bound is $f_a \leq 1.1 \times 10^9$ GeV in the conventional model, but $f_a \leq 6.4 \times 10^{13}$ GeV in the unitarity-conserving model, which is independent of $\lambda$. A new isocurvature bound for conventional PQ inflation is found to be 650 times stricter than previous estimates. Lowering the reheating temperature slightly in the unitarity-conserving model prevents PQ symmetry restoration, enabling high $f_a$ values beyond the cosmological upper bound $\sim 10^{12}$ GeV.

单位性守恒的PQ暴胀模型预测的标量谱指数在ACT中心值的1$\sigma$范围内，而传统PQ暴胀模型则超过2$\sigma$偏低。当$\lambda = 0.1$时，传统模型的轴子等曲率上限为$f_a \leq 1.1 \times 10^9$ GeV，而单位性守恒模型为$f_a \leq 6.4 \times 10^{13}$ GeV，且后者与$\lambda$无关。发现传统PQ暴胀的新等曲率边界比以往估计严格650倍。略微降低单位性守恒模型的再加热温度可防止PQ对称性恢复，使$f_a$值超过宇宙学上限$\sim 10^{12}$ GeV。

Conclusion: Only the unitarity-conserving PQ inflation model is consistent with current CMB observations (ACT) and allows the axion decay constant $f_a$ to reach values above $\sim 10^{12}$ GeV without fine-tuning the PQ self-coupling $\lambda$, making it more viable for axion dark matter models with high $f_a$. The conventional model faces severe tension with data and tighter isocurvature bounds unless $\lambda$ is extremely small.

只有单位性守恒的PQ暴胀模型既符合当前CMB观测（ACT），又允许轴子衰变常数$f_a$在无需精细调节PQ自耦合$\lambda$的情况下达到高于$\sim 10^{12}$ GeV的值，使其在高$f_a$轴子暗物质模型中更具可行性。传统模型除非$\lambda$极小，否则会面临与数据的严重紧张以及更严格的等曲率约束。

Abstract: We compare conventional non-minimally coupled Peccei-Quinn (PQ) inflation with a version of the model in which unitarity conservation is imposed by additional Jordan frame interactions. Assuming instantaneous reheating, the unitarity-conserving model is within 1$σ$ agreement with the central value of the scalar spectral index reported by the ACT collaboration, whereas conventional PQ inflation is more than 2$σ$ below the ACT central value. In the case where dark matter is composed of axions and PQ symmetry is not restored after inflation, the axion isocurvature constraint of the unitarity-conserving model typically allows a much larger axion decay constant $f_{a}$ than the conventional model, with the conventional model upper bound being larger only if the PQ self-coupling is extremely small, $λ< 10^{-12}$. For $λ= 0.1$, the axion isocurvature upper bounds are $f_{a} \leq 1.1 \times 10^{9} $ GeV for conventional PQ inflation and $f_{a} \leq 6.4 \times 10^{13}$ GeV for unitarity-conserving PQ inflation, with the latter bound being independent of $λ$. We also find a new isocurvature upper bound for conventional PQ inflation which is 650 times smaller than the existing bound. A modest reduction of the reheating temperature of the unitarity-conserving model from its maximum possible value will ensure that the PQ symmetry is not restored after inflation, allowing values of $f_{a}$ up to $6.4 \times 10^{13}$ GeV. Thus only the unitarity-conserving PQ inflation model allows $f_{a}$ to access values greater than the symmetry restoration cosmological upper bound $\sim 10^{12}$ GeV with naturally large values of the PQ self-coupling.

### [35] [Constraining The Neutrino-Nucleon Cross Section with the Ultrahigh-Energy KM3NeT Event](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28941)
*Toni Bertólez-Martínez,Dan Hooper*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: KM3NeT's observation of a $\\sim 220 \\, {\\rm PeV}$ neutrino muon track enables probing of physics at center-of-mass energies beyond current accelerator capabilities. A single event sets an upper limit on the neutrino-nucleon cross section: $\\sigma_{\ uN} < 40 \\, \\sigma_{\  uN}^{\\rm SM}$ at $E_{\\rm CM} \\sim 20 \\, {\\rm TeV}$. This constrains Beyond the Standard Model scenarios, with future neutrino telescopes offering competitive sensitivity to new physics.\n\nKM3NeT观测到一个约220 PeV中微子产生的μ子轨迹，使得我们能够探测超越现有加速器能力的质心能量下的物理过程。利用这一单个事件，我们对中微子-核子截面设定了上限：在质心能量约20 TeV下，$\\sigma_{\  uN} < 40 \\, \\sigma_{\  uN}^{\\rm SM}$。该结果可用于限制多种超出标准模型的情景。未来的超大体积中微子望远镜有望显著增强对此散射截面的限制，并在某些情况下可与加速器探测新物理的能力相媲美。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The detection of ultra-high-energy neutrinos allows access to center-of-momentum energies beyond those achievable at human-made accelerators like the LHC. Such events offer a unique window into neutrino interactions at previously unprobed energy scales, enabling tests of the Standard Model and searches for new physics through deviations in the neutrino-nucleon cross section.\n\n探测极高能中微子使我们能够触及人类制造的加速器（如LHC）无法达到的质心能量。这类事件为研究此前未被探测的能量尺度上的中微子相互作用提供了独特窗口，从而可通过中微子-核子截面的偏差来检验标准模型并寻找新物理。

Method: Using the observed $\\sim 220 \\, {\\rm PeV}$ muon track from a neutrino interaction detected by KM3NeT, the authors infer kinematic properties of the incoming neutrino and estimate the corresponding center-of-mass energy ($E_{\\rm CM} \\sim 20 \\, {\\rm TeV}$). They compare the survival probability of such a high-energy neutrino through Earth with expectations under different cross-section hypotheses, deriving an upper limit on $\\sigma_{\  uN}$ relative to the Standard Model prediction via statistical inference.\n\n利用KM3NeT探测到的约220 PeV中微子产生μ子轨迹，作者推断入射中微子的运动学特性，并估算相应的质心能量（约20 TeV）。他们将如此高能中微子穿过地球后的存活概率与不同截面假设下的预期进行比较，通过统计推断得出相对于标准模型预测的$\\sigma_{\  uN}$上限。

Result: An upper limit on the neutrino-nucleon cross section is established as $\\sigma_{\  uN} < 40 \\, \\sigma_{\  uN}^{\\rm SM}$ at $E_{\\rm CM} \\sim 20 \\, {\\rm TeV}$ from a single high-energy event. This constraint applies to Beyond the Standard Model scenarios that predict enhanced neutrino cross sections, such as those involving leptoquarks, extra dimensions, or new neutral currents.\n\n基于单一高能事件，建立了中微子-核子截面的上限：在$E_{\\rm CM} \\sim 20 \\, {\\rm TeV}$下，$\\sigma_{\  uN} < 40 \\, \\sigma_{\  uN}^{\\rm SM}$。该限制适用于预测中微子截面增强的超出标准模型情景，例如涉及leptoquarks、额外维度或新中性流的模型。

Conclusion: High-energy astrophysical neutrinos serve as powerful probes of particle interactions at energy scales inaccessible to terrestrial accelerators. Even a single event can place meaningful constraints on the neutrino-nucleon cross section, complementing collider searches. Future large-volume neutrino observatories will significantly improve sensitivity, potentially reaching competitiveness with accelerator-based new physics searches.\n\n高能天体物理中微子是探测地面加速器无法触及能量尺度下粒子相互作用的强大工具。即使单个事件也能对中微子-核子截面施加有意义的限制，补充对撞机搜索。未来的大体积中微子观测站将显著提高灵敏度，可能在新物理探测方面与基于加速器的实验竞争。

Abstract: KM3NeT's detection of a muon track produced by a $\sim 220 \, {\rm PeV}$ neutrino provides an opportunity to probe physics at center-of-momentum energies greater than those probed by the Large Hadron Collider or other existing particle accelerators. In this study, we use this single event to place an upper limit on the neutrino-nucleon cross section of $σ_{νN} < 40 \, σ_{νN}^{\rm SM}$ at $E_{\rm CM} \sim 20 \, {\rm TeV}$. This result can be used to constrain a variety of scenarios beyond the Standard Model. With future very large volume neutrino telescopes, constraints on the neutrino-nucleon scattering cross section are expected to become substantially more stringent and, in some scenarios, could become competitive with accelerator probes of new physics.

### [36] [Fermion scattering in a Bose-Einstein condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29000)
*César E. Echevarría,José F. Nieves,Francisco Orbe,Sarira Sahu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study fermion spinors and propagators in a scalar Bose-Einstein condensate background, deriving dispersion relations and scattering rates with helicity-dependent kinematics, revealing a Van Hove-like singularity due to zero group velocity at specific momentum. Our results apply to dark matter-electron scattering and neutrino/electron propagation in scalar dark matter backgrounds.

我们研究了标量玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚背景下费米子的旋量和传播子，推导出具有手征依赖性的色散关系和散射率，并发现由于特定动量下群速度为零而出现类似范霍夫奇点的现象。我们的结果适用于暗物质-电子散射以及中微子/电子在标量暗物质背景中的传播等场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To extend previous work on fermion propagation in scalar Bose-Einstein condensates by computing the corresponding spinors and propagators, enabling the calculation of interaction rates and thermal corrections, which are essential for phenomenological applications such as dark matter detection and neutrino physics.

扩展此前关于费米子在标量玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚中传播的研究，通过计算相应的旋量和传播子，以实现相互作用速率及热修正的计算，这对于暗物质探测和中微子物理等现象学应用至关重要。

Method: We employ Yukawa-type coupling models between fermions and scalar fields in a BEC background. Using quantum field theory techniques, we derive the fermion spinors, propagators, and dispersion relations. We compute the scattering rate of a generic fermion $\chi$ off background fermions, taking into account helicity-dependent kinematics and singularities arising from vanishing group velocities.

我们在玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚背景下采用费米子与标量场之间的汤川型耦合模型。利用量子场论技术，推导出费米子旋量、传播子和色散关系，并计算了通用费米子$\chi$与背景费米子之间的散射率，考虑了手征依赖的动力学以及由群速度消失引起的奇点。

Result: We obtain compact analytical expressions for fermion spinors and propagators in the BEC background. The dispersion relations exhibit helicity dependence, leading to a mode with zero group velocity at a critical momentum, resulting in a Van Hove-like divergence in the scattering rate. This singularity enhances the differential cross section similarly to condensed matter systems with saddle points in their band structure.

我们得到了玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚背景下费米子旋量和传播子的简洁解析表达式。色散关系表现出手征依赖性，在临界动量处导致某一模式的群速度为零，从而在散射率中产生类似范霍夫的发散。该奇点像凝聚态系统中能带结构鞍点一样增强了微分截面。

Conclusion: The framework developed here provides a solid basis for computing fermionic processes in scalar BEC backgrounds, including thermal and higher-order corrections. The presence of a Van Hove-like singularity in the scattering rate due to helicity-dependent dispersion opens new observational signatures, particularly relevant for cosmic-ray electron cooling via dark matter-electron scattering and neutrino propagation in scalar dark matter environments.

本文建立的框架为在标量玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚背景下计算费米过程（包括热修正和高阶修正）提供了坚实基础。由于手征依赖的色散关系导致散射率中出现类似范霍夫的奇点，这为通过暗物质-电子散射引起的宇宙射线电子冷却以及中微子在标量暗物质环境中的传播等现象提供了新的可观测信号。

Abstract: In a recent work, we considered the propagation of fermions in the background of a scalar Bose-Einstein (BE) condensate. Using some illustrative Yukawa-type coupling models between the fermions and the scalar fields, we determined the dispersion relations of the fermions and the scalar modes in various models. To complement that work, here we consider the corresponding fermion spinors and propagators, which are required for the calculation of rates of processes involving the fermions, as well as the thermal, and/or higher order, corrections to such rates. We obtain and present here concise formulas which are useful for those applications. As an application and for illustrative purposes we specifically calculate the rate for a generic fermion (which we denote by $χ$) with the fermions in the BE background, using commonly used models for the fermion interactions. Due to the fact that the background fermion dispersion relations are helicity dependent, the kinematics have some unique and non-standard features. For example, at a particular value of the momentum one of the fermion modes has zero group velocity, which leads to a singularity in the scattering rate of the type of the Van Hove singularity in the density of states of some condensed matter systems. The results of the framework presented here, besides their merit in their own right, can be useful in specific contexts and applications, such as cosmic-ray electron cooling through dark matter-electron scattering, and similar ones involving neutrino and/or electron propagation in a scalar Dark Matter background.

### [37] [Probing Heavy Neutral Higgs Bosons via Single Vector-Like Bottom Quark Production at the HL-LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29076)
*Rachid Benbrik,Mbark Berrouj,Mohammed Boukidi,Mohamed Ech-chaouy,Kholoud Kahime,Khawla Salime*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores the discovery potential of a singly produced vector-like bottom quark $B$ in an extended Type-II Two-Higgs-Doublet Model, focusing on the exotic decay $B \to \phi b$ with $\phi = H, A$ and subsequent $\phi \to t\bar{t}$, leading to a final state with a lepton, missing energy, and multiple $b$-jets. Using full simulation at $\sqrt{s}=14$ TeV, the study shows that this exotic decay can dominate (BR ~50%) in the alignment limit. While cut-based analysis requires high luminosity for $5\sigma$ discovery, an XGBoost-based multivariate analysis enhances sensitivity, enabling discovery up to $m_B \simeq 1.3$ TeV ($600~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$) and $1.6$ TeV ($3~\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$), even with 15% systematic uncertainties.

本文研究了在扩展的II型双希格斯二重态模型中单生成的矢量型底夸克$B$的发现前景，重点关注非标准衰变$B \to \phi b$（其中$\phi = H, A$）及其后续的$\phi \to t\bar{t}$过程，最终产生一个带电轻子、缺失横动量和多个$b$喷注。在$\sqrt{s}=14$ TeV下进行了信号和标准模型背景的完整模拟。结果表明，在对齐极限下，这种奇异衰变通道的分支比可达约50%，超过传统衰变模式。传统的基于 cuts 的分析需要极高的积分亮度才能实现$5\sigma$发现，而基于XGBoost的多变量分析显著提升了信噪分辨能力，即使存在15%的系统误差，也能在$600~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$下将发现上限提升至$m_B \simeq 1.3$ TeV，在$3~\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$下提升至$1.6$ TeV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore non-standard decay channels of vector-like quarks in an extended Two-Higgs-Doublet Model, particularly when conventional decays are suppressed. The presence of additional scalars ($H, A$) allows for exotic decays such as $B \to \phi b$, which could dominate in certain parameter regions like the alignment limit, offering new discovery opportunities at the LHC.

研究动机是探索在扩展双希格斯二重态模型中矢量型夸克的非标准衰变通道，尤其是在传统衰变被压低的情况下。额外标量粒子($H, A$)的存在使得如$B \to \phi b$之类的奇异衰变成为可能，并且在对齐极限等特定参数区域中可能占主导地位，从而为LHC上的新物理发现提供新途径。

Method: The authors consider a Type-II 2HDM extended by an $SU(2)_L$ vector-like $(T,B)$ doublet, focusing on singly produced $B$ quarks. They analyze the decay chain $B \to \phi b \to (t\bar{t})b$, with $\phi = H/A$, leading to a final state with one lepton, missing transverse energy, and multiple $b$-jets. Full Monte Carlo simulation of signal and SM backgrounds is performed at $\sqrt{s} = 14$ TeV. Both cut-based and XGBoost-based multivariate analyses are employed to optimize signal selection and enhance significance, with systematic uncertainties up to 15% included in the evaluation.

作者考虑了一个由$SU(2)_L$矢量型$(T,B)$双重态扩展的II型2HDM，聚焦于单生成的$B$夸克。他们分析了衰变链$B \to \phi b \to (t\bar{t})b$（其中$\phi = H/A$），最终态包含一个轻子、缺失横动量和多个$b$喷注。在$\sqrt{s} = 14$ TeV下对信号和标准模型背景进行了完整的蒙特卡洛模拟。采用了基于 cuts 和基于XGBoost的多变量分析方法来优化信号选择并提高显著性，并包含了高达15%的系统误差。

Result: The exotic decay $B \to \phi b$ can dominate over standard model-like decays, reaching branching ratios of $\sim 50\%$ for both $H$ and $A$ in the alignment limit. A conventional cut-based analysis achieves $5\sigma$ discovery only at high luminosities, while an XGBoost-based multivariate analysis significantly improves sensitivity, allowing $5\sigma$ discovery up to $m_B \simeq 1.3$ TeV with $600~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ and up to $m_B \simeq 1.6$ TeV with $3~\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$, even with 15\% systematic uncertainties.

奇异衰变$B \to \phi b$在对齐极限下可主导于标准模型类衰变，对$H$和$A$的分支比均可达约50%。传统的基于 cuts 的分析仅在高亮度下才能实现$5\sigma$发现，而基于XGBoost的多变量分析显著提高了灵敏度，即使存在15%的系统误差，也能在$600~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$下将发现上限提升至$m_B \simeq 1.3$ TeV，在$3~\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$下提升至$1.6$ TeV。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that exotic decay channels of vector-like bottom quarks in extended Higgs sectors can be dominant and offer enhanced discovery prospects at the LHC. The use of machine learning techniques such as XGBoost substantially improves the reach compared to traditional cut-based methods, making it possible to probe $B$-quark masses up to 1.6 TeV in realistic experimental conditions.

研究表明，在扩展希格斯部门中，矢量型底夸克的奇异衰变通道可以占主导地位，并为LHC上的发现提供更强的前景。使用XGBoost等机器学习技术相比传统基于 cuts 的方法显著扩展了探测范围，使得在现实实验条件下探测高达1.6 TeV的$B$夸克质量成为可能。

Abstract: We investigate the discovery prospects of a singly produced vector-like bottom quark in the Type-II Two-Higgs-Doublet Model extended by an $SU(2)_L$ vector-like $(T,B)$ doublet. We focus on the non-standard decay chain $B \to φb$, followed by $φ\to t\bar{t}$, where $φ= H$ or $A$, leading to a final state with one charged lepton, missing transverse energy, and multiple $b$-jets. We perform a full simulation of both signal and Standard Model backgrounds at $\sqrt{s}=14$ TeV. We show that the exotic channels $B \to φb$ can dominate over the conventional decay modes, reaching branching ratios of order $50\%$ for both neutral scalars in the alignment limit. A conventional cut-based analysis provides a $5σ$ discovery significance only at sufficiently high integrated luminosity. By contrast, an XGBoost-based multivariate analysis substantially improves the signal-background discrimination and extends the discovery reach up to $m_B \simeq 1.3$ TeV with $600~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ and up to $m_B \simeq 1.6$ TeV with $3~\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$, even in the presence of systematic uncertainties as large as $15\%$.

### [38] [The effects of a scalar singlet Leptoquark at the $Z$ factory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29125)
*Dazhuang He,Yu Zhang,Hao Sun*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates the observability of a scalar singlet leptoquark (LQ) in $\mu$- and $\tau$-pair production at a $Z$ factory. While LQ effects are negligible in $\mu$-pair final states, they produce a measurable $-0.7\%$ deviation in $\tau$-pair production, sensitive to left-handed couplings. An analytic expression is provided for LQ effects as a function of mass and couplings, with stable kinematic distributions. Future precision at the $Z$ factory will tightly constrain LQ parameter space.

本文研究了标量单态leptoquark（LQ）在Z工厂中μ和τ对产生过程中的可观测性。LQ效应对μ末态影响可忽略，但在τ对产生中引起约-0.7%的可观测偏差，对左手耦合敏感。文章提供了LQ效应关于质量和耦合的解析表达式，微分分布显示其在运动学区域稳定。未来Z工厂的测量精度将对LQ理论参数空间施加更严格限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explore whether a scalar singlet leptoquark (LQ), proposed to explain charged-current B-anomalies, can be tested at future $Z$ factories through its effects in $\ell^+\ell^-$ final states, particularly distinguishing between $\mu^+\mu^-$ and $\tau^+\tau^-$ channels where chiral couplings may lead to observable deviations.

探索为解释带电流B反常而提出的标量单态leptoquark（LQ）是否可通过未来Z工厂中轻子对（$\ell^+\ell^-$）末态进行检验，特别是区分μ和τ通道中手征耦合可能导致可观测偏差的情况。

Method: We compute the LQ contributions to $Z \to \ell^+\ell^-$ and $e^+e^- \to \ell^+\ell^-$ at the $Z$ pole using effective field theory techniques, focusing on left-handed couplings. We derive an analytic formula for the relative correction to the cross section in $\tau$-pair production as a function of LQ mass ($M_{\rm LQ}$) and Yukawa couplings ($y_L$). Kinematic distributions are analyzed to assess stability of the signal. Projected experimental precision at future $Z$ factories is used to set constraints on the coupling parameter space.

采用有效场论方法计算LQ对$Z \to \ell^+\ell^-$和$Z极点处e^+e^- \to \ell^+\ell^-$过程的贡献，聚焦于左手耦合。推导出τ对产生截面相对修正关于LQ质量（$M_{\rm LQ}$）和Yukawa耦合（$y_L$）的解析公式。分析运动学分布以评估信号稳定性，并利用未来Z工厂预期精度约束耦合参数空间。

Result: The LQ contribution to $\mu^+\mu^-$ is highly suppressed, while in $\tau^+\tau^-$ production, a deviation of $\sim -0.7\%$ is found for both 1 TeV and 2 TeV LQ masses, primarily due to left-handed interactions. The effect is identical in both $Z$ decay and $e^+e^-$ annihilation at the $Z$ pole. A phenomenological function $\Delta\sigma/\sigma_0 \propto |y_L|^2 / (M_{\rm LQ}^2)$ quantifies the correction. Differential distributions show flat kinematic behavior, indicating robust detectability. Expected measurement precision at future $Z$ factories will constrain $|y_L|$ to $\mathcal{O}(0.1)$.

LQ对μ对产生的贡献被高度压低，而在τ对产生中，对于1 TeV和2 TeV的LQ质量均发现约-0.7%的偏差，主要源于左手相互作用。该效应在Z衰变和Z极点处的e+e-湮灭中相同。一个唯象函数$\Delta\sigma/\sigma_0 \propto |y_L|^2 / (M_{\rm LQ}^2)$量化了修正幅度。微分分布呈平坦运动学行为，表明可稳健探测。未来Z工厂的预期测量精度将把$|y_L|$约束至$\mathcal{O}(0.1)$量级。

Conclusion: Although scalar singlet LQs addressing $B$-anomalies leave negligible traces in $\mu^+\mu^-$ channels at $Z$ factories, their effects in $\tau^+\tau^-$ production are potentially observable due to enhanced left-handed couplings. The derived analytic expression enables direct mapping of experimental data to LQ parameters. Future high-precision measurements at $Z$ factories will provide stringent tests of such leptoquark scenarios, complementing high-energy collider searches.

尽管解决B反常的标量单态LQ在Z工厂的μ对通道中留下可忽略的痕迹，但由于增强的左手耦合，其在τ对产生中的效应可能可观测。所推导的解析表达式可实现实验数据到LQ参数的直接映射。未来Z工厂的高精度测量将对此类leptoquark情景提供严格检验，补充高能对撞机搜索。

Abstract: We evaluate the observability of the effects of a scalar singlet leptoquark (LQ) in $μ$ and $τ$-pair productions at the $Z$ factory. In the scenario addressing the charged-current anomalies, the LQ contributions to $μ$-pair final state are negligible. In contrast, a sizable contribution arises in the $τ$-pair production, which is identical in both $Z$ decay and $e^+e^-$ collider at $Z$ pole. These effects are mainly sensitive to left-handed interaction, showing a maximum deviation of about $-0.7\%$ for both 1\,TeV and 2\,TeV LQ. The suppression of new physics effects from the heavy LQ can be compensated by the enlarged couplings parameter space. For the $τ$-pair production channel, we further specify the coupling constraints corresponding to the expected measurement precision at the future $Z$ factory. Moreover, we provide an analytic function in terms of the LQ mass and couplings to quantify the LQ effects. The differential distributions in the collision process indicate that the LQ effects remain stable throughout the kinematic region. Meanwhile, the measurement sensitivity of the $τ$-pair final state at the future $Z$ factory is expected to impose further constraints on the LQ theory.

### [39] [Role of electromagnetic corrections in the $ππ$ distributions of $ψ^\prime \to J/ψππ$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29208)
*Zhao-Sai Jia,Gang Li,Zhen-Hua Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The cusp structure near the $\pi^+\pi^-$ threshold in the $\pi^0\pi^0$ invariant mass spectrum is analyzed using nonrelativistic effective field theory with coupled $\pi^0\pi^0$ and $\pi^+\pi^-$ channels, showing that Coulomb interactions enhance the cusp and modify its magnitude by 2%-3%, which is crucial for precise extraction of $S$-wave $\pi\pi$ scattering lengths.

在包含 $\pi^0\pi^0$ 和 $\pi^+\pi^-$ 耦合道的非相对论有效场论框架下，分析了 $\pi^+\pi^-$ 阈值附近的 $\pi^0\pi^0$ 不变质量谱中的尖端结构，结果表明库仑相互作用增强了该尖端，并使其幅度改变约 2%-3%，这对于精确提取 $S$ 波 $\pi\pi$ 散射长度至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The $\pi\pi$ scattering lengths are fundamental parameters in low-energy QCD, and precision measurements require accurate treatment of final-state interactions, especially near thresholds where cusp structures appear due to channel coupling and electromagnetic effects. The process $\psi' \to J/\psi \pi\pi$ provides a clean environment to study these effects, motivating a rigorous theoretical analysis including both strong and Coulomb interactions.

$\pi\pi$ 散射长度是低能 QCD 中的基本参数，其精密测量需要对阈值附近由于道耦合和电磁效应产生的尖端结构进行精确处理最终态相互作用。过程 $\psi' \to J/\psi \pi\pi$ 提供了一个研究这些效应的干净环境，促使我们开展包含强和库仑相互作用的严格理论分析。

Method: We employ nonrelativistic effective field theory (NREFT) with coupled channels $\pi^0\pi^0$ and $\pi^+\pi^-$, incorporating $\pi\pi$ final-state rescattering via Lippmann-Schwinger-type equations. Both strong interaction amplitudes and Coulomb photon exchanges are included perturbatively. The invariant mass spectrum is computed from the squared modulus of the production amplitude, which includes loop corrections from intermediate charged pion pairs.

我们采用包含 $\pi^0\pi^0$ 和 $\pi^+\pi^-$ 耦合道的非相对论有效场论（NREFT），通过类似 Lippmann-Schwinger 的方程纳入 $\pi\pi$ 最终态再散射。强相互作用振幅和库仑光子交换均以微扰方式包含。不变质量谱由产生振幅模平方计算得到，其中包含来自中间带电π介子对的圈图修正。

Result: The inclusion of Coulomb interactions enhances the cusp structure at the $\pi^+\pi^-$ threshold in the $\pi^0\pi^0$ spectrum, increasing its magnitude by approximately 2%-3%. This correction is significant for high-precision extractions of the $S$-wave $\pi\pi$ scattering length combination $a_0 - a_2$. The full coupled-channel amplitude provides a ready-to-use formula for fitting experimental data near $\pi\pi$ thresholds.

包含库仑相互作用增强了 $\pi^0\pi^0$ 谱中 $\pi^+\pi^-$ 阈值处的尖端结构，使其幅度增加约 2%-3%。这一修正对于高精度提取 $S$ 波 $\pi\pi$ 散射长度组合 $a_0 - a_2$ 具有重要意义。完整的耦合道振幅为拟合 $\pi\pi$ 阈值附近的实验数据提供了即用型公式。

Conclusion: Electromagnetic corrections, particularly Coulomb interactions between charged pions, play a critical role in shaping the near-threshold cusp in the $\pi^0\pi^0$ invariant mass distribution. Their inclusion is essential for sub-percent level precision in determining $\pi\pi$ scattering lengths from processes like $\psi' \to J/\psi \pi\pi$. The developed NREFT framework with coupled channels serves as a robust tool for analyzing fine structures in hadronic spectra near thresholds.

电磁修正，特别是带电π介子之间的库仑相互作用，在塑造 $\pi^0\pi^0$ 不变质量分布阈值附近的尖端结构中起着关键作用。为了从 $\psi' \to J/\psi \pi\pi$ 等过程中以亚百分比精度确定 $\pi\pi$ 散射长度，必须包含这些修正。所发展的包含耦合道的 NREFT 框架为分析阈值附近强子谱中的精细结构提供了一个可靠的工具。

Abstract: The cusp structure at the $π^+π^-$ threshold in the $π^0π^0$ invariant mass spectrum serves as a sensitive probe for extracting the $S$-wave $ππ$ scattering lengths in processes where an $S$-wave $π^0π^0$ pair is produced in the final states. Within the framework of nonrelativistic effective field theory with coupled channels $π^0π^0$ and $π^+π^-$, we revisit the near-threshold structures in the $π^0π^0$ spectrum of $ψ^\prime \to J/ψππ$. Our analysis incorporates the $ππ$ final-state rescattering, including both strong and Coulomb interactions. It turns out that the cusp near the $π^+π^-$ threshold becomes more prominent when Coulomb interactions are included. The electromagnetic correctionsare found to alter the magnitude of the threshold cusp by about 2%-3%, underscoring the necessity of including these effects in precision determinations of the $ππ$ scattering lengths. The coupled-channel amplitude constructed in this work provides a ready-to-use theoretical framework for experimental analyses of fine structures near $ππ$ thresholds.

### [40] [Determining the NJL Coupling and AMM in Magnetized QCD Matter via Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29269)
*Zigeng Ding,Fan Lin,Xinyang Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We use a physics-informed machine learning framework to determine the magnetic field dependence of the coupling constant $G(eB)$ and quark anomalous magnetic moment $v_2(eB)$ in the NJL model, using lattice QCD data on quark condensates as constraints. By embedding the NJL gap equation into a differentiable neural network, we extract smooth functional forms that reproduce inverse magnetic catalysis (IMC). Our results show that both $G$ and $v_2$ are suppressed with increasing magnetic field, offering new insights into the QCD vacuum under strong magnetic fields.

我们利用基于物理信息的机器学习框架，通过格点QCD数据约束下的NJL模型间隙方程，确定了耦合常数$G(eB)$和夸克反常磁矩$v_2(eB)$随磁场的变化形式。该方法通过可微分神经网络提取出能准确再现逆磁催化（IMC）效应的连续函数，结果表明强磁场下$G$和$v_2$均被平滑抑制，为理解强磁场中QCD真空的微观响应提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The phase structure of QCD matter under strong magnetic fields is of great interest in heavy-ion physics and astrophysics. While lattice QCD simulations provide first-principles insights, they are computationally expensive and limited in scope. Effective models like the NJL model are widely used but require phenomenological inputs for parameters such as the coupling $G$ and the quark AMM. The observed phenomenon of inverse magnetic catalysis (IMC)—where the chiral condensate decreases with increasing magnetic field—challenges simple theoretical explanations. Therefore, there is a pressing need to systematically connect effective models with non-perturbative lattice data to extract physically meaningful, field-dependent parameterizations.

在强磁场下的QCD物质相结构对重离子物理和天体物理具有重要意义。虽然格点QCD模拟提供了第一性原理的见解，但其计算成本高且适用范围有限。像NJL模型这样的有效理论虽广泛应用，但仍需对耦合常数$G$和夸克反常磁矩（AMM）等参数进行唯象设定。实验上观察到的逆磁催化（IMC）现象——即手征凝聚随磁场增强而减小——挑战了传统理论解释。因此，亟需一种系统方法将有效模型与非微扰格点数据结合，以提取具有物理意义的场依赖参数化形式。

Method: We construct a physics-informed neural network (PINN) that incorporates the NJL model's chiral gap equation as a differentiable physics constraint. The network takes the magnetic field $eB$ as input and outputs functional forms for $G(eB)$ and $v_2(eB)$. These functions are then used to compute the quark condensate via the gap equation. The loss function includes a data fidelity term comparing predictions to lattice QCD condensate values and a regularization term enforcing smoothness. Gradient-based optimization is employed to train the network, ensuring that the learned parameters simultaneously satisfy physical consistency and empirical accuracy.

我们构建了一个物理信息神经网络（PINN），将NJL模型的手征间隙方程作为可微分物理约束嵌入其中。网络以磁场强度$eB$为输入，输出$G(eB)$和$v_2(eB)$的函数形式，并通过间隙方程计算夸克凝聚。损失函数包含与格点QCD数据拟合的数据保真项以及平滑性正则化项。采用基于梯度的优化方法训练网络，确保所学习的参数同时满足物理自洽性和经验准确性。

Result: The trained model successfully reproduces the inverse magnetic catalysis behavior observed in lattice QCD data. We find that both the coupling constant $G(eB)$ and the AMM ratio $v_2(eB)$ decrease monotonically with increasing $eB$, indicating a weakening of chiral interactions and magnetic response in the medium. The extracted functional forms are smooth and physically plausible, suggesting a suppression of four-fermion interactions and reduced spin alignment under strong fields. Notably, the simultaneous inclusion of both $G(eB)$ and $v_2(eB)$ allows for a more accurate description than models fixing either parameter.

训练后的模型成功再现了格点QCD中观测到的逆磁催化行为。我们发现耦合常数$G(eB)$和反常磁矩比$v_2(eB)$均随$eB$单调递减，表明介质中的手征相互作用和磁响应减弱。提取出的函数形式平滑且符合物理直觉，暗示四费米子相互作用在强场下被抑制，自旋排列能力下降。值得注意的是，同时引入$G(eB)$和$v_2(eB)$的场依赖性比固定任一参数的模型具有更高的描述精度。

Conclusion: By combining effective field theory with machine learning under physics constraints, we establish a robust framework to extract field-dependent parameters in the NJL model from lattice data. Our results support the interpretation of IMC as arising from the magnetic-field-induced suppression of the coupling strength and quark spin response. This approach opens new avenues for integrating ab initio data into effective theories, enhancing their predictive power and microscopic foundation.

通过将有效场论与受物理约束的机器学习相结合，我们建立了一个从格点数据中提取NJL模型场依赖参数的稳健框架。结果支持逆磁催化源于磁场诱导的耦合强度和夸克自旋响应抑制的观点。该方法为将第一性原理数据融入有效理论开辟了新途径，提升了其预测能力和微观基础。

Abstract: In this study, we investigate the phase structure of magnetized QCD matter by determining the field-dependent parameters of the Nambu-Jona-Lasinio (NJL) model through a physics-informed machine learning framework. Specifically, we focus on extracting the optimal functional forms for the running coupling constant $G(eB)$ and the quark anomalous magnetic moment (AMM) ratio $v_2(eB)$, utilizing lattice QCD-computed quark condensate data as the ``ground truth". By embedding the NJL gap equation as a differentiable physics-constrained module, our neural network pipeline identifies continuous parameter functions that accurately reproduce the inverse magnetic catalysis (IMC) effect. Our results demonstrate that the magnetic field smoothly suppresses both $G$ and $v_2$. This approach not only bridges the gap between effective models and lattice data but also provides new microscopic insights into the response of the QCD vacuum to strong magnetic fields.

### [41] [Entanglement in the $θ$-vacuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29287)
*Sebastian Grieninger,Dmitri E. Kharzeev,Eliana Marroquin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We compute the entanglement entropy and spectrum of the vacuum in the massive Schwinger model at finite $\theta$, revealing enhanced entanglement at $\theta = \pi$ due to competition between electric-flux vacuum branches. Using a chirally rotated Hamiltonian, we preserve $\theta$-periodicity and avoid lattice artifacts. A narrowed entanglement gap occurs near $m/g \simeq 0.33$. The Bisognano--Wichmann entanglement Hamiltonian matches the modular Hamiltonian in the infrared, validating its use on the lattice. Entanglement serves as a probe of $\theta$-vacuum structure.

我们计算了在有限$\theta$角下有质量Schwinger模型中真空态的纠缠熵和纠缠谱，揭示了在$\theta = \pi$时由于不同电通量真空分支之间的竞争导致纠缠增强的现象。通过使用手性旋转哈密顿量，我们保持了$\theta$的周期性并避免了格点效应。在$ m/g \simeq 0.33 $附近出现了纠缠能隙的显著变窄。Bisognano--Wichmann纠缠哈密顿量在红外区域与模哈密顿量一致，验证了其在格点上的适用性。纠缠可观测量可作为探测$\theta$-真空结构的有效工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The $\theta$-dependence of vacuum structure in gauge theories leads to rich non-perturbative phenomena, such as CP violation and topological effects. In 1+1D QED (the Schwinger model), the $\theta$ term influences vacuum degeneracy and phase structure. However, lattice formulations often break $\theta$-periodicity or introduce artifacts, especially at $\theta=\pi$. Understanding how entanglement—particularly entanglement entropy and spectrum—responds to $\theta$ provides a quantum-informational window into vacuum topology and competing ground states. The goal is to clarify the origin of entanglement enhancement at $\theta=\pi$ and assess whether it signals critical behavior or universal physics.

在规范场论中，$\theta$对真空结构的依赖性导致丰富的非微扰现象，如CP破坏和拓扑效应。在1+1维QED（Schwinger模型）中，$\theta$项影响真空简并性和相结构。然而，格点公式通常会破坏$\theta$的周期性或在$\theta=\pi$处引入格点效应。理解纠缠（特别是纠缠熵和纠缠谱）如何响应$\theta$变化，为研究真空拓扑和共存基态提供了量子信息视角。目标是阐明在$\theta=\pi$处纠缠增强的起源，并判断其是否标志着临界行为或普适物理。

Method: We employ a chirally rotated lattice Hamiltonian formulation that preserves the $2\pi$ periodicity of $\theta$ at the operator level and correctly reproduces the massless limit without $\theta$-dependent lattice artifacts. We numerically compute the reduced density matrix for a spatial bipartition to obtain the entanglement entropy and entanglement spectrum across a range of $\theta$ values and fermion masses $m/g$. We analyze the competition between electric-flux sectors in the vacuum by examining the spectral weight distribution. Additionally, using the Bisognano--Wichmann (BW) theorem, we construct a lattice version of the entanglement Hamiltonian and compare it with the exact modular Hamiltonian derived from the reduced density matrix, focusing on low-energy (infrared) modes.

我们采用一种手性旋转的格点哈密顿量形式，该形式在算符层面保持了$\theta$的$2\pi$周期性，并且在无质量极限下不产生依赖于$\theta$的格点效应。通过对空间进行二分，数值计算约化密度矩阵，从而获得在不同$\theta$值和费米子质量$ m/g $下的纠缠熵和纠缠谱。通过分析真空中电通量扇区间的竞争关系及谱权重分布来研究其物理起源。此外，基于Bisognano--Wichmann（BW）定理构建格点上的纠缠哈密顿量，并将其与从约化密度矩阵得到的精确模哈密顿量进行比较，重点关注低能（红外）模式。


Result: Entanglement entropy exhibits a robust peak at $\theta = \pi$ across all studied mass values, signaling maximal quantum fluctuations due to competition between vacuum branches with opposite electric-field orientation. This enhancement originates from fermion pair creation and reflects the point of maximal overlap between distinct flux vacua. The entanglement spectrum reveals a narrowing of the entanglement gap near the critical mass ratio $m/g \simeq 0.33$, suggesting emergent scale invariance or proximity to a quantum phase transition. The Bisognano--Wichmann entanglement Hamiltonian shows strong agreement with the exact modular Hamiltonian in the infrared sector, indicating that the spatially weighted local Hamiltonian accurately captures long-wavelength entanglement properties. The chirally rotated formulation avoids spurious $\theta$-dependent artifacts and correctly describes open boundary conditions.

纠缠熵在所有研究的质量值下均在$\theta = \pi$处表现出明显的峰值，表明由于具有相反电场取向的真空分支之间的竞争，量子涨落达到最大。这种增强源于费米子对的产生，反映了不同通量真空之间最大重叠的状态。纠缠谱显示，在临界质量比$ m/g \simeq 0.33 $附近纠缠能隙显著变窄，暗示可能出现的标度不变性或接近量子相变。Bisognano--Wichmann纠缠哈密顿量在红外区域与精确的模哈密顿量高度一致，表明空间加权的局域哈密顿量能够准确描述长波长的纠缠特性。手性旋转形式避免了虚假的$\theta$相关格点效应，并正确描述了开边界条件。

Conclusion: Entanglement observables serve as sensitive probes of the $\theta$-dependent vacuum structure in gauge theories. The enhancement of entanglement entropy at $\theta = \pi$ is a generic feature arising from competition between topologically distinct vacuum sectors, maximized when these are degenerate. The narrowing of the entanglement gap near $m/g \simeq 0.33$ hints at possible criticality, warranting further investigation. The success of the BW entanglement Hamiltonian on the lattice supports the idea that entanglement dynamics in conformal-like regimes can be captured by effective geometric Hamiltonians. The chirally rotated Hamiltonian provides a robust framework for studying $\theta$-physics and entanglement in systems with open boundaries.

纠缠可观测量是探测规范理论中$\theta$依赖真空结构的敏感工具。在$\theta = \pi$处纠缠熵的增强是一种普遍特征，源于拓扑上不同的真空扇区之间的竞争，并在这些扇区简并时达到最大化。在$ m/g \simeq 0.33 $附近纠缠能隙的变窄暗示可能存在临界行为，值得进一步研究。Bisognano--Wichmann纠缠哈密顿量在格点上的成功应用支持了在类共形区域中纠缠动力学可通过有效几何哈密顿量描述的观点。手性旋转哈密顿量为研究具有开边界系统的$\theta$物理和纠缠提供了稳健框架。

Abstract: We compute the entanglement entropy and the entanglement spectrum of the vacuum state in the massive Schwinger model at a finite $θ$ angle. The $θ$ term is implemented through a chirally rotated lattice Hamiltonian that preserves the periodicity in $θ$ already at the operator level and maintains the correct massless limit without $θ$-dependent lattice artifacts. We clarify the physical origin of entanglement entropy enhancement at $θ=π$ by relating it to the competition between distinct electric-flux vacuum branches. We show that the peak near $θ=π$ persists across the range of masses studied and corresponds to the point of maximal competition between distinct vacuum branches with opposite electric-field orientation, where quantum fluctuations due to fermion pair creation are maximized. While this entropy enhancement is generic, a pronounced narrowing of the entanglement gap occurs only near the critical mass ratio $m/g\simeq0.33$. Using the Bisognano--Wichmann (BW) theorem, we construct a lattice BW entanglement Hamiltonian and compare it with the exact modular Hamiltonian obtained from the reduced density matrix. We observe agreement between these Hamiltonians in the infrared sector, indicating that the entanglement Hamiltonian is well approximated by a spatially weighted microscopic Hamiltonian. These results establish entanglement observables as sensitive probes of the $θ$-dependent vacuum structure and highlight the chirally rotated formulation as a natural framework for open boundary conditions. Additionally, we discuss possible applications to entanglement in topological insulators and quantum wires.

### [42] [Two-Loop Spacelike Splitting Amplitudes in Full-Color QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27123)
*Federico Buccioni,Hanyu Fang,Kai Yan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We present the first complete two-loop spacelike splitting amplitudes in full-color QCD for all partonic channels and helicity configurations, confirming universal contributions from N=4 sYM and identifying new collinear factorization-violating (CFV) effects that cancel in color-summed squared amplitudes, supporting single-parton collinear factorization at third order in QCD.

我们首次给出了全色QCD中所有部分子通道和螺旋构型下的两圈类空间分裂振幅的完整结果，确认了来自N=4 sYM理论的普适性贡献，并发现了新的在色荷求和平方振幅中抵消的共线因子化破坏（CFV）效应，支持了QCD三阶下单部分子共线因子化的普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the factorization properties of QCD scattering amplitudes in the collinear limit is essential for precision predictions in collider physics. While previous studies in N=4 sYM revealed certain universal structures and CFV effects, it remains crucial to extend these investigations to full QCD to assess their generality and identify new dynamics absent in supersymmetric theories.

理解共线极限下QCD散射振幅的因子化性质对对撞机物理的精确预测至关重要。尽管N=4 sYM中的先前研究揭示了某些普适结构和CFV效应，但仍需将这些研究扩展到全QCD，以评估其普适性并识别超对称理论中缺失的新动力学机制。

Method: We compute two-loop spacelike splitting amplitudes using modern amplitude techniques, including spinor-helicity formalism, generalized unitarity, and infrared factorization constraints. Calculations are performed in dimensional regularization, retaining full color dependence and covering all relevant partonic channels (gg, gq, qq, etc.) and helicity configurations.

我们采用现代振幅技术计算两圈类空间分裂振幅，包括旋量-螺旋度形式、广义幺正性以及红外因子化约束。计算在维度正规化下进行，保留完整的色荷依赖性，并覆盖所有相关部分子通道（gg, gq, qq等）和螺旋构型。

Result: We obtain the first complete set of two-loop spacelike splitting amplitudes in full-color QCD. We confirm the presence of universal contributions previously observed in N=4 sYM and discover new sources of collinear factorization-violating (CFV) terms. Crucially, all CFV contributions vanish upon color summation in squared amplitudes, ensuring consistency with single-parton collinear factorization at $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^3)$.

我们获得了全色QCD中首个完整的两圈类空间分裂振幅集合。我们确认了此前在N=4 sYM中观察到的普适性贡献的存在，并发现了新的共线因子化破坏（CFV）项来源。关键的是，所有CFV贡献在平方振幅的色荷求和后消失，确保了在$\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^3)$阶上单部分子共线因子化的一致性。

Conclusion: Single-parton collinear factorization holds universally for jet cross sections in QCD at third order, despite the presence of CFV effects at the amplitude level. The cancellation of CFV terms in color-summed observables underscores the robustness of factorization in QCD and highlights the importance of considering gauge-invariant quantities when assessing factorization properties.

尽管在振幅层面存在CFV效应，单部分子共线因子化在QCD三阶下对喷注截面仍然普遍成立。CFV项在色荷求和观测量中的抵消凸显了QCD中因子化的稳健性，并强调了在评估因子化性质时考虑规范不变量的重要性。

Abstract: The study of QCD scattering amplitudes in the collinear regime provides crucial insight into the factorization properties of hadronic cross sections. In this paper, we present the first complete results for two-loop spacelike splitting amplitudes in full-color QCD, in all partonic channels and helicity configurations. We confirm the universality of a class of contributions already found in N=4 super Yang--Mills (sYM) theory, and identify previously unknown sources of collinear factorization-violating (CFV) effects. Consistent with recent observations in N=4 sYM, all CFV contributions cancel in color-summed squared amplitudes, implying the universality of single-parton collinear factorization for jet cross sections at third order in QCD.

### [43] [Baryonic vortices in rotating nuclear matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29325)
*Kazuya Mameda,Muneto Nitta,Zebin Qiu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study baryonic vortices in rotating nuclear matter using chiral perturbation theory, identifying two types—local and global vortices—both carrying baryon number as a topological charge from $\pi_3(S^3)$. While local vortices involve charged pion condensation with phase winding at the boundary, global vortices are formed by neutral pion condensation. Typically disfavored due to energy divergence, global vortices become physically viable under finite-size constraints imposed by causality in rotation. An energetic competition between the two arises, tunable via rotation, system size, and baryon chemical potential, suggesting a significant role for global vortices in dense QCD matter.

我们利用手征微扰理论研究旋转核物质中的重子涡旋，识别出两种类型——局域涡旋和整体涡旋，二者均以$\pi_3(S^3)$对应的拓扑荷携带重子数。局域涡旋在边界处具有带电π介子凝聚和相位缠绕，而中性π介子沿涡旋核心内的旋转轴变化；整体涡旋则由中性π介子的凝聚和相位缠绕形成，带电π介子在内部沿旋转轴变化。尽管整体涡旋通常因能量对数发散而在无限系统中被排除，但我们证明旋转系中因果性导致的有限尺寸约束可物理地正则化该发散，使其成为可行的激发态。研究揭示了两种涡旋之间的能量竞争，可通过旋转、系统尺寸和重子化学势调节，表明此前被忽视的整体涡旋在旋转致密QCD物质的拓扑结构中可能起重要作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Topological excitations in dense QCD matter, such as Skyrmions and vortices, play a crucial role in understanding the non-perturbative structure of nuclear matter under extreme conditions. In rotating systems—such as those realized in heavy-ion collisions or neutron stars—vorticity is expected to influence the phase structure and topological content of quantum chromodynamics (QCD). However, the role of global vortices, typically dismissed due to their divergent energy in infinite systems, remains unexplored under realistic, finite-size physical constraints. This work aims to re-examine the viability of global baryonic vortices in rotating nuclear matter within chiral perturbation theory ($\chi$PT), particularly under causality-enforced finite-size effects, and assess their competition with local vortex configurations.

在极端条件下，致密QCD物质中的拓扑激发（如Skyrmion和涡旋）对于理解核物质的非微扰结构至关重要。在旋转系统（如重离子碰撞或中子星）中，涡旋性预期会影响量子色动力学（QCD）的相结构和拓扑内容。然而，在真实物理条件下受有限尺寸约束时，通常因无限系统中能量发散而被忽略的整体涡旋的作用仍未被探索。本工作旨在利用手征微扰理论（$\chi$PT）重新审视旋转核物质中整体重子涡旋的可行性，特别是在因果性导致的有限尺寸效应下，并评估其与局域涡旋构型的竞争关系。

Method: We employ chiral perturbation theory ($\chi$PT) as the low-energy effective field theory of QCD to describe nuclear matter under rotation. By analyzing the homotopy group structure $\pi_3(S^3) \simeq \mathbb{Z}$, we identify baryon number as a topological charge carried by vortex configurations. We construct explicit solutions for both local and global vortices: the local vortex features a charged pion condensate with phase winding at spatial infinity and neutral pion variation along the rotation axis in the core; the global vortex exhibits neutral pion condensation with phase winding, while charged pions vary inside. The energy divergence of the global vortex is analyzed and regularized by imposing a finite radius dictated by the speed-of-light limit in a rotating frame—i.e., $R_{\text{max}} = c/\Omega$, ensuring causality. We compute and compare the energies of both configurations as functions of angular velocity $\Omega$, system size $R$, and baryon chemical potential $\mu_B$, revealing an energetic competition.

我们采用手征微扰理论（$\chi$PT）作为QCD的低能有效场论来描述旋转下的核物质。通过分析同伦群结构$\pi_3(S^3) \simeq \mathbb{Z}$，我们将重子数识别为涡旋构型所携带的拓扑荷。我们构造了局域和整体涡旋的显式解：局域涡旋在空间无穷远处具有带电π介子凝聚和相位缠绕，核心内中性π介子沿旋转轴变化；整体涡旋则表现出中性π介子的凝聚和相位缠绕，而带电π介子在内部变化。整体涡旋的能量发散通过在旋转系中施加由光速极限决定的有限半径（即$R_{\text{max}} = c/\Omega$）进行分析和正则化，以保证因果性。我们计算并比较了两种构型的能量随角速度$\Omega$、系统尺寸$R$和重子化学势$\mu_B$的变化，揭示了它们之间的能量竞争。

Result: We find two distinct topological vortex solutions in rotating nuclear matter: (1) the local vortex, analogous to the vortex Skyrmion at finite isospin density, with charged pion condensation and phase winding at the boundary; (2) the global vortex, supported by neutral pion condensation and phase winding. Crucially, the logarithmic infrared divergence in the energy of the global vortex is tamed by the finite-size cutoff $R \leq c/\Omega$, imposed by causality in the rotating frame. This renders the global vortex energetically viable. Furthermore, the energy comparison shows a tunable competition between the two vortex types: at higher rotation rates $\Omega$, smaller system sizes, or lower $\mu_B$, the global vortex becomes favored over the local one. Thus, the global vortex is not only physically allowed but can dominate under certain conditions.

我们在旋转核物质中发现了两种不同的拓扑涡旋解：(1) 局域涡旋，类似于有限同位旋密度下的涡旋Skyrmion，其边界处存在带电π介子凝聚和相位缠绕；(2) 整体涡旋，由中性π介子的凝聚和相位缠绕支撑。关键的是，整体涡旋能量中的对数红外发散被旋转系中因果性所要求的有限尺寸截断$R \leq c/\Omega$抑制，使其在能量上可行。此外，能量比较显示两种涡旋类型之间存在可调的竞争关系：在较高转速$\Omega$、较小系统尺寸或较低$\mu_B$下，整体涡旋比局域涡旋更受青睐。因此，整体涡旋不仅在物理上允许，而且在特定条件下可占主导地位。

Conclusion: Global baryonic vortices, though traditionally discarded in infinite systems due to energy divergence, are physically admissible in causally constrained rotating frames owing to finite-size regularization. Together with local vortices, they form a pair of competing topological excitations in rotating dense nuclear matter, with the balance controlled by $\Omega$, $R$, and $\mu_B$. This work highlights the importance of global vortices in the topological classification of QCD matter under rotation and suggests that they may significantly influence the structure and dynamics of dense matter in heavy-ion collisions and compact stars.

尽管整体重子涡旋传统上因能量发散而在无限系统中被舍弃，但在受因果性限制的旋转系中，由于有限尺寸正则化而成为物理上可接受的激发态。它们与局域涡旋共同构成旋转致密核物质中一对竞争的拓扑激发，其平衡由$\Omega$、$R$和$\mu_B$调控。本工作强调了整体涡旋在旋转下QCD物质拓扑分类中的重要性，并表明其可能显著影响重离子碰撞和致密星体中致密物质的结构与动力学。

Abstract: We investigate baryonic vortices as topological excitations in rotating nuclear matter within the framework of chiral perturbation theory. We identify two distinct configurations: local and global vortices, both carrying the baryon number as the topological charge associated with the third homotopy group $π_3(S^3)$. For the local vortex, similar to the vortex Skyrmion in a finite isospin chemical potential, charged pions form the condensate on the boundary and have a phase winding, while the neutral pion varies along the rotation axis inside the vortex core. On the other hand, a global vortex is formed by the condensate and phase winding of the neutral pion, while the charged pions vary on the inside along the rotation axis. Crucially, although global vortices are usually discarded in infinite systems due to logarithmic divergence in energy, we demonstrate that the finite-size constraint dictated by causality in a rotating frame regularizes the divergence physically, rendering the global vortex a viable excitation. We reveal an energetic competition between global and local vortex states, under the tunable parameters of rotation, system size, and baryon chemical potential. Our results suggest that the previously overlooked global vortex can play a significant role in the topological structure of rotating dense QCD matter.

### [44] [Search for Light Scalars in the TRSM at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29395)
*Aman Desai,Kristin Lohwasser,Mohamed Ouchemhou,Tania Robens,Prasenjit Sanyal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study the production of Beyond the Standard Model light scalar states in association with a vector boson ($Vh_2$, with $V = W^\\pm, Z$) at the LHC. We consider the scenario where the Standard Model scalar sector is extended by two real scalar singlets, where these additional scalars have mass $ M_i \\leq M_{h_{125}}$. In this work, the scalar boson $h_2$ decays via $h_2 \\to h_1 h_1 \\to 4b$, while the associated vector boson decays either into a pair of oppositely charged leptons or into a single charged lepton and a neutrino. We analyze the signal using LHC detector parameterizations and evaluate its statistical significance at a center-of-mass energy of 13.6~TeV for integrated luminosities of 300~fb$^{-1}$ and 3000~fb$^{-1}$ corresponding to the LHC Run 3 and High Luminosity LHC, respectively. Our preliminary results indicate promising discovery prospects for this channel serving as a complementary probe of extended scalar sectors.\n\n我们研究了在LHC上矢量玻色子（$Vh_2$，其中$V = W^\\pm, Z$）伴随产生超越标准模型的轻标量态。我们考虑了标准模型标量部分通过两个实标量单态扩展的情形，这些额外的标量具有质量$ M_i \\leq M_{h_{125}}$。在此工作中，标量玻色子$h_2$通过$h_2 \\to h_1 h_1 \\to 4b$衰变，而伴随的矢量玻色子衰变为一对带相反电荷的轻子或一个带电轻子和一个中微子。我们使用LHC探测器参数化分析信号，并在13.6 TeV质心能量下评估其统计显著性，积分亮度分别为300 fb$^{-1}$和3000 fb$^{-1}$，对应LHC Run 3和高亮度LHC。我们的初步结果表明，该通道具有良好的发现前景，可作为扩展标量部门的补充探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore extensions of the Standard Model scalar sector through the production of light scalar states in association with vector bosons, which can provide insights into physics beyond the Standard Model and test scenarios involving additional scalar singlets that are not easily accessible through conventional Higgs searches.\n\n动机是通过与矢量玻色子伴随产生的轻标量态来探索标准模型标量部门的扩展，这可以提供对超越标准模型物理的见解，并测试涉及额外标量单态的情景，这些情景无法通过传统的希格斯搜索轻易获得。

Method: We consider a model with two real scalar singlets added to the Standard Model, leading to three physical scalar states including the observed 125 GeV Higgs boson. The production process $pp \\to Vh_2$ is studied at the LHC with $\\sqrt{s} = 13.6$ TeV. Detector simulations and kinematic cuts are applied to isolate the signal $Vh_2 \\to V(h_1h_1) \\to V(4b)$, with $V \\to \\ell^+\\ell^-$ or $\\ell^\pm\\nu$. Statistical significance is evaluated using profile likelihood methods for integrated luminosities of 300 fb$^{-1}$ and 3000 fb$^{-1}$.\n\n我们考虑将两个实标量单态加入标准模型的模型，导致包括观测到的125 GeV希格斯玻色子在内的三个物理标量态。在$\\sqrt{s} = 13.6$ TeV的LHC上研究了产生过程$pp \\to Vh_2$。应用探测器模拟和运动学截断来分离信号$Vh_2 \\to V(h_1h_1) \\to V(4b)$，其中$V \\to \\ell^+\\ell^-$或$\\ell^\pm\\nu$。使用轮廓似然方法在300 fb$^{-1}$和3000 fb$^{-1}$的积分亮度下评估统计显著性。

Result: Our analysis shows that the $Vh_2 \\to V(4b)$ channel with leptonic vector boson decays offers detectable signals at the LHC. For certain benchmark points in the two-singlet extension model, the statistical significance reaches above $5\\sigma$ at 3000 fb$^{-1}$, indicating strong discovery potential. Sensitivity is also present at 300 fb$^{-1}$, though below discovery threshold, allowing for early tests during Run 3.\n\n我们的分析表明，在LHC上，带有轻子型矢量玻色子衰变的$Vh_2 \\to V(4b)$通道提供了可检测的信号。对于双单态扩展模型中的某些基准点，在3000 fb$^{-1}$时统计显著性达到$5\\sigma$以上，显示出强大的发现潜力。在300 fb$^{-1}$时也存在灵敏度，尽管低于发现阈值，但允许在Run 3期间进行早期测试。

Conclusion: The search for $Vh_2$ production with $h_2 \\to h_1 h_1 \\to 4b$ provides a promising avenue for probing extended scalar sectors at the LHC. This channel complements traditional Higgs searches and enhances sensitivity to light scalar states that may be overlooked in standard analyses, particularly in models with multiple scalar singlets.\n\n寻找$Vh_2$产生并伴随$h_2 \\to h_1 h_1 \\to 4b$为在LHC上探测扩展标量部门提供了一条有希望的途径。该通道补充了传统的希格斯搜索，并增强了对可能在标准分析中被忽视的轻标量态的敏感性，特别是在具有多个标量单态的模型中。

Abstract: We study the production of Beyond the Standard Model light scalar states in association with a vector boson ($Vh_2$, with $V = W^\pm, Z$) at the LHC. We consider the scenario where the Standard Model scalar sector is extended by two real scalar singlets, where these additional scalars have mass $ M_i \leq M_{h_{125}}$. In this work, the scalar boson $h_2$ decays via $h_2 \to h_1 h_1 \to 4b$, while the associated vector boson decays either into a pair of oppositely charged leptons or into a single charged lepton and a neutrino. We analyze the signal using LHC detector parameterizations and evaluate its statistical significance at a center-of-mass energy of 13.6~TeV for integrated luminosities of 300~fb$^{-1}$ and 3000~fb$^{-1}$ corresponding to the LHC Run 3 and High Luminosity LHC, respectively. Our preliminary results indicate promising discovery prospects for this channel serving as a complementary probe of extended scalar sectors.\\ RBI-ThPhys-2026-04, COMETA-2026-04

### [45] [Flavor-deconstructed neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29448)
*Avelino Vicente*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A flavor-deconstructed model with gauge non-universality across fermion families is proposed, where sequential dominance in both neutrinos and charged leptons naturally emerges, offering an explanation for the lepton sector's flavor structure.

一种基于味解构的模型被提出，该模型在不同费米子族间具有非普适规范对称性，中微子和带电轻子中的序列主导（sequential dominance）自然出现，从而解释了轻子部门的味结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The flavor puzzle in the Standard Model—particularly the hierarchical structure of fermion masses and mixing angles—remains unexplained. One promising direction is gauge non-universal theories (flavor deconstruction), where each fermion family has its own gauge group. However, incorporating neutrino physics into such frameworks is challenging due to their small masses and large mixing angles, motivating the need for a consistent mechanism that explains both charged leptons and neutrinos within this paradigm.

标准模型中的味难题——特别是费米子质量与混合角的层级结构——仍未得到解释。一个有前景的方向是采用非普适规范理论（即味解构），其中每个费米子族拥有独立的规范群。然而，由于中微子质量极小且混合角较大，将中微子物理纳入此类框架存在挑战，因此需要在此范式下统一解释带电轻子和中微子的机制。

Method: The paper reviews existing approaches to flavor deconstruction and proposes a simple model based on extending the Standard Model gauge group to $SU(3)_L \times SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$ per family, with spontaneous symmetry breaking at different scales. The structure of Yukawa couplings and right-handed neutrino Majorana masses is arranged so that sequential dominance arises naturally via hierarchical vacuum expectation values and fermion localization in extra dimensions or through discrete symmetries.

本文回顾了现有的味解构方法，并提出了一个简单模型：将标准模型规范群扩展为每族对应的 $SU(3)_L \times SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$，并通过不同能标的自发对称破缺实现。通过分层的真空期望值以及额外维度中的费米子局域化或离散对称性，安排了 Yukawa 耦合和右手型中微子马约拉纳质量的结构，使得序列主导自然产生。

Result: The proposed model successfully generates sequential dominance in the lepton sector, leading to realistic neutrino mass hierarchies and large mixing angles, while also reproducing the observed hierarchy in charged lepton masses. The flavor-deconstructed setup avoids dangerous flavor-changing neutral currents (FCNCs) due to the separation of gauge interactions by family.

所提出的模型在轻子部门成功实现了序列主导，导致了合理的中微子质量层级和大混合角，同时再现了带电轻子质量的观测层级。由于不同族之间的规范相互作用分离，该味解构设置避免了危险的味变中性流（FCNCs）问题。

Conclusion: Flavor deconstruction provides a viable framework for addressing the flavor puzzle in the lepton sector. By naturally realizing sequential dominance for both neutrinos and charged leptons, the model demonstrates how gauge non-universality can lead to realistic flavor structures without fine-tuning, offering new insights into the origin of fermion hierarchies.

味解构为解决轻子部门的味难题提供了一个可行的框架。通过在中微子和带电轻子中自然实现序列主导，该模型展示了非普适规范对称性如何无需精细调节即可导出真实的味结构，为费米子层级起源提供了新的见解。

Abstract: A tentative approach to explain the flavor puzzle consists of embedding the Standard Model in a larger gauge symmetry that contains a separate gauge group for each fermion family. In such gauge non-universal (or flavor-deconstructed) theories, neutrinos pose some challenges. I will discuss existing ideas in the literature and present a simple model in which flavor deconstruction naturally leads to sequential dominance for both neutrinos and charged leptons, thus providing a viable explanation for the flavor structure of the lepton sector.
