### [46] [Top-Yukawa contributions to $pp\to b\bar{b}H$: two-loop leading-colour amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29480)
*Heribertus Bayu Hartanto,Rene Poncelet*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We compute two-loop scattering amplitudes for bottom-quark pair production in association with a Higgs boson at the LHC, focusing on contributions proportional to the top-quark Yukawa coupling, using the massless bottom-quark approximation and the heavy-top-quark limit. The finite remainder is expressed in terms of one-mass pentagon functions, with rational coefficients reconstructed via finite-field methods.

我们计算了在LHC上Higgs玻色子伴随底夸克对产生的两圈散射振幅，重点关注与顶夸克Yukawa耦合成正比的项，采用底夸克无质量近似和重顶夸克极限。有限部分振幅用单质量五边形函数表示，并通过有限域方法解析重构有理系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Precision studies of Higgs-boson interactions with bottom quarks are essential for testing the Standard Model and probing new physics. The two-loop QCD corrections, especially those involving the dominant top-Yukawa coupling, are crucial for reducing theoretical uncertainties in $ b\bar{b}H $ production. Existing calculations often rely on approximations; improving their accuracy within controlled limits enhances phenomenological reliability.

精确研究Higgs玻色子与底夸克相互作用对于检验标准模型和探索新物理至关重要。涉及主导顶夸克Yukawa耦合的两圈QCD修正对于降低$ b\bar{b}H $产生过程中的理论不确定性至关重要。现有计算常依赖近似方法，在可控极限内提高其精度可增强唯象可靠性。

Method: We employ perturbative QCD at next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO), computing two-loop amplitudes in the leading-colour and heavy-top-quark approximations. The bottom quark is treated as a massless parton. The loop integrals are reduced to a basis of one-mass pentagon functions using integration-by-parts (IBP) identities. Finite remainders are constructed from numerical evaluations over finite fields, enabling analytic reconstruction of rational coefficients via computational algebraic geometry techniques.

我们在领头色和重顶夸克近似下，采用微扰QCD在次次领头阶（NNLO）计算两圈振幅。底夸克被视为无质量部分子。利用分部积分（IBP）恒等式将圈积分约化为单质量五边形函数基。通过对有限域的数值计算，结合计算代数几何技术，实现有理系数的解析重构。

Result: The two-loop amplitude for $ b\bar{b}H $ production is obtained with full dependence on the physical kinematics, expressed compactly in terms of one-mass pentagon functions. Rational coefficients are determined analytically using finite-field sampling. This result includes all planar two-loop diagrams mediated by the top-Yukawa coupling and provides a key ingredient for NNLO QCD predictions in the heavy-top limit. It also contributes to the $ HH \to 2j $ channel within Higgs+2-jet production.

得到了$ b\bar{b}H $产生的两圈振幅，完整依赖于物理运动学变量，并以单质量五边形函数紧凑表示。利用有限域采样解析确定了有理系数。该结果包含了由顶Yukawa耦合介导的所有平面两圈图，是重顶极限下NNLO QCD预言的关键组成部分，同时也贡献于Higgs+2-喷注产生中的$ HH \to 2j $道。

Conclusion: We present a high-precision calculation of two-loop amplitudes for $ b\bar{b}H $ production in the heavy-top and massless-bottom approximations. The use of one-mass pentagon functions and finite-field methods enables analytic results with high numerical stability. This work advances the state-of-the-art in Higgs phenomenology at NNLO and supports more accurate collider data analysis.

我们在重顶夸克和无质量底夸克近似下，给出了$ b\bar{b}H $产生两圈振幅的高精度计算。使用单质量五边形函数和有限域方法实现了具有高数值稳定性的解析结果。本工作推进了NNLO下Higgs唯象学的前沿，支持更精确的对撞机数据分析。

Abstract: We derive two-loop scattering amplitudes for bottom-quark pair production in association with a Higgs boson at the LHC, focusing on terms proportional to the top-quark Yukawa coupling. We treat the bottom quark as a massless parton and employ both the leading-colour and heavy-top-quark approximations. The finite remainder of the two-loop amplitude is expressed in terms of one-mass pentagon functions, and the corresponding rational coefficients are reconstructed analytically from evaluations over finite fields. The scattering processes considered in this work also constitute a subset of Higgs+2-jet production at the LHC in the heavy-top-quark approximation.

</details>


### [47] [Two-Dimensional Transverse-Momentum Subtraction and Semi-Inclusive Deep-Inelastic Scattering at N$^3$LO in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29673)
*Liang Dong,Shen Fang,Jun Gao,Hai Tao Li,Ding Yu Shao,Hua Xing Zhu,Yu Jiao Zhu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We present the first N$^3$LO calculation of unpolarized semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering (SIDIS) in perturbative QCD, based on a novel two-dimensional transverse-momentum subtraction method that respects QCD factorization. The framework ensures excellent perturbative convergence, reduced scale dependence, and allows arbitrary kinematic cuts, enabling high-precision nucleon structure studies at the Electron-Ion Collider.

我们提出了第一个在微扰QCD中非极化半轻深非弹性散射（SIDIS）的N$^3$LO计算，基于一种新颖的二维横动量减法方法，该方法符合QCD因子化。该框架具有优异的微扰收敛性、降低的能标依赖性，并允许任意运动学截断，为电子-离子对撞机上的高精度核子结构研究奠定了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Precision studies of nucleon structure and QCD hadronization require high-order theoretical predictions for SIDIS processes. Existing calculations lack full N$^3$LO accuracy, limiting the ability to match the precision of upcoming experiments like those at the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC). A robust, differential framework is needed to handle arbitrary experimental cuts and reduce theoretical uncertainties.

对核子结构和QCD强子化的精密研究需要SIDIS过程的高阶理论预测。现有计算缺乏完整的N$^3$LO精度，限制了与即将开展的电子-离子对撞机（EIC）实验精度相匹配的能力。因此需要一个稳健且全微分的理论框架来处理任意实验截断并减少理论不确定性。

Method: We develop a new two-dimensional transverse-momentum ($q_T$) subtraction scheme motivated by QCD factorization, which systematically regulates soft and collinear divergences in the cross-section calculation. This method enables the first full N$^3$LO computation for unpolarized SIDIS by consistently combining fixed-order matrix elements with factorized soft and jet functions. The subtraction is performed differentially in hadron transverse momentum and energy fraction $z$, preserving full kinematic information.

我们发展了一种新的二维横动量（$q_T$）减法方案，其动机来自QCD因子化，可系统地调节截面计算中的软和共线发散。该方法通过一致地结合固定阶矩阵元与因子化的软函数和喷注函数，实现了对非极化SIDIS的首次完整N$^3$LO计算。减法在强子横动量和能量分数$z$上微分进行，保留了完整的运动学信息。

Result: The N$^3$LO corrections are generally moderate but become significant near kinematic thresholds, where they improve prediction accuracy. Perturbative convergence is excellent, with reduced renormalization and factorization scale variations compared to lower orders. The fully differential framework supports arbitrary selection cuts, making it directly applicable to realistic EIC analyses. Our results establish a solid theory foundation for precision tomography of the nucleon.

N$^3$LO修正总体适中，但在运动学阈值区域显著，提升了预测精度。微扰收敛性优异，相较于低阶结果，重整化和因子化能标变化显著减小。全微分框架支持任意选择截断，可直接应用于真实的EIC分析。我们的结果为核子精密层析成像建立了坚实的理论基础。

Conclusion: We have achieved the first N$^3$LO calculation for unpolarized SIDIS using a factorization-motivated $q_T$ subtraction method. This breakthrough enables high-precision QCD phenomenology for nucleon structure studies, meeting the projected accuracy of EIC data. The method is generalizable to polarized SIDIS and other semi-inclusive processes, opening new avenues for precision strong interaction physics.

我们使用基于因子化的$q_T$减法方法，首次实现了非极化SIDIS的N$^3$LO计算。这一突破使核子结构研究中的高精度QCD唯象学成为可能，满足了EIC数据预期的精度要求。该方法可推广至极化SIDIS及其他半轻过程，为高精度强相互作用物理开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Identified hadron production is essential for the study of nucleon structure and QCD hadronization at high energies. We present the first calculation of unpolarized semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering (SIDIS) at next-to-next-to-next-to-leading order (N$^3$LO) in perturbative QCD. Our calculation is based on a novel method of two-dimensional transverse-momentum subtraction motivated by QCD factorization of soft and collinear singularities. The N$^3$LO corrections are moderate in general but can be significant in threshold regions, and exhibit excellent perturbative convergence and reduced scale variations. The fully differential framework allows for arbitrary selection cuts and directly enables precision nucleon tomography at the upcoming Electron-Ion Collider, establishing the theory foundation needed to match the anticipated experimental accuracy. Generalization of the method to calculations of polarized SIDIS is also feasible.

### [48] [Sensitivity of Two-Body Non-Leptonic Branching Fractions to Theoretical Mass Variations in Heavy-Light Mesons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29767)
*Manakkumar Parmar,Ajay Kumar Rai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The study examines how theoretical mass variations in heavy-light mesons affect two-body non-leptonic branching fractions, showing that Gaussian masses are crucial for bottom mesons while hydrogenic masses better describe charm decays due to kinematic compensation; the framework is extendable to exotic meson decays.

本研究考察了重-轻介子中理论质量变化对两体非轻子分支比的影响，表明高斯质量对底介子至关重要，而氢型质量通过运动学补偿更准确描述粲介子衰变；该框架可推广至奇特介子衰变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the impact of theoretical mass models (Gaussian vs. hydrogenic wavefunctions) on predicted branching fractions in heavy-light meson decays, particularly where factorization approaches face limitations due to relativistic effects and final-state interactions.

为了理解理论质量模型（高斯与氢型波函数）对重-轻介子衰变分支比预测的影响，特别是在因子化方法因相对论效应和末态相互作用而受限的情况下。

Method: Using naive factorization with $N = 3$ and the large-$N$ limit ($N \to \infty$), branching fractions are computed with phenomenological masses derived from Gaussian and hydrogenic wavefunctions; sensitivity analyses are performed across $D$, $D_s$, $B$, and $B_s$ decays.

采用朴素因子化（$N = 3$）和大-$N$极限（$N \to \infty$），利用来自高斯和氢型波函数的现象学质量计算分支比，并在$D$、$D_s$、$B$和$B_s$衰变中进行敏感性分析。

Result: For bottom mesons, Gaussian masses with $N=3$ agree well with data, and $N\to\infty$ offers no improvement; in charm decays, hydrogenic masses—despite underestimating mass—yield better agreement for color-suppressed channels by acting as a kinematic regulator that offsets overestimated factorized amplitudes.

对于底介子，高斯质量结合$N=3$与实验数据吻合良好，而$N\to\infty$无改进；在粲介子衰变中，尽管氢型质量低估了质量，但作为运动学调节器能抵消被高估的因子化振幅，从而在颜色压低道中给出更好结果。

Conclusion: Accurate mass modeling via Gaussian wavefunctions is essential for bottom meson decays, whereas hydrogenic mass underestimation provides a compensatory kinematic effect in charm decays; combining Gaussian-based predictions with factorization offers a predictive framework for unobserved exotics like excited $B_c$ and $T_{bb}$ tetraquarks.

通过高斯波函数的精确质量建模对底介子衰变至关重要，而氢型质量低估在粲介子衰变中提供了补偿性运动学效应；将基于高斯的质量预测与因子化结合，为激发态$B_c$和$T_{bb}$四夸克态等未观测奇特粒子提供了可预测框架。

Abstract: This study investigates the sensitivity of two-body non-leptonic branching fractions to theoretical mass variations in heavy-light mesons ($D$, $D_s$, $B$, and $B_s$). Utilizing the factorization framework, we compare predictions derived from phenomenological masses evaluated with Gaussian and hydrogenic wavefunctions. For bottom meson decays, naive factorization with the number of color $N = 3$ aligns well with experimental data, and the $N \to \infty$ limit offers no improvement. Furthermore, the theoretical mass variation between wavefunction models induces a pronounced, non-linear sensitivity in the branching fractions, establishing the accurate Gaussian mass as a crucial baseline. Conversely, in the charm sector, naive factorization is inherently limited by final-state interactions due to insufficient relativistic recoil. While the $N \to \infty$ limit partially compensates for this, the systematically lower hydrogenic mass yields more accurate rates for several color-suppressed channels. This mass underestimation acts as a necessary kinematic regulator, cleanly offsetting the inflated amplitudes inherent to charm factorization. Ultimately, combining reliable Gaussian mass predictions with factorization provides a simple formalism extendable to the decay properties of unobserved exotics, such as excited $B_c$ mesons and $T_{bb}$ tetraquarks.

### [49] [Constraining the Neutrino Mixing Matrix via Single-Sector Charged-Lepton Rotations in the JUNO Precision Era](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29876)
*Alessio Giarnetti,Simone Marciano,Davide Meloni*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study how charged-lepton mixing with a single two-by-two rotation affects the structure of the neutrino mixing matrix $U_\nu$, deriving compact analytical sum rules for its entries using latest PMNS data, including JUNO's precise $\theta_{12}$ measurement.

我们研究了带电轻子混合中单个二维旋转如何影响中微子混合矩阵 $U_\nu$ 的结构，并利用最新的PMNS数据（包括JUNO对 $\theta_{12}$ 的精确测量）推导出其矩阵元的紧凑解析求和规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The high-precision measurement of the PMNS matrix, especially $\theta_{12}$ from JUNO, motivates a deeper investigation into the structure of the neutrino mass matrix and possible underlying flavor symmetries. By simplifying the charged-lepton mixing matrix $U_l$ to a single two-by-two rotation, we aim to uncover testable relations in $U_\nu$ that could reveal fundamental patterns.

PMNS矩阵的高精度测量，特别是JUNO对 $\theta_{12}$ 的测量，促使人们深入探究中微子质量矩阵的结构及潜在的味对称性。通过将带电轻子混合矩阵 $U_l$ 简化为单个二维旋转，我们旨在揭示 $U_\nu$ 中可检验的关系，从而发现基本规律。

Method: We assume the charged-lepton mixing matrix $U_l$ contains only one non-trivial two-by-two rotation in either the (1,2), (1,3), or (2,3) sector. Using the relation $U_{\rm PMNS} = U_l^\dagger U_\nu$, we solve for $U_\nu = U_l U_{\rm PMNS}$ and derive analytical expressions for its elements in terms of the observed mixing angles and phase. We employ the latest global fit values, particularly the precise $\theta_{12}$ from JUNO, to constrain the form of $U_\nu$ in each scenario.

我们假设带电轻子混合矩阵 $U_l$ 仅在 (1,2)、(1,3) 或 (2,3) 扇区包含一个非平凡的二维旋转。利用关系式 $U_{\rm PMNS} = U_l^\dagger U_\nu$，我们求解 $U_\nu = U_l U_{\rm PMNS}$，并以观测到的混合角和相位表示其矩阵元，推导出解析表达式。我们采用最新的全局拟合值，特别是JUNO给出的精确 $\theta_{12}$，以约束每种情形下 $U_\nu$ 的形式。

Result: For each rotation sector, we obtain compact sum-rule-like formulae connecting the entries of $U_\nu$ to the PMNS parameters. These formulae allow us to predict unmeasured or weakly constrained phases and magnitudes in $U_\nu$, and provide testable predictions for models with specific flavor structures. The inclusion of JUNO's $\theta_{12}$ significantly tightens these constraints.

针对每个旋转扇区，我们得到了将 $U_\nu$ 矩阵元与PMNS参数关联起来的紧凑类求和规则公式。这些公式使我们能够预测 $U_\nu$ 中未测量或弱约束的相位和模量，并为具有特定味结构的模型提供可检验的预测。引入JUNO的 $\theta_{12}$ 数据显著加强了这些约束。

Conclusion: Assuming a simple structure for $U_l$ with a single two-by-two rotation leads to predictive and testable forms for $U_\nu$. The recent precision data, especially from JUNO, enable stringent tests of such flavor hypotheses and offer a pathway to probe the origin of neutrino mixing patterns.

假设 $U_l$ 具有单个二维旋转的简单结构，会导致 $U_\nu$ 出现可预测且可检验的形式。最近的高精度数据，尤其是来自JUNO的数据，使得对这类味假设的严格检验成为可能，并为探索中微子混合模式的起源提供了途径。

Abstract: The unprecedented precision now being achieved in the measurement of the Pontecorvo--Maki--Nakagawa--Sakata (PMNS) lepton mixing matrix opens a new window onto the underlying structure of the neutrino mass matrix and the possibly associated flavor symmetries. In this work, we investigate the constraints imposed on the unitary matrix $U_ν$ that diagonalises the neutrino mass matrix, under the hypothesis that the charged-lepton mixing matrix $U_l$ consists of a single two-by-two rotation in one of the three sectors: (1,2), (1,3), or (2,3). For this analysis, we considered the latest global fit which incorporates the precision measurement of $θ_{12}$ from the JUNO experiment. For each scenario, we also derive analytical expressions for the entries of $U_ν$ in terms of the measured PMNS parameters to obtain compact sum-rule-like formulae.

### [50] [Perturbative QCD fitting of the $e^+e^-$ to hadrons KEDR and BESIII data for R(s) and $α_s$ determination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29803)
*A. L. Kataev,K. Yu. Todyshev*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper analyzes $e^+e^-$ annihilation R-ratio data from KEDR and BESIII collaborations using truncated perturbative QCD at energies below the charm threshold, extracting values of $\alpha_s(M_Z)$ at different orders of perturbation theory.

本文通过在低于粲夸克阈值的能量下对KEDR和BESIII合作组的$e^+e^-$湮灭R比数据使用截断的微扰QCD进行分析，提取了不同微扰阶数下的$\alpha_s(M_Z)$值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To determine the strong coupling constant $\alpha_s(M_Z)$ from low-energy $e^+e^-$ annihilation data by applying perturbative QCD up to various orders, and to study how truncation order affects the extracted value, especially near resonances like $J/\Psi$.

旨在通过应用不同阶数的微扰QCD从低能$e^+e^-$湮灭数据中确定强耦合常数$\alpha_s(M_Z)$，并研究截断阶数对提取结果的影响，特别是在如$J/\Psi$等共振区域附近。

Method: The authors fit the experimental R-ratio data from KEDR and BESIII using fixed-order perturbative QCD expressions truncated at different orders (up to NNLO), combined with renormalization group $\beta$-function analysis. The truncation scale is set at the $J/\Psi$ mass. Analytical continuation effects are carefully considered.

作者使用在不同阶数（最高至NNLO）截断的固定阶微扰QCD表达式拟合来自KEDR和BESIII的R比实验数据，并结合重整化群$\beta$-函数分析，截断尺度设为$J/\Psi$质量，并仔细考虑了解析延拓效应。

Result: Next-to-leading order (NLO) and next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) fits to the combined KEDR and BESIII data yield $\alpha_s(M_Z) = 0.1179^{+0.0051}_{-0.0069}$ and $\alpha_s(M_Z) = 0.1221^{+0.0063}_{-0.0723}$, respectively, showing a noticeable dependence on the perturbative order.

对联合KEDR与BESIII数据的下一阶（NLO）和下二阶（NNLO）拟合分别给出$\alpha_s(M_Z) = 0.1179^{+0.0051}_{-0.0069}$和$\alpha_s(M_Z) = 0.1221^{+0.0063}_{-0.0723}$，显示出对微扰阶数的明显依赖性。

Conclusion: The extracted value of $\alpha_s(M_Z)$ depends significantly on the order of perturbative truncation in QCD, highlighting the importance of higher-order corrections and careful treatment of non-perturbative effects such as those near the $J/\Psi$ resonance. Fixed-order perturbation theory applications must account for analytical continuation and truncation systematics.

提取的$\alpha_s(M_Z)$值显著依赖于QCD中微扰截断的阶数，突显了高阶修正以及对$J/\Psi$共振附近非微扰效应的细致处理的重要性。固定阶微扰理论的应用必须考虑解析延拓和截断系统误差。

Abstract: The experimental data collected by KEDR and BESIII collaborations at the energies below charming quark thresholds are compared with the coordinally truncated at different orders of perturbation theory QCD expressions for the $e^+e^-$ annihilation R-ratio and the renormalization group $β$-function. The fits demonstrate the dependence of the extracted $α_s(M_Z)$ values from orders of the truncation of the corresponding approximations. The next-to-leading order and next-to-next-to-leading order fits of the combined KEDR data and BESIII data , truncated at the mass scale of $J/Ψ$ meson, give the following results $α_s(M_Z)= 0.1179^{+0.0051}_{-0.0069}$ and $α_s(M_Z)=0.1221^{+0.0063}_{-0.0723}$. The subjects related to the applications of the fixed orders of perturbation theory expansions and careful treatment of the analytical continuation effects are commented.

### [51] [From Sub-eikonal DIS to Quark Distributions and their High-Energy Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.30000)
*Giovanni Antonio Chirilli*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper establishes an operator-level connection between the high-energy dipole description of deep-inelastic scattering and the standard light-ray operator formalism at finite Bjorken $x_B$, showing that the first sub-eikonal correction gives rise to a quark TMD-like operator which, in the inclusive limit, reproduces standard nonlocal quark and helicity distributions. This bridge is further confirmed via the leading-twist non-local OPE in the high-energy limit. The study also reformulates high-energy evolution equations at $x_B=0$ using dipole-type operators, revealing Bessel-type solutions and recovering the Kirschner-Lipatov exponent in the double-logarithmic regime.

本文在高能偶极子描述与有限Bjorken $x_B$下的标准光射线算符形式之间建立了算符层面的联系，表明首项次前因子修正对应一个类夸克TMD的光射线算符，在兼容量子极限下可重构标准非局域夸克和螺旋度分布。此桥梁亦通过高能极限下的领头扭度非局域OPE独立验证。研究进一步将$ x_B=0 $处的高能演化方程重写为偶极型算符组合，揭示了贝塞尔型解，并在双对数区域恢复Kirschner-Lipatov指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the relationship between the small-$x$ high-energy (dipole) framework and the conventional partonic picture based on light-ray operators is a fundamental challenge in QCD. While the eikonal approximation captures the leading behavior at small $x$, sub-eikonal corrections are necessary to connect with measurable parton distributions at finite $x_B$. The motivation is to establish a rigorous operator-level correspondence that unifies these two descriptions.

理解小-$x$高能（偶极子）框架与基于光射线算符的传统部分子图像之间的关系是QCD中的基本挑战。虽然前因子近似捕捉了小$x$下的主导行为，但需要次前因子修正以连接有限$ x_B $下的可观测部分子分布。动机在于建立统一这两种描述的严格算符级对应关系。

Method: The author analyzes the sub-eikonal expansion of the photon-nucleon scattering amplitude in the shockwave background, identifying the relevant light-ray operators at first sub-eikonal order. By integrating over phase space, the inclusive limit is taken to recover standard twist-2 parton distributions. Independently, the high-energy limit of the leading-twist non-local operator product expansion (OPE) is computed to confirm matching. For evolution at $x_B=0$, the renormalization group equations are rewritten in terms of bilocal dipole-type operators whose small-size behavior is manifest, and solutions are analyzed in both transverse-momentum and longitudinally-ordered regimes.

作者分析了冲击波背景下光子-核子散射振幅的次前因子展开，识别出首阶次前因子下的相关光射线算符。通过对相空间积分取兼容量子极限以恢复标准扭度-2部分子分布。独立地，计算了领头扭度非局域OPE的高能极限以确认匹配。对于$ x_B=0 $处的演化，重写重整化群方程为双局域偶极型算符形式，使其小尺寸行为显式呈现，并在横向动量和纵向排序区域分析解。

Result: At the differential level, the first sub-eikonal correction is governed by a quark transverse momentum dependent (TMD)-like light-ray operator. Upon full phase-space integration, this reconstructs the standard non-local quark and helicity distributions at finite $x_B$. This result is independently confirmed from the high-energy limit of the leading-twist non-local OPE. For evolution at $x_B=0$, rewriting in dipole-type bases makes the small-dipole power suppression and leading-log structure explicit. In the double-logarithmic approximation, Bessel-type solutions emerge when transverse phase space is independent; under longitudinal ordering, one recovers the energy logarithm and the Kirschner-Lipatov exponent with full $C_F$ color factor at finite $N_c$.

在微分层次上，首阶次前因子修正由类夸克TMD的光射线算符主导。经全相空间积分后，可重构有限$ x_B $下的标准非局域夸克与螺旋度分布。该结果亦由领头扭度非局域OPE的高能极限独立证实。在$ x_B=0 $处的演化中，使用偶极型基使小偶极子幂抑制和领头对数结构显式可见；在双对数近似下，当横向相空间独立时出现贝塞尔型解；在纵向排序下则恢复能量对数，并在对称双对数区以完整$ C_F $颜色因子恢复Kirschner-Lipatov指数。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a precise operator-level bridge between the shockwave (small-$x$) formalism and the non-local light-cone OPE, valid beyond the eikonal limit. The first sub-eikonal correction encodes TMD-like physics and reduces to inclusive parton distributions when integrated. The reformulation of evolution equations using dipole-type operators clarifies the all-order high-energy structure, especially in the double-logarithmic regime where it recovers known exponents with full color dependence. This provides a unified framework connecting high-energy QCD dynamics to standard collinear factorization.

本文建立了冲击波（小-$x$）形式与非局域光锥OPE之间精确的算符级桥梁，适用于超越前因子极限的情形。首阶次前因子修正编码了类TMD物理，并在积分后还原为兼容量子部分子分布。使用偶极型算符重写演化方程澄清了全阶高能结构，尤其在双对数区域恢复具有完整色因子依赖的已知指数。这为高能QCD动力学与标准共线因子化提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Relating the high-energy dipole description of deep-inelastic scattering to the standard light-ray operator formulation at finite Bjorken $x_B$ is essential for connecting the small-$x$ framework to the usual partonic description. I demonstrate that this connection already emerges at the first sub-eikonal order. At the differential level, the first sub-eikonal correction is governed by a quark TMD-like light-ray operator. In the inclusive limit, after complete phase-space integration, it reconstructs the standard nonlocal quark and helicity distributions at nonzero $x_B$. I then show independently that the same inclusive operator content follows from the high-energy limit of the leading-twist non-local operator product expansion, thereby establishing an explicit operator-level bridge between the shock-wave formalism and the non-local light-cone expansion.
  I further discuss the high-energy evolution of the corresponding operators at $x_B=0$. Rewriting the evolution equations in terms of dipole-type operator combinations, I identify an operator basis whose bilocal building blocks vanish in the zero-dipole-size limit, making the small-dipole behavior and the leading-logarithmic structure manifest. In the double-logarithmic approximation the evolution equations admit the usual mixed longitudinal-transverse Bessel-type solution when the transverse phase space is treated independently. When the transverse phase space is instead constrained by longitudinal ordering, the second logarithm is converted into a logarithm of energy, and in the symmetric double-logarithmic regime one recovers the fixed-coupling Kirschner-Lipatov exponent with the full finite-$N_c$ color factor $C_F$.

</details>


### [52] [A New Way to Detect Axions from $\rm{A\bar{Q}Ns}$ Captured in the Earth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29904)
*Ionel Lazanu,Konstantin Zioutas*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper discusses axion quark nuggets (AQNs) and axion antiquark nuggets (A$\bar{Q}$Ns) as macroscopic dark matter candidates that could simultaneously explain dark matter and the matter-antimatter asymmetry in the Universe. These dense, micron-sized composites consist of a quark core in a color-superconducting state, an electrosphere, and a stabilizing domain wall. If they exist, A$\bar{Q}$Ns may produce detectable axions, potentially observable in next-generation liquid noble gas neutrino detectors due to their large target volumes.

本文讨论了轴子夸克团（AQNs）和反轴子夸克团（A$\bar{Q}$Ns）作为宏观暗物质候选者，可能同时解释暗物质和宇宙中物质-反物质对称性破缺问题。这些高密度、微米尺度的复合体由色超导态夸克核心、电偶极层和维持稳定性的畴壁构成。若其存在，A$\bar{Q}$Ns产生的轴子可能在下一代液态惰性气体中微子实验中被探测到，得益于其实验装置的巨大活性体积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore non-WIMP dark matter candidates, specifically macroscopic composite systems like AQNs and A$\bar{Q}$Ns, which arise naturally in certain QCD and axion models. These objects could resolve two major puzzles: the nature of dark matter and the origin of matter-antimatter asymmetry, while also offering testable predictions for current experiments.

研究动机在于探索非WIMP类暗物质候选者，特别是如AQNs和A$\bar{Q}$Ns这类在QCD与轴子模型中自然出现的宏观复合系统。这些天体可能同时解决两大难题：暗物质的本质以及物质-反物质不对称性的起源，并为当前实验提供可检验的预测。

Method: Theoretical modeling of AQNs and A$\bar{Q}$Ns based on Witten's original idea of strange quark matter and Zhitnitsky's 2003 extension incorporating axion dynamics. The analysis focuses on the internal structure—color-superconducting quark core, electrosphere, and domain wall—and the resulting astrophysical signatures, particularly axion emission from A$\bar{Q}$Ns. Detection prospects are evaluated via interaction rates in liquid noble gas detectors (e.g., XENON, LZ, DARWIN), leveraging their large target masses and low thresholds.

基于Witten的奇异夸克物质构想及Zhitnitsky于2003年引入轴子动力学的扩展，对AQNs与A$\bar{Q}$Ns进行理论建模。分析聚焦于其内部结构——色超导夸克核心、电偶极层和畴壁，及其产生的天体物理信号，特别是A$\bar{Q}$Ns发射的轴子。通过评估液态惰性气体探测器（如XENON、LZ、DARWIN）中的相互作用率，利用其大靶质量和低阈值特性来研究探测前景。

Result: It is shown that axions produced by A$\bar{Q}$Ns could be detectable in upcoming liquid noble gas-based neutrino experiments due to their large active volumes and sensitivity to rare events. The predicted signal arises from axion conversion or scattering within the detector medium, providing a novel observational window for macroscopic dark matter.

研究表明，由于液态惰性气体中微子实验具有巨大的活性体积和对稀有事件的高灵敏度，A$\bar{Q}$Ns产生的轴子可能被下一代实验探测到。该信号源于轴子在探测介质中的转换或散射过程，为宏观暗物质提供了新的观测窗口。

Conclusion: Axion quark nuggets represent a compelling alternative to WIMP dark matter, capable of addressing both the dark matter puzzle and the matter-antimatter asymmetry. Their experimental signature—axion production from A$\bar{Q}$Ns—offers a promising detection channel in next-generation liquid noble gas experiments, transforming previously inaccessible theoretical constructs into falsifiable physics.

轴子夸克团是WIMP暗物质的一个极具吸引力的替代方案，能够同时解决暗物质之谜和物质-反物质对称性问题。其实验信号——来自A$\bar{Q}$Ns的轴子产生——为下一代液态惰性气体实验提供了有希望的探测途径，将原本不可触及的理论构想转化为可证伪的物理学内容。

Abstract: Macroscopic dark matter with dominating strong interactions, supposed to be composites, represents an alternative to the most popular WIMP particles. Predicted in various models as strangelets, nuclearites, nuggets, having different internal structures and properties, but not yet observed experimentally, these forms of dark matter are associated with the existence of a large number of still unexplained observations. Nuggets, initially predicted by Witten, were reconsidered from the point of view of their internal structure and further theorized in 2003 by Zhitnitsky as axion quark nuggets and axion antiquark nuggets, as being made of quarks in a superconducting colour state, in the core, an electrosphere of electrons or positrons and a domain wall that maintain the stability of the macros with an incredible density, mass in the gram range and radius on the order of micrometers. If the existence of $\rm{AQNs}$ and $\rm{A\bar{Q}Ns}$ is demonstrated, two major open problems in physics could be addressed simultaneously: they would constitute viable dark matter candidates and, at the same time, provide a natural mechanism for restoring matter-antimatter symmetry in the Universe. The experimental evidence of the $\rm{AQNs}$ and $\rm{A\bar{Q}Ns}$ is a challenge for current and future experiments. The present study demonstrates that if these macroscopic systems exist, axions produced by $\rm{A\bar{Q}N}$s could be detected by the next generation of neutrino physics experiments using liquid noble gases, due to their huge active volumes.

### [53] [Bargmann Invariants and Correlated Geometric CP-Violating Structures in Neutral Meson Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29976)
*Swarup Sangiri*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper constructs rephasing-invariant Bargmann invariants in neutral meson systems to study CP-violating interference effects geometrically. Third- and fourth-order cyclic phase invariants are derived from mixing and decay amplitudes, encoding nontrivial geometric phases tied to CP violation that vanish when CP is conserved. These invariants reveal quartic combinations of CKM elements analogous to the Jarlskog invariant and lead to a new rephasing-invariant ratio enhancing sensitivity to non-factorizable CP-violating correlations.

本文在中性介子系统中构建了重相不变的Bargmann不变量，以几何方式研究CP破坏干涉效应。通过混合参数和衰变振幅导出了三阶和四阶循环相位不变量，其编码的非平庸几何相位与CP破坏相关，在CP守恒时消失。这些不变量揭示了CKM矩阵元的四次组合，类似于Jarlskog不变量，并提出一个新的重相不变比值，可增强对不可分解的CP破坏关联结构的敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To provide a geometric, rephasing-invariant framework for understanding CP violation in neutral meson systems by leveraging Bargmann invariants, which capture interference between mixing and decay processes without dependence on arbitrary phase choices.

为理解中性介子系统中的CP破坏提供一个几何化且重相不变的框架，利用Bargmann不变量捕捉介子-反介子混合与衰变过程间的干涉，而不依赖于任意相位选择。

Method: Constructed cyclic Bargmann invariants of third and fourth order using heavy and light mass eigenstates and decay-projected states from correlated meson decays. Derived explicit expressions in terms of mixing parameters and decay amplitudes, and related them to CKM matrix elements and time-dependent CP asymmetry parameters.

利用中性介子相关衰变中的质量本征态和衰变投影态构造三阶和四阶循环Bargmann不变量。用混合参数和衰变振幅推导出显式表达式，并将其与CKM矩阵元和时间依赖的CP不对称参数关联起来。

Result: Explicit formulas for third- and fourth-order Bargmann invariants are obtained, showing that their geometric phases encode CP-sensitive interference between mixing and decay amplitudes. These phases vanish in the CP-conserving limit. The invariants contain quartic weak-phase structures analogous to the Jarlskog invariant. A new rephasing-invariant ratio of third- to fourth-order invariants isolates non-factorizable CP-violating correlations and enhances sensitivity to small CP violations.

得到了三阶和四阶Bargmann不变量的显式公式，表明其几何相位编码了对CP敏感的混合与衰变振幅干涉。这些相位在CP守恒极限下消失。不变量包含类似于Jarlskog不变量的四次弱相结构。提出一个新的三阶与四阶不变量之比，作为重相不变量，可分离不可分解的CP破坏关联，并增强对微小CP破坏的敏感性。

Conclusion: Bargmann invariants offer a powerful geometric language for CP violation in neutral meson systems, naturally incorporating rephasing invariance and revealing nontrivial interference structures beyond factorizable contributions. They connect fundamental CKM physics to observable time-dependent CP asymmetries through geometric phases, providing new tools for precision tests of CP symmetry.

Bargmann不变量为中性介子系统中的CP破坏提供了有力的几何语言，自然包含重相不变性，并揭示了超越可分解贡献的非平庸干涉结构。它们通过几何相位将基本的CKM物理与可观测的时间依赖CP不对称联系起来，为精确检验CP对称性提供了新工具。

Abstract: Bargmann invariants provide a rephasing-invariant description of phase relations among quantum states and offer a geometric perspective on interference phenomena. In this work, we investigate their role in neutral meson systems by constructing cyclic products involving the heavy and light mass eigenstates together with decay-projected states arising from correlated meson decays. Explicit expressions for third-order and fourth-order invariants are obtained in terms of mixing parameters and decay amplitudes. The analysis shows that the associated geometric phases encode CP-sensitive interference effects between meson-antimeson mixing and decay amplitudes and become trivial in the CP-conserving limit. Expressing the decay amplitudes in terms of CKM matrix elements reveals quartic combinations with analogous rephasing-invariant weak-phase structure to that of the Jarlskog invariant.
  We further introduce a rephasing-invariant ratio constructed from third- and fourth-order Bargmann invariants, which isolates correlated CP-violating structures that cannot, in general, be factorized into independent decay-channel contributions and can enhance sensitivity to small deviations from CP symmetry. The invariants can also be related to parameters governing time-dependent CP asymmetries in neutral meson decays, thereby providing a geometric interpretation of observable CP-violating interference effects.

### [54] [NNLO QCD corrections to unpolarized and polarized electroweak structure functions in semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.30012)
*Saurav Goyal,Sven-Olaf Moch,Vaibhav Pathak,V. Ravindran*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) QCD corrections for unpolarized and polarized semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering (SIDIS) mediated by electroweak gauge bosons are computed, including full flavor-dependent partonic contributions from both neutral and charged currents. The results significantly reduce theoretical scale uncertainties and enhance precision for future Electron-Ion Collider (EIC) physics.

下一代对撞机（EIC）物理的理论精度，计算了由电弱规范玻色子介导的非极化和极化半轻深度非弹性散射（SIDIS）的次次领头阶（NNLO）QCD修正，包括来自中性流和荷电流的完整味相关部分子贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering (SIDIS) is a key process for probing the internal structure of nucleons and extracting parton distribution functions (PDFs) and fragmentation functions (FFs). Achieving high theoretical precision requires perturbative quantum chromodynamics (pQCD) calculations beyond leading order. While next-to-leading order (NLO) computations have been standard, NNLO corrections are essential to match the projected experimental precision of the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC), reduce renormalization and factorization scale dependence, and minimize theoretical systematic uncertainties in global PDF/FF analyses.

半轻深度非弹性散射（SIDIS）是探测核子内部结构并提取部分子分布函数（PDFs）和碎裂函数（FFs）的关键过程。实现高理论精度需要超越领头阶的部分子量子色动力学（pQCD）计算。尽管次领头阶（NLO）计算已是标准，但次次领头阶（NNLO）修正对于匹配电子-离子对撞机（EIC）预期的实验精度、减少重整化和因子化尺度依赖性以及最小化全局PDF/FF分析中的理论系统误差至关重要。

Method: The calculation is performed within the framework of perturbative QCD at NNLO. All relevant structure functions for both unpolarized and polarized SIDIS are computed, considering electroweak interactions mediated by $\gamma^*$, $Z$, and $W^\pm$ bosons. Both neutral current (NC: $\gamma^*/Z$) and charged current (CC: $W^\pm$) channels are included. The computation incorporates all partonic subprocesses ($qg$, $qq$, $q\bar{q}$, etc.) with full dependence on quark flavors. Infrared singularities are handled using appropriate subtraction schemes (e.g., antenna subtraction or $q_T$-slicing), ensuring finite cross sections after mass factorization. The results are implemented in a numerical code for phenomenological studies.

该计算在次次领头阶（NNLO）的微扰QCD框架内进行。计算了非极化和极化SIDIS的所有相关结构函数，考虑了由$\gamma^*$、$Z$和$W^\pm$玻色子介导的电弱相互作用。包含了中性流（NC: $\gamma^*/Z$）和荷电流（CC: $W^\pm$）通道。计算结合了所有部分子子过程（$qg$、$qq$、$q\bar{q}$等），具有完整的夸克味依赖性。红外奇点通过适当的减法方案（如antenna减法或$q_T$-切片）处理，确保质量因子化后的截面有限。结果已实现在用于现象学研究的数值代码中。

Result: The NNLO corrections are found to be sizable across a range of kinematics accessible at the EIC, particularly for certain structure functions and asymmetries. The inclusion of NNLO terms leads to a significant reduction in the residual dependence on the renormalization and factorization scales—often by a factor of 2 or more—demonstrating improved perturbative convergence. This enhanced stability increases the reliability of theoretical predictions. Numerical results show that NNLO effects can shift NLO predictions by non-negligible amounts, which will impact extractions of PDFs and FFs in global analyses.

发现在EIC可及的运动学范围内，NNLO修正显著，尤其针对某些结构函数和不对称性。包含NNLO项显著减少了对重整化和因子化尺度的残余依赖性——通常减少两倍或更多——表明微扰收敛性改善。这种增强的稳定性提高了理论预测的可靠性。数值结果显示，NNLO效应会使NLO预测发生不可忽略的偏移，这将影响全局分析中PDF和FF的提取。

Conclusion: Complete NNLO QCD corrections for electroweak-mediated SIDIS processes, including both NC and CC channels with full flavor dependence, have been calculated. These results represent a major advancement in theoretical precision for nucleon structure studies. The reduced scale dependence and sizable NNLO effects underscore the necessity of including these corrections for accurate interpretation of data from the Electron-Ion Collider and for high-precision extractions of parton distribution and fragmentation functions in future global analyses.

已计算出包含完整味依赖性的电弱介导SIDIS过程（包括NC和CC通道）的完整NNLO QCD修正。这些结果代表了核子结构研究理论精度的重大进展。减少的尺度依赖性和显著的NNLO效应强调了在精确解释电子-离子对撞机数据以及未来全局分析中高精度提取部分子分布和碎裂函数时包含这些修正的必要性。

Abstract: We present results for unpolarized and polarized semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering mediated by electroweak gauge bosons at next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) in perturbative quantum chromodynamics. The results include all relevant structure functions arising from both neutral current (NC) and charged current (CC) interactions, incorporating contributions from all partonic channels with full flavor dependence. These corrections are crucial for improving the theoretical precision. A detailed numerical analysis of the NNLO corrections demonstrates their phenomenological importance, revealing sizable effects and a significant reduction in residual scale dependence in the kinematic range probed by the future Electron-Ion-Collider. These results will serve as a critical input for future global extractions of parton distributions functions and fragmentation functions.

### [55] [Role of the equivalence principle in gauge and axial symmetries of Yukawa coupling, and the strong CP problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.30024)
*Konstantin V. Grigorishin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The equivalence principle in gravity plays a fundamental role in the Yukawa coupling between scalar and fermion fields, prevents strong CP violation, and renders the axion hypothesis unnecessary.

等效原理在引力中对标量场与费米子场之间的汤川耦合起着根本作用，阻止了强CP破坏，使得轴子假设变得不必要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To investigate the role of the equivalence principle in gravity concerning Yukawa couplings and its implications for CP invariance and topological defect formation.

研究等效原理在引力中关于汤川耦合的作用及其对CP不变性和拓扑缺陷形成的含义。

Method: Analyzed the impact of the equivalence principle on scalar-fermion interactions and examined the conditions under which topological defects like vortices and monopoles form, particularly in systems with global gauge symmetry. Also studied the emergence of domain walls between different vacua and consequences for CP symmetry.

分析了等效原理对标量-费米子相互作用的影响，并检查了涡旋和磁单极等拓扑缺陷在仅具有全局规范对称性的系统中形成的条件。还研究了不同真空之间域壁的出现以及对CP对称性的影响。

Result: The Kibble-Zurek mechanism for topological defect formation breaks down in systems with only global gauge symmetry. Different vacua separated by domain walls can exist. The equivalence principle strongly suppresses CP violation, making the axion solution to the strong CP problem redundant.

在仅具有全局规范对称性的系统中，Kibble-Zurek机制对拓扑缺陷的形成失效。可能存在被域壁分隔的不同真空。等效原理强烈抑制CP破坏，使得为解决强CP问题而提出的轴子假设变得多余。

Conclusion: The equivalence principle not only governs gravitational interactions but also has profound implications for particle physics, particularly in forbidding strong CP violation and eliminating the need for axions as a solution.

等效原理不仅支配引力相互作用，而且对粒子物理有深远影响，特别是在禁止强CP破坏和消除对轴子作为解决方案的需求方面。

Abstract: It is demonstrated the fundamental role of the equivalence principle in gravity for the Yukawa coupling between scalar and fermion fields. The Kibble-Zurek mechanism for formation of topological defects as vortexes and monopoles breaks down in system with a global gauge symmetry only. At the same time, the different vacuums can occur, which are separated be domain walls. The equivalence principle makes the strong violation of CP invariance impossible. Thus the axion hypothesis becomes redundant.

### [56] [A Covariant Phase Space Approach to Einstein-AEther Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28851)
*Walter Arata,Stefano Liberati,Giulio Neri*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We derive a consistent first law of black hole thermodynamics in Einstein-AEther gravity by introducing a disformal frame for each mode with propagation speed $c_s$, showing that the entropy splits into gravitational and AEther contributions. This reconciles conflicting approaches to universal horizon thermodynamics in the probe limit $c_s \to +\infty$.

我们通过为传播速度为$c_s$的每种模式引入一个离散共形框架，在爱因斯坦-以太引力中推导出一致的黑洞热力学第一定律，表明熵可分为引力部分和以太部分。这在探针极限$c_s \to +\infty$下解决了普遍视界热力学中不同方法之间的冲突。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In Lorentz-violating theories like Einstein-AEther gravity, different modes propagate at different speeds, leading to multiple causal horizons and making black hole thermodynamics ambiguous. Previous attempts struggled to define a unified first law and resolve discrepancies in universal horizon thermodynamics, particularly between area-law entropy assumptions and Hawking temperature prescriptions.

在像爱因斯坦-以太引力这样的洛伦兹破缺理论中，不同模式以不同速度传播，导致多个因果视界，使黑洞热力学变得模糊。以往尝试难以定义统一的第一定律，并解决普遍视界热力学中的差异，特别是在面积律熵假设与霍金温度规定之间。

Method: We employ the covariant phase space formalism with boundaries and introduce a disformal frame for each mode of speed $c_s$, where its causal horizon becomes a Killing horizon, enabling a Wald-type derivation of the first law. The result is mapped back to the original frame. We also develop an extended thermodynamics framework allowing variation of couplings, yielding generalized Smarr relations. The probe limit $c_s \to +\infty$ is analyzed to connect with universal horizon thermodynamics.

我们采用带边界的协变相空间形式，并为每个速度为$c_s$的模式引入一个离散共形框架，使其因果视界成为克illing视界，从而实现Wald型第一定律的推导。然后将结果映射回原始框架。我们还开发了一个扩展热力学框架，允许耦合常数变化，得到广义Smarr关系。分析了探针极限$c_s \to +\infty$以联系普遍视界热力学。

Result: The first law takes the form $dE = \frac{\kappa}{8\pi} dA + \mu dQ + T dS_{\text{AEther}}$, where $S_{\text{AEther}}$ is an irreducible entropic contribution from the AEther field interpreted as heat due to AEther flux across the horizon. The total entropy splits as $S_{\text{total}} = S_{\text{grav}} + S_{\text{AEther}}$. Generalized Smarr relations are derived. In the limit $c_s \to +\infty$, our framework reconciles two previously conflicting prescriptions: (i) fixing entropy as proportional to area and deriving temperature, and (ii) imposing Hawking temperature and inferring entropy.

第一定律的形式为$dE = \frac{\kappa}{8\pi} dA + \mu dQ + T dS_{\text{AEther}}$，其中$S_{\text{AEther}}$是以太场的一个不可约熵贡献，可解释为由于以太穿过视界的通量而产生的热量。总熵分为$S_{\text{total}} = S_{\text{grav}} + S_{\text{AEther}}$。推导出了广义Smarr关系。在$c_s \to +\infty$极限下，我们的框架调和了两种先前冲突的方法：(i) 将熵固定为与面积成正比并推导温度；(ii) 施加霍金温度并推断熵。

Conclusion: Black hole thermodynamics in Lorentz-violating gravity requires accounting for additional horizon charges beyond geometry. The AEther contributes an intrinsic entropic term linked to its flux through the horizon, leading to a split entropy structure. This resolves long-standing tensions in universal horizon thermodynamics and establishes a robust framework via disformal mappings and covariant phase space methods.

在洛伦兹破缺引力中，黑洞热力学需要考虑超出几何之外的额外视界荷。以太通过其穿过视界的通量贡献了一个内在的熵项，导致熵的分裂结构。这解决了普遍视界热力学中长期存在的矛盾，并通过离散共形映射和协变相空间方法建立了稳健的框架。

Abstract: Black hole thermodynamics in Lorentz-violating gravity is subtle because different excitations propagate at different speeds and hence identify different causal horizons. We revisit Einstein--AEther gravity using the covariant phase space formalism with boundaries and derive a consistent first law for stationary black holes. For a mode of propagation speed $c_s$, we introduce a disformal frame in which the corresponding causal horizon is a Killing horizon, so that the standard Wald-type derivation can be carried out. The result is then mapped back to the original frame, where it mantains the same structure. The associated horizon charge contains, besides the usual Komar term, an irreducible entropic AEther contribution that can be interpreted as heat due to the AEther flux across the horizon; accordingly, the total entropy splits into a gravitational part and an AEther part. We further develop an extended-thermodynamics framework in which the couplings of the theory are allowed to vary, obtaining generalized Smarr relations. Finally, we analyze the probe-mode limit $c_s \to +\infty$, clarifying its connection to universal-horizon thermodynamics and resolving the apparent tension in the literature between approaches that (i) fix the entropy to be proportional to the area and infer a corresponding temperature, and (ii) impose the Hawking temperature associated with modes peeling from the universal horizon and infer the entropy. Once the independent AEther contribution is properly taken into account, the two prescriptions are reconciled.

</details>


### [57] [Charged scalar fields on Reissner--Nordström spacetimes II: late-time tails and instabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28861)
*Dejan Gajic*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper establishes the first pointwise decay estimates for charged scalar fields on near-extremal Reissner–Nordström black holes without assuming small charge, using physical-space energy methods under the assumption of global integrated energy decay. It shows inverse-power-law decay with oscillations at late times and proves asymptotic instabilities along future null infinity and the event horizon in the extremal case.

本文利用纯物理空间的能量方法，在不假设标量场电荷小的前提下，首次建立了近极值Reissner–Nordström黑洞背景下带电标量场的逐点衰减估计。在假设全局积分能量衰减成立的前提下，证明了带振荡的逆幂律长尾行为，并证明了辐射场在未来零无穷远以及极值情形下未来事件视界上的渐近不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the late-time behaviour and stability properties of charged scalar fields on black hole backgrounds is crucial for nonlinear studies in general relativity, particularly in the context of the Einstein–Maxwell–scalar field system. Previous results often relied on small-charge assumptions; this work removes that restriction to enable progress toward extremal and near-extremal regimes relevant for the strong cosmic censorship and black hole instability conjectures.

理解黑洞背景下带电标量场的晚期行为和稳定性对于广义相对论中的非线性研究至关重要，尤其是在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量场系统中。以往结果通常依赖于小电荷假设；本工作移除了这一限制，以推动与强宇宙审查假设和黑洞不稳定性猜想相关的极值和近极值情形的研究。

Method: The analysis is based entirely on physical-space energy estimates, avoiding Fourier-based techniques. The method assumes global integrated energy decay (proven in a companion paper [Gaj26]) and uses weighted energy norms, multiplier vector fields, and hierarchies of $r$-weighted estimates near null infinity and the horizon to derive precise pointwise decay rates for the charged scalar field $\phi$ satisfying $\Box_g \phi - i q F(\cdot, \nabla \phi) = 0$, where $q$ is the charge and $F$ the electromagnetic field.

分析完全基于物理空间的能量估计，避免使用傅里叶方法。该方法假设全局积分能量衰减（在伴生论文[Gaj26]中已证），并利用加权能量范数、乘子矢量场以及在零无穷远和视界附近的$r$加权估计层级，推导出满足$\Box_g \phi - i q F(\cdot, \nabla \phi) = 0$的带电标量场$\phi$的精确逐点衰减率，其中$q$为电荷，$F$为电磁场。

Result: The paper proves that solutions to the charged scalar wave equation exhibit oscillatory late-time tails with inverse-power-law decay rates. It provides the first pointwise decay estimates without small-charge assumptions. Furthermore, it establishes asymptotic instabilities of the radiation field along future null infinity $\mathcal{I}^+$ and, in the extremal case, along the future event horizon $\mathcal{H}^+$. These instabilities manifest as non-decaying or growing components in the transverse derivatives of the field.

本文证明了带电标量波方程的解表现出具有逆幂律衰减的振荡型晚期尾项。首次在无小电荷假设下给出了逐点衰减估计。此外，还证明了辐射场在未来零无穷远$\mathcal{I}^+$以及极值情形下在未来事件视界$\mathcal{H}^+$上的渐近不稳定性，这些不稳定性表现为场的横向导数中不衰减甚至增长的成分。

Conclusion: The energy-based physical-space framework developed here enables robust control over the late-time dynamics of charged scalar fields on near-extremal Reissner–Nordström spacetimes. The derived pointwise decay and oscillatory tails, together with the proven instabilities, provide essential foundations for future nonlinear studies, including spherically symmetric Einstein–Maxwell–charged scalar field models and possibly extremal Kerr settings.

本文发展的基于能量的物理空间框架，能够稳健地控制近极值Reissner–Nordström时空上带电标量场的晚期动力学行为。所导出的逐点衰减与振荡尾项，连同已被证明的不稳定性，为未来的非线性研究（包括球对称Einstein–Maxwell–charged scalar field模型乃至可能的极值Kerr时空）提供了重要基础。

Abstract: This is the second part of a series of papers deriving the precise, late-time behaviour and (in)stability properties of charged scalar fields on near-extremal Reissner--Nordström spacetimes via energy estimates. In this paper, we use purely physical-space based methods to establish the precise late-time behaviour of solutions to the charged scalar field equation in the form of oscillating and decaying late-time tails that satisfy inverse-power laws, assuming global integrated energy decay estimates, which are proved in the companion paper [Gaj26].
  This paper provides the first pointwise decay estimates for charged scalar fields on black hole backgrounds without an assumption of smallness of the scalar field charge.
  We also prove the existence of asymptotic instabilities for the radiation field along future null infinity and, in the extremal case, also along the future event horizon. Both the energy methods and the precise late-time asymptotics derived in this paper are expected to play an important role in future nonlinear studies of black hole dynamics in the context of the spherically symmetric (Einstein--)Maxwell--charged scalar field equations, as well as in the context of extremal Kerr spacetimes.

### [58] [The Depletion of Collisionless Dark Matter Spikes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28866)
*Charlie Sharpe,Yonadav Barry Ginat,Thomas F. M. Spieksma,Bence Kocsis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The classic Gondolo-Silk model predicts a steep dark matter (DM) density spike ($\rho \propto r^{-7/3}$) around massive black holes (MBHs), potentially detectable via gravitational-wave dephasings in EMRIs. However, this study shows that in realistic nuclear star clusters (NSCs), multi-mass stellar dynamics drive DM to a shallower $r^{-3/2}$ Bahcall-Wolf profile within $\lesssim 1\,\mathrm{Gyr}$ due to enhanced relaxation from mass segregation. Furthermore, post-Newtonian 3-body simulations reveal that EMRIs eject DM via slingshot interactions, irreversibly depleting the inner spike over several Gyrs. As two-body relaxation is inefficient and collisionless DM cannot refill the gap, detectable DM-induced dephasings for LISA may be suppressed, especially for MBHs below $10^5\text{--}10^6\,M_\odot$, significantly narrowing the parameter space for observable DM spikes.

经典的Gondolo-Silk模型预测在大质量黑洞（MBH）周围存在陡峭的暗物质（DM）密度尖峰（$\rho \propto r^{-7/3}$），可能通过EMRI中的引力波去相位效应被探测到。然而，本研究表明，在真实的核星团（NSC）中，多质量恒星动力学通过质量分层增强了弛豫效应，使DM在$\lesssim 1\,\mathrm{Gyr}$内形成更浅的$r^{-3/2}$ Bahcall-Wolf分布。此外，后牛顿三体模拟显示，EMRI通过弹弓相互作用将DM粒子抛射出去，在数十亿年内不可逆地耗尽内部尖峰。由于二体弛豫效率低下且无碰撞DM无法有效填补相空间空缺，LISA对质量低于$10^5\text{--}10^6\,M_\odot$的MBH可能难以探测到显著的DM去相位信号，大幅缩小了可观测DM尖峰的参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Gondolo-Silk model of adiabatic black hole growth predicts a steep $r^{-7/3}$ dark matter (DM) density spike around massive black holes (MBHs), which could induce detectable gravitational-wave dephasings in intermediate or extreme mass-ratio inspirals (IMRIs/EMRIs). However, this model assumes spherical symmetry, collisionless DM, and neglects the complex stellar environment of real nuclear star clusters (NSCs). The motivation of this work is to reassess the viability of such DM spikes in more realistic astrophysical settings, incorporating multi-mass stellar dynamics, two-body relaxation effects, and direct interactions between EMRIs and DM particles, to determine whether detectable DM signatures can persist over cosmological timescales.

Gondolo-Silk模型基于黑洞绝热增长预言了围绕大质量黑洞（MBH）的陡峭$r^{-7/3}$暗物质（DM）密度尖峰，可能在中等或极端质量比旋进（IMRI/EMRI）中产生可探测的引力波去相位效应。然而，该模型假设球对称性、无碰撞DM，并忽略了真实核星团（NSC）中复杂的恒星环境。本研究的动机是，在更真实的天体物理条件下重新评估此类DM尖峰的可行性，纳入多质量恒星动力学、二体弛豫效应以及EMRI与DM粒子之间的直接相互作用，以确定在宇宙时标上是否仍能维持可观测的DM特征信号。

Method: The authors employ a two-pronged approach: (1) 1D orbit-averaged Fokker-Planck (FP) simulations of isotropic nuclear star clusters (NSCs) with a multi-mass stellar population to model the long-term evolution of the dark matter (DM) distribution under two-body relaxation enhanced by mass segregation; (2) post-Newtonian 3-body simulations to capture strong, non-perturbative interactions between EMRIs and individual DM particles in the deep potential well near the MBH, where the FP formalism breaks down. These methods allow them to track both secular diffusion-driven relaxation and direct dynamical ejection (slingshot mechanism) of DM, assessing the stability and observability of DM spikes over gigayear timescales.

作者采用双管齐下的方法：(1) 使用包含多质量恒星群体的各向同性核星团（NSC）的一维轨道平均福克-普朗克（Fokker-Planck, FP）模拟，以建模在质量分层增强的二体弛豫下暗物质（DM）分布的长期演化；(2) 采用后牛顿三体模拟，捕捉在靠近MBH的强引力势阱中EMRI与单个DM粒子之间的强非微扰相互作用——这一区域FP形式论失效。这些方法使他们能够同时追踪由缓变扩散驱动的弛豫过程以及DM的直接动力学抛射（弹弓机制），从而评估DM尖峰在数十亿年时标上的稳定性与可观测性。

Result: The Fokker-Planck simulations show that mass segregation in multi-mass NSCs enhances stellar relaxation, driving the DM density profile from the predicted $r^{-7/3}$ spike to the shallower $r^{-3/2}$ Bahcall-Wolf equilibrium within $\lesssim 1\,\mathrm{Gyr}$. In the innermost regions, post-Newtonian 3-body simulations demonstrate that EMRIs dynamically eject DM particles via gravitational slingshots, leading to irreversible depletion of the central DM spike over several gigayears. This depletion is not replenished because two-body relaxation is too slow and collisionless DM cannot efficiently repopulate the cleared phase space. Consequently, DM densities are reduced by several orders of magnitude, suppressing gravitational-wave dephasings below LISA's detection threshold for MBHs with masses $\lesssim 10^5\,M_\odot$ at $z=3$, extending up to $\lesssim 10^6\,M_\odot$ for high EMRI rates ($\mathcal{O}(300\text{--}1000)\,\mathrm{Gyr}^{-1}$).

福克-普朗克模拟表明，多质量核星团（NSC）中的质量分层增强了恒星弛豫，使暗物质（DM）密度分布从预测的$r^{-7/3}$尖峰在$\lesssim 1\,\mathrm{Gyr}$内演化为更浅的$r^{-3/2}$ Bahcall-Wolf平衡态。在最内层区域，后牛顿三体模拟显示，EMRI通过引力弹弓机制将DM粒子动力学抛射出去，导致中心DM尖峰在数十亿年内发生不可逆耗尽。由于二体弛豫过慢且无碰撞DM无法有效填充被清空的相空间，这种耗尽无法得到补充。结果，DM密度下降数个数量级，使得对于红移$z=3$、质量$\lesssim 10^5\,M_\odot$的MBH（高EMRI率情况下可达$\lesssim 10^6\,M_\odot$），其引力波去相位效应低于LISA的探测阈值。

Conclusion: The combination of enhanced two-body relaxation due to mass segregation in realistic NSCs and irreversible DM ejection by EMRIs via slingshot interactions strongly suppresses the formation and persistence of steep DM spikes around MBHs. As a result, the parameter space for detectable DM-induced gravitational-wave dephasings in EMRIs—particularly for lower-mass MBHs—is dramatically reduced. This challenges the standard assumption of persistent $r^{-7/3}$ spikes and implies that LISA observations may not easily reveal clean DM signatures unless specific conditions (e.g., very low EMRI rates or recent MBH formation) are met.

由于真实核星团（NSC）中质量分层导致的增强二体弛豫，以及EMRI通过弹弓相互作用对DM的不可逆抛射，共同强烈抑制了MBH周围陡峭DM尖峰的形成与维持。因此，EMRI中可探测的DM诱导引力波去相位效应的参数空间——尤其是对较低质量MBH——被大幅压缩。这挑战了$r^{-7/3}$尖峰长期存在的标准假设，意味着除非满足特定条件（如极低EMRI率或MBH近期形成），否则LISA观测可能难以揭示清晰的DM特征信号。

Abstract: Dense concentrations of dark matter (DM) surrounding black holes provide a compelling opportunity to probe the nature of DM. In the classic Gondolo-Silk model, the adiabatic growth of a massive black hole (MBH) in a DM cusp produces a steep density spike ($ρ\propto r^{-7/3}$), potentially inducing measurable gravitational-wave dephasings in intermediate and extreme mass-ratio inspirals (IMRIs/EMRIs). We challenge this paradigm by considering a collisionless spike embedded in a realistic nuclear star cluster (NSC). Using 1D orbit-averaged Fokker-Planck (FP) simulations of isotropic NSCs, we show that mass segregation in a multi-mass stellar cusp accelerates relaxation, relative to single-mass models, thereby driving the DM to the lower density $r^{-3/2}$ Bahcall-Wolf profile within $\lesssim 1 \mathrm{Gyr}$. In the inner regions, where the FP description breaks down, we model strong triple interactions between DM particles and EMRIs using post-Newtonian 3-body simulations. We show that EMRIs eject DM particles via slingshots, depleting the inner spike over a few Gyrs. Because EMRI number densities are too low to drive two-body relaxation, and collisionless DM cannot efficiently repopulate the depleted phase space, this depletion is irreversible. While the extent of EMRI-induced depletion depends on the EMRI rate and mass, we find reductions in DM densities by several orders of magnitude. Hence, DM-induced dephasings for EMRIs may fall below the detectability threshold of LISA for MBHs at $z = 3$ (2.14 Gyr) with masses $\lesssim 10^{5}\,M_\odot$ (for an $\mathcal{O}(10) \, \mathrm{Gyr}^{-1}$ EMRI rate), extending to $\lesssim 10^6\,M_\odot$ for more optimistic rates of $\mathcal{O}(300-1000) \, \mathrm{Gyr}^{-1}$. Our findings substantially reduce the parameter space over which MBHs can host detectable collisionless DM spikes.

### [59] [Charged scalar fields on Reissner--Nordström spacetimes I: integrated energy estimates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28874)
*Dejan Gajic*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper establishes global, weighted integrated energy decay and boundedness estimates for charged scalar fields on near-extremal Reissner--Nordström spacetimes, extending to non-extremal cases under mode stability assumptions. It is the first part of a series providing a global quantitative analysis of charged scalar fields on asymptotically flat black holes without small charge assumptions, addressing challenges analogous to those in extremal Kerr for neutral waves.

本文建立了近极值Reissner--Nordström时空上带电标量场的全局加权积分能量衰减与有界性估计，并在实轴模式稳定的假设下推广至非极值情形。作为系列论文的第一部分，它首次在无小电荷假设的渐近平坦黑洞背景下对带电标量场方程进行了全局定量分析，触及了类似于极值Kerr时空中中性波方程所面临的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The dynamics of charged scalar fields on black hole backgrounds are poorly understood compared to neutral fields, especially in the near-extremal regime where red-shift degeneracy and superradiance coexist. Understanding their late-time behaviour is crucial for probing the stability of charged black holes and serves as a model for more complex systems like extremal Kerr. This work aims to rigorously derive energy estimates that capture this interplay without relying on smallness assumptions for the field's charge.

相较于中性场，带电标量场在黑洞背景下的动力学仍缺乏理解，尤其是在红移效应退化与超辐射共存的近极值区域。理解其晚期行为对于探测带电黑洞的稳定性至关重要，并可为更复杂的系统（如极值Kerr）提供模型参考。本研究旨在严格推导能够刻画这种相互作用的能量估计，且不依赖于场电荷的小量假设。

Method: The authors employ a vector field method using carefully constructed multipliers and commutators adapted to the geometry of (near-)extremal Reissner--Nordström spacetimes. They derive degenerate and non-degenerate energy estimates, incorporating red-shift effects and handling superradiance through frequency-localized analysis and bootstrap arguments. The analysis includes both asymptotically flat and de Sitter variants, with extension to sub-extremal cases contingent on the assumption of real-axis mode stability.

作者采用向量场方法，构造了适应于（近）极值Reissner--Nordström时空几何的乘子与对易子。他们推导了退化与非退化的能量估计，结合红移效应，并通过频率局域化分析与自举论证处理超辐射问题。分析涵盖了渐近平坦与de Sitter两种情形，对次极值情况的推广则依赖于实轴模式稳定的假设。

Result: Global, weighted integrated energy decay and energy boundedness estimates are proven for solutions to the charged scalar field equation on near-extremal Reissner--Nordström(--de Sitter) spacetimes. These results extend to non-extremal Reissner--Nordström black holes assuming mode stability on the real axis. The estimates reveal a coupling between red-shift degeneration and superradiance, mirroring key difficulties in the analysis of the wave equation on extremal Kerr.

证明了近极值Reissner--Nordström(--de Sitter)时空中带电标量场方程解的全局加权积分能量衰减与能量有界性估计。在实轴模式稳定的假设下，这些结果可推广至非极值Reissner--Nordström黑洞。估计揭示了红移退化与超辐射之间的耦合，反映了极值Kerr时空中波动方程分析中的关键难点。

Conclusion: This work provides the first rigorous global energy estimates for charged scalar fields on near-extremal black holes without small charge restrictions. It lays the foundation for a complete understanding of late-time tails and (in)stability in such settings, and highlights deep structural parallels between charged scalar fields on Reissner--Nordström and neutral fields on extremal Kerr spacetimes.

本工作首次在无小电荷限制下，为近极值黑洞上的带电标量场提供了严格的全局能量估计。它为完全理解此类背景下的晚期尾部行为与（非）稳定性奠定了基础，并揭示了Reissner--Nordström上带电标量场与极值Kerr时空中中性场之间深刻的结构类比。

Abstract: This is the first part of a series of papers deriving the precise, late-time behaviour and (in)stability properties of charged scalar fields on near-extremal Reissner--Nordström spacetimes via energy estimates. In this paper, we establish global, weighted integrated energy decay and energy boundedness estimates for solutions to the charged scalar field equation on (near-)extremal Reissner--Nordström(--de Sitter) spacetimes. These estimates extend to Reissner--Nordström spacetimes away from extremality under the assumption of mode stability on the real axis.
  Together with the companion paper [Gaj26], this paper forms the first global quantitative analysis of the charged scalar field equation on asymptotically flat black hole spacetimes, without a smallness assumption on the scalar field charge. Due to a coupling of the degeneration of the red-shift effect with the presence of superradiance at the linearized level, charged scalar fields on Reissner--Nordström spacetimes also probe some of the main difficulties encountered when studying the (neutral) wave equation on extremal Kerr spacetimes.

### [60] [Spin the black circle II: tidal heating and torquing of a rotating black hole by a test mass on generic orbits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28982)
*Rossella Gamba,Danilo Chiaramello,Estuti Shukla,Simone Albanesi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents a numerical study of energy and angular momentum fluxes at the horizon of a Kerr black hole due to a test particle on equatorial geodesics, including circular, eccentric, and hyperbolic orbits. The study reveals complex flux behavior such as multiple peaks and sign changes, indicative of transitions between superradiant and non-superradiant regimes. A factorized and resummed analytical model is proposed, accurately predicting the onset of superradiance within 10% for over 73% of configurations, while existing post-Newtonian models show large errors (~100%) in the strong-field regime.

本文对克尔黑洞视界上的能量和角动量通量进行了数值研究，考虑了测试粒子在赤道面上的圆轨道、椭圆轨道和双曲线轨道。研究揭示了通量的复杂行为，如多峰结构和符号变化，表明存在超辐射与非超辐射区域之间的转换。作者提出了一种因子化和重求和的解析模型，能够在超过73%的构型中以10%以内的精度预测超辐射起始频率。然而，现有的后牛顿模型在强场区域误差可达~100%，显示出改进通量表达式的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Horizon fluxes are crucial for understanding black hole dynamics and probing their fundamental properties, especially in strong gravitational fields. While well-studied for circular orbits, less is known about eccentric and hyperbolic trajectories, which are increasingly relevant for extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) and unbound encounters in astrophysical environments. The motivation is to extend the understanding of horizon fluxes beyond circular motion and assess the validity and accuracy of current analytical approximations, particularly in the strong-field regime where numerical relativity is computationally expensive.

视界通量对于理解黑洞动力学及其基本性质至关重要，尤其是在强引力场中。尽管圆轨道情形已被广泛研究，但关于椭圆和双曲线轨道的知识仍较缺乏，而这些轨道在极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）和天体物理环境中的无界相遇事件中日益重要。本研究旨在将视界通量的理解从圆轨道推广到更一般的轨道，并评估当前解析近似方法的有效性和精度，特别是在数值相对论计算代价高昂的强场区域。

Method: The authors perform a numerical calculation of the horizon fluxes of energy and angular momentum for a test particle moving along equatorial geodesics around a Kerr black hole. They solve the Teukolsky equation using semi-analytical and numerical methods to compute the gravitational perturbations and extract the horizon fluxes. Various orbital types — circular, eccentric, and hyperbolic — are considered across a broad range of orbital parameters (e.g., semi-latus rectum, eccentricity) and black hole spins. These numerical results are compared with post-Newtonian (PN) analytical expressions, and a new factorized and resummed analytical representation is proposed to improve agreement, especially near the superradiant threshold.

作者通过数值方法计算测试粒子沿克尔黑洞赤道测地线运动时的视界能量和角动量通量。他们利用半解析与数值方法求解Teukolsky方程，计算引力扰动并提取视界通量。研究涵盖了广泛的轨道参数（如半通径、偏心率）和黑洞自旋下的圆轨道、椭圆轨道和双曲线轨道。然后将这些数值结果与后牛顿（PN）解析表达式进行比较，并提出一种新的因子化与重求和的解析表示形式，以改善特别是在超辐射阈值附近的吻合度。

Result: Numerical results confirm known flux behaviors for circular orbits and reveal new features for eccentric and hyperbolic orbits: instantaneous fluxes can display multiple peaks and sign reversals, signaling transitions between superradiant and non-superradiant emission. The proposed factorized and resummed analytical model predicts the onset frequency of superradiance to within $10\%$ for $\gtrsim 73\%$ of configurations, outperforming standard PN expansions. This model exactly recovers the circular-orbit limit regardless of the perturbative order. For orbit-averaged and peak fluxes, analytical models achieve $\lesssim 10\%$ relative errors at large separations and low eccentricities, but exhibit $\sim \mathcal{O}(100\%)$ deviations in the strong-field regime.

数值结果重现了圆轨道已知的通量行为，并揭示了椭圆和双曲线轨道的新特征：瞬时通量可呈现多个峰值和符号反转，标志着超辐射与非超辐射发射之间的转换。所提出的因子化与重求和模型能在$\gtrsim 73\%$的构型中以$10\%$以内精度预测超辐射起始频率，优于标准后牛顿展开。该模型无论微扰阶数如何，均能精确还原圆轨道极限。对于轨道平均和峰值通量，解析模型在大分离距离和低偏心率下相对误差$\lesssim 10\%$，但在强场区域偏差可达$\sim \mathcal{O}(100\%)$。

Conclusion: The study highlights the complexity of horizon fluxes in generic orbits around Kerr black holes, going beyond the simpler circular case. It demonstrates that superradiant effects can intermittently turn on and off during eccentric or unbound motion, leading to rich temporal structure in the fluxes. The proposed factorized and resummed analytical framework significantly improves predictions for the onset of superradiance and provides a promising direction for modeling fluxes in EMRI systems. However, significant discrepancies in the strong-field regime indicate the need for further refinement of analytical models using numerical data.

本研究表明，在克尔黑洞周围一般轨道上的视界通量具有超越简单圆轨道情形的复杂性。它证明在椭圆或无界运动过程中，超辐射效应可能间歇性开启和关闭，导致通量出现丰富的时间结构。所提出的因子化与重求和解析框架显著提升了对超辐射起始的预测能力，为极端质量比旋进（EMRI）系统的通量建模提供了有前景的方向。然而，强场区域的显著差异表明，仍需结合数值数据进一步优化解析模型。

Abstract: Horizon fluxes of energy and angular momentum are a key strong-field effect in the dynamics of black holes, encoding direct information about their nature. In this work, we present a numerical study of these fluxes for a test particle orbiting a Kerr black hole on equatorial geodesics, covering circular, eccentric, and hyperbolic trajectories across a wide range of orbital parameters and black hole spins. We reproduce known results for circular orbits and uncover a richer phenomenology for eccentric and hyperbolic ones: the instantaneous fluxes can exhibit multiple peaks and sign changes, indicating a complex interplay between superradiant and non-superradiant regimes. We then compare these results against existing analytical post-Newtonian expressions, exploring resummation strategies to improve their performance against numerical data. In particular, we propose a factorized and resummed representation of the horizon fluxes that predicts the onset frequency of the superradiant regime to within $10\%$ for $\gtrsim 73\%$ of configurations for both the energy and angular momentum fluxes. This representation exactly reduces to the circular limit by construction, independently of the perturbative order of the remaining analytical terms. For peak and orbit-averaged fluxes, the analytical models achieve acceptable accuracy -- with relative errors at the $10\%$ level or below -- at large separations and low eccentricities. However, they can exhibit deviations of $\sim \mathcal{O}(100\%)$ in the strong-field regime, motivating the need for improved flux prescriptions and further investigations.

### [61] [No hair but plenty of feathers: are birds black holes?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29064)
*Andrew Laeuger,Taylor Knapp*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper humorously explores a linguistic coincidence between the bird 'chirp' and gravitational wave 'chirps,' suggesting—satirically—that bird vocalizations, particularly the Northern cardinal's, can be modeled using compact binary merger waveforms, with tongue-in-cheek implications for extreme physics and cosmology.

本文以幽默方式探讨了鸟类‘鸣叫’（chirp）与引力波‘啁啾信号’（chirp）之间的语言巧合，讽刺性地提出可以用致密双星并合的波形来建模某些鸟类（如北卡罗莱纳雀）的叫声，并半开玩笑地暗示其可能关联极端物态或超出标准模型的物理现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivated by the shared use of the word "chirp" in ornithology and gravitational wave astronomy, the authors explore whether this linguistic overlap can inspire a playful, satirical analogy between bird vocalizations and GW signals from compact binaries.

受到‘chirp’一词在鸟类学与引力波天文学中共同使用的启发，作者探索这一语言重叠是否能激发一种戏谑性的类比：将鸟类叫声与致密双星产生的引力波信号相联系。

Method: The authors analyze the time-reversed audio waveform of the Northern cardinal's chirp and compare it qualitatively to theoretical gravitational wave templates of high mass ratio, precessing black hole binaries, noting similarities and anomalies reminiscent of detector glitches or exotic physics.

作者分析了北卡罗莱纳雀鸣叫的时间反演音频波形，并将其与高质比、进动黑洞双星的理论引力波模板进行定性比较，指出其相似性以及类似探测器异常或新物理的现象。

Result: The time-reversed chirp of the Northern cardinal shows a superficial resemblance to GW chirp signals from extreme-mass-ratio mergers, with features suggesting unphysical parameter values or beyond-Standard-Model effects; other bird species' chirps resemble data glitches in GW detectors rather than astrophysical signals.

北卡罗莱纳雀时间反演后的鸣叫在表面上类似于极端质量比并合事件的引力波啁啾信号，其特征暗示非物理的参数值或超出标准模型的效应；其他鸟类的鸣叫则更像引力波探测器中的数据伪迹而非天体物理信号。

Conclusion: While no real physical connection exists, the pun-based analogy highlights the importance of waveform morphology in both bioacoustics and gravitational wave astronomy. The paper concludes with a satirical proposal that the Big Bang, not the chicken or egg, came first.

尽管不存在真实的物理联系，但基于双关语的类比突显了波形形态在生物声学与引力波天文学中的重要性。论文最后以讽刺方式提出：宇宙大爆炸才是‘先于鸡与蛋’的真正起源。

Abstract: The imitative verb "chirp" is thought to originate from 16th-century Middle English. Meanwhile, this same word has been used to describe the gravitational waves (GWs) emitted from the merger of compact objects, such as black holes and neutron stars, since at least the 1990s. Motivated purely by this linguistic overlap, we study whether the chirps of birds can be modeled by compact binary waveforms. In particular, we consider a test case of the Northern cardinal (Cardinalis cardinalis), finding that its time-reversed chirp can be approximately modeled by that of a high mass ratio, precessing black hole binary, with a number of indications towards extreme matter effects or beyond the Standard Model physics. Importantly, this waveform correspondence is not so straightforward for all bird species, as some chirp morphologies are far more akin to glitches seen in GW observatories. With these comparisons made, we propose an alternative solution to the longstanding philosophical conundrum: rather than the chicken or the egg, perhaps it was the Big Bang which truly came first.

### [62] [Photon emission from the ISCO of a rotating black hole in Asymptotic Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29156)
*Miguel A. Enrí quez,Luis A. Sánchez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We investigate photon escape probability (PEP) and maximum observable blueshift (MOB) from the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) of a rotating black hole in asymptotic safety (AS), finding that quantum gravity effects enhance PEP and MOB for high-spin black holes despite reducing ISCO radius.

我们研究了渐近安全（AS）中旋转黑洞内最稳定圆轨道（ISCO）的光子逃逸概率（PEP）和最大可观测蓝移（MOB），发现尽管量子引力效应减小了ISCO半径，但对于高自旋黑洞，PEP和MOB反而增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand how quantum gravity effects in asymptotic safety modify observable signatures near the ISCO of rotating black holes, particularly photon escape properties and blueshifts, which are key probes of strong-gravity regimes.

旨在理解渐近安全中的量子引力效应如何改变旋转黑洞ISCO附近可观测特征，特别是光子逃逸特性和蓝移，这些是强引力区域的关键探针。

Method: We compute the photon escape probability (PEP) and maximum observable blueshift (MOB) for emissions from the ISCO of a subextremal Kerr-like black hole in asymptotic safety, using an effective metric that incorporates quantum corrections via a running Newton constant $G(r)$. The ISCO radius is determined by solving the geodesic equations with modified orbital stability conditions due to quantum effects. These results are compared with classical Kerr predictions.

我们基于渐近安全中带有量子修正的有效度规（通过运行的牛顿常数$G(r)$实现），计算次极值Kerr型黑洞ISCO发射的光子逃逸概率（PEP）和最大可观测蓝移（MOB）。ISCO半径通过求解受量子效应影响的测地线方程及轨道稳定性条件得到，并与经典Kerr结果进行比较。

Result: Quantum gravity effects in AS reduce the ISCO radius, as expected. However, for black holes with high spin, increasing the quantum parameter toward its critical value leads to increased PEP and MOB, contrary to naive expectations. This indicates that quantum effects become dominant over classical background geometry at the ISCO scale. We also identify correlations between these enhancements and deformations in the black hole shadow boundary.

AS中的量子引力效应如预期般减小了ISCO半径。然而，对于高自旋黑洞，当量子参数趋近其临界值时，PEP和MOB反而增加，违背直觉预期。这表明在ISCO尺度上，量子效应已主导经典背景几何。我们还发现了这些增强现象与黑洞阴影边界的形变之间的关联。

Conclusion: The increase in PEP and MOB with stronger quantum effects reveals a nontrivial interplay between quantum gravity and strong-field gravitational dynamics near high-spin black holes. These results demonstrate that observables related to photon emission from the ISCO can serve as sensitive probes of quantum gravity in asymptotic safety, even when classical and quantum geometries predict similar structural changes like smaller ISCO radii.

PEP和MOB随量子效应增强而上升，揭示了量子引力与高自旋黑洞附近强场动力学之间的非平庸相互作用。结果表明，即使经典与量子几何预测类似结构变化（如更小的ISCO半径），ISCO光子发射相关可观测量仍可作为渐近安全中量子引力的敏感探针。

Abstract: We study the isotropic emission of photons from the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) of a subextremal rotating black hole (BH) in asymptotic safety (AS). We calculate both the photon escape probability (PEP) and the maximum observable blueshift (MOB) of photons to reach infinity, and compare with the corresponding results for photon emission from the ISCO of a classical Kerr BH. In AS, quantum gravity effects reduce the radius of the ISCO, therefore quantum gravity effects should reduce the PEP and MOB of photons from emitters moving on the ISCO. We show that this is not the case and that, when rotating BHs with high spin are considered and the quantum parameter (which encodes the quantum gravity effects) increases towards its critical value, which is different for different spin values, the PEP and MOB also increase despite the reduction in ISCO radius. Our results on the PEP show explicitly how quantum gravity effects start to dominate over the classical background at the level of the ISCO. We also discuss the relation between these quantum gravity modifications and particular features of the shadow of a rotating BH in AS.
