### [63] [Testing classical-quantum gravity with geodesic deviation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29230)
*Tomoya Hirotani,Akira Matsumura*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates the phenomenological implications of a novel semiclassical gravity model proposed by Oppenheim et al., focusing on quantum fluctuations in geodesic deviation induced by coupling to a classical gravitational field. The authors derive the strain spectrum from these fluctuations and demonstrate that the original model is testable with current gravitational-wave detectors. They also propose two modified models: one consistent with the Einstein equations and another incorporating environment-induced noise, comparing their predictions with the original model and perturbative quantum gravity.

本文研究了Oppenheim等人提出的新型半经典引力模型的现象学影响，重点关注由量子系统与经典引力场耦合引起的测地线偏离的量子涨落。作者推导出相应的应变谱，并证明当前引力波探测器足以检验原始模型。此外，他们构建了两个改进模型：一个显式满足爱因斯坦方程的修正模型，以及一个包含环境诱导噪声的经典-量子模型，并将其预测与原始模型和微扰量子引力进行比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Oppenheim et al. model introduces a new framework for gravity as a classical entity interacting with quantum matter via stochastic fluctuations, potentially offering a path toward quantum gravity without quantizing spacetime. However, its consistency with general relativity and observational viability remain unclear. This work aims to assess whether the model produces observable signatures—specifically in geodesic deviation—and whether it can be distinguished from alternative formulations and established theories like perturbative quantum gravity.

Oppenheim等人的模型引入了一种新框架，将引力视为通过随机涨落与量子物质相互作用的经典实体，可能为不需对时空进行量子化的量子引力理论提供路径。然而，该模型与广义相对论的一致性及其可观测性尚不清楚。本研究旨在评估该模型是否在测地线偏离中产生可观测信号，以及能否将其与其它理论形式（如微扰量子引力）区分开来。

Method: The authors analyze quantum fluctuations of geodesic deviation within the original Oppenheim et al. model using a semiclassical approach where the gravitational field remains classical but couples stochastically to quantum matter. They derive the strain power spectrum analytically by solving the stochastic geodesic deviation equation. Two extensions are constructed: (1) a modified version ensuring manifest conservation of the stress-energy tensor and compliance with the Einstein equation, and (2) a model including environmental decoherence effects through additional noise terms. Predictions for strain spectra from all three models are compared with each other and with those from perturbative quantum gravity.

作者采用半经典方法分析原始Oppenheim等人模型中的测地线偏离量子涨落，其中引力场保持经典但以随机方式与量子物质耦合。通过求解随机测地线偏离方程，解析推导出应变功率谱。他们构建了两个扩展模型：(1) 一种修正版本，确保能动张量守恒且显式满足爱因斯坦方程；(2) 引入环境退相干效应并通过额外噪声项建模。所有三个模型的应变谱预测结果相互比较，并与微扰量子引力的结果对比。

Result: The original Oppenheim et al. model predicts a strain spectrum $S_h(f)$ that scales as $f^{-5}$ at low frequencies, which lies within the sensitivity range of current gravitational-wave observatories such as LIGO and LISA. The modified model preserving the Einstein equation yields a suppressed spectrum due to additional constraints, while the environment-induced noise model produces enhanced fluctuations depending on the noise parameters. These differences allow observational discrimination between the models.

原始Oppenheim等人模型预测的应变谱$S_h(f)$在低频段按$f^{-5}$标度变化，落在当前引力波观测设备（如LIGO和LISA）的灵敏度范围内。保持爱因斯坦方程成立的修正模型由于附加约束导致谱幅抑制；而环境诱导噪声模型则根据噪声参数增强涨落。这些差异使得可通过观测区分不同模型。

Conclusion: The study shows that the original Oppenheim et al. model is falsifiable with existing technology, marking an important step toward experimental tests of semiclassical gravity. The proposed modifications improve theoretical consistency or incorporate realistic decoherence, yielding distinct observational signatures. Together, these results highlight the potential of gravitational-wave astronomy to probe foundational aspects of quantum gravity and the quantum-classical interface.

研究表明，原始Oppenheim等人模型可通过现有技术进行证伪，标志着向实验检验半经典引力迈出了重要一步。所提出的修正模型提升了理论自洽性或引入了更真实的退相干机制，产生不同的可观测特征。这些结果共同凸显了引力波天文学在探索量子引力基础问题及量子-经典界面方面的潜力。

Abstract: A novel semiclassical gravity model proposed by Oppenheim et al., that consistently describes interactions between quantum systems and a classical gravitational field, has recently attracted considerable attention. However, the limitations and phenomenological viability of this model have not yet been thoroughly investigated. In this work, based on the model, we study quantum fluctuations of geodesic deviation coupled with a classical gravitational field. We analytically derive the strain spectrum expected from the fluctuations and show that the original Oppenheim et al. model can be tested with the current observational sensitivity of gravitational-wave experiments. Furthermore, motivated by the novel semiclassical model, we construct two additional models: a modified Oppenheim et al. model that is manifestly consistent with Einstein equation, and a classical-quantum model with environment-induced noise. We analyze the strain spectra predicted by these two models through comparison with those of the original Oppenheim et al. model and perturbative quantum gravity.

### [64] [Quantum Einsteinian Cubic Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29304)
*Nephtalí Eliceo Martínez Pérez,Cupatitzio Ramírez Romero*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We study the minisuperspace quantization of Cosmological Einsteinian Cubic Gravity (CECG), a higher-curvature modification of general relativity that maintains second-order Friedmann equations. Using canonical transformations and Dirac's constraint formalism, we construct the Wheeler-DeWitt equation, finding exact solutions in the flat case and WKB approximations for closed and inflationary models.

我们研究宇宙学爱因斯坦三次引力（CECG）的极小超空间量子化，这是一种保持弗里德曼方程二阶性的高曲率修正引力理论。通过正则变换和狄拉克约束形式，构造了惠勒-德维特方程，在平直情况下获得精确解，并在闭合与暴胀模型中得到WKB近似解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cosmological Einsteinian Cubic Gravity (CECG) offers a novel extension of General Relativity with cubic curvature terms that modify early-universe dynamics without introducing additional propagating degrees of freedom or losing second-order field equations. The motivation is to explore quantum cosmological effects in this theory, particularly how higher-curvature corrections influence the Wheeler-DeWitt equation and wave function of the universe.

宇宙学爱因斯坦三次引力（CECG）通过三次曲率项为广义相对论提供了新的扩展，能在不引入额外传播自由度或破坏二阶场方程的前提下修改早期宇宙动力学。本文旨在探索该理论中的量子宇宙学效应，特别是高曲率修正如何影响惠勒-德维特方程和宇宙波函数。

Method: We derive the Hamiltonian formulation of FRW cosmology in CECG using Ostrogradski's method and apply Dirac's algorithm for constrained systems. Due to the fifth-degree polynomial dependence of the momentum $p_a$ on $\dot{a}$, we perform canonical transformations $(a,p_a)\to(A,P)$ to obtain an explicit Hamiltonian constraint. We then carry out Wheeler-DeWitt quantization, solving the resulting higher-derivative quantum equation exactly for $k=0$ and via WKB approximation for $k=1$ and in the presence of an inflaton field $\phi$.

我们使用奥斯特罗格拉茨基方法推导CECG中FRW宇宙学的哈密顿形式，并应用狄拉克约束系统算法。由于动量$p_a$对$\dot{a}$呈五次多项式依赖，我们实施正则变换$(a,p_a)\to(A,P)$以获得显式的哈密顿约束。随后进行惠勒-德维特量子化，对$k=0$情形精确求解所得高阶导数量子方程，并对$k=1$及含暴胀场$\phi$的情形采用WKB近似求解。

Result: The non-standard kinetic structure leads to a higher-derivative Wheeler-DeWitt equation. For spatially flat universes ($k=0$), we find exact analytical solutions to the quantum equation. For spatially closed universes ($k=1$), we obtain WKB-type approximate solutions. In the presence of a scalar inflaton field $\phi$ with an inflationary potential, the WKB wave functions exhibit strong correlations between configuration variables and their conjugate momenta, suggesting semiclassical suppression of singularities.

非标准动能结构导致高阶导数的惠勒-德维特方程。对于空间平坦宇宙（$k=0$），我们找到了量子方程的精确解析解；对于空间闭合宇宙（$k=1$），获得了WKB型近似解。当存在具有暴胀势的标量暴胀场$\phi$时，WKB波函数表现出构型变量与其共轭动量之间的强关联，暗示奇点可能被半经典机制抑制。

Conclusion: CECG admits a consistent minisuperspace quantization despite its higher-curvature origin. The resulting quantum framework yields exact and semiclassical solutions that reflect the modified gravitational dynamics. These results extend the application of the Cosmological Bootstrap approach to higher-derivative gravity and suggest that cubic curvature terms can influence the early universe's quantum behavior while avoiding ghosts and maintaining second-order classical equations.

尽管CECG源于高曲率项，仍可实现一致的极小超空间量子化。所得到的量子框架产生了反映修正引力动力学的精确与半经典解。这些结果将宇宙学自举（Cosmological Bootstrap）方法的应用扩展到高阶导数引力，并表明三次曲率项可在避免鬼态且保持经典二阶方程的同时影响早期宇宙的量子行为。

Abstract: We study Cosmological Einsteinian Cubic Gravity (CECG) arXiv:1810.08166v3 in the context of minisuperspace quantum cosmology. CECG is a modification of Einstein's gravity by cubic curvature terms that yield a nontrivial contribution to the dynamics of FRW backgrounds while keeping the Friedmann equations at second order. First, we study the Hamiltonian formulation of the effective one-dimensional FRW CECG action using Ostrogradski's canonical variables and Dirac's algorithm for constrained systems. Since the momentum $p_a$ conjugate to the scale factor is a polynomial of degree five in $\dot{a}$, we implement canonical transformations $(a,p_a)\to (A,P)$ that enable us to write the Hamiltonian constraint explicitly. Second, we perform the Wheeler-DeWitt quantization using the new canonical variables. Although FRW CECG has no extra degree of freedom besides the scale factor, its non-standard Hamiltonian yields a higher-derivative Wheeler-DeWitt equation. We obtain exact solutions for the spatially flat case, and WKB-type solutions for the spatially closed case. Finally, we consider a homogeneous scalar field $φ$ with inflationary potential and obtain WKB wave functions leading to strong correlations between coordinates and momenta.

### [65] [Revisiting the Coprecessing Frame in the Presence of Orbital Eccentricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29307)
*Lucy M. Thomas,Katerina Chatziioannou,Sam Johar,Taylor Knapp,Michael Boyle*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The coprecessing frame transformation, commonly used in gravitational waveform modeling to simplify precession effects, is evaluated for eccentric and precessing compact binaries using numerical relativity simulations. While it reduces waveform mismatches and aids surrogate modeling by removing dominant modulations, it does not fully decouple precession from eccentricity, leaving mismatches above the accuracy threshold ($\sim 0.01$) for large inclinations.

共动进动参考系变换是引力波形建模中用于简化进动效应的常用方法，本文利用数值相对论模拟评估了其在偏心且进动的致密双星系统中的表现。尽管该方法降低了波形失配并有助于代理模型构建，但未能完全解耦进动与轨道偏心的影响，在大倾角情况下波形失配仍高于精度阈值（$\sim 0.01$）。



<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Accurate waveform models for compact binaries must include both spin precession and orbital eccentricity, yet current methods based on the coprecessing frame may not adequately separate these effects, especially when both are significant. This work aims to assess whether the coprecessing frame remains effective in such regimes using high-fidelity numerical relativity data.

致密双星系统的精确波形模型必须同时包含自旋进动和轨道偏心效应，而当前基于共动进动参考系的方法可能无法充分分离这些效应，尤其是在两者均显著的情况下。本研究旨在利用高保真度的数值相对论数据评估该参考系在此类极端情况下的有效性。


Method: We analyze 20 numerical relativity simulations that fully incorporate spin precession and eccentricity in the strong-field regime. Waveforms are compared in both the inertial and coprecessing frames, with mismatches evaluated against the eccentric, spin-aligned SEOBNRv5EHM model. The performance of the coprecessing frame in reducing amplitude and phase modulations is assessed, along with its utility in constructing reduced-order surrogate models.

我们分析了20个数值相对论模拟，这些模拟在强场区域完整包含了自旋进动和轨道偏心效应。在惯性系和共动进动参考系中对波形进行比较，并以偏心自旋对齐模型SEOBNRv5EHM为基准计算波形失配。评估了共动进动参考系在降低振幅和相位调制方面的表现及其在构建降阶代理模型中的实用性。


Result: Waveform mismatches decrease in the coprecessing frame relative to the inertial frame but remain above $\sim 0.01$, particularly at large inclinations, indicating incomplete decoupling of precession and eccentricity effects. However, the coprecessing frame effectively removes dominant amplitude and phase modulations, enabling more efficient surrogate modeling with lower errors for a fixed number of basis elements.

相较于惯性系，共动进动参考系中的波形失配有所降低，但仍高于$\sim 0.01$，特别是在大倾角情况下，表明进动与偏心效应未被完全解耦。然而，该参考系能有效去除主要的振幅和相位调制，使得在固定基元数量下代理模型误差更低，建模更高效。


Conclusion: The coprecessing frame remains a valuable tool in waveform modeling for precessing and eccentric binaries, particularly for reducing waveform complexity and aiding surrogate construction. However, its inability to fully isolate precession from eccentricity highlights the need for further improvements, such as modeling mode asymmetries, to achieve the required accuracy for next-generation gravitational wave detectors.

共动进动参考系仍是建模进动且偏心双星系统波形的有力工具，尤其在降低波形复杂性和辅助代理模型构建方面具有优势。然而，其无法完全将进动从偏心中分离出来，凸显了进一步改进的必要性，例如引入模式非对称性建模，以满足下一代引力波探测器所需的精度要求。


Abstract: Accurate inclusion of both spin precession and orbital eccentricity effects in gravitational waveform models represents a key hurdle in our ability to fully characterize the properties of compact binaries. Virtually all efforts to model precession rely on a coprecessing frame transformation, a time-dependent spatial rotation that tracks the dominant emission direction and simplifies the waveform morphology. We assess the utility of the coprecessing frame transformation to separate out the effect of the precession of the orbital plane from the waveform in the presence of non-negligible orbital eccentricity. We rely on 20 numerical relativity simulations, which include the complete physical effects of spin precession and eccentricity in the strong-field, and compare waveforms in both the inertial and coprecessing frames. Comparing against the eccentric, spin-aligned model SEOBNRv5EHM, we find that while the waveform mismatches decrease in the coprecessing frame, they remain above the level required for accurate waveform modeling, $\sim$ 0.01 or higher for large inclinations. Further improvements, e.g., modeling mode asymmetries as already pursued for quasicircular binaries, will likely prove essential. We also find that by removing the dominant amplitude and phase modulations from the waveform, the coprecessing frame facilitates surrogate modeling, achieving lower errors at a fixed number of basis elements compared to the inertial frame. Our results demonstrate both the utility and the limitations of the coprecessing frame as a cornerstone in waveform modeling for eccentric and precessing binaries.

</details>


### [66] [Extracting Energy from Magnetized Rotating Black Holes in Horndeski Gravity via the Magnetic Penrose Process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29319)
*Ke Wang,Xiao-Xiong Zeng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We study energy extraction from rotating black holes in Horndeski gravity via the Magnetic Penrose Process, analyzing how efficiency depends on the scalar hair parameter $h$, magnetic field strength $B$, and particle decay radius $r_x$. The results reveal rich dependence of efficiency on these parameters, especially non-trivial behavior when $\hat{q} B < 0$.

我们通过磁彭罗斯过程研究了在Horndeski引力中从旋转黑洞提取能量的问题，分析了效率如何依赖于标量毛参数$h$、磁场强度$B$和粒子衰变半径$r_x$。结果揭示了效率对这些参数的丰富依赖关系，特别是当$\hat{q} B < 0$时的非平凡行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The investigation aims to understand how scalar hair in Horndeski gravity modifies energy extraction mechanisms from rotating black holes, particularly through the Magnetic Penrose Process, and how this differs from general relativity predictions.

该研究旨在理解Horndeski引力中的标量毛如何改变从旋转黑洞提取能量的机制，特别是通过磁彭罗斯过程，并探究其与广义相对论预测的区别。

Method: We map the ergosphere and regions of negative energy in the spacetime of a rotating black hole in Horndeski gravity with a uniform magnetic field. We perform theoretical analysis combined with numerical simulations to compute energy extraction efficiency as a function of the hair parameter $h$, charge-to-mass ratio $\hat{q}$, magnetic field $B$, and decay radius $r_x$.

我们在具有均匀磁场的Horndeski引力旋转黑洞时空中绘制了能层和负能量区域，结合理论分析与数值模拟，计算了能量提取效率作为毛参数$h$、荷质比$\hat{q}$、磁场$B$和衰变半径$r_x$的函数。

Result: Larger hair parameter $h$ reduces the size of the ergosphere and negative energy regions. For $\hat{q} B \geq 0$: if $r_x > 2$, efficiency decreases with $h$; if $r_x < 2$, efficiency increases with $h$; if $r_x = 2$, efficiency is independent of $h$. For $\hat{q} B < 0$, efficiency dependence on $h$ is more complex, showing either monotonic decrease or non-monotonic (increase-then-decrease) behavior depending on $r_x$ and $\hat{q}B$. Without magnetic field, efficiency is negative and unphysical for $r_x > 2$. When $\hat{q} B \geq 0$, larger $h$ leads to lower maximum efficiency. When $\hat{q} B < 0$ and $B$ is large, hairy black holes can achieve positive high efficiency at large $r_x$, while Kerr black holes yield negative efficiency.

较大的毛参数$h$会减小能层和负能区的范围。当$\hat{q} B \geq 0$时：若$r_x > 2$，效率随$h$增大而减小；若$r_x < 2$，效率随$h$增大而增大；若$r_x = 2$，效率与$h$无关。当$\hat{q} B < 0$时，效率对$h$的依赖更复杂，根据$r_x$和$\hat{q}B$的不同，可能单调递减或先增后减。无磁场时，当$r_x > 2$，效率为负且无物理意义。当$\hat{q} B \geq 0$，$h$越大，最大效率越低。当$\hat{q} B < 0$且$B$较大时，带毛黑洞在大$r_x$处可实现正的高效率，而Kerr黑洞的效率仍为负。

Conclusion: Scalar hair in Horndeski gravity significantly influences energy extraction efficiency via the Magnetic Penrose Process. The sign and magnitude of $\hat{q}B$ play crucial roles in determining the dependence of efficiency on $h$, with novel regimes where hairy black holes outperform Kerr black holes in energy extraction, especially under strong magnetic fields.

Horndeski引力中的标量毛通过磁彭罗斯过程显著影响能量提取效率。$\hat{q}B$的符号和大小在决定效率对$h$的依赖关系中起关键作用，在强磁场下尤其存在带毛黑洞优于Kerr黑洞的新机制。

Abstract: In Horndeski gravity, we investigate how to extract energy from a rotating black hole immersed in a uniform magnetic field $B$ based on the Magnetic Penrose Process. We map the ergosphere and negative energy regions of this spacetime, and analyze the relationship between the energy extraction efficiency and the hair parameter through both theoretical analysis and numerical simulations. The results show that the larger the hair parameter $h$, the smaller the ergosphere and negative energy regions of the black hole. For the same decay radius, in the case of $\hat{q} B \geq 0$, if the decay radius $r_x > 2$, the efficiency decreases as $h$ increases; if $r_x < 2$, the efficiency increases as $h$ increases; if $r_x = 2$, the efficiency is independent of $h$. However, when $\hat{q}B < 0$, except for the special case $r_x = 2$ where the efficiency is independent of $h$, the variation of efficiency with $h$ depends on the specific values of $r_x$ and $\hat{q}B$, and may exhibit either monotonic decrease or an initial increase followed by a decrease. We also find that in the absence of a magnetic field, the efficiency is negative and meaningless when $r_x > 2$, and such cases are excluded. In addition, when $\hat{q} B \geq 0$, the larger the $h$, the lower the maximum efficiency; when $\hat{q} B < 0$, in the case of a small magnetic field, the efficiency is negative and meaningless, while in the case of a large magnetic field, the efficiency of the black hole with hair is positive at high decay radius and reaches a high value, whereas the efficiency of the Kerr black hole remains negative.

</details>


### [67] [Mexican Burrowing Toads as gravitational wave detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29334)
*Frederic V. Hessman,Christian Jooss*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We propose that the Mexican Burrowing Toad may detect gravitational waves via magnetoreception and internal Raman-amplified phonon-magnon signals in ferromagnetic neural structures, inspired by the similarity between their calls and neutron star/black hole merger waveforms. Despite no detection in recordings, we suggest large-scale toad deployment as a low-cost supplement to LIGO/VIRGO.

我们提出，墨西哥穴居蟾蜍可能通过神经系统中铁磁物质内的声子-磁振子信号与拉曼放大机制感知引力波，其叫声与中子星/黑洞并合的引力波信号相似。尽管录音中未发现信号，但我们建议大规模使用这类蟾蜍作为LIGO/VIRGO光学干涉仪的低成本补充手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gravitational wave detection is currently limited to highly expensive facilities like LIGO and VIRGO. We explore a biologically inspired, low-cost alternative by investigating whether certain amphibians, specifically the Mexican Burrowing Toad, might naturally detect spacetime strains due to unique neuro-magnetic sensitivities.

引力波探测目前局限于LIGO和VIRGO等高成本设施。我们探索一种受生物启发的低成本替代方案，研究某些两栖动物（特别是墨西哥穴居蟾蜍）是否因其独特的神经-磁敏感性而天然具备感知时空应变的能力。

Method: We compare the acoustic waveform of Mexican Burrowing Toad calls to templates of gravitational wave signals from compact binary coalescences. We hypothesize a detection mechanism involving ferromagnetic material in the toad's nervous system converting gravitational strain into magnons and phonons, amplified via a Raman laser process. We analyze synchronized vocalizations from a pond population for phase anomalies indicative of passing gravitational waves.

我们将墨西哥穴居蟾蜍叫声的声学波形与致密双星并合的引力波模板进行比较。我们假设其神经系统中的铁磁材料可将引力应变转换为磁振子和声子，并通过拉曼激光过程放大。我们分析池塘种群同步鸣叫中可能由引力波引起的相位异常。

Result: No statistically significant phase shifts were detected in the toad calls during the observation period. No corresponding gravitational wave event was reported by LIGO/VIRGO, consistent with our null result. The hypothesized amplification mechanism remains speculative but theoretically intriguing.

在观测期间，蟾蜍叫声中未检测到显著的相位偏移。LIGO/VIRGO也未报告相应的引力波事件，与我们的零结果一致。所假设的放大机制仍属推测，但理论上有一定吸引力。

Conclusion: While we find no evidence that Mexican Burrowing Toads detect gravitational waves, the conceptual framework—linking biological magnetoreception, coherent quantum excitations (magnons, phonons), and nonlinear amplification—opens a novel interdisciplinary direction at the intersection of general relativity, condensed matter physics, and sensory biology. We propose further study of such systems as potential bio-hybrid detectors.

尽管我们未发现墨西哥穴居蟾蜍能探测引力波的证据，但这一概念框架——结合生物磁感应、相干量子激发（磁振子、声子）与非线性放大——开辟了广义相对论、凝聚态物理与感觉生物学交叉的新方向。我们提议进一步研究此类系统作为潜在的生物-混合探测器的可能性。

Abstract: It is generally assumed that gravitational waves are extremely difficult to detect. However, we show that the call of the Mexican Burrowing Toad has an amazing resemblance to cosmic gravitational wave signals due to the merging of neutron stars and/or black holes. It is known that toads exhibit magnetoreception - the ability to detect magnetic fields - and that magnetic fields thus subtly affect ion channel activities in toad neurons. We speculate that gravitational strains produce phonons and magnons in a ferromagnetic substance embedded in the nervous system of the toads and that these coherent signals are exponentially amplified by a Raman laser mechanism to the point where they can be detected. The fine tuning necessary for this mechanism to work would help to explain why this species of toad show this remarkable ability and others do not. We analyze the sound of a pond full of Mexican Burrowing Toads in the hopes of detecting slight phase shifts in their calls due to a gravitational wave event. No effect was found and the the LIGO/VIRGO consortia have not reported an event during the recording, illustrating the power of this approach. We suggest the massive use of these toads would be an inexpensive way to support the operation of optical interferometric gravitational wave detector facilities.

### [68] [Phase space analysis in $f(R,L_{m})$ gravity with scalar field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29337)
*Y. Kalpana Devi,Rahul Bhagat,B. Mishra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies the cosmological dynamics of $f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$ gravity with a scalar field, using dynamical system analysis to identify critical points and their stability via center manifold theory. The model includes linear and exponential dependence on the matter Lagrangian and is extended by a generalized scalar field with exponential potential. Results show matter-dominated and accelerated phases, a transition from deceleration to acceleration, and late-time de Sitter-like behavior, offering a viable alternative to dark energy without a cosmological constant.

本文研究了含标量场的$f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$引力模型的宇宙学动力学，通过动力系统分析方法引入无量纲变量构建自治系统，利用中心流形理论分析非双曲临界点的稳定性。模型包含物质拉格朗日量的线性和指数依赖，并进一步引入具有动能项和指数自相互作用势的广义标量场。结果表明模型可实现物质主导和加速膨胀阶段，以及从减速到加速的转变，晚期趋向于类德西特相，为无需宇宙学常数的暗能量提供了可行替代机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The observed late-time cosmic acceleration remains unexplained within general relativity without invoking dark energy or a cosmological constant. This motivates the exploration of modified gravity theories such as $f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$ gravity, where the gravitational action depends on both the Ricci scalar $R$ and the matter Lagrangian $\mathcal{L}_m$, potentially encoding additional geometric-matter couplings. Including a scalar field may further enrich the dynamics and provide stable late-time solutions consistent with observations.

观测到的晚期宇宙加速膨胀在广义相对论框架下无法解释，除非引入暗能量或宇宙学常数。这促使人们探索如$f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$引力等修改引力理论，其中引力作用量同时依赖于里奇标量$R$和物质拉格朗日量$\mathcal{L}_m$，可能蕴含额外的几何-物质耦合。引入标量场可进一步丰富动力学行为，并提供与观测一致的稳定晚期解。

Method: The authors employ dynamical system analysis by defining dimensionless variables to transform the cosmological equations into an autonomous system. Critical points are identified as fixed points of this system, and their stability is analyzed using linear perturbation and center manifold theory due to non-hyperbolicity. The model is first studied in its pure $f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$ form with linear and exponential dependence on $\mathcal{L}_m$, then extended by adding a minimally coupled scalar field with kinetic term and exponential potential. Cosmological parameters such as the deceleration parameter $q$ and effective equation of state $w_{\rm eff}$ are derived from the solutions.

作者通过定义无量纲变量将宇宙学方程转化为自治系统，采用动力系统分析方法。临界点被识别为该系统的不动点，由于其非双曲性，使用线性微扰和中心流形理论分析其稳定性。模型首先以纯$f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$形式研究，包含对$\mathcal{L}_m$的线性和指数依赖，然后通过添加最小耦合的具有动能项和指数势的标量场进行扩展。宇宙学参数如减速度参数$q$和有效状态方程$w_{\rm eff}$由解导出。

Result: Several critical points are found corresponding to matter-dominated, radiation-dominated, and accelerated expansion phases. A physically viable trajectory shows a transition from a decelerated to an accelerated universe. Due to non-hyperbolic nature, center manifold analysis confirms the stability of late-time solutions. With the scalar field extension, stable late-time attractors emerge, and the effective equation of state $w_{\rm eff} \rightarrow -1$, while the deceleration parameter $q \rightarrow -1$, indicating a de Sitter-like late-time evolution. Energy conditions and phase space structure are also examined.

发现多个对应于物质主导、辐射主导和加速膨胀相的临界点。存在一条物理上可行的轨迹，显示从减速到加速宇宙的转变。由于非双曲性，中心流形分析确认了晚期解的稳定性。在标量场扩展下，出现稳定的晚期吸引子，有效状态方程$w_{\rm eff} \rightarrow -1$，减速度参数$q \rightarrow -1$，表明晚期趋向类德西特演化。同时检验了能量条件和相空间结构。

Conclusion: The $f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$ gravity framework with scalar field extensions provides a consistent and viable alternative to $\Lambda$CDM for explaining late-time cosmic acceleration. The model naturally realizes a transition from matter domination to accelerated expansion and admits stable de Sitter-like attractors at late times, without requiring a cosmological constant. This highlights the potential of generalized matter-geometry coupling in modified gravity as a mechanism for dark energy.

含标量场扩展的$f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$引力框架为解释晚期宇宙加速提供了一种一致且可行的$\Lambda$CDM替代方案。该模型自然实现了从物质主导到加速膨胀的过渡，并在晚期存在稳定的类德西特吸引子，无需引入宇宙学常数。这凸显了修改引力中广义物质-几何耦合作为暗能源机制的潜力。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the cosmological dynamics of the $f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$ gravity framework with a particular focus on the contributions of the scalar field. Considering a functional form that includes linear and exponential dependence on the matter Lagrangian, we perform a detailed dynamical system analysis by introducing appropriate dimensionless variables and constructing the corresponding autonomous system. The critical points are obtained and analyzed, and due to their non-hyperbolic nature, center manifold theory is employed to determine their stability. The analysis reveals the existence of matter-dominated and accelerated phases of the Universe, along with a transition from a decelerated to an accelerated expansion. We further extend the model by incorporating a minimally coupled generalized scalar field with a kinetic term and an exponential self-interacting potential, which enriches the dynamical behavior and leads to stable late-time attractor solutions. The evolution of cosmological parameters, including the deceleration parameter and the effective equation of state, indicates that the model approaches a de Sitter-like phase at late times. These results demonstrate that the $f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$ gravity framework, with scalar field extensions, provides a viable mechanism to explain the late-time acceleration of the Universe without invoking a cosmological constant.

### [69] [Gravitational waves from gaps of neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29514)
*Akira Dohi,Asuka Ito,Shota Kisaka*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The pulsar magnetosphere, particularly the outer gap region, may emit detectable continuous gravitational waves due to rapid electromagnetic energy variations; the estimated strain is $\sim2\times10^{-24}$, within reach of future detectors like the Einstein Telescope.

脉冲星磁层（特别是外间隙区域）可能由于快速的电磁能量变化发射可探测的连续引力波；估计的应变约为$\sim2\times10^{-24}$，在爱因斯坦望远镜等未来探测器的探测范围之内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To investigate whether pulsar magnetospheres can produce detectable continuous gravitational waves (GWs), especially through time-varying electric-field energy densities from charge-discharge processes, and to reassess previous claims about GW emission from polar cap regions.

旨在研究脉冲星磁层是否能通过电荷-放电过程引起时变电场能量密度从而产生可探测的连续引力波，并重新评估此前关于极帽区域引力波辐射的结论。

Method: We model gravitational wave emission from different magnetospheric gap regions (polar cap and outer gap), incorporating relativistic effects and the dynamics of electromagnetic energy variation. The strain amplitude is calculated using general relativity, taking into account the quadrupole formula and time-dependent electric field contributions.

我们对磁层中不同间隙区域（极帽和外间隙）的引力波辐射进行建模，纳入相对论效应和电磁能量变化的动力学。利用广义相对论中的四极公式并考虑时变电场的贡献来计算应变振幅。

Result: The gravitational wave strain from the polar cap region is found to be too small, contradicting earlier studies. In contrast, the outer gap produces a strain of $\sim2\times10^{-24}$, which is within the sensitivity range of next-generation detectors such as the Einstein Telescope.

极帽区域产生的引力波应变过小，与早期研究结果相矛盾。相比之下，外间隙区域产生的应变为$\sim2\times10^{-24}$，处于下一代探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜）的灵敏度范围内。

Conclusion: The outer gap in the pulsar magnetosphere is a promising source of continuous gravitational waves, offering a new window to probe magnetospheric physics via future GW observations.

脉冲星磁层中的外间隙是连续引力波的一个有希望的来源，为通过未来的引力波观测探索磁层物理提供了新窗口。

Abstract: The pulsar magnetosphere is a potential source of continuous gravitational waves due to the rapid charge-discharge process in short timescale, varying the electric-field energy density. We estimate the strain of the continuous gravitational waves, considering relativistic effects and different gap regions. We find that the strain from the polar cap is too small, in contrast to previous results. On the other hand, the strain from the outer gap is as large as $\sim2\times10^{-24}$, enough for future gravitational-wave detection such as the Einstein Telescope. Our result presents a new approach for the future detection of gravitational waves to probe the physics in the magnetosphere.

### [70] [Towards Gravitational Wave Turbulence within the Hadad-Zakharov metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29699)
*Benoît Gay,Eugeny Babichev,Sébastien Galtier,Karim Noui*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates gravitational wave turbulence in general relativity using the Hadad-Zakharov (HZ) metric, analyzing the compatibility of the Einstein equations in the weakly nonlinear regime. Analytical results are supported by numerical simulations with the GPU-based TIGER code, showing the emergence of dual energy and wave action cascades, a Kolmogorov-Zakharov spectrum, and intermittent coherent structures. Despite challenges in satisfying all Einstein equations numerically, key signatures of wave turbulence—such as monofractal scaling in gauge-invariant metric components—are observed.

本文在广义相对论框架下，利用Hadad-Zakharov (HZ) 度规研究引力波湍流，分析弱非线性 regime 中爱因斯坦方程的相容性。通过基于GPU的新代码TIGER进行数值模拟，结果支持解析结论，显示出能量与波作用的双重级联、Kolmogorov-Zakharov谱以及间歇性相干结构。尽管在数值上精确满足所有爱因斯坦方程存在困难，但规范不变度规分量展现出波湍流典型的单分形标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gravitational wave turbulence remains poorly understood within full general relativity, particularly regarding the consistency of approximate metrics like the HZ ansatz under the exact Einstein equations. The compatibility of the seven Einstein equations for the four HZ metric functions has not been systematically addressed, despite being crucial for the physical validity of any turbulent solution. This work aims to fill this gap by investigating whether a consistent weakly nonlinear regime exists and whether genuine turbulent dynamics emerge.

引力波湍流在完整广义相对论中的行为仍不清楚，特别是像HZ度规这样的近似解是否能满足精确的爱因斯坦方程。对于HZ度规中四个函数需满足七个爱因斯坦方程的相容性问题，此前未被系统研究，尽管这对解的物理有效性至关重要。本工作旨在填补这一空白，探究是否存在一致的弱非线性 regime 并激发出真实的湍流动力学。

Method: We employ the Hadad-Zakharov (HZ) diagonal metric ansatz, governed by four scalar functions subject to seven (six independent) Einstein equations. Compatibility conditions are analyzed analytically in the weakly nonlinear regime. Numerical simulations are performed using TIGER, a new GPU-accelerated code solving the evolution equations for the metric components. We monitor the Ricci and Kretschmann scalars to assess constraint violation and physical degrees of freedom. Spectral analysis is used to identify energy and wave action cascades, including the Kolmogorov-Zakharov spectrum. Statistical properties are studied via structure functions and probability distributions of canonical variables and metric components.

我们采用Hadad-Zakharov (HZ) 对角度规试探解，其由四个标量函数构成，并受七个（六个独立）爱因斯坦方程约束。在弱非线性 regime 下对相容性条件进行解析分析。使用TIGER——一种新型基于GPU加速的代码——求解度规分量的演化方程。通过监控Ricci和Kretschmann标量来评估约束违反程度及物理自由度的存在。利用谱分析识别能量与波作用的级联现象，包括Kolmogorov-Zakharov谱。通过结构函数和正则变量与度规分量的概率分布研究统计特性。

Result: We find that the Einstein equations can be compatible in the weakly nonlinear regime under specific conditions, supporting the validity of the HZ ansatz. Numerical simulations show that gravitational wave turbulence corresponds to the propagation of a real physical degree of freedom, as indicated by the behavior of the Ricci and Kretschmann scalars. A dual cascade of energy and wave action is observed, with the latter exhibiting the Kolmogorov-Zakharov spectrum $I_\omega \sim \omega^{-3/2}$. Canonical variables tend toward nearly Gaussian statistics interspersed with intermittent coherent structures, while gauge-invariant metric components display monofractal scaling—a hallmark of classical wave turbulence.

我们发现，在特定条件下，爱因斯坦方程在弱非线性 regime 下可以相容，从而支持HZ试探解的有效性。数值模拟显示，引力波湍流对应真实物理自由度的传播，这由Ricci和Kretschmann标量的行为所表明。观察到能量与波作用的双重级联，后者呈现出Kolmogorov-Zakharov谱 $I_\omega \sim \omega^{-3/2}$。正则变量趋向于近高斯统计，其间穿插间歇性相干结构，而规范不变度规分量表现出单分形标度行为——这是经典波湍流的标志性特征。

Conclusion: Our analysis demonstrates that gravitational wave turbulence can be consistently described within general relativity using the HZ metric in the weakly nonlinear regime, provided compatibility conditions are met. The emergence of dual cascades, the Kolmogorov-Zakharov spectrum, and monofractal scaling confirms the applicability of wave turbulence theory to gravity. However, precise enforcement of all Einstein constraints remains a numerical challenge. Future work should focus on improving numerical accuracy and exploring strong-field regimes where deviations from classical turbulence may occur.

我们的分析表明，只要满足相容性条件，利用HZ度规可在弱非线性 regime 下一致地描述广义相对论中的引力波湍流。双重级联、Kolmogorov-Zakharov谱和单分形标度的出现证实了波湍流理论在引力中的适用性。然而，精确满足所有爱因斯坦约束仍是数值上的挑战。未来的工作应集中在提高数值精度，并探索强场 regime，其中可能出现偏离经典湍流的行为。

Abstract: The theory of gravitational wave turbulence describes the long-term statistical behaviour of a set of weakly nonlinear interacting waves. In this paper, we aim to study aspects of gravitational turbulence within the framework of general relativity using the Hadad-Zakharov (HZ) metric. The latter is parameterised by four functions (the coefficients of a diagonal metric) that must satisfy seven non-trivial Einstein equations, six of which are independent. The issue of their mutual compatibility is therefore essential, yet it has so far been overlooked. In this work, we argue that these equations can be compatible in the weakly nonlinear regime under specific conditions. Our analytical investigation is complemented by direct numerical simulations performed with a new GPU-based code, TIGER. A comparative analysis of the evolution of the Ricci and Kretschmann scalars indicates that gravitational wave turbulence corresponds to the propagation of a genuine physical degree of freedom. These numerical findings, however, must be interpreted with caution, given the difficulty of satisfying all seven Einstein equations simultaneously with sufficient accuracy. On the other hand, our simulations reproduce well the expected properties of the wave turbulence regime, with the emergence of a dual cascade of energy and wave action, and for the latter the observation of the Kolmogorov-Zakharov spectrum. In addition, our analysis reveals that the canonical variables of the problem evolve towards a nearly Gaussian statistical distribution punctuated by intermittent coherent (spatially localised and long-living) structures. In contrast to the canonical variables, the structure functions of the gauge-invariant metric components exhibit monofractal behaviour, which is a classical property of wave turbulence.

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the relation between bound states and quasinormal modes within black hole perturbation theory in the context of spectral instability. Our analysis indicates that the reliability of such spectral mapping stretches beyond the domain of validity of the analytic continuation employed to connect the perturbative bound-state problem to the corresponding open-system dynamics. However, for the numerical scheme proposed by Völkel to work, the transformations of the metric parameters must be carried out in a region where the underlying Taylor expansion is convergent. These findings contribute to the effort to scrutinize the conditions under which bound states faithfully encode quasinormal spectra and to shed light on the underlying physics of black hole spectral instability.

### [72] [Tidal deformations of general-relativistic multifluid compact stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29726)
*Ethan Carlier,Nicolas Chamel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper develops a general-relativistic multifluid framework to model adiabatic tidal deformations in compact stars, incorporating mutual entrainment between fluid components. Using Carter's variational formalism, the authors derive equilibrium and perturbation equations for arbitrary-order tidal responses. They show analytically that nondissipative entrainment does not alter adiabatic tidal deformabilities, implying no effect on gravitational-wave signals prior to resonance excitations. Applications to superfluid neutron stars and dark matter admixed stars are discussed.

本文采用Carter的多流体变分方法，建立了广义相对论下的多流体框架，用于描述致密星中绝热潮汐形变。研究推导了任意阶引力电和引磁潮汐响应的平衡与扰动方程，并分析了非耗散互嵌（mutual entrainment）对潮汐形变的影响。通过解析方法，作者证明互嵌不改变绝热潮汐响应，因此在内模共振激发前不会影响引力波信号。文章进一步讨论了该结论在超流中子星和含暗物质致密星中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gravitational-wave observations, particularly from binary inspirals like GW170817, have made tidal deformability a key probe of the dense-matter equation of state (EoS). As third-generation detectors will measure higher-order tidal effects with greater precision, more sophisticated stellar models beyond the perfect-fluid approximation are needed. Multifluid dynamics, which naturally incorporates phenomena like superfluidity and dark matter admixture, provides a richer microphysical description essential for interpreting future data.

引力波观测（如GW170817）使潮汐形变成为探测致密物质状态方程（EoS）的关键手段。随着第三代探测器能够更精确地测量高阶潮汐效应，需要超越理想流体近似的更先进恒星模型。多流体动力学能自然包含超流性和暗物质混合等现象，为解释未来数据提供了更丰富的微观物理描述。

Method: The authors employ Carter's multifluid variational formalism to construct a fully general-relativistic model of compact stars with multiple interacting fluids. They derive the hydrostatic equilibrium equations and linearized perturbation equations for stationary gravitoelectric and gravitomagnetic tidal fields of arbitrary multipolar order. The analysis includes mutual entrainment—a nondissipative coupling where the momentum of one fluid depends on the currents of others. An analytical equation of state for multifluid systems is used to assess the impact of entrainment on tidal deformabilities.

作者采用Carter的多流体变分形式，构建了具有多个相互作用流体的致密星全广义相对论模型。他们推导了定态引力电和引磁潮汐场（任意多极阶）下的流体静力学平衡方程和线性化扰动方程。分析中包含了互嵌效应——一种非耗散耦合，其中一个流体的动量依赖于其他流体的流。使用多流体系统的解析状态方程来评估互嵌对潮汐形变的影响。

Result: The study shows that mutual entrainment does not affect adiabatic tidal deformabilities in compact stars. This is demonstrated analytically using a generic multifluid EoS: while entrainment modifies internal fluid dynamics, it leaves the external gravitational field and tidal Love numbers unchanged during adiabatic, stationary tides. Consequently, entrainment-induced effects do not appear in the gravitational-wave phase during the early inspiral, unless dynamical processes like resonant mode excitations occur later. Results apply to both superfluid neutron stars and dark matter admixed configurations.

研究表明，互嵌不影响致密星的绝热潮汐形变。通过通用多流体EoS的解析分析表明：尽管互嵌改变了内部流体动力学，但在绝热、定态潮汐下，外部引力场和潮汐Love数保持不变。因此，在早期旋进阶段的引力波相位中不会出现由互嵌引起的效应，除非后期发生内模共振等动力学过程。该结果适用于超流中子星和含暗物质星体构型。

Conclusion: While multifluid models are essential for capturing complex microphysics in compact stars, nondissipative entrainment does not influence adiabatic tidal responses or the associated gravitational-wave signal during the inspiral phase. Thus, for pre-merger GW astronomy, perfect-fluid models remain sufficient for predicting tidal deformabilities. However, multifluid effects may become observable in dynamic regimes, such as during resonance crossings or post-merger oscillations, motivating further study in those contexts.

尽管多流体模型对于捕捉致密星中复杂微观物理至关重要，但非耗散互嵌并不影响旋进阶段的绝热潮汐响应及相关引力波信号。因此，在并合前的引力波天文学中，理想流体模型仍足以预测潮汐形变。然而，多流体效应可能在动态区域（如共振穿越或并合后振荡）变得可观测，这激励了在这些情境下的进一步研究。

Abstract: Over the past decade, gravitational-wave astronomy has opened a new window onto the extreme states of matter inside compact stars. At some point during the inspiral of a binary system, each star starts to experience adiabatic tides, characterized by tidal deformabilities. The dominant tidal deformability, first measured with the GW170817 event, has already constrained the dense-matter equation of state. With the advent of third-generation detectors, tidal deformabilities are expected to be inferred with much higher precision, potentially revealing subleading tidal contributions. This motivates the development of more accurate compact-star models that incorporate richer microphysics. With this in mind, we move beyond the commonly adopted perfect-fluid approximation and model compact stars through a multifluid framework. In this work, we present the fully general-relativistic description of adiabatic tidal deformations of compact stars composed of an arbitrary number of interacting fluids, using Carter's multifluid variational formalism. A distinctive feature of this approach is the presence of nondissipative mutual entrainment between fluid species. We derive the hydrostatic equilibrium equations for multifluid configurations, along with the perturbed equations governing stationary gravitoelectric and gravitomagnetic tidal responses of arbitrary order. We then investigate how entrainment modifies the corresponding tidal deformabilities. Using an analytical representation of the multifluid equation of state, we show that entrainment leaves adiabatic tidal responses unchanged and therefore produces no measurable effect on the gravitational-wave signal emitted during the inspiral long before the excitation of internal mode resonances. We subsequently discuss two specific applications: superfluid neutron stars and dark matter admixed compact stars.

### [73] [QTAM: QTransform Amplitude Modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29785)
*Lorenzo Asprea,Francesco Sarandrea,Alessio Romano,Jacob Lange,Federica Legger,Sara Vallero*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We introduce Q-Transform Amplitude Modulation (QTAM), a fully invertible, shift-invariant Constant-Q Transform method that enables efficient, low-latency time-frequency analysis for gravitational wave data by applying amplitude modulation principles to achieve lossless decimation and exact signal reconstruction.

我们提出Q-变换幅度调制（QTAM），一种完全可逆且具有平移不变性的常数-Q变换方法，通过应用幅度调制原理实现无损降采样和精确信号重建，从而实现引力波数据的高效低延迟时频分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Time-frequency analysis in gravitational wave detection suffers from a trade-off between computational efficiency and shift-invariance. Critically sampled transforms lack robustness for pattern recognition due to sensitivity to time shifts, while overcomplete transforms generate excessive data redundancy, making them unsuitable for low-latency processing. Moreover, existing compression methods are lossy and destroy phase coherence needed for accurate signal reconstruction. There is a pressing need for a method that combines shift-invariance, invertibility, and computational efficiency.

引力波探测中的时频分析面临计算效率与平移不变性之间的权衡。临界采样变换因对时间偏移敏感而不适用于模式识别，而过完备变换产生过多数据冗余，不适合低延迟处理。此外，现有的压缩方法是有损的，会破坏准确信号重建所需的相位一致性。迫切需要一种结合平移不变性、可逆性和计算效率的方法。

Method: QTAM models the output of the Constant-Q Transform as a complex envelope modulated by a high-frequency carrier, inspired by AM radio broadcasting. The high-frequency components are spectrally shifted to baseband, enabling lossless decimation without phase distortion. This approach preserves both time-shift invariance and full invertibility. The algorithm is implemented with native GPU acceleration to meet low-latency requirements (O(1s)). Linearity and invertibility are mathematically proven, ensuring exact reconstruction of the original signal.

QTAM受AM广播启发，将常数-Q变换输出建模为由高频载波调制的复包络。通过频谱搬移到基带实现无损降采样而不引入相位失真。该方法保持了时间平移不变性和完全可逆性。算法采用原生GPU加速以满足低延迟要求（O(1s)）。其线性和可逆性经过数学证明，确保原始信号的精确重建。

Result: QTAM achieves full invertibility with machine precision, preserving phase coherence and enabling exact signal reconstruction. It provides shift-invariant time-frequency representations with reduced data redundancy, making it suitable for low-latency pipelines. GPU-accelerated implementation operates within O(1s) latency bounds. We demonstrate its effectiveness in denoising and disentangling overlapping transient signals, including GW chirps and instrumental glitches, on real and injected GW data.

QTAM实现了机器精度下的完全可逆性，保持了相位一致性并支持精确信号重建。它提供了具有较低数据冗余的平移不变时频表示，适用于低延迟流水线。GPU加速实现可在O(1s)延迟范围内运行。我们在真实和注入的引力波数据上验证了其在去噪及分离重叠瞬态信号（包括GW啁啾和仪器毛刺）方面的有效性。

Conclusion: QTAM bridges the gap between computational efficiency, shift-invariance, and invertibility in time-frequency analysis for gravitational wave astronomy. By leveraging amplitude modulation principles, it enables robust, low-latency signal processing pipelines essential for next-generation observatories. The method opens new avenues for deep learning applications requiring phase-coherent, high-resolution spectrograms.

QTAM弥合了引力波天文学中时频分析的计算效率、平移不变性和可逆性之间的差距。通过利用幅度调制原理，它为下一代观测站所需的强大低延迟信号处理流水线铺平了道路。该方法为需要相位相干高分辨率谱图的深度学习应用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We present Q-Transform Amplitude Modulation (QTAM), a novel, fully invertible implementation of the Constant-Q Transform algorithm, designed to enable robust signal denoising and the disentanglement of overlapping transient events in current and next generation gravitational wave (GW) observatories. Time-frequency (TF) analysis faces a fundamental dichotomy: critically sampled transforms are computationally efficient but lack time-shift invariance, limiting their efficacy for robust pattern recognition and Deep Learning applications. While alternative approaches such as the Dual-Tree Complex Wavelet Transform provide efficient approximate shift-invariance, their wavelet constructions remain tied to dyadic scale frequency tilings that are poorly matched to the simultaneous representation of GW chirps and instrumental glitches. Conversely, overcomplete transforms provide the necessary shift-invariance and tunable frequency resolution, but their implementations generate highly redundant data volumes that are prohibitive for low-latency (LL) processing. Furthermore, standard attempts to compress these dense representations rely on lossy interpolation, destroying the phase coherence required to reconstruct the signal. QTAM bridges this gap by employing a methodology inspired by Amplitude Modulation radio broadcasting. By modeling the Q-transform output as a slowly varying complex envelope carried by a deterministic high-frequency term, we achieve lossless data decimation via spectral shifting to baseband. We demonstrate that QTAM is linear and fully invertible, allowing exact reconstruction of the original signal with machine precision while retaining the shift-invariance of dense spectrograms. Leveraging native GPU acceleration, QTAM enables TF pipelines to operate within LL O(1s) bounds. We validate the method's potential for denoising and disentanglement on GW data and signal injections.

### [74] [Beyond Expectation Values: Generalized Semiclassical Expansions for Matrix Elements of Gauge Coherent States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29826)
*Haida Li,Hongguang Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We derive an asymptotic expansion for off-diagonal coherent-state matrix elements of non-polynomial operators in gauge theories with holomorphic coherent states, using stationary-phase analysis and operator-level Taylor remainder control. Applied to Loop Quantum Gravity, the method improves accuracy over diagonal expansions by preserving the full holomorphic structure via the off-diagonal Berezin symbol, especially for well-separated coherent-state labels.

我们推导了在具有全纯相干态表示的规范理论中，非多项式算符的非对角相干态矩阵元的渐近展开。该方法结合稳相近似与算符层面的泰勒余项处理，在适当假设下提供明确的半经典误差控制。应用于圈量子引力中的体积和通量相关算符时，相比传统的对角展开（如arXiv:gr-qc/0607101提出），新公式通过围绕真正的非对角Berezin符号展开，保持了几何相位的完整全纯结构，在数值测试中尤其当相干态标签分离较远时，能更精确地复现基准矩阵元。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In Loop Quantum Gravity (LQG) and other gauge theories with holomorphic coherent states, accurate computation of off-diagonal matrix elements of geometric operators (e.g., volume, flux) is essential for semiclassical analysis and transition amplitude calculations. However, standard diagonal expansions around expectation values fail to capture interference effects and lose holomorphic covariance when coherent states are well separated. This motivates the development of a systematic off-diagonal expansion that respects the full complex structure and provides controlled semiclassical approximations.

在具有全纯相干态的圈量子引力等规范理论中，几何算符（如体积、通量）的非对角矩阵元的精确计算对于半经典分析和跃迁振幅计算至关重要。然而，围绕期望值的标准对角展开在相干态分离较远时无法捕捉干涉效应，并破坏全纯协变性。因此，亟需发展一种系统性的非对角展开方法，以保持完整的复结构并提供可控的半经典近似。

Method: The method combines stationary-phase approximation with rigorous operator-level estimation of the Taylor remainder. Starting from the holomorphic representation of coherent states, we expand non-polynomial operators (e.g., $\sqrt{\hat{E}^2}$) in terms of creation and annihilation operators, and compute matrix elements $\langle z' | \hat{O} | z \rangle$ asymptotically by identifying dominant contributions near critical points of the phase function. Crucially, the expansion is organized around the off-diagonal Berezin symbol $\langle z' | \hat{O} | z \rangle / \langle z' | z \rangle$, preserving holomorphicity, rather than the diagonal symbol $\langle z | \hat{O} | z \rangle$. Error bounds are derived using norm estimates on remainder terms in the operator Taylor series.

该方法结合稳相近似与算符层面上泰勒级数余项的严格估计。从相干态的全纯表示出发，将非多项式算符（如$\sqrt{\hat{E}^2}$）用产生和湮灭算符展开，并通过对相位函数临界点附近的主导贡献进行渐近计算得到矩阵元$\langle z' | \hat{O} | z \rangle$。关键在于，展开围绕非对角Berezin符号$\langle z' | \hat{O} | z \rangle / \langle z' | z \rangle$进行，而非对角符号$\langle z | \hat{O} | z \rangle$，从而保持全纯性。误差界通过对算符泰勒级数中余项的范数估计得出。

Result: The resulting asymptotic expansion accurately reproduces benchmark off-diagonal matrix elements in LQG for volume and flux operators, outperforming the diagonal expansion in regimes where the coherent-state labels $z$ and $z'$ are significantly separated. The error is shown to scale semiclassically as $\sim 1/|z - z'|$ under suitable assumptions, and the expansion maintains exact holomorphic symmetry. Numerical tests confirm improved fidelity, especially in capturing oscillatory interference patterns absent in diagonal approximations.

所得到的渐近展开在圈量子引力中准确复现了体积和通量算符的基准非对角矩阵元，在相干态标签$z$与$z'$相距较远的情况下优于对角展开。在适当假设下，误差按半经典尺度$\sim 1/|z - z'|$衰减，且展开保持精确的全纯对称性。数值测试证实其保真度更高，尤其能够捕捉对角近似中缺失的振荡干涉模式。

Conclusion: By shifting the expansion center from diagonal to off-diagonal Berezin symbols, we obtain a more accurate and structurally faithful semiclassical approximation for matrix elements in holomorphic gauge theories. This approach restores full holomorphic covariance and is particularly effective for computing transition amplitudes between distinguishable semiclassical states. It provides a robust framework for precision semiclassical calculations in Loop Quantum Gravity and potentially other systems with coherent-state path integrals.

通过将展开中心从对角Berezin符号转向非对角Berezin符号，我们获得了在全纯规范理论中更为精确且结构上更忠实的半经典近似。该方法恢复了完整的全纯协变性，特别适用于可区分半经典态之间的跃迁振幅计算。它为圈量子引力中的高精度半经典计算以及可能的其他具有相干态路径积分的系统提供了坚实框架。

Abstract: We derive an asymptotic expansion for off-diagonal coherent-state matrix elements of non-polynomial operators in gauge theories admitting holomorphic coherent-state representations. The derivation combines stationary-phase analysis with an operator-level treatment of the Taylor remainder, and yields explicit semiclassical error control under stated assumptions. As a primary application, we formulate the expansion for volume and flux related operators in Loop Quantum Gravity and compare it with the standard diagonal expansion proposed in arXiv:gr-qc/0607101. By organizing the expansion around the genuine off-diagonal Berezin symbol rather than a diagonal expectation value, the resulting formula preserves the full holomorphic structure of the geometric phase and reproduces benchmark matrix elements accurately in the numerical regimes tested here, particularly when the coherent-state labels are well separated.

### [75] [Exceptional Points in Quasinormal Spectra of Hairy Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22261)
*Lang Cheng,Xiaobo Guo,Yuhan Li,Jun Tao,Peng Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We identify an exceptional point (EP) in the scalar quasinormal mode (QNM) spectrum of hairy black holes in Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory and show that an EP ansatz—including a linear-in-time resonant term—provides a more accurate description of ringdown signals than the standard damped-mode decomposition.

我们识别了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中带毛黑洞标量准正规模（QNM）谱中的一个例外点（EP），并表明包含随时间线性增长项的EP试探波形比基于独立衰减模式叠加的标准试探波形能更准确地描述铃宕信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Exceptional points are unique features in non-Hermitian systems where both eigenvalues and eigenfunctions coalesce. While EPs have been studied in various physical contexts, their manifestation in black hole QNM spectra and implications for gravitational wave ringdown remain largely unexplored, especially in theories beyond general relativity such as those with scalar hair.

例外点是非厄米系统中本征值与本征函数同时合并的独特现象。尽管EP已在多种物理体系中被研究，但其在黑洞准正规模谱中的实现及对引力波铃宕信号的影响仍鲜有探索，尤其是在广义相对论以外的含标量毛理论中。

Method: We scan the parameter space of hairy black holes in the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory to locate an EP in the scalar QNM spectrum. We then generate time-domain waveforms and extract QNMs using both the standard exponential decay ansatz and an EP ansatz that includes a resonant term proportional to $ t e^{-i\omega t} $. The performance and robustness of both models are compared via waveform fitting.

我们在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论的带毛黑洞参数空间中进行扫描，以定位标量QNM谱中的例外点；随后生成时域波形，并分别使用标准指数衰减试探形式和包含$ t e^{-i\omega t} $共振项的EP试探形式提取准正规模，通过波形拟合比较两种模型的表现与鲁棒性。

Result: An exceptional point is identified in the scalar QNM spectrum where two modes coalesce in both frequency and mode shape. Time-domain simulations confirm that the EP ansatz, including the $ t $-linear resonant term, provides a better fit to the ringdown signal near the EP. Even when using the standard ansatz, residual features such as slow amplitude decay and phase locking reflect the underlying spectral coalescence.

在标量QNM谱中识别到一个例外点，其中两个模式在频率和模态形状上均发生合并。时域模拟证实，包含$ t $线性项的EP试探波形在EP附近对铃宕信号具有更优的拟合效果；即使使用标准试探波形，残余特征如缓慢的振幅衰减和相位锁定仍反映出底层的谱合并现象。

Conclusion: The presence of exceptional points in hairy black hole spacetimes has observable consequences for ringdown dynamics. The EP ansatz offers a more physically accurate and robust framework for modeling ringdown near spectral degeneracies, which could improve tests of gravity with gravitational wave observations.

带毛黑洞时空中例外点的存在对铃宕动力学具有可观测效应。EP试探波形为在谱简并附近建模铃宕提供了更符合物理实际且鲁棒的框架，有望提升利用引力波观测检验引力理论的能力。

Abstract: Exceptional points (EPs) in quasinormal mode (QNM) spectra are non-Hermitian degeneracies at which both the eigenvalues and eigenfunctions coalesce. In this paper, we identify an EP in the scalar QNM spectrum of hairy black holes in the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory by scanning the parameter space. We then investigate its implications for ringdown signals by extracting QNMs from time-domain waveforms. Our results show that an EP ansatz, which includes a resonant contribution containing a term linear in time, provides a more robust description of ringdown at the EP than the standard ansatz based on a superposition of independent damped modes. In particular, it captures the resonant contribution associated with spectral coalescence more naturally, and even when the waveform is fitted with the standard ansatz, the resulting fit may still exhibit characteristic features of the EP ansatz.

</details>


### [76] [Bridging Quantum and Semiclassical Volume: A Numerical Study of Coherent State Matrix Elements in Loop Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29839)
*Haida Li,Hongguang Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We develop and implement a generalized numerical algorithm to compute the quantum action of the volume operator in Loop Quantum Gravity on arbitrary spin-network states, validate it against analytical results in the semiclassical regime, and study its behavior in both regular and irregular geometries, showing convergence to classical volumes and revealing quantum corrections in non-semiclassical regimes.

我们开发并实现了一种广义数值算法，用于计算圈量子引力中体积算符在任意自旋网络态上的量子作用，通过与半经典区域的解析结果对比验证了该算法的高精度，并研究了规则与不规则几何下其行为，表明在半经典极限下趋向经典多面体体积，并揭示了深量子区域中的量子修正效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The volume operator plays a central role in the quantum dynamics of Loop Quantum Gravity (LQG), yet its full quantum action on generic spin-network states—especially gauge-variant or highly irregular ones—remains difficult to compute analytically. A robust numerical approach is needed to bridge between formal theory and physical predictions, particularly in exploring the quantum-to-classical transition and potential deviations in deep quantum regimes.

体积算符在圈量子引力（LQG）的量子动力学中起核心作用，但其在一般自旋网络态（尤其是规范变异或高度不规则态）上的完整量子作用难以解析计算。需要一种稳健的数值方法来连接形式理论与物理预言，特别是在探索量子到经典的过渡以及深量子区域可能的偏离时。

Method: We formulate a generalized numerical algorithm that diagonalizes the volume operator on arbitrary spin-network nodes, incorporating both gauge-invariant (SU(2)-invariant) and gauge-variant configurations. The algorithm computes eigenvalues and eigenvectors of the volume operator matrix, and is applied to evaluate coherent state expectation values $\langle V \rangle$ and matrix elements $\langle \psi_i | V | \psi_j \rangle$. These are compared with known analytical expressions in the semiclassical limit, such as those based on polyhedral volume formulas and twisted geometries.

我们构建了一种广义数值算法，可对任意自旋网络节点上的体积算符进行对角化，涵盖规范不变（SU(2)-不变）和规范变型构型。该算法计算体积算符矩阵的本征值与本征向量，并用于计算相干态期望值 $\langle V \rangle$ 和矩阵元 $\langle \psi_i | V | \psi_j \rangle$。这些结果与半经典极限下的已知解析表达式（如基于多面体体积公式和扭曲几何的表达式）进行对比。

Result: The numerical results match analytical predictions with high precision in the semiclassical regime, validating the algorithm. We find that the largest eigenvalue of the volume operator converges to the classical polyhedral volume for regular nodes. In irregular configurations, while the semiclassical behavior persists, relative eigenvalue magnitudes shift significantly in the deep quantum regime, indicating geometry-dependent quantum corrections. Coherent state expectation values accurately reproduce semiclassical volumes.

数值结果在半经典区域与解析预测高度吻合，验证了算法的有效性。我们发现，对于规则节点，体积算符的最大本征值趋近于经典多面体体积。在不规则构型中，尽管半经典行为仍然存在，但在深量子区域相对本征值大小发生显著变化，表明存在依赖几何的量子修正。相干态期望值能精确复现半经典体积。

Conclusion: Our generalized algorithm enables accurate computation of the volume operator's quantum action across a wide range of spin-network states. It confirms the emergence of classical geometry from LQG in the semiclassical limit and reveals non-trivial quantum geometric effects in non-regular configurations, providing a powerful tool for studying quantum dynamics and semiclassical consistency in Loop Quantum Gravity.

我们的广义算法能够精确计算体积算符在广泛自旋网络态上的量子作用。它证实了在半经典极限下经典几何从圈量子引力中涌现，并揭示了非规则构型中的非平庸量子几何效应，为研究圈量子引力中的量子动力学和半经典一致性提供了有力工具。

Abstract: In Loop Quantum Gravity, the quantum action of the volume operator is crucial in understanding quantum dynamics. In this work, we implement a generalized numerical algorithm that can compute the quantum action of the volume operator on a broad class of gauge-variant and gauge-invariant spin-network states. This algorithm is later used to calculate the coherent state expectation value and coherent state matrix elements of the volume operator. By comparing the results generated by our numerical model with the analytical results in various scenarios at the near-semiclassical region, not only is our numerical model validated with high accuracy, but it also provides a complete picture of how the full quantum action of the volume operator connects with its semiclassical approximations. We further find that the maximal eigenvalue approaches the classical polyhedral volume in the semiclassical regime. For irregular geometries, we also observe that the relative volume magnitudes can change in the deep quantum regime.

### [77] [Resolution of the cosmological constant problem by unimodular gravity and signature reversal symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29918)
*Recai Erdem*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper proposes a solution to the second cosmological constant problem within unimodular gravity by embedding our 4D spacetime as a brane in a higher-dimensional bulk with $ D = 2(2n + 1) $ dimensions and imposing signature reversal symmetry.

本文通过将我们的四维时空嵌入到具有符号反转对称性的高维体空间（$ D = 2(2n + 1) $）中的膜上，在非模引力框架下提出了对第二个宇宙学常数问题的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The cosmological constant problem consists of two parts: the fine-tuning problem (why observed vacuum energy is vastly smaller than theoretical predictions) and the coincidence problem (why it has this particular small value). While unimodular gravity addresses the first, it does not resolve the second. The author aims to solve the second problem using extra dimensions and discrete symmetries.

宇宙学常数问题包含两个部分：微调问题（为何观测到的真空能量远小于理论预测）和巧合问题（为何它具有这个特定的小值）。虽然非模引力解决了第一个问题，但未解决第二个问题。作者旨在利用额外维度和离散对称性来解决第二个问题。

Method: The 4-dimensional spacetime is considered as a brane embedded in a higher-dimensional bulk with dimension $ D = 2(2n + 1) $. The key ingredient is the imposition of signature reversal symmetry, which identifies spacetimes with metric signatures $ (+,-,-,-,...) $ and $ (-,+,+,+,...) $, effectively making the cosmological constant sign-insensitive and constraining its value through topological or symmetry arguments.

将四维时空视为嵌入在维度为 $ D = 2(2n + 1) $ 的高维体空间中的膜。关键在于施加符号反转对称性，该对称性将具有度量符号 $ (+,-,-,-,...) $ 和 $ (-,+,+,+,...) $ 的时空等同起来，从而有效地使宇宙学常数对符号不敏感，并通过拓扑或对称性论证限制其数值。

Result: The combination of brane-world setup in $ D = 2(2n + 1) $ dimensions and signature reversal symmetry leads to a mechanism that dynamically selects a unique (and naturally small) value for the effective 4D cosmological constant, potentially solving the second cosmological constant problem.

在 $ D = 2(2n + 1) $ 维中结合膜世界设定与符号反转对称性，导致一种动力学机制选择唯一的（且自然小的）有效四维宇宙学常数，可能解决第二个宇宙学常数问题。

Conclusion: The second cosmological constant problem can be resolved in unimodular gravity if our universe is a brane in a higher-dimensional space with $ D = 2(2n + 1) $ and signature reversal symmetry is imposed, offering a novel symmetry-based explanation for the observed smallness of dark energy.

如果我们的宇宙是在具有 $ D = 2(2n + 1) $ 维和符号反转对称性的高维空间中的膜，则第二个宇宙学常数问题可以在非模引力中得到解决，为暗能量的微小性提供了一种基于对称性的新解释。

Abstract: The (old) cosmological constant problem consists of two different problems. The first is the huge discrepancy between the value of the cosmological constant deduced from observations and its value expected from cosmological constant-like theoretical contributions (such as vacuum expectation value of Higgs potential). The second problem is why the value of the cosmological constant has its particular (very small) value. It is well-known that unimodular gravity solves the first problem while it leaves the second problem unsolved. In this paper I show that the second problem may also be resolved in the context of unimodular gravity by letting our 4-dimensional spacetime be a brane in a D = 2(2n + 1) dimensional bulk and imposing the signature reversal symmetry

### [78] [Quantizing the exterior region of a Schwarzschild-AdS black hole leads to a resolution of the information paradox on a quantum level](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27339)
*Claus Gerhardt*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper proposes a quantum gravity model to resolve the black hole information paradox by establishing unitary equivalence between the quantized exterior and interior regions of a Schwarzschild-AdS black hole through matching eigenvalue multiplicities.

本文提出了一种量子引力模型，通过匹配特征值重数，在史瓦西-反德西特黑洞的外部和内部区域的量子化之间建立幺正等价性，从而解决黑洞信息悖论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to address the black hole information paradox in the context of quantum gravity, particularly by understanding how quantum states evolve across the exterior and interior regions of a Schwarzschild-AdS black hole without loss of unitarity.

研究动机是解决量子引力框架下的黑洞信息悖论，特别是理解量子态在史瓦西-反德西特黑洞外部与内部区域间演化时如何保持幺正性而不丢失信息。

Method: The authors quantize both the exterior and interior regions of a Schwarzschild-AdS black hole. They solve a hyperbolic equation whose solutions are products of temporal eigenfunctions $w_i$ (with non-degenerate eigenvalues) and spatial eigendistributions $v_{ij}$ (with degeneracy $m_i \geq 1$). The ambiguity in choosing $m_i$ for the exterior region is resolved by adopting the values determined from the interior quantization, where $m_i$ can be fixed by maximization.

作者对史瓦西-反德西特黑洞的外部和内部区域进行量子化，求解一个双曲型方程，其解为时间本征函数$w_i$（特征值无简并）与空间本征分布$v_{ij}$（重数$m_i \geq 1$）的乘积。通过采用内部区域量子化中由最大化确定的$m_i$值，解决了外部区域中$m_i$选择的不确定性问题。

Result: The eigenvalues of the temporal Hamiltonian are identical in both regions. By equating the multiplicities $m_i$ in the exterior to those in the interior, a unitary equivalence is established between the Hilbert spaces and Hamiltonians of the two regions, thereby eliminating the information paradox at the quantum level.

时间哈密顿量的特征值在两个区域中相同。通过将外部区域的重数$m_i$设为与内部一致，在两个区域的希尔伯特空间与哈密顿量之间建立了幺正等价性，从而在量子层面上消除了信息悖论。

Conclusion: There is no information paradox in the quantum description of Schwarzschild-AdS black holes when unitary equivalence between the quantized exterior and interior regions is enforced via consistent eigenvalue multiplicities.

当通过对特征值重数的一致选择在量子化的外部与内部区域之间强制实现幺正等价时，史瓦西-反德西特黑洞的量子描述中不存在信息悖论。

Abstract: We quantize the exterior region of a Schwarzschild-AdS black hole using our model of quantum gravity. The resulting hyperbolic equation is solved by products of temporal eigenfunctions $w_i$, the eigenvalues of which all have multiplicity one, and spatial eigendistributions $v_{ij}$ having the same eigenvalues but with multiplicities $1\le m_i$, where the $m_i$ could in principle be arbitrarily large. Regarding only the exterior region, there was no guidance how to determine the values of the $m_i$. However, considering also the quantization of the interior region, where the same question did not arise since the $m_i$ could be chosen by maximizing the value, it seemed logical to choose the same values, too, in the exterior case. Since the eigenvalues in the interior are the same because the temporal Hamiltonian is the same in both cases, this choice defined a unitary equivalence between the respective Hilbert spaces and the respective Hamiltonians. Hence, there is no information paradox on a quantum level.

</details>


### [79] [Waveform degeneracy of binary systems and Lagrange three-body systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29991)
*Carlos Jaimel Doctolero,Ian Vega*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates the gravitational waveform degeneracy between quasi-circular binary systems and Lagrange three-body systems up to 0.5PN order, showing that their mass quadrupole waveforms can be nearly identical, leading to potential observational ambiguity in gravitational wave detection.

本文研究了准圆形双星系统与拉格朗日三体系统在0.5PN阶下的引力波形简并性，发现它们的质量四极波形可能几乎相同，从而导致引力波探测中的潜在观测模糊性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The discovery of gravitational waves from compact binaries has raised interest in whether other exotic systems, such as three-body configurations, could mimic binary signals. The Lagrange three-body system, with its equilateral triangular orbit, provides a concrete example to test waveform degeneracies and assess potential confusion in data analysis.

紧凑双星引力波的发现引发了人们对其他奇特系统（如三体构型）是否可能模仿双星信号的兴趣。拉格朗日三体系统因其等边三角轨道为检验波形简并性和评估数据分析中潜在混淆提供了具体范例。

Method: The authors compute the mass quadrupole radiation from both quasi-circular binary systems and Lagrange three-body systems up to 0.5PN order. They derive conditions under which the plus and cross polarization modes of the two systems match, identifying degeneracy parameters. They analyze stability constraints on the Lagrange triple and compute waveform overlaps using the advanced LIGO noise curve.

作者计算了准圆形双星系统和拉格朗日三体系统在0.5PN阶下的质量四极辐射，推导出两种系统在加号和交叉偏振模式匹配的条件，并识别简并参数。他们分析了拉格朗日三重态的稳定性约束，并使用先进LIGO噪声曲线计算波形重叠率。

Result: A two-parameter degeneracy exists in the mass quadrupole waveform between binary and Lagrange systems, allowing for indistinguishable waveforms up to coalescence time when masses are nearly symmetric. Normalized overlaps exceed 0.97 for advanced LIGO sensitivity. At 0.5PN beyond quadrupole, a unique degeneracy exists but corresponds to an unstable Lagrange configuration.

质量和四极波形存在一个双参数简并性，使得当质量接近对称时，双星与拉格朗日系统在并合时间前的波形无法区分。对于先进LIGO灵敏度，归一化重叠率超过0.97。在四极之外的0.5PN阶，存在唯一简并情况，但对应的拉格朗日构型不稳定。

Conclusion: Quasi-circular binary systems can be observationally degenerate with certain Lagrange three-body systems in gravitational wave signals up to 0.5PN order, posing challenges for source identification. While stable triples can mimic binaries in the quadrupole approximation, higher-order effects break the degeneracy except for unstable configurations.

准圆形双星系统在引力波信号中可能与某些拉格朗日三体系统在0.5PN阶下出现观测简并，给源识别带来挑战。尽管稳定三重态可在四极近似下模拟双星，但高阶效应会打破简并性，除非是不稳定构型。

Abstract: A particular solution to the three-body problem is the circular Lagrange three-body system, where the masses move in circular orbits such that they always constitute an equilateral triangle. Such a system has been found to emit gravitational waves with a waveform similar to that of a binary system. In this work, we study the gravitational waveform degeneracy between quasi-circular binary systems and Lagrange three-body systems up to 0.5PN order. Assuming we know the parameters of a given binary system, we determine the parameters of the Lagrange triple that produces the same waveform as that of the binary. We show that there exists a mass quadrupole degeneracy in both the plus and cross modes, characterized by two parameters. We also find that there are binary systems and linearly stable Lagrange three-body systems that can have the same mass quadrupole waveform up to the coalescence time. In such cases, the normalized overlap of the waveforms with respect to the power spectral density of the advanced LIGO design remains above 0.97 as long as the binary has nearly symmetric masses. Beyond the mass quadrupole, there is a unique degeneracy at the 0.5PN. However, the Lagrange triple that satisfies this degeneracy is unstable.

### [80] [What does the Universe sound like?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29996)
*Francesco Iacovelli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper computes the collective sound of gravitational waves from approximately $10^6$ synthetic compact binary coalescence events in 2026, revealing a low-frequency rumble termed the 'Universal harmony,' suitable for relaxation and reflection on spacetime dynamics.

引力波探测器无法像电磁望远镜那样提供视觉图像，因此需要以直观易懂的方式呈现引力波数据。将引力波信号转化为声音为公众参与及解读宇宙中的剧烈过程提供了新方法。

Method: The author generates $\sim10^6$ synthetic compact binary coalescence (CBC) events expected in 2026 and models their gravitational-wave signals. 作者生成了2026年预期的约$10^6$个合成致密双星并合（CBC）事件，并模拟其引力波信号。通过适当的时间缩放和频率映射将这些信号转换为音频，然后进行平均，以产生来自CBC的随机引力波背景的连续听觉表示。

Result: The resulting audio is a coherent, low-frequency rumble—dubbed the $Universal\ harmony$—that emerges from the superposition of many CBC events. 结果音频是一种由多个CBC事件叠加产生的连贯低频隆隆声，被称为$Universal\ harmony$。尽管单个啁啾信号短暂且瞬态，但高事件率导致近乎连续的声音，峰值位于次声波到可听低频范围内。

Conclusion: By transforming gravitational-wave data into sound, the study provides an accessible and immersive way to experience the dynamic nature of spacetime. The 'Universal harmony' represents not only a scientific visualization tool but also a bridge between science and human sensory experience.

通过将引力波数据转化为声音，本研究提供了一种可及且沉浸式的方式来体验时空的动态本质。‘宇宙和谐’不仅是一种科学可视化工具，也是连接科学与人类感官体验的桥梁。

Abstract: Unlike electromagnetic telescopes, gravitational-wave (GW) detectors cannot produce pretty pictures, but we can convert GW signals into sound. I compute what the Universe actually sounds like by averaging over $\sim10^6$ synthetic compact binary coalescence events occurring throughout 2026. The result: a soothing, low-frequency rumble, perfect for sleeping, meditation, or contemplating the violent nature of spacetime. This is the $Universal\ harmony$, audio file included!

### [81] [The scalar--Maxwell--$Λ(x)$ system: Wormhole spacetimes without nonlinear electrodynamics in unimodular gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.30003)
*G. Alencar,T. M. Crispim*

TL;DR: We construct exact traversable wormhole solutions in Unimodular Gravity (UG) coupled to a phantom scalar field and standard linear Maxwell electrodynamics, where the spacetime is supported by a dynamical cosmological term $\Lambda(x)$. This avoids the need for Non-Linear Electrodynamics (NED), demonstrating UG's advantage in enabling non-trivial topologies with simpler matter content.

我们构建了在非体引力（Unimodular Gravity, UG）中耦合幻象标量场与标准线性麦克斯韦电动力学的精确可穿越虫洞解，其时空由动力学宇宙学项 $\Lambda(x)$ 支持。该方法避免了对非线性电动力学（Non-Linear Electrodynamics, NED）的需求，展示了UG在使用更简单物质场实现非平凡拓扑结构方面的优势。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In General Relativity, constructing traversable wormholes usually requires exotic matter and Non-Linear Electrodynamics (NED), which are theoretically challenging. The motivation is to find a physically plausible and mathematically simpler framework for wormhole construction by leveraging modified gravity—specifically Unimodular Gravity—which allows for energy exchange between matter and the vacuum via a dynamical $\Lambda(x)$.

在广义相对论中，构造可穿越虫洞通常需要奇异物质和非线性电动力学（NED），这在理论上具有挑战性。本文的动机是利用修正引力——特别是允许通过动力学项 $\Lambda(x)$ 实现物质与真空之间能量交换的非体引力（UG）——寻找一种物理上更合理且数学上更简洁的虫洞构造框架。

Method: We solve the gravitational field equations in Unimodular Gravity, where the trace-free Einstein equations are supplemented by a variable cosmological term $\Lambda(x)$ determined by the contracted Bianchi identity. Assuming spherical symmetry and a static metric with shape function $b(r)$ and redshift function $\phi(r)$, we couple a phantom scalar field and linear Maxwell electrodynamics. By imposing specific geometric conditions on $b(r)$, we obtain exact analytical solutions for the wormhole spacetime and derive the corresponding $\Lambda(x)$, scalar, and electromagnetic profiles.

我们在非体引力中求解引力场方程，其中无迹爱因斯坦方程通过由收缩比安基恒等式确定的动力学宇宙学项 $\Lambda(x)$ 补充。假设球对称性和带有形函数 $b(r)$ 与红移函数 $\phi(r)$ 的静态度规，我们耦合了一个幻象标量场和线性麦克斯韦电动力学。通过对 $b(r)$ 施加特定几何条件，我们获得了虫洞时空的精确解析解，并推导出相应的 $\Lambda(x)$、标量场和电磁场分布。

Result: Exact traversable wormhole solutions are obtained where the energy conditions are effectively satisfied through the interplay of a phantom scalar field and the dynamical $\Lambda(x)$, while the electromagnetic field remains governed by standard linear Maxwell theory—eliminating the need for NED. The model shows that UG enables consistent semi-classical wormhole geometries supported by well-understood classical fields, provided $b(r)$ meets certain asymptotic and flare-out conditions.

我们得到了精确的可穿越虫洞解，其中幻象标量场与动力学 $\Lambda(x)$ 的相互作用有效满足了能量条件，而电磁场仍由标准线性麦克斯韦理论描述——从而无需引入NED。结果表明，只要形函数 $b(r)$ 满足一定的渐近性和外张条件，UG即可支持由熟知的经典场构成的一致半经典虫洞几何。

Conclusion: Unimodular Gravity provides a novel and powerful framework for constructing exact traversable wormholes without relying on Non-Linear Electrodynamics. The introduction of a dynamical $\Lambda(x)$ enables energy exchange between matter and the vacuum, allowing standard Maxwell fields and a phantom scalar to support the geometry. This highlights UG as a promising arena for exploring quantum-influenced spacetime topologies using semi-classical tools.

非体引力提供了一个新颖且强大的框架，可用于构造无需依赖非线性电动力学的精确可穿越虫洞。动力学项 $\Lambda(x)$ 的引入实现了物质与真空之间的能量交换，使得标准麦克斯韦场与幻象标量场足以支撑虫洞几何。这凸显了UG作为利用半经典工具探索受量子效应影响的时空拓扑结构的潜在平台的重要性。

Abstract: In General Relativity, constructing exact traversable wormholes coupled to electromagnetic fields typically requires complex Non-Linear Electrodynamics (NED). We demonstrate that Unimodular Gravity (UG) elegantly resolves this limitation. By relaxing energy-momentum conservation, UG introduces a dynamical cosmological term, $Λ(x)$, enabling a semi-classical energy exchange between matter and the vacuum. Exploiting this mechanism, we construct exact Scalar-Maxwell-$Λ(x)$ wormholes. We show that, provided the shape function $b(r)$ satisfies specific geometric conditions, these exact spacetimes can be fully supported by a phantom scalar field and standard linear Maxwell electrodynamics. This approach entirely bypasses NED, highlighting UG as a powerful framework for modeling non-trivial topologies with simplified, well-understood classical fields.

</details>
