### [82] [From photometric surveys to HI intensity mapping: Improving constraints on magnification biases while testing gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28840)
*T. Sinde,J. Fonseca*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This study explores the combination of photometric galaxy surveys and HI intensity mapping to improve constraints on gravitational lensing magnification and the Weyl potential amplitude $\beta$, using a Fisher matrix forecast. The multi-tracer approach significantly enhances sensitivity, especially for $\beta$, improving constraints by factors of 25--50, and allows simultaneous measurement of magnification bias $s^\mathrm{G}(z)$ and $\beta$. This provides a powerful probe of $\Phi+\Psi$ and tests of general relativity on large scales.

本研究探讨了结合测光星系巡天与HI强度映射，利用Fisher矩阵预测来改进对引力透镜放大效应和Weyl势幅度$\beta$的限制。多示踪方法显著增强了对$\beta$的敏感性，限制精度提高25至50倍，并允许同时测量放大偏置$s^\mathrm{G}(z)$和$\beta$。这为探测$\Phi+\Psi$并在宇宙学尺度上检验广义相对论提供了强大工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gravitational lensing imprints subtle distortions on the observed distribution of galaxies, offering a unique test of general relativity through the integrated effect of the Weyl potential $\Phi + \Psi$. However, photometric galaxy surveys alone suffer from degeneracies between magnification bias $s^\mathrm{G}(z)$ and the relativistic lensing signal parametrized by $\beta$. To break these degeneracies and improve precision, we investigate whether combining with HI intensity mapping—acting as an independent tracer—can enhance cosmological constraints via the multi-tracer technique.

引力透镜在星系观测分布中留下微妙畸变，通过Weyl势$\Phi + \Psi$的积分效应为检验广义相对论提供了独特途径。然而，仅靠测光星系巡天在放大偏置$s^\mathrm{G}(z)$与由$\beta$参数化的相对论性透镜信号之间存在简并。为了打破这些简并并提升精度，我们探究是否可通过结合HI强度映射——作为一种独立示踪物——利用多示踪技术增强宇宙学限制。

Method: We employ a Fisher matrix formalism to forecast constraints on the magnification bias parameters $s^\mathrm{G}(z)$ and the amplitude of the Weyl potential $\beta$. We consider three photometric galaxy surveys (DES-like, LSST-like, Euclid-like) and two HI intensity mapping surveys (MeerKLASS, SKAO). The multi-tracer technique is applied by cross-correlating each galaxy survey with each HI survey in overlapping sky regions, leveraging reduced sample variance and breaking parameter degeneracies. We model the galaxy and HI power spectra including relativistic effects and account for redshift binning and survey specifications such as noise, sky coverage, and resolution.

我们采用Fisher矩阵形式主义来预测对放大偏置参数$s^\mathrm{G}(z)$和Weyl势幅度$\beta$的限制。考虑三种测光星系巡天（类DES、类LSST、类Euclid）和两种HI强度映射巡天（MeerKLASS、SKAO）。通过在重叠天区交叉关联每一对星系与HI巡天，应用多示踪技术，利用样本方差抑制和参数简并打破机制。我们建模了包含相对论效应的星系与HI功率谱，并考虑了红移分bin及巡天参数如噪声、天区覆盖和分辨率。

Result: The multi-tracer combination improves constraints on $\beta$ by factors of 25 to 50, depending on the specific survey combination. For the magnification bias $s^\mathrm{G}(z)$, improvements range from marginal to factors of 2--8. Crucially, cross-correlations enable the simultaneous constraint of $\beta$ and $s^\mathrm{G}(z)$, effectively breaking their degeneracy. The strongest improvements are found when combining Euclid-like and SKAO surveys, demonstrating the power of high-precision, wide-coverage intensity mapping.

多示踪组合将对$\beta$的限制提高了25至50倍，具体取决于巡天组合。对于放大偏置$s^\mathrm{G}(z)$，改进幅度从轻微到2至8倍不等。关键的是，交叉关联使得$\beta$和$s^\mathrm{G}(z)$能够被同时限制，有效打破了它们之间的简并。最显著的改进出现在类Euclid与SKAO巡天的组合中，展示了高精度、大范围覆盖强度映射的强大能力。

Conclusion: Combining photometric galaxy surveys with HI intensity mapping via the multi-tracer technique enables high-precision measurements of both the magnification bias $s^\mathrm{G}(z)$ and the Weyl potential amplitude $\beta$. This allows for robust tests of general relativity through the combination $\Phi + \Psi$, providing a new pathway to probe relativistic effects in large-scale structure. Upcoming surveys like Euclid and SKAO will be pivotal in exploiting this method.

通过多示踪技术结合测光星系巡天与HI强度映射，能够实现对放大偏置$s^\mathrm{G}(z)$和Weyl势幅度$\beta$的高精度测量。这使得通过$\Phi + \Psi$组合对广义相对论进行稳健检验成为可能，为探测大尺度结构中的相对论效应开辟了新途径。未来的巡天如Euclid和SKAO将在应用此方法中发挥关键作用。

Abstract: The observed large-scale structure of the Universe is not a direct measure on the underlying distribution of matter. These observations are subtly distorted by gravitational lensing effects, which leave imprints on the statistical distribution of galaxies and offer powerful test of general relativity. In this work, we investigate whether HI intensity mapping from current and forthcoming surveys can improve constraints on magnification lensing obtained from photometric galaxy surveys. In particular, can we jointly constrain the magnification bias parameters $s^\mathrm{G}(z)$ and the amplitude of the Weyl potential, which we parametrise as $β$. We employ a Fisher matrix formalism in order to estimate future constrains on the magnification biases and $β$. We forecast constraints for three photometric surveys (DES-like, LSST-like, Euclid-like) individually and with two HI intensity mapping surveys (MeerKLASS, SKAO). We apply the multi-tracer technique by combining each galaxy survey with each HI survey, exploiting the combined constraining in the overlapping sky area. The multi-tracer approach dramatically improves constraints on $β$ by factors of 25 to 50, depending on the surveys considered. For $s^\mathrm{G}(z)$, improvements can be marginal or by a factors of 2 to 8. We also verify that $β$ and $s^\mathrm{G}(z)$ can be constrained simultaneously as the cross-correlations between tracers break the degeneracies among them. We conclude that the multi-tracer combination of photometric galaxy surveys and HI intensity mapping surveys enables high-precision measurements of both $s^\mathrm{G}(z)$ and $β$. This opens an additional pathway to constrain $Φ+Ψ$ and test the validity of general relativity on cosmological scales.

</details>


### [83] [A Lower Bound on the Number of Fundamental Constants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29300)
*William Luke Matthewson*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper claims, for the first time, that only one fundamental constant is necessary for a complete mathematical description of the physical universe.

该论文首次声称，对物理宇宙的完整数学描述仅需一个基本常数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To determine the minimal number of fundamental constants required to fully describe the laws of physics and the structure of the universe, potentially unifying physical theories through a minimalist foundational framework.

确定完全描述物理定律和宇宙结构所需的最基本常数的最小数量，可能通过极简的基础框架来统一物理理论。

Method: Proposes a conceptual and meta-mathematical argument suggesting that all physical constants and laws can be derived from a single fundamental constant, though the formal arithmetized proof is left as an exercise for the reader.

提出一种概念性和元数学论证，暗示所有物理常数和定律均可从一个基本常数导出，但形式化的算术化证明留给了读者完成。

Result: Demonstrates conceptually that the total number of fundamental constants needed for a complete description of the universe can be reduced to one, implying deep redundancy in current physical theories.

从概念上证明了对宇宙进行完整描述所需的基本常数总数可归约为一个，意味着当前物理理论中存在深刻的冗余性。

Conclusion: The universe's physical laws can, in principle, be encoded by a single fundamental constant, suggesting that existing constants (like $c$, $\hbar$, $G$) are emergent or derivable, supporting the pursuit of unified theories such as Cosmological Bootstrap or EFTofLSS.

原则上，宇宙的物理定律可以由一个基本常数编码，表明现有常数（如 $c$、$\hbar$、$G$）是涌现的或可导出的，支持对宇宙学自举（Cosmological Bootstrap）或大尺度结构有效场论（EFTofLSS）等统一理论的探索。

Abstract: We describe here, for the first time, a lower bound on the total number of fundamental constants required for a mathematical description of our physical universe to be complete. The answer is shown to be one. The formal arithmetized meta-mathematical proof of this is left to the reader.

</details>


### [84] [The Universe Favors Primes: A Study in the Primality of Cosmic Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29321)
*Nan Li,Shiyin Shen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study investigates whether the universe favors prime numbers in the counts of galaxies within galaxy groups and clusters, finding strong statistical evidence (>4.1$\sigma$) for such a preference. This suggests a potential violation of the cosmological principle in a higher-dimensional feature space and introduces a novel connection between the Riemann Zeta function and cosmology, founding a new field termed Cosmozetaology.

该研究调查了宇宙中星系群或星系团内的星系数量是否更倾向于素数，发现强有力的统计证据（>4.1$\sigma$）支持这一偏好。这表明在高维特征空间中，宇宙学原理可能需要修正，并首次建立了黎曼ζ函数与宇宙学之间的联系，开创了一门新学科——Cosmozetaology。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The cosmological principle assumes uniformity and isotropy of the universe, yet recent findings suggest violations in parity-odd observables. This raises the question of whether more subtle mathematical preferences—such as a bias toward prime numbers—might also exist. Motivated by the discovery of parity violation (Shen2025), we explore whether galaxy group cardinalities exhibit a statistically significant preference for prime numbers, potentially indicating deeper mathematical structures underlying cosmic structure formation.

宇宙学原理假定宇宙的均匀性和各向同性，但近期研究显示存在宇称奇性可观测量的破坏。这引发了一个问题：是否存在更微妙的数学偏好——例如对素数的偏向？受Shen2025发现宇称破缺的启发，我们探索星系群成员数量是否在统计上显著倾向于素数，可能揭示宇宙结构形成背后更深层的数学结构。

Method: We analyze the largest available galaxy group catalogs (e.g., from SDSS and DESI surveys), extracting the number of galaxies $N_{\rm gal}$ in each identified group or cluster. We compute the prime number occurrence rate and compare it to randomized null models that preserve the size distribution but randomize group membership. Statistical significance is assessed via bootstrap resampling and Monte Carlo simulations, while controlling for selection effects and completeness. Additionally, we explore correlations between $\zeta(s)$ (Riemann Zeta function) and spatial clustering patterns using harmonic analysis in logarithmic number space.

我们分析目前最大的星系群目录（如来自SDSS和DESI巡天的数据），提取每个已识别星系群或星系团中的星系数量$N_{\rm gal}$。计算素数出现率，并与保持大小分布但随机化成员分配的零模型进行比较。通过自助重采样和蒙特卡洛模拟评估统计显著性，同时控制选择效应和完备性。此外，我们在对数数量空间中使用谐波分析探索$\zeta(s)$（黎曼ζ函数）与空间成团模式之间的关联。

Result: We observe a statistically significant excess of galaxy groups with prime-numbered membership, exceeding 4.1$\sigma$ compared to null models. The effect persists across redshift bins and survey volumes. Furthermore, we detect a non-trivial correlation between the distribution of $N_{\rm gal}$ and the non-trivial zeros of the Riemann Zeta function $\zeta(s)$, particularly near the critical line $\Re(s) = 1/2$. This leads to the proposal of a new framework — Cosmozetaology — linking analytic number theory to large-scale structure.

我们观测到具有素数成员数量的星系群存在统计上显著的过剩，相比零模型超过4.1$\sigma$。该效应在不同红移区间和巡天体积中均存在。此外，我们检测到$N_{\rm gal}$分布与黎曼ζ函数$\zeta(s)$非平凡零点之间存在非平庸关联，尤其靠近临界线$\Re(s) = 1/2$。这促使我们提出一个新框架——Cosmozetaology，将解析数论与大尺度结构联系起来。

Conclusion: The cosmological principle may require extension into a higher-dimensional mathematical feature space where number-theoretic properties like primality play a physical role. The observed prime preference in galaxy group counts and its link to the Riemann Zeta function suggest a deep, previously unrecognized connection between fundamental mathematics and cosmological structure formation. This work lays the foundation for Cosmozetaology as a new interdisciplinary field at the intersection of number theory, quantum gravity, and observational cosmology.

宇宙学原理可能需要扩展到一个高维数学特征空间，在其中诸如素性等数论性质发挥物理作用。观测到的星系群计数中对素数的偏好及其与黎曼ζ函数的联系，暗示了基础数学与宇宙结构形成之间存在深刻且此前未被认识的关联。这项工作为Cosmozetaology奠定了基础，使其成为数论、量子引力与观测宇宙学交叉的一门新兴跨学科领域。

Abstract: The cosmological principle states that the universe is uniform and does not favor any specific position or direction. However, research conducted by \cite{Shen2025} has revealed that the universe demonstrates a notable inclination towards parity-odd states. Furthermore, it remains uncertain whether the universe also favors prime numbers. In this study, we examine the largest available catalogs of galaxy groups to investigate this hypothesis. Specifically, we assess whether the number of galaxies within a galaxy group or cluster is more likely to be a prime number. Our results strongly suggest that the universe does indeed have a preference for prime numbers, with findings exceeding the 4.1 sigma significance threshold. This insight explains why the Primes consistently triumphs over Unicorn. Consequently, it may be necessary to consider revising the cosmological principle in the context of a higher-dimensional feature space. Moreover, our research establishes a connection between the Riemann Zeta function and cosmology pioneeringly, paving the way for the development of Cosmozetaology.

</details>


### [85] [Robustness of cosmic void statistics: insights from SDSS DR7 and the ELUCID simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29706)
*Youcai Zhang,Xiaohu Yang,Hong Guo,Peng Wang,Feng Shi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: A systematic study of cosmic voids using SDSS DR7 galaxies and ELUCID simulation subhaloes reveals that void morphology (e.g., sphericity, triaxiality) is robust across different observational and simulation conditions, while size distributions and density profiles are sensitive to identification algorithms and tracer bias.

系统性地利用SDSS DR7星系和ELUCID模拟子晕分析宇宙空洞表明，空洞的形态学（如球形度、三轴性）在不同观测与模拟条件下具有鲁棒性，而尺寸分布和密度轮廓则对识别算法和示踪偏差敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To assess the reliability of cosmic void statistics in observations and simulations, particularly in light of redshift-space distortions (RSD), tracer bias, and algorithmic dependencies.

为了评估宇宙空洞统计量在观测与模拟中的可靠性，特别是考虑到红移空间畸变（redshift-space distortions, RSD）、示踪偏差（tracer bias）以及算法依赖性的影响。

Method: Applied two void-finding methods—\texttt{VoidFinder} (geometry-based) and watershed-based algorithms—on SDSS DR7 galaxies and ELUCID subhaloes in real space, redshift space, and reconstructed volumes. Used the \texttt{VAST} toolkit for consistent void identification and compared void properties including size distributions, radial density profiles, sphericity, and triaxiality.

在SDSS DR7星系和ELUCID子晕上应用了两种空洞识别方法——基于几何的\texttt{VoidFinder}和基于分水岭的算法，涵盖实空间、红移空间和重构体积；使用\texttt{VAST}工具包进行一致的空洞识别，并比较了空洞属性，包括尺寸分布、径向密度轮廓、球形度和三轴性。

Result: Void morphology (sphericity and triaxiality) is stable across different reconstructions and tracers, indicating robustness. Void size distributions and density profiles depend strongly on the algorithm: watershed methods yield larger voids and higher compensation walls than \texttt{VoidFinder}. Tracer bias significantly affects density profiles only for massive subhaloes ($>10^{11.5}\,h^{-1}{\rm M}_\odot$). High agreement between SDSS, ELUCID reconstruction, and full simulation confirms fidelity of constrained simulations.

空洞形态（球形度与三轴性）在不同重构与示踪器间稳定，表现出强鲁棒性；尺寸分布与密度轮廓则强烈依赖算法：分水岭法产生比\texttt{VoidFinder}更大的空洞和更高的补偿墙。示踪偏差仅对大质量子晕（$>10^{11.5}\,h^{-1}{\rm M}_\odot$）的密度轮廓有显著影响。SDSS、ELUCID重构与全模拟盒之间高度一致，验证了约束模拟的高保真度。

Conclusion: Cosmic void statistics exhibit a clear hierarchy of robustness: morphological properties are reliable across observational and simulation settings, while size and density measurements require careful consideration of algorithm choice and tracer bias. This supports the use of void morphology as a robust cosmological probe.

宇宙空洞统计量展现出明确的鲁棒性层级：形态学性质在不同观测与模拟设置下可靠，而尺寸与密度测量需谨慎考虑算法选择与示踪偏差。这支持将空洞形态作为稳健的宇宙学探针。

Abstract: We present a systematic analysis of the statistical properties of cosmic voids using galaxies from the Sloan Digital Sky Survey Data Release 7 (SDSS DR7) and subhaloes from the ELUCID constrained simulation. By comparing voids identified in redshift space, real space, and reconstructed volumes, we assess the impact of redshift-space distortions (RSD) and tracer bias. Using the \texttt{VAST} toolkit, we apply both the geometry-based \texttt{VoidFinder} algorithm and watershed-based methods. We find that void properties are not equally robust. The three-dimensional morphology of voids, quantified by their sphericity and triaxiality, remains stable across different reconstructions and tracer selections. In contrast, void size distributions and radial density profiles depend strongly on the identification algorithm, with watershed-based methods systematically producing larger voids and higher compensation walls than \texttt{VoidFinder}. Using the full ELUCID simulation box, we show that tracer bias mainly affects void density profiles, with noticeable changes only for the most massive subhaloes ($>10^{11.5}\,h^{-1}{\rm M}_\odot$). The agreement between SDSS observations, the ELUCID reconstruction, and the full simulation box demonstrates the high fidelity of constrained simulations and reveals a clear hierarchy in the robustness of void statistics.

</details>


### [86] [Dark radiation from Kerr primordial black holes: the role of superradiance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29790)
*Nayun Jia,Chen Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Light primordial black holes (PBHs) evaporating before BBN can produce dark radiation (DR) via Hawking radiation, particularly gravitons, contributing to $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$. However, if a beyond-the-Standard-Model (BSM) boson exists with Compton wavelength comparable to the PBH's gravitational radius, superradiant instabilities extract the BH's spin into a bosonic cloud, suppressing graviton emission and thus reducing $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$. While gravitational waves (GWs) from the cloud add DR, they only compensate significantly when superradiance and evaporation timescales match; otherwise, GWs are diluted by expansion. Consequently, existing $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ constraints on PBHs must be reevaluated in the presence of such BSM bosons.

轻的原初黑洞（PBH）若在大爆炸核合成（BBN）前完全蒸发，可通过霍金辐射产生暗辐射（DR），尤其是引力子，从而贡献有效相对论性粒子数 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$。然而，若存在超越标准模型（BSM）的玻色子，其康普顿波长与PBH引力半径相当，则超辐射不稳定性会将黑洞角动量提取为玻色云，抑制引力子产生，从而降低 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$。尽管该云发出的引力波（GW）可部分补偿暗辐射，但仅当超辐射与蒸发时标相近时才显著；否则引力波过早发射并被宇宙膨胀稀释。因此，在存在此类BSM玻色子时，必须重新评估基于 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ 的PBH质量与自旋限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Primordial black holes (PBHs) are candidate probes of early-universe physics and potential dark matter constituents. Light PBHs that evaporate before Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN) can leave imprints in the effective number of relativistic species ($N_{\rm eff}$) through Hawking radiation of gravitons. However, if the particle spectrum includes a light BSM boson, superradiant instabilities—driven by wave amplification around spinning BHs—can develop, extracting BH angular momentum into macroscopic bosonic clouds. This process modifies the standard Hawking evaporation picture, yet its impact on $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ has not been systematically studied. The motivation is to self-consistently include superradiance in the cosmological evolution of PBHs and assess how it alters DR predictions and observational bounds.

原初黑洞（PBH）是早期宇宙物理的探针及潜在暗物质候选者。在大爆炸核合成（BBN）前蒸发的轻PBH可通过霍金辐射引力子影响有效相对论性粒子数（$N_{\rm eff}$）。然而，若粒子谱中存在轻的超越标准模型（BSM）玻色子，超辐射不稳定性（由自旋黑洞周围的波放大驱动）可能发展，将黑洞角动量转化为宏观玻色云。这一过程改变了标准的霍金蒸发图景，但其对 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ 的影响尚未系统研究。本文动机在于自洽地将超辐射纳入PBH的宇宙学演化，评估其如何改变暗辐射预测及观测限制。

Method: The authors simultaneously solve coupled differential equations governing the cosmological evolution of: PBH mass and spin (including Hawking evaporation and superradiant angular momentum loss), occupation number of the superradiant bosonic mode, comoving entropy, and energy densities of radiation, dark radiation, and the superradiant cloud. They model the superradiant growth rate using analytical approximations from black hole perturbation theory, incorporating level transitions when modes become non-resonant due to BH mass/spin evolution. Gravitational wave emission from the cloud is included as a source of dark radiation. The full system is evolved from PBH formation until complete evaporation, and $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ is computed by comparing the final DR density to the cosmic neutrino background.

作者同时求解一组耦合微分方程，描述以下量的宇宙学演化：PBH质量与自旋（包括霍金蒸发与超辐射导致的角动量损失）、超辐射玻色模式的占据数、共动熵、以及辐射、暗辐射和超辐射云的能量密度。他们使用黑洞微扰理论中的解析近似来建模超辐射增长速率，并在由于黑洞质量/自旋演化导致模式失谐时引入能级跃迁。来自玻色云的引力波辐射被作为暗辐射源包含在内。整个系统从PBH形成演化至完全蒸发，通过将最终暗辐射密度与宇宙中微子背景比较来计算 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$。

Result: Superradiance generically suppresses $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ from PBHs by extracting angular momentum before it can be converted into gravitons via Hawking radiation. This 'starves' the dominant DR production channel. Gravitational waves from the superradiant cloud contribute an additional $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$, but this compensates only when the superradiant growth time and BH evaporation time are comparable. If superradiance occurs too early, the GWs are redshifted away by cosmic expansion; if too late, there is insufficient time for significant GW emission. For typical parameters, the net effect is a reduction in total $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ compared to models ignoring superradiance. Consequently, current observational bounds on PBH abundance based on $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ are weakened in the presence of light BSM bosons.

超辐射通常会抑制PBH产生的 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$，因为它在角动量通过霍金辐射转化为引力子之前就将其提取。这‘剥夺’了主导的暗辐射产生通道。来自超辐射云的引力波贡献额外的 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$，但仅当超辐射增长时标与黑洞蒸发时标相当时才能有效补偿。若超辐射发生过早，引力波会被宇宙膨胀红移稀释；若过晚，则无足够时间产生显著引力波。在典型参数下，总 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ 相比忽略超辐射的模型有所减少。因此，在存在轻BSM玻色子时，基于 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ 的当前PBH丰度观测限制被削弱。

Conclusion: The presence of light BSM bosons induces superradiant instabilities in spinning primordial black holes, which alter their evaporation products and suppress the dark radiation signal typically used to constrain them. As a result, $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ bounds on PBH mass and spin derived without accounting for superradiance are no longer valid and must be revised. This work highlights the importance of including quantum field theoretical effects like superradiance in early-universe cosmology when new light degrees of freedom are present, especially for interpreting cosmological observables in BSM scenarios.

轻BSM玻色子的存在会在自旋原初黑洞中引发超辐射不稳定性，改变其蒸发产物并抑制通常用于约束它们的暗辐射信号。因此，未考虑超辐射效应而得出的基于 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ 的PBH质量与自旋限制不再成立，必须加以修正。本工作强调了当存在新的轻自由度时，在早期宇宙宇宙学中包含诸如超辐射等量子场论效应的重要性，尤其在解释BSM情景下的宇宙学观测量时。

Abstract: Light primordial black holes (PBHs) that fully evaporate before Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN) produce dark radiation (DR) via Hawking radiation of gravitons, contributing to the effective number of relativistic species $ΔN_{\rm eff}$. If the particle spectrum contains a beyond-the-Standard-Model (BSM) boson with Compton wavelength comparable to the black hole (BH) gravitational radius, superradiant instability extracts angular momentum from the BH into a bosonic cloud, whose gravitational wave (GW) emission contributes an additional source of DR. By simultaneously evolving the BH mass and spin, superradiant mode occupation numbers, comoving entropy and cosmological energy densities in an expanding early-universe background, we find that superradiance generically suppresses $ΔN_{\rm eff}$: by extracting angular momentum before Hawking radiation can convert it into gravitons, superradiance starves the dominant dark-radiation channel. The GWs emitted by the superradiant cloud can partially compensate this loss, but only when the superradiant and BH evaporation timescales are comparable; otherwise the cloud GWs are emitted too early and diluted by cosmological expansion. The results imply that existing $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ bounds on PBH mass and spin derived without superradiance must be revisited if BSM bosons are present in the particle spectrum.

</details>


### [87] [CROCS Data Release I: Constraints on the Hubble Constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29879)
*Luke Weisenbach,Sophie L. Newman,Kieran Graham,Sai S. Dhavala,Benjamin Floyd,Neel Shah,Gemini 3 Flash,The CROCS Collaboration*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper claims to resolve the Hubble tension—a $5.5\sigma$ discrepancy in measurements of $H_0$ between Planck and SH0ES—by identifying "imperial biasing systematics" (IBS) arising from unit inconsistencies. Converting all data to metric units reconciles the values, yielding $H_0 = 69.00\pm0.420\,\text{km}\,\text{s}^{-1}\,\text{Mpc}^{-1}$, thus allegedly ending the tension.

本文声称通过发现“英制偏差系统性误差”（IBS）解决了哈勃张力——即普朗克与SH0ES在$H_0$测量上的$5.5\sigma$差异。通过将所有数据转换为公制单位，得到$H_0 = 69.00\pm0.420\,\text{km}\,\text{s}^{-1}\,\text{Mpc}^{-1}$，从而调和了高红移与低红移数据，据称彻底解决了该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Hubble tension represents a major challenge to the $\Lambda$CDM model, with persistent $5.5\sigma$ disagreement between early- and late-universe measurements of $H_0$. This motivates novel explanations, including potential hidden systematics. The CROCS collaboration was formed to explore interdisciplinary solutions without bias.

哈勃张力对$\Lambda$CDM模型构成重大挑战，早期宇宙（普朗克）与晚期宇宙（SH0ES）对$H_0$的测量存在持续的$5.5\sigma$分歧。这促使研究者探索新机制，包括潜在的隐藏系统误差。CROCS合作项目因此成立，旨在跨学科、无偏见地寻求解决方案。

Method: A statistical analysis of Planck and SH0ES data was performed, identifying what the authors call "Imperial Biasing Systematics" (IBS)—systematic errors due to the use of non-metric units in astronomical measurements. By converting all datasets to consistent metric units, the discrepancy is corrected. The analysis includes data from CROCS Data Release 1, based on $\sim3$ days and 27 minutes of observation.

对普朗克与SH0ES数据进行了统计分析，识别出所谓“英制偏差系统性误差”（IBS）——即天文学测量中使用非公制单位导致的系统误差。通过将所有数据集转换为一致的公制单位来修正此偏差。分析基于CROCS第一轮数据发布，对应约3天27分钟的观测。

Result: The IBS effect is detected at $5\sigma$ significance. After correction, the Hubble constant is measured as $H_0 = 69.00 \pm 0.420\,\text{km}\,\text{s}^{-1}\,\text{Mpc}^{-1}$, consistent with both original datasets when unit systematics are accounted for. The authors claim this resolves the Hubble tension.

IBS效应以$5\sigma$显著性被探测到。修正后，哈勃常数为$H_0 = 69.00 \pm 0.420\,\text{km}\,\text{s}^{-1}\,\text{Mpc}^{-1}$，在考虑单位系统误差后与原始数据集一致。作者声称这已解决哈勃张力。

Conclusion: The Hubble tension arises not from new physics or cosmological discrepancies, but from inconsistent unit usage across experiments. Converting all cosmological data to metric units eliminates the $5.5\sigma$ discrepancy, resolving the tension. The CROCS collaboration recommends universal adoption of SI units in cosmology.

哈勃张力并非源于新物理或宇宙学差异，而是因实验间单位使用不一致所致。将所有宇宙学数据转换为国际单位制（SI）可消除$5.5\sigma$差异，从而解决问题。CROCS合作组建议宇宙学界全面采用SI单位。

Abstract: Recent cosmological surveys and datasets have highlighted a variety of tensions to the concordance model of our universe, $Λ$CDM. Of particular interest is the Hubble tension, the $5.5σ$ discrepancy between measurements of the Hubble constant $H_0$ using high redshift CMB data from Planck ($67.27\pm0.60$km$\text{s}^{-1}\text{Mpc}^{-1}$) and low redshift supernovae from SH0ES ($73.2\pm1.3$km$\text{s}^{-1}\text{Mpc}^{-1}$). To avoid stepping on any toes, we have initiated the CROCS collaboration to resolve this tension, gathering experts from across many fields of cosmology, astrophysics, astronomy, machine learning, data science, philosophy, and astrology. In this paper, we present findings from CROCS Data Release 1, corresponding to the first $\sim3$ days and 27 minutes (rest frame) of observation. We perform a robust statistical analysis, showing that Planck and SH0ES both suffer from imperial biasing systematics (IBS) at $5σ$ significance. Accounting for these errors by converting to metric units reconciles the high and low redshift data, with $H_0 = 69.00\pm0.420$km$\text{s}^{-1}\text{Mpc}^{-1}$. We thus report that our results are sufficient to end the Hubble tension for good.

</details>


### [88] [Galactic Constellations in DESI DR1 and the Scales of Cosmological Homogeneity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29912)
*Claire Lamman*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We discover galactic constellations—visually recognizable shapes formed by galaxies—in DESI's first data release, including "Pisces Grandis," "The DESI Stick Woman," and "W," and develop a public platform to crowdsource constellation discovery; analysis of constellation sizes supports the cosmological principle and $\Lambda$-CDM.

我们发现了星系星座——由星系构成的视觉可辨识图案——位于DESI首批数据发布中，包括“大双鱼座”、“DESI火柴人”和“W”，并开发了一个公共平台以众包方式收集星座发现；对星座尺寸的分析支持宇宙学原理和$\Lambda$-CDM模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Modern large-scale structure surveys like DESI map vast volumes of the universe with unprecedented density and precision. While statistical analyses dominate cosmology, human pattern recognition remains powerful for exploring complex datasets. We aim to engage the public in scientific exploration and use identified patterns as an unconventional test of cosmic homogeneity.

像DESI这样的现代大尺度结构巡天以前所未有的密度和精度绘制了宇宙的广阔区域。尽管统计分析主导着宇宙学研究，人类的模式识别能力在探索复杂数据集方面仍然强大。我们的目标是让公众参与科学探索，并将识别出的模式作为宇宙均匀性的一种非传统检验手段。

Method: We visually inspect a dense subset of DESI's first data release (EDR and D1) in 3D using interactive visualization tools. Users of our public web platform (cmlamman.github.io/galactic-constellations) are invited to identify and submit constellations. We collect 93 such user-discovered configurations and analyze their angular and physical sizes, comparing the distribution to expectations from $\Lambda$-CDM simulations and random point distributions.

我们使用交互式可视化工具在三维空间中目视检查DESI首批数据（EDR和D1）的密集子集。我们邀请公共网络平台（cmlamman.github.io/galactic-constellations）的用户识别并提交星座。我们收集了93个由用户发现的构型，并分析它们的角度和物理尺寸，将其分布与$\Lambda$-CDM模拟和随机点分布的预期进行比较。

Result: We identify several striking visual constellations, including "Pisces Grandis" (a large arc resembling a fish), "The DESI Stick Woman", and "W". The website has enabled public participation, leading to 93 reported constellations. The size distribution of these constellations is statistically consistent with homogeneous random realizations under $\Lambda$-CDM, showing no evidence for anomalous clustering at macroscopic scales.

我们识别出多个显著的视觉星座，包括“大双鱼座”（一个类似鱼的大型弧形）、“DESI火柴人”和“W”。该网站促进了公众参与，已报告93个星座。这些星座的尺寸分布在统计上与$\Lambda$-CDM下的均匀随机实现一致，未显示出宏观尺度上的异常聚类证据。

Conclusion: Galactic constellations serve as a novel interface between cosmological data and public engagement. While primarily artistic and educational, the statistical properties of human-identified patterns provide an independent, albeit unconventional, consistency check of the cosmological principle and large-scale homogeneity predicted by $\Lambda$-CDM.

星系星座为宇宙学数据与公众参与之间提供了一种新颖的接口。虽然主要是艺术性和教育性的，但人类识别图案的统计特性为宇宙学原理以及$\Lambda$-CDM预测的大尺度均匀性提供了一项独立但非传统的自洽性检验。

Abstract: We present galactic constellations: charming shapes in large cosmological surveys. By exploring a dense subset of DESI's first data release, we discover distinctive constellations including "Pisces Grandis", "The DESI Stick Woman", and "W". We additionally develop a public website for anyone to explore DESI data, find their own constellations, and share their creations: see cmlamman.github.io/galactic-constellations. Early users of the site discovered 93 constellations. We analyze the size of these constellations as an unconventional probe of homogeneity, finding consistency with the cosmological principle and Lambda-CDM.

</details>


### [89] [Constraining Lyman-Werner Feedback from Velocity Acoustic Oscillations in the Cosmic Dawn 21 cm Signal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29947)
*Xi Du,Bin Yue,Furen Deng,Yidong Xu,Yan Gong,Ely D. Kovetz,Xuelei Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study explores the use of Velocity Acoustic Oscillation (VAO) features in the 21 cm power spectrum as a probe of Lyman-Werner (LW) feedback during Cosmic Dawn. Using semi-numerical simulations and a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN), the authors show that VAO wiggles can accurately recover LW feedback efficiency in noise-free conditions, though SKA-low observations require very long integration times ($>10^4$ hours) for meaningful constraints.

本研究探讨了利用宇宙黎明时期21厘米功率谱中的速度声学振荡（VAO）特征作为莱曼- Werner （LW）反馈的探针。通过半数值模拟和卷积神经网络（CNN），作者表明在无噪声条件下，VAO振荡可以准确恢复LW反馈效率，尽管SKA-low观测需要超过$10^4$小时的积分时间才能获得有意义的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lyman-Werner (LW) radiation from Population III stars regulates star formation by dissociating H$_2$, but its feedback efficiency is poorly constrained due to lack of direct observations. The dark matter-baryon relative velocity imprints VAO features in the 21 cm power spectrum, which are sensitive to the minimum halo mass for cooling—making them a potential indirect probe of LW feedback. This work aims to assess whether VAO signatures can be used to constrain LW feedback parameters.

第三星族星发出的莱曼- Werner （LW）辐射通过解离H$_2$来调节恒星形成，但由于缺乏直接观测，其反馈效率仍不明确。暗物质与重子之间的相对速度会在21厘米功率谱中留下VAO特征，这些特征对冷却所需的最小晕质量敏感，使其成为LW反馈的潜在间接探针。本研究旨在评估是否可以利用VAO信号来限制LW反馈参数。

Method: We employ semi-numerical 21 cm lightcone simulations to model the 21 cm signal during Cosmic Dawn under varying LW feedback strengths. We compute the multi-frequency angular power spectrum (MAPS) to isolate VAO features and train a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) to infer the LW feedback efficiency and baseline cooling threshold. Instrumental effects for the SKA-low AA* configuration are considered under optimistic foreground removal assumptions.

我们采用半数值21厘米光锥模拟，在不同LW反馈强度下建模宇宙黎明时期的21厘米信号。计算多频角功率谱（MAPS）以分离VAO特征，并训练卷积神经网络（CNN）推断LW反馈效率和基线冷却阈值。考虑了SKA-low AA*配置下的仪器效应，并基于乐观的前景消除假设进行分析。

Result: In the absence of instrumental noise, the CNN accurately recovers the LW feedback efficiency from VAO features. However, when instrumental noise and realistic observational settings are included (SKA-low AA*), meaningful constraints on LW feedback require integration times exceeding $10^4$ hours, even under optimistic foreground subtraction. The VAO signal is strongly suppressed if LW feedback raises the minimum halo mass above the streaming-sensitive regime.

在无仪器噪声的情况下，CNN能够从VAO特征中准确恢复LW反馈效率。然而，当包含仪器噪声和实际观测条件（SKA-low AA*）时，即使在乐观的前景扣除假设下，要对LW反馈施加有意义的约束仍需超过$10^4$小时的积分时间。如果LW反馈将最小晕质量提升至高于流动敏感区域，则VAO信号会显著被抑制。

Conclusion: Velocity Acoustic Oscillations (VAO) in the 21 cm power spectrum provide a physically robust signature of early star formation processes and are highly sensitive to LW feedback. While current radio interferometers like SKA-low face significant observational challenges, VAO features remain a promising pathway toward indirectly constraining Pop III star formation and radiative feedback during Cosmic Dawn.

21厘米功率谱中的速度声学振荡（VAO）为早期恒星形成过程提供了物理上稳健的特征，且对LW反馈高度敏感。尽管当前如SKA-low等射电干涉仪面临重大观测挑战，VAO特征仍是间接约束宇宙黎明时期第三星族星形成及辐射反馈的有前途途径。

Abstract: During Cosmic Dawn, Pop III stars could be formed in minihalos through molecular hydrogen (H$_2$) cooling. The minimum halo mass required for H$_2$ cooling is highly sensitive to Lyman-Werner (LW) radiation, which dissociates H$_2$ and regulates star formation. However, the efficiency of LW feedback remains poorly constrained due to the lack of direct observations of Pop III stars. The dark matter-baryon relative streaming velocity suppresses star formation in low-mass halos and imprints characteristic Velocity Acoustic Oscillation (VAO) features in the 21 cm power spectrum. These features are particularly sensitive to the cooling threshold mass: if LW feedback raises the minimum halo mass above the streaming-sensitive regime, the VAO signal is strongly suppressed. This makes the VAO wiggles a promising indirect probe of LW feedback during Cosmic Dawn. We investigate the feasibility of constraining LW feedback parameters using semi-numerical 21 cm lightcone simulations. We compute the multi-frequency angular power spectrum (MAPS) to isolate the VAO features and train a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) to infer the LW feedback efficiency and the baseline cooling threshold. We find that in the absence of instrumental noise, the LW feedback efficiency can be accurately recovered from the VAO features. However, for the SKA-low AA* configuration, meaningful constraints require integration times exceeding $10^4$ hours under optimistic foreground assumptions. Nonetheless, our results demonstrate that VAO features provide a physically robust and potentially powerful probe of LW feedback at Cosmic Dawn.

</details>
